<p>41b.5</p>dang / /sring mo'i 'du shes bskyed bgyi chags gyur na/ /mi gtsang nyid du yang dag bsam par bgyi/ /g.yo ba'i sems ni thos mtshungs bu lta bur/ /gter bzhin srog dang 'dra bar bsrung bgyi ste/ /gdug pa dug dang mtshon dang dgra bo dang / /me bzhin 'dod pa'i bde la yid 'byung
<p>41b.6</p>mdzod/ /'dod pa rnams ni phung khrol bskyed pa ste/ /rgyal ba'i dbang pos kim+pa'i 'bras 'drar gsungs/ /de dag spang bgyi de yi lcags sgrog gis/ /'khor ba'i btson rar 'jig rten 'di dag bcings/ /gang dag dbang po drug yul rnams la ni/ /rtag tu mi brten g.yo dang gang dag
<p>41b.7</p>cig /g.yul ngor dgra tshogs las rgyal de dag las/ /mkhas rnams dang po dpa' rab lags par 'tshal/ /bud med gzhon nu'i lus ni logs shig tu/ /dri nga ba dang sgo dgu dod pa dang / /mi gtsang kun snod 'dra ba dgang dka' dang / /pags pas g.yogs dang rgyan yang
<p>42a</p>
<p>42a.1</p>logs shig gzigs/ /ji ltar mdze can srin bus nyen pa ni/ /bde ba'i don du me la kun bstan kyang / /zhi bar mi 'gyur de dang 'dra bar ni/ /'dod pa rnams la chags pa'ang mkhyen par mdzod/ /don dam gzigs par bgyi slad dngos rnams la/ /tshul
<p>42a.2</p>bzhin yid la bgyid pa de goms mdzod/ /de dang 'dra bar yon tan ldan pa yi / /chos gzhan 'ga' yang mchis pa ma lags so/ /skyes bu rigs gzugs thos dang ldan rnams kyang / /shes rab tshul khrims bral ba bkur ma lags/ /de ltas gang la yon tan 'di gnyis
<p>42a.3</p>ldan/ /de ni yon tan gzhan dang bral yang mchod/ /'jig rten mkhyen pa rnyed dang ma rnyed dang / /bde dang mi bde snyan dang mi snyan dang / /bstod smad ces bgyi 'jig rten chos brgyad po/ /bdag gi yid yul min par mgo snyoms mdzod/ /khyod kyis bram ze dge slong lha dang ni/ /
<p>42a.4</p>mgron dang yab yum dag dang btsun mo dang / /'khor gyi slad du'ang sdig pa mi bgyi ste/ /dmyal ba'i rnam smin skal nod 'ga' ma mchis/ /sdig pa'i las rnams spyad pa 'ga' yang ni/ /de yi mod la mtshon bzhin mi gcod kyang / /'chi ba'i dus la bab na sdig pa yi/ /las kyi
<p>42a.5\] 'bras bu gang lags mngon par 'gyur/ /dad dang tshul khrims thos dang gtong ba dang / /dri med ngo tsha shes dang khrel yod dang / /shes rab nor bdun lags par thub pas gsungs/ /nor gzhan phal pa don ma mchis rtogs mdzod/ /rgyan po 'gyed dang 'dus la lta ba dang / /le lo
<p>42a.6</p>sdig pa'i grogs la brten pa dang / /chang dang mtshan mo rgyu ba ngan song ba/ /grags pa nyams par 'gyur ba de drug spang / /nor rnams kun gyi nang na chog shes pa/ /rab mchog lags par lha mi'i ston pas gsungs/ /kun tu chog shes mdzod cig chog mkhyen na/ /nor mi
<p>42a.7</p>bdog kyang yang dag 'byor pa lags/ /des pa bdog mang ji ltar sdug bsngal ba/ /'dod pa chung rnams de lta ma lags te/ /klu mchog rnams la mgo bo ji snyed pa/ /de las byung ba'i sdug bsngal de snyed do/ /rang bzhin dgrar 'brel gshed ma lta bu dang / /khyim thab brnyas 
<p>42b</p>
<p>42b.1</p>bgyid rje mo lta bu dang / /chung ngu'ang rku ba chom rkun lta bu yi/ /chung ma gsum po de dag rnam par spang / /sring mo lta bur rjes mthun gang yin dang / /mdza' mo bzhin du snying la 'bab pa dang / /ma bzhin phan par 'dod dang bran mo bzhin/ /dbang gyur gang yin rigs kyi lha bzhin
<p>42b.2</p>bkur/ /kha zas sman dang 'dra bar rigs pa yis/ /'dod chags zhe sdang med par bsten bgyi ste/ /rgyags phyir ma lags bsnyems pa'i phyir ma lags/ /'tshag phyir ma lags lus gnas 'ba' zhig phyir/ /rig pa'i bdag nyid nyin par mtha' dag dang / /mtshan mo thun gyi stod smad
<p>42b.3</p>bzlas nas ni/ /mnal tshe'ang 'bras bu med par mi 'gyur bar/ /dran dang ldan par de dag bar du mnol/ /byams dang snying rje dag dang dga' ba dang / /btang snyoms rtag tu yang dag bsgom mdzod cig /gong ma brnyes par ma gyur de lta na'ang / /tshangs pa'i 'jig rten bde ba thob
<p>42b.4</p>par 'gyur/ /'dod spyod dga' dang bde dang sdug bsngal dag /rnam par spangs pa'i bsam gtan bzhi po yis/ /tshangs dang 'od gsal dag dang dge rgyas dang / /'bras bu che lha rnams dang skal mnyam thob / /rtag dang mngon par zhen dang gnyen po med/ /yon tan gtso ldan bzhi
<p>42b.5\] las byung ba'i las/ /dge dang mi dge rnam lnga chen po ste/ /de bas dge ba spyod la brtson par bgyi/ /lan tshwa srang 'gas chu ni nyung ngu zhig /ro bskyur bgyid kyi gang+gA'i klung min ltar/ /de bzhin sdig pa'i las ni chung ngu yang / /dge ba'i rtsa ba yang la mkhyen par bgyi/ /rgod
<p>42b.6</p>dang 'gyod dang gnod sems rmugs pa dang / /gnyid dang 'dod la 'dun dang the tshom ste/ /sgrib pa lnga po 'di dag dge ba'i nor/ /'phrog pa'i chom rkun lags par mkhyen par mdzod/ /dad dang brtson 'grus dag dang dran pa dang / /ting 'dzin shes rab chos mchog lnga nyid de/ /
<p>42b.7</p>'di la mngon brtson mdzod cig 'di dag ni/ /stobs dbang zhes bgyi rtse mor gyur pa'ang lags/ /na rga 'chi sdug bral dang de bzhin du/ /las ni bdag gir byas las ma 'das zhes/ /de ltar yang dang yang du sems pa ni/ /de yi gnyen po'i sgo nas rgyags mi 'gyur/ /
<p>43a</p>
<p>43a.1</p>gal te mtho ris thar pa mngon bzhed na/ /yang dag lta la goms pa nyid du mdzod/ /gang zag log par lta bas legs spyad kyang / /thams cad rnam par smin pa mi bzad ldan/ /mi ni yang dag nyid du mi bde zhing / /mi rtag bdag med mi gtsang rig par bgyi/ /dran pa nye bar
<p>43a.2</p>ma bzhag rnams kyis ni/ /phyin ci log bzhir lta ba phung khrol ba/ /gzugs ni bdag ma yin zhes gsungs te bdag /gzugs dang mi ldan gzugs la bdag gnas min/ /bdag la gzugs mi gnas te de bzhin du/ /phung po lhag ma bzhi yang stong rtogs bgyi/ /phung po 'dod rgyal
<p>43a.3</p>las min dus las min/ /rang bzhin las min ngo bo nyid las min/ /dbang phyug las min rgyu med can min te/ /mi shes las dang sred las byung rig mdzod/ /tshul khrims brtul zhugs mchog 'dzin rang lus la/ /phyin ci log par lta dang the tshom ste/ /kun du sbyor ba 'di gsum thar pa yi/ /
<p>43a.4</p>grong khyer sgo 'gegs lags par mkhyen par gyis/ /thar pa bdag la rag las 'di la ni/ /gzhan gyis grogs bgyir ci yang ma mchis pas/ /thos dang tshul khrims bsam gtan ldan pa yis / /bden pa rnam pa bzhi la 'bad par mdzod/ /lhag pa'i tshul khrims lhag pa'i shes rab
<p>43a.5</p>dang / /lhag pa'i sems la rtag tu bslab par bgyi/ /bslab pa brgya rtsa lnga bcu lhag cig ni/ /gsum po 'di nang yang dag 'du bar 'gyur/ /dbang phyug lus rtog dran pa bde gshegs kyis/ /bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam du nye bar bstan/ /de ni bsgrims nas mngon par bsrung bgyi ste/ /
<p>43a.6</p>dran pa nyams pas chos kun 'jig par 'gyur/ /tshe ni gnod mang rlung gis btab pa yi/ /chu yi chu bur bas kyang mi rtag na/ /dbugs rngub dbugs 'byung gnyid kyis log pa las/ /sad khom gang lags de ni ngo mtshar che/ /lus mtha' thal ba mthar skam mthar 'drul zhing / /tha
<p>43a.7</p>mar mi gtsang snying po ma mchis pa/ /rnam par 'jig dengs myags par 'gyur ba ste/ /so sor 'gyes chos can du mkhyen par mdzod/ /sa dang lhun po rgya mtsho nyi ma bdun/ /'bar bas bsregs pa'i lus can 'di dag kyang / /thal ba yang ni lus par mi 'gyur na/ /shin tu nyam chung mi lta
<p>43b</p>
<p>43b.1</p>smos ci 'tshal/ /de ltar 'di kun mi rtag bdag med de/ /skyabs med mgon med gnas med de slad du/ /'khor ba chu shing snying po med pa las / /mi mchog khyod kyi thugs ni dbyung bar mdzod/ /rgya mtsho gcig gnas gnya' shing bu ga dang / /rus sbal phrad pa bas kyang dud 'gro las/ /mi nyid
<p>43b.2</p>ches thob dka' bas mi dbang gis/ /dam chos spyod pas de 'bras mchis par mdzod/ /gang zhig gser snod rin chen spras pa yis/ /ngan skyugs 'phyags par bgyid pa de bas ni/ /gang zhig mi ru skyes nas sdig pa dag /bgyid pa de ni ches rab blun pa lags/ /mthun par gyur pa'i
<p>43b.3</p>yul du gnas pa dang / /skyes bu dam pa la ni brten pa dang / /bdag nyid legs smon sngon yang bsod nams bgyis / /'khor lo chen po bzhi ni khyod la mnga'/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa tshangs par spyod/ /yongs su rdzogs pa thub pas gsungs de'i phyir/ /skyes bu dam pa
<p>43b.4</p>bstan bgyi rgyal ba la/ /brten nas rab tu mang pos zhi ba thob/ /log par lta ba 'dzin dang dud 'gro dang / /yi dwags nyid dang dmyal bar skye ba dang / /rgyal ba'i bka' med pa dang mtha' 'khob tu / /kla klor skye dang glen zhing lkugs pa nyid/ /tshe ring lha nyid gang yang rung bar ni/ /skye ba zhes
<p>43b.5</p>bgyi mi khom skyon brgyad po/ /de dag dang bral khom pa rnyed nas ni/ /skye ba bzlog pa'i slad du 'bad par mdzod/ /des pa 'dod pas phongs dang 'chi ba dang / /na dang rga sogs sdug bsngal du ma yi/ /'byung gnas 'khor ba la ni skyo mdzad cing / /'di yi nyes pa'i shas kyang gsan par
<p>43b.6</p>mdzod/ /pha ni bu nyid ma ni chung ma nyid/ /skye bo dgrar gyur pa dag bshes nyid dang / /bzlog pa nyid du mchi bas de slad du/ /'khor ba dag na nges pa 'ga' ma mchis/ /re res rgya mtsho bzhi bas lhag pa yi/ /'o ma 'thungs te da dung so so yi/ /skye bo'i rjes su 'brang ba'i 'khor ba pas/ /
<p>43b.7</p>de bas chos mang nyid cig btung 'tshal lo/ /re re'i bdag nyid rus pa'i phung po ni/ /lhun po mnyam pa snyed cig 'das gyur te/ /ma yi thug mtha' rgya shug tshi gu tsam/ /ri lur bgrangs kyang sa yis lang mi 'gyur/ /brgya byin 'jig rten mchod 'os gyur nas ni / /las kyi dbang gis phyir yang
<p>44a</p>
<p>44a.1</p>sa steng lhung / /'khor los sgyur ba nyid du gyur nas kyang / /'khor ba dag tu yang bran nyid du 'gyur/ /mtho ris bu mo'i nu ma rked pa la/ /reg pa'i bde ba yun ring myong nas slar/ /dmyal bar 'thag gcod dbang ba'i 'khrul 'khor gyis / /reg pa shin tu mi bzad bsten
<p>44a.2</p>'tshal lo/ /rkang pa'i reg pas nem par bde bzod pa/ /lhun po'i spo la yun ring gnas nas ni/ /slar yang me mur ro myag rgyu ba yi/ /sdug bsngal mi bzad phog snyam bgyid 'tshal lo/ /mtho ris bu mos 'brongs shing dga' ba dang / /rnam par mdzes 'tshal son par rtses nas slar/ /
<p>44a.3</p>'dab ma ral gri 'dra tshal nags rnams kyis/ /rkang lag rna ba sna gcod 'thob par 'gyur/ /dal gyis 'bab pa lha yi bu mo ni/ /gdong mdzes gser gyi pad+ma lhan bzhugs nas/ /slar yang dmyal ba'i chu bo rab med par/ /tsha sgo bzod brlag chu tshan 'jug 'tshal lo/ /lha
<p>44a.4</p>yul 'dod bde shin tu chen po dang / /tshangs nyid chags bral bde ba thob nas slar/ /mnar med me yi bud shing gyur pa yi / /sdug bsngal rgyun mi 'chad pa bstan 'tshal lo/ /nyi ma zla ba nyid thob rang lus kyi/ /'od kyis 'jig rten mtha' dag snang byas te/ /slar yang mun nag smag
<p>44a.5</p>tu phyin gyur nas/ /rang gi lag pa brkyang ba'ang mi mthong 'gyur/ /de ltar nongs par 'gyur 'tshal bsod nams ni/ /rnam gsum mar me'i snang ba rab bzhes shig /gcig pu nyi ma zla bas mi brdzi ba'i/ /mun nag mtha' yas nang du 'jug 'tshal lo/ /sems can nyes par spyad
<p>44a.6</p>pa spyod rnams la/ /yang sos thig nag rab tu tsha ba dang / /bsdus 'joms ngu 'bod mnar med la sogs pa'i/ /dmyal ba rnams su rtag tu sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /kha cig til bzhin 'tshir te de bzhin gzhan/ /phye ma zhib mo bzhin du phye mar rlog /kha cig sog les 'dra ste de
<p>44a.7</p>bzhin gzhan/ /sta re mi bzad so rnon rnams kyis gshags/ /de bzhin gzhan dag khro chu bzhu ba yi/ /khu ba 'bar ba 'khrigs pa ldud par bgyid/ /kha cig lcags kyi gsal shing rab 'bar ba / /tsher ma can la kun du rgyud par bgyid/ /kha cig lcags kyi mche ba ldan pa'i khyi/ /
<p>44b</p>
<p>44b.1</p>gtum pos dbad cing lag pa gnam du bsgreng / /dbang med gzhan dag lcags mchu rnon po dang / /sen mo mi bzad ldan pa'i khwa rnams 'thog /kha cig srin bu sbur ba sna tshogs dang / /sha sbrang sbrang bu mchu rings khri phrag dag /reg na mi bzad rma srol cher 'byin pas/ /za bar bgyid
<p>44b.2</p>cing 'gre ldog smre sngags 'don/ /kha cig mdag me 'bar ba'i tshogs su ni/ /rgyun mi 'chad par rab bsreg kha yang bgrad / /kha cig lcags las byas pa'i zangs chen du/ /spyi'u tshugs 'bras kyi cung 'phed bzhin du 'tshed/ /sdig can dbugs 'byung 'gags pa tsam zhig
<p>44b.3</p>gi /dus kyis bar du chod rnams dmyal ba yi/ /sdug bsngal gzhal yas thos nas rnam stong du/ /mi 'jig gang lags rdo rje'i rang bzhin no/ /dmyal ba bris pa mthong dang thos pa dang / /dran dang bklags dang gzugs su bgyis rnams kyang / /'jigs pa skye bar 'gyur
<p>44b.4</p>na mi bzad pa'i/ /rnam smin nyams su myong na smos ci 'tshal/ /bde ba kun gyi nang na sred zad pa/ /bde ba'i bdag por bgyid pa ji lta bar/ /de bzhin sdug bsngal kun gyi nang na ni/ /mnar med dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal rab mi bzad/ /'di na nyin gcig mdung thung sum brgya yis/ /rab
<p>44b.5</p>tu drag btab sdug bsngal gang lags pa/ /des ni dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal chung ngu la'ang / /'ol yang mi bgyid char yang mi phod do/ /de ltar sdug bsngal shin tu mi bzad lo/ /bye ba phrag brgyar nyams su myong yang ni/ /ji srid mi dge de zad ma gyur pa/ /de srid srog dang 'bral bar mi
<p>44b.6</p>'gyur ro/ /mi dge'i 'bras 'di rnams kyi sa bon ni/ /lus ngag yid kyi nyes spyad khyod kyis ni/ /ci nas de rdul tsam yang ma mchis pa/ /de ltar nyid kyi rtsal gyis 'bad par mdzod/ /dud 'gro'i skye gnas na yang gsod pa dang / /bcings dang brdeg sogs sdug bsngal sna tshogs
<p>44b.7</p>pa/ /zhi 'gyur dge ba spangs pa rnams la ni/ /gcig la gcig za shin tu mi bzad pa/ /kha cig mu tig bal dang rus pa dang / /sha dang pags pa'i ched du 'chi bar 'gyur/ /dbang med gzhan dag rdog pa lag pa dang / /lcags dang lcags kyu 'debs pas btab ste bkol/ /
<p>45a</p>
<p>45a.1</p>yi dwags na yang 'dod pas phongs pa yis / /bskyed pa'i sdug bsngal rgyun chags mi 'chos pa/ /bkres skom grang dro ngal dang 'jigs pa yis/ /bskyed pa shin tu mi bzad bsten 'tshal lo/ /kha cig kha ni khab kyi mig tsam la/ /lto ba ri yi gtos
<p>45a.2</p>tsam bkres pas nyen/ /mi gtsang gyi nar bor ba cung zad kyang / /'tshal ba'i mthu dang ldan pa ma lags so/ /kha cig pags rus lus shing gcer bu ste / /ta la'i yang tog bskams pa lta bu lags/ /kha cig mtshan zhing kha nas 'bar ba ste/ /zas su 'bar ba'i khar babs
<p>45a.3</p>bye ma 'tshal/ /smad rigs 'ga' ni rnag dang phyi sa dang / /khrag sogs mi gtsang ba yang mi rnyed de/ /phan tshun gdong du 'tshog cing mgrin pa nas/ /lba ba byung ba smin pa'i rnag 'tshal lo/ /yi dwags rnams la sos ka'i dus su ni/ /zla ba'ang tsha la dgun ni nyi ma'ang grang / /
<p>45a.4</p>ljon shing 'bras bu med 'gyur 'di dag gis/ /bltas pa tsam gyis klung yang bskam par 'gyur/ /bar chad med par sdug bsngal rten gyur pa/ /nyes par spyad pa'i las kyi zhags pa ni/ /sra bas bcings pa'i lus can kha cig lo/ /lnga stong dag dang khrir yang 'chi mi 'gyur/ /
<p>45a.5</p>de ltar yi dwags rnams kyis sna tshogs pa'i/ /sdug bsngal ro gcig thob pa gang lags pa/ /de yi rgyu ni skye bo 'jungs dga' ba/ /ser sna 'phags min lags par sangs rgyas gsungs / /mtho ris na yang bde chen de dag gi /'chi 'pho'i sdug bsngal nyid ni de bas che/ /de
<p>45a.6</p>ltar bsams nas ya rabs rnams kyis ni/ /zad 'gyur mtho ris slad du sred mi bgyi/ /lus kyi kha dog mi sdug 'gyur ba dang / /stan la mi dga' me tog phreng rnying dang / /gos la dri ma chags dang lus las ni/ /sngon chad med pa'i rngul 'byung zhes bgyi ba/ /mtho ris 'chi
<p>45a.7</p>'pho sbron bgyid 'chi ltas lnga/ /lha yul gnas pa'i lha rnams la 'byung ste/ /sa steng mi rnams 'chi bar 'gyur ba dag /sbron par byed pa'i 'chi ltas rnams dang 'dra/ /lha yi 'jig rten dag nas 'phos pa la/ /gal te dge ba'i lhag ma 'ga' med na/ /de nas dbang med
<p>45b</p>
<p>45b.1</p>dud 'gro yi dwags dang / /dmyal bar gnas pa gang yang rung bar 'gyur/ /lha min dag na'ang rang bzhin gyis lha yi/ /dpal la sdang phyir yid kyi sdug bsngal che/ /de dag blo dang ldan yang 'gro ba yi/ /sgrib pas bden pa mthong ba ma mchis so/ /'khor ba de 'dra lags pas
<p>45b.2</p>lha mi dang / /dmyal ba yi dwags dud 'gro rnams dag tu/ /skye ba bzang po ma lags skye ba ni/ /gnod pa du ma'i snod gyur lags mkhyen mdzod/ /mgo 'am gos la glo bur me shor na/ /de dag bzlog phyir bgyi ba btang nas kyang / /yang srid med par bgyi slad 'bad 'tshal te/ /de 
<p>45b.3</p>bas ches mchog dgos pa gzhan ma mchis/ /tshul khrims dag dang bsam gtan shes rab kyis / /mya ngan 'das zhi dul ba dri med pa'i/ /go 'phang mi rga mi 'chi zad mi 'tshal/ /sa chu me rlung nyi zla bral thob mdzod/ /dran dang chos rab 'byed dang brtson 'grus dang / /dga' dang shin tu
<p>45b.4</p>sbyangs dang ting 'dzin dang / /btang snyoms 'di bdun byang chub yan lag ste/ /mya ngan 'das thob bgyid pa'i dge tshogs lags/ /shes rab med par bsam gtan yod min te/ /bsam gtan med par yang ni shes rab med/ /gang la de nyid yod pas srid pa yi/ /rgya mtsho gnag
<p>45b.5</p>rjes lta bur 'tshal bar bgyi/ /lung ma bstan pa bcu bzhi 'jig rten na/ /nyi ma'i gnyen gyis rab gsungs gang dag lags/ /de dag rnams la bsam par mi bgyi ste/ /de yis blo ni zhi bar bgyid ma lags/ /ma rig pa las las te de las ni/ /rnam shes de las ming dang
<p>45b.6</p>gzugs rab 'byung / /de las skye mched drug ste de las ni / /reg pa kun du 'byung bar thub pas gsungs/ /reg pa las ni tshor ba kun 'byung ste/ /tshor ba'i gzhi las sred pa 'byung bar 'gyur/ /sred pas len pa bskyed par 'gyur ba ste/ /de las srid pa srid las skye ba
<p>45b.7</p>lags/ /skye ba yod na mya ngan na rga dang / /'dod pas phongs dang 'chi dang 'jigs sogs kyi/ /sdug bsngal phung po shin tu che 'byung ste/ /skye ba 'gags pas 'di kun 'gag par 'gyur/ /rten cing 'brel par 'byung 'di rgyal ba yi/ /gsung gi mdzod kyi gces pa zab
<p>46a</p>
<p>46a.1</p>mo ste/ /gang gis 'di ni yang dag mthong ba des / /sangs rgyas de nyid rig pas rnam mchog mthong / /yang dag lta dang 'tsho dang rtsol ba dang / /dran dang ting 'dzin dag dang las mtha' dag /yang dag rtog nyid lam gyi yan lag brgyad/ /'di ni zhi bar bgyi
<p>46a.2</p>slad bsgom par bgyi / /skye 'di sdug bsngal sred pa zhes bgyi ba/ /de ni de yi kun 'byung rgya chen te/ /'di 'gog pa ni thar pa lags te de/ /'thob bgyid 'phags lam yan lag de brgyad lags/ /de ltar 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi po dag /mthong bar bgyi slad rtag tu brtson
<p>46a.3</p>par bgyi/ /pang na dpal gnas khyim pa rnams kyis kyang / /shes pas nyon mongs chu bo las brgal gyi/ /gang dag chos mngon bgyis pa de dag kyang / /gnam las babs pa ma lags lo tog bzhin/ /sa rum las 'thon ma lags de dag sngon/ /nyon mongs rag las so
<p>46a.4</p>so'i skye bor bas/ /bsnyengs dang bral la mang du gsol ci 'tshal/ /phan pa'i gdams ngag don po 'di lags te/ /khyod kyis thugs dul mdzod cig bcom ldan gyis/ /sems ni chos kyi rtsa ba lags par gsungs/ /khyod la de skad gdams pa gang lags de/ /bas par
<p>46a.5</p>dge slong gis kyang bgyi bar dka'/ /'di la gang zhig spyod pa'i ngo bo de'i/ /yon tan bstan pas sku tshe don yod mdzod/ /kun gyi dge ba kun la yi rang zhing / /nyid kyi legs par spyad pa rnam gsum yang / /sangs rgyas nyid thob bgyi slad yongs bsngos nas/ /de nas dge
<p>46a.6</p>ba'i phung po 'di yis khyod/ /skye ba dpag tu med par lha mi yi/ /'jig rten kun gyi rnal 'byor dbang mdzad nas/ /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang spyod pa yis/ /'gro ba nyam thag mang po rjes bzung ste/ /'khrungs nas na rga 'dod chags zhe sdang rnams/ /bsal te
<p>46a.7</p>sangs rgyas zhing du bcom ldan 'das/ /'od dpag med dang 'dra bar 'jig rten gyi/ /mgon po sku tshe dpag tu med par mdzod/ /shes rab tshul khrims gtong 'byung grags chen dri ma med/ /lha yul nam mkha' dang ni sa steng rgyas mdzad nas/ /sa la mi dang mtho ris lha ni
<p>46b</p>
<p>46b.1</p>na chung mchog /bde dgas dga' ba nges par rab tu zhi mdzad de/ /nyon mongs nyam thag sems can tshogs kyi 'jigs skye dang / /'chi ba zhi mdzad rgyal ba'i dbang po nyid brnyes nas/ /'jig rten las 'das ming tsam zhi la mi bsnyengs pa/ /mi bgres nongs pa mi mnga'i go 'phang
<p>46b.2</p>brnyes par mdzod/ /bshes pa'i spring yig slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ /mdza' bo rgyal po bde spyod la bskur ba rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nya de ba dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban de dpal brtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab
<p>46b.3</p>pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ shri Sh+ya le kha/ bod skad du/ slob ma la springs pa'i spring yig /dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gis mdzad pa shin tu dka' spyad sngon byung ba/ /mi'am ci dang lha mo rnams kyis rab bsnyad na/ /bdud kyi bu mo
<p>46b.4</p>bzhin ras pad+ma'i nags tshal dag /da ltar zla ba'i zer gyis phog pa bzhin du zum/ /bkra shis yid 'ong shin tu rmad byung sku mnga' ba/ /bsod nams chung ngu'i skye bos mthong ba rnyed dka' ba/ /'jig rten mngon par 'dod pa'i re ba bsgrub pa gang / /yid bzhin nor bu lta bur gzhan don
<p>46b.5</p>ro gcig spyod/ /gang zhig rtag tu pha rol bde bas bde 'gyur zhing / /gzhan dag sdug bsngal gyur pas mchog tu 'o brgyal ba/ /thugs rje chen pos yon tan shin tu bskrun pa gang / /de nyid rang gi bde sdug spangs te bzhugs pa yin/ /gang zhig gzhan gyi don du dbu rnams gcod
<p>46b.6</p>byed kyang / /pad+ma lta bur dgyes pa'i spyan 'byed gzigs mdzad cing / /nyid kyi don du gdugs dkar gcig gis khebs pa lta'i/ /sa yang ral gri so bdar rnon po lta bur dgongs/ /zla ba yar gyi ngo ltar yon tan gsal ba rdzogs/ /nyes pa'i mun pa sel mdzad gcig pu yid
<p>46b.7</p>du 'ong / /'jig rten phan la brtson pa rab tu gsal ba byung / /de shar zla ba bzhin du 'gro ba bsil bar mdzad/ /bstan pa rin chen mchog ltar bzang la 'phan med pa/ /rnam par dag tshul gang yin klu mgo gdengs ka can/ /chen po rnams kyis gtsug gi rgyan bzhin gus mnos
<p>47a</p>
<p>47a.1</p>nas/ /sa yi steng na gnas pa'i rab rib sel bar mjad/ /chos kyi sprin de phan pa mdzad pa'i don du g.yos/ /chos kyi bdud rtsi mya ngan 'das pa mchog gi rgyu/ /ro gcig gdung ba sel ba char chu bzhin du bab/ /de ni snod la brten nas ro rnams du mar gyur/ /
<p>47a.2</p>snod yangs zab la dri ma med cing gsal ba yi/ /bsam pa dang ldan khur kun bzod pa gang dag la/ /skye bo kun gyis nye bar spyad bya de gnas pa/ /mtsho chen mi yi gzugs can de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig skye nang rga shi sel ba'i bdud rtsi de/ /thob par mi byed mi spyod 'dzin
<p>47a.3</p>par mi byed pa/ /de dag nyes mang gti mug thibs pos bslad pa ste/ /yun ring nad kyis thebs pa sman chen mi bsten bzhin/ /'gro ba kun gyi mig gcig dri ma med pa gang / /de nis rnams gsum po'i spyi mthun sgron ma ste/ /bstan pa legs par rnyed nas gang zhig 'dor ba
<p>47a.4</p>de/ /gti mug shin tu rmad byung dag gis gtses par zad/ /byang chub khang bzangs bgrod lam them skas lta bu yi/ /bslab gzhi bcas pa rnams la rkang tshugs rton pa rnams/ /rjes su sgrub pas go 'phang che mthor phyin 'gyur te/ /ldog par byed pa rang gi sa ni gnyug mar
<p>47a.5</p>ltung / /skye ba'i rgya mtsho shin tu rgal dka' rgal 'dod pa/ /su zhig tshul khrims gzings gyur lag tu 'ong ba spang / /'phags pa'i ded dpon dang bral lam rgyus mi shes pa/ /'brog dgon 'khyams na ci ste yun rings gdungs mi byed/ /'khor ba'i ri sul khrod kyi g.yang
<p>47a.6</p>sar lhung gyur pa/ /mun nag thibs po'i nang nas ldang bar brtson pa gang / /yon tan smyug ma'i phreng ba bar ma dor 'dor ba/ /de dag shugs drag nyam nga'i ltung bar 'og tu ltung / /gang dag gcig pu'ang yid kyis nges par rab brtags ste/ /yang dag lam dang lhan cig
<p>47a.7</p>'grogs par byed pa de/ /sa steng dkyil na gtso bor gyur pa dam pa ste/ /slob ma mchog des bla mar bkur ba nyid du 'gyur/ /ngo tsha yon tan tshogs skyed ma gcig ya rabs mo/ /mchog tu g.yo med byams pa lta bu'i rjes 'brang ba/ /bden dang gzhung la dga' ba'i gzi
<p>47b</p>
<p>47b.1</p>brjid ldan pa rnams/ /srog ni bde blag gtong bar byed kyi dam bcas min/ /re zhig skye bo kun gyis dpyas dang sdig pa yis/ /'gro ba kun la dmyal ba mi bzod phar zhog gi /rang bzhin rnal ma bor nas smod pa sdug bsngal ba/ /mkhas la sa steng de las sdug bsngal
<p>47b.2</p>gzhan ci yod/ /gang zhig thub pa rnams kyis srol btod chos kyi lam/ /rgya chen gru dang 'dra ba rnyed nas slar 'dor ba/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i klong 'khyil gar mkhan 'dra rnams la/ /dga' bas nges par de yi sems bslus 'gyur ba snyam/ /gang zhig 'khor ba'i 'khor
<p>47b.3</p>lo rtag tu 'khor gyur pa'i/ /nang du zhugs nas bsti ba tsam la bder sems pa/ /de ni nges par dbang med rim gyis brgya phrag tu/ /'gro ba mnyam dang mi mnyam kun du 'khyam par 'gyur/ /shin tu mi bzad dri nga mi gtsang gtser bas bgags/ /rab tu dog pa mun
<p>47b.4</p>nag thibs por 'dug pa'i mi/ /mngal gnas dmyal ba lta bu'i nang du de zhugs nas/ /lus yongs bskum la sdug bsngal chen po brnag dgos so/ /de ni rim gyis til mar btsir spyad sra ba yis/ /btsir ba ltar byas de nas ci zhig ltar de btsa'/ /'on kyang mod la
<p>47b.5</p>de srog mi 'dor gang yin pa/ /sdug bsngal nye bar spyad pa'i rnam par mtho btsams mod/ /mi gtsang de nang gnas bcas 'phel ba'i lus de ni/ /mngal gnas rlam pas dkris shing dri nga mi bzad ldang / /gzir bas gnod pa bdo ste rma rmen zhig pa ltar/ /gyur pa de yi skyon
<p>47b.6</p>gyis sngon gyi dran pa spong / /byis lus nye bar spyod pa kun la mi 'bongs pa/ /mi brten 'khor ba spangs te mkhrang pa'i dngos gyur nas/ /dar la babs pa'i ri dbang btsan po'i ri sul du/ /sbrul gdug gnas gyur mu la bag rkyang spyod par byed/ /bsam brlag de ni de nas kyang
<p>47b.7</p>lhung la/ /lhung bzhin mi gtsigs spyod pa mi 'dor ba/ /byis pa bdag lus sdug pa rga ba dang / /'chi ba med pa nyid du sems pa lta/ /rmongs pa de ni thub dbang gis bstan pa'i/ /lam bzang rnam par spangs nas lam min par/ /glang po myos pa lcags kyu med pas gzhan/ /
<p>48a</p>
<p>48a.1</p>bab dgu phye mar rlog pa bzhin du 'gro/ /de nas de ni mi 'dod bzhin du mgor/ /brtse med rga bas rdog pa nan mnan nas/ /skra dkar lcags kyu bdar ba rnon po yis/ /glang chen rdzi bos glang chen bzhin du 'debs/ /'on kyang de ni spyod la skyor 'byin pas/ /dge
<p>48a.2</p>ba'am 'jigs pa bzhin du spang bar 'gyur/ /rmongs pa bya ba min byed bdag skyes pa/ /smyug ma 'bru chags lta bur brlag par zad/ /de nas de ni 'chi bdag dga' ba'i spun/ /gzhil ba'i bcos thabs med pas bzung nas ni/ /rgas pa'i ngo bo'i cha bdag 'ongs nas ni/ /
<p>48a.3</p>rgod pa bzhin du spyi nas 'dzin par byed/ de nas de ni lhu tshigs rnams 'bye zhing / /blo yang bslad 'gyur 'gro ba nyams par 'gyur/ /lus kyang dengs nas shig shig por 'gyur la/ /nges par sdig pa 'phel ba kho nar 'gyur/ /dbang po rnams kyang rim gyis zhum nas
<p>48a.4</p>ni/ /yul la chags kyang nus pa nyams par 'gyur/ /gnas skabs gang du 'di 'gro gyur ba de/ /gal te dmyal na yod na de nyid 'jigs/ /bdag gis ji ltar de bzhin 'di ma byas/ /ci ste de ltar de byas 'gro ba nyams/ /bdag gis ci ste 'di ltar 'chi bdag ni/ /mgo
<p>48a.5</p>bor rdog pas gnon pa 'phrigs ma gyur/ /mya ngan rdo rje de lta de lta bur/ /sems la gnod pa rnams kyis de gtses nas/ /nye du'i skye bo dud mo'i mchi rgyun can/ /sdug bsngal snying ni rdo rje lta bus bltas/ /gnad kyi gshis su 'jebs par gzir nas ni/ /shin tu mi bzad mun
<p>48a.6</p>rum 'jug par 'gyur/ /'bad pa lhur blangs srung ba byas pa'i lus/ /yid 'ong 'dris pa rnam par 'dor bar 'gyur/ /gshin rje'i zhags pas dam du btags pa ste/ /co do 'bal zhing cho nges 'debs byed kyang / /de yis glengs pa nye du'i skye bo yis/ /rang gi dus sgra ldir ba
<p>48a.7</p>bzhin mi thos/ /bgrod dka' chu dang pha bang thag thug 'dom pa'i bar/ /tsher ma rnon pos 'dzings pa nyam nga'i lam dag du/ /dus kyi zhags pas ske nas btags te gshin rje'i mi/ /gtum po rnams kyis dbyug pas bda' zhing khrid par 'gyur/ /mi bzad skam pas rgyang
<p>48b</p>
<p>48b.1</p>nas chu klung dri med pa/ /mthong nas btung bar 'dod de song na de nyid kyang / /skra shad nya lcibs tshogs dang rnag sungs 'dres pa dang / /'dam rdzab khrag dang phyi sas gang ba'i chur 'gyur ro/ /dus rlabs rlung langs chu 'thor ri rtse bsil 'gyur zhing / /tsan dan ljon pa sngon 'khrungs ma la yar song
<p>48b.2</p>nas/ /de yang 'di la nags sreg me lce rnos 'khrigs shing / /mgal dum 'gyel ba mang pos rad rod can du 'gyur/ /chu gter rlabs 'jigs 'phang mtho gyes pa las byung ba'i/ /dbu ba tsher ma lhag ge stug par song na yang / /de yang 'di la bye tshan khu ba dmar rtsub pa'i/ /
<p>48b.3</p>rlung dmar 'jebs pa 'tshub pa'i mya ngan nyid du 'gyur/ /'di ni de gnas char sprin ldang bar 'dod na yang / /sprin las lcags mda'i char pa dud 'thul mdag mar bcas/ /tsha tsha rdo rje'i pha bang dmar 'phrog ser mdog lta bu yi/ /glog phreng dmar ser 'gyu ba lus la char du 'bab/ /tsha bas
<p>48b.4</p>nyen la bu yug kyang ni tshar 'gyur la/ /lhags pas nyam thag pa la me yang grang byed do/ /shin tu mi bzad las yongs smin pas rnam rmongs pa/ /'di la sna tshogs 'di kun phyin ci log tu snang / /khab mig tsam gyi kha la dpag tshad mang 'jigs pa'i//lto can nyam thag rgya mtsho chen
<p>48b.5</p>po'i chu 'thung kyang / /mgul phugs yangs pa nyid du phyin par ma gyur par/ /kha yi dugs kyis chu yi thigs pa skam par 'gyur/ /ral pa'i tshogs mang spungs pas bsgyings pa'i khyi dag gis/ /mche ba gzong rings rdo rje'i rtse mos lus dbad cing / /chu bo rab med thal skyo me lces gang
<p>48b.6</p>ba'i ngogs/ /rdo ba zur rnon mi bzad rtse rnon can du bdas/ /spu gri rnos gtams lcug tshal lo ma ral gri yi/ /nang du thang chad rgyugs na lus smas skyabs med pa/ /rtse gsum mdung thung dang ni ral gri rnos gang ba'i/ /khron pa gshin rje'i kha bas thu ba'i nang du lhung / /nyi tshan gyis gdung
<p>48b.7</p>bzod dka' rlag par dga' ba'i lus/ /ljon shing lo ma sngo stug mthong nas song ba dang / /de yi lo ma mtshon brgya lhung bas lus dbad cing / de na yun ring dud mo las shes brlag par gnas/ /bud med kun nas me lce brgya phrag 'thon pa'i mi/ /me stag phreng ba 'khrigs pa'i rgyan gyis
<p>49a</p>
<p>49a.1</p>gzhag gyur cing / /sog le lta bu'i rtsub pa'i lus kyi zon med pa/ shin tu sdug pa'i tshul du bcum nas 'khyud par byed/ /ri dang mnyam du lug ru 'jigs su rung ba gnyis/ /'dus pa'i phrag tu lus kun phye mar rlog cing 'joms/ /cung zad bsil
<p>49a.2</p>ba'i rlung zhig langs pas brtas nas de/ /de bzhin phyir yang lan brgyar kun nas phye mar rlog /bse khyi bong bu ce spyang stong phrag gis bred nas/ /shal ma ri mtho mi bzad de la myur 'dzegs na/ /tsher ma'i tshogs kha thur du bltas pas thal 'byin cing / /zug rngu tshabs po che dag
<p>49a.3</p>khong rlag nub par 'gyur/ /gshin rje'i lag na thogs pa dus kyi zhags pa lta'i/ /sbrul sdug mgo 'phang bstod pas dam gzhag gzhungs nas ni/ gson por kha dang bya gar kang ka bya rgod kyis/ /de na gnas pa'i mig dag tsham tshom med par 'dru/ /de lus de dag gi mchu rdo rje rtse
<p>49a.4</p>mo ltas/ /brtsam pa med dbang nyam thag nga ro 'byin byed cing / /thur du babs na lcags tsher gyen du kha bltas pa/ /sbom ba rno ba mang pos lus phug dran pa nyams/ /de bas kha cig mdung rtse gsum pa 'bar ba dang / /zug rngu rnon pos lus dbang thur du 'bab mi nus/ /de
<p>49a.5</p>tshe mtshon cha bdar ba'i mchu can khwa rnams kyis/ /kun du drangs pas rgyu lto brang breng nar zhang 'thor/ /kha cig ri bo'i g.yang sa ya ngar g.yang du lhung / /kha cig 'bru mar skol ba'i zangs chen nang du ltung / /gzhan dag phye ma sreg pa me stag 'phro ba yi/ /sa gzhi rkang pa gzhag pa'i
<p>49a.6</p>gnas mi thod par lhung / /kha cig 'bu sbrang phra mo lcig lcig 'dug pa yi/ /tshogs kyis lus rmugs bam zhing rnam par 'drul/ /las kyi rang bzhin snyi la 'tsho ba thogs pa rnams/ /bskyod pa tsam yang bya bar mi nus bzhin du gson/ /lhags pa dpe med rus pa la yang thim
<p>49a.7</p>pa yis/ /lus sbrebs 'dar zhing bskur nas gum gum por 'dug pa/ /chu bur brgya byung rdol ba las skyes srog chags kyi/ /ral gris dbad nas zhag dang chu ser rkang bcas 'dzag /dkos thag so 'thams skra dang spu rnams g.yengs gyur pa/ /mig dang rna ba lkog ma gnod
<p>49b</p>
<p>49b.1</p>pas kun gzir zhing / /lus dang sems kyi bar dag rab tu klong gyur nas/ /grang ba'i dmyal bar gnas shing shin tu 'o dod 'bod/ /dmyal me du ba mched dku mnam pa 'thul bas gnam mdog 'gyur/ /me lce'i lag mang rnam par 'phros nas phyogs kyi dkyil 'khor
<p>49b.2</p>khebs/ /rus gong dkar dum phreng ba'i rgyan gyis spud pa skyi g.ya' ba/ /glang chen pags gyon bsdigs thabs kye ma kyi hud zer ba bzhin/ /la lar me stag che 'phro 'khrug pa 'ur sgra tog yar la/ /zhag gis bab na skad ngan bod pa'i rtse zhil chil chil 'bar/ /brang gi rus
<p>49b.3</p>pa'i khong du thal la lhag lhag sgra grags pa/ /bskal pa'i dus kyi me yis bskyod du med pa'i nang du lhung / /glo nas rtswa skam rnying las sbar ba lta bur me tshogs 'bar/ /mgrin dang kha nas me lce 'bar ba dud bcas bstung mar 'byung / /khong ltogs pa nas lug nang khrol nar bas
<p>49b.4</p>kun bred cing / /brda mi phrad pa'i skad chen tsam zhig 'don par byed par zad/ /sdug bsngal che las thar par 'dod pas de dag yang dang yang / /sgo bye gseb gzhan mthong nas thag ring ci zhig ltar te 'byer/ /gang tshe las kyi sgo 'phar dam pos de yang bcad 'gyur pa/ /de tshe yi mug
<p>49b.5</p>bzod blag sdug bsngal gzhan yang 'byung bar 'gyur/ /mnga' chen rno tshogs 'bar ba char bzhin 'bab pa'i rjes la yang / /dmyal ba'i srung mas dbyug pas btab cing mchi ma 'dzag bzhin du/ /lcags zhun khu ba me stag 'bar ba'i phreng bas 'khrigs pa ldud/ /kha sna rna ba'i bu ga
<p>49b.6</p>dag nas dud 'thul gyen du 'byung / /mig dang glad spris rdol gyi bar du kun sreg cing / /glad pa'i rgyas la 'bar ba'i me lce smug nag tshogs/ /me de khros pa lta bur de yi lus phung la/ /bud shing skam po bcer la sbar ba bzhin du mched/ /skye bo de srog ri gzar klung gi chu ltar g.yo/ /dmyal
<p>49b.7</p>ba'i me yang der zad tsha ba'ang der zad de/ /las rnams ji ltar thams cad shin tu mi bzad pa/ /snang bar 'gyur ba de ltar yongs su sgyur bar byed/ /skye bo rang gi las kyis dbang med 'chal spyod pa/ /brgya la sdig nas dmyal ba dag nas thar na yang / /'jig rten 'gro ba mtha' dag bye
<p>50a</p>
<p>50a.1</p>ba 'phyes rnams su/ /mi yi dngos po shin tu rnyed par dka' ba nyid/ /gal te kla klo dmyal ba'i srung dang spyod mtshungs sam/ /dud 'gro phan tshun za bar byed pa'i nang dag tu/ /skye ba thob par 'gyur na gang gi phyir yang ni/ /g.yang du lhung bar 'gyur
<p>50a.2</p>ba'i ngang tshul de nyid bsten/ /gang zhig thob nas skye ba'i rgya mtsho mthar 'byin cing / /byang chub mchog gi sa bon dge ba'ang 'debs gyur pa/ /yid bzhin nor bu bas kyang yon tan lhag pa yi/ /mi nyid de ni su zhig 'bras bu med par byed/ /bde gshegs lam bsten
<p>50a.3</p>'gro ba 'dren par chas gyur cing / /sems kyi stobs chen mi yis rnyed pa gang yin pa'i/ /lam de lha dang klu yis mi rnyed lha min dang / /mkha' lding rig 'dzin mi'am ci ste lto 'phyes min/ /mi yi dngos po shin tu rnyed dka' rnyed gyur nas/ /don du brnag pa gang
<p>50a.4</p>yin de ni brtun te bsgrub/ /mar me'i me lce shugs drag rlung gis bskyod pa lta'i/ /tshe ni skad cig gnas pa'i gdengs yang yod ma yin/ /'di ni sang bya 'di ni thang cig 'og tu bya/ /'di ni de'u re bya zhes skye bo sems pa na/ /gshin rje be con nag thogs zur gyis lta ba
<p>50a.5</p>yi/ /mig rtsa dmar khros ma rangs gad mos re snyam 'debs/ /sos ka me tog rgyas pa'i dus [(]'de [,]'di [)]'byung bar 'gyur/ /zla ba gsal bas mtshon pa'i ston dus 'di 'byung zhes/ /skye bo thams cad dga' 'gyur bdag gi tshe 'di ni/ /zad par 'gyur zhes shin tu mi
<p>50a.6</p>dgar 'gyur ba med/ /zla ba'i dkyil 'khor rgyas pa nye bar brgyan byas shing / /rked 'chings char chen sprin gyi 'khrigs pas 'khyud gyur pa/ /ri rtse'i nags kyi mthongs der chags pa med pa ni/ /rlung ltar g.yo ba'i rang bzhin tshe gtugs skal ba che/ /nags mthongs ri
<p>50a.7</p>dgas rgyu ba'i tshogs kyis bsten byas la/ /kun nas nyams dga' bzang po de ni skyid pa gang / /de ci dga' ba'i nags tshal lha mo'i nyams bag tu/ /thel gyis 'bebs pa'i rdo leb can la yod 'gyur snyam/ /nags klung chu gtsang dogs kyi dben pa skyid pa gang / /
<p>50b</p>
<p>50b.1</p>de ci lha yi bu mo dri zhim byugs pa yi/ /lan bu'i rgyan du thogs pa'i rgyu ldan me tog tshogs/ /mdzes pa'i zil gnon lha yi chu la 'ang yod 'gyur ram/ /rtsa ba 'bras bu shun pa lo ma phun sum tshogs pa'i ljon shing ldan/ /nags tshal ltos med ri bo'i
<p>50b.2</p>chu rgyun bsil 'bab chags pa med pa'i gnas/ /chu klung yangs pa'i mtha' ru 'bras bu me tog lhung bas brgyan pa yi/ /nyams dga' bas mthar ci zhig med de dmyal sdong khyim gyis bslus te sdod/ /ri sul yangs par skye bo bun long med pas rab bde ba/ /nyer spyod
<p>50b.3</p>rgya chen nags tshal sngo 'khrungs phreng bas sbrengs/ /chu ngogs snyan pa phu chu'i rgyun 'dra rnga ltar snyan pa yis/ /bdag cag nyon mongs yul ma yin zhes 'don la sgrogs pa bzhin/ /'dod pa rnams dang 'byor dang srid gsum rgyal ba yis/ /sgyu ma smig rgyu chu zla dba' rlabs 'dra
<p>50b.4</p>bar gsungs/ /rmi lam lta bu'i ngan spyod 'khrul bas bslus pa yi/ /byis pa gang dag de la chags pa dmyal bar ltung / /yul dang dug mtshungs dang po myong ba tsam na bde/ /yul dang dug mtshungs rnam smin rtsub pas mi bzad pa/ /yul dang dug mtshungs gti mug mun pas
<p>50b.5</p>thibs por byed/ /yul dang dug mtshungs shugs bzlog dka' zhing g.yo ba yin/ /dug dang yul rnams blo yis nges par brtags byas na/ /nyis na dug bla mi bzad rang bzhin yul rnams min/ /dug ni skye ba gcig la dug tu 'gyur bar zad/ /yul ni tshe rabs gzhan
<p>50b.6</p>la'ang dug tu 'gyur bar byed/ /dug ni dug dang bsres nas rab tu zhi bar 'gyur/ /gsang sngags mchog dang dug sel sman gyis gso bar rung / /dug ni thabs ldan spyad na mi la phan 'gyur gyi/ /dug chen yul ni nam yang de lta ma yin no/ /ji ltar glang bu khron zab kha nas
<p>50b.7</p>'khrungs pa yi/ /rtswa lo kham 'ga' tsam la yid ni chags gyur pa/ /rnyed pa grub pa med par g.yang du ltung ba ltar/ /'tsho ba'i 'jig rten bde ldan 'dod pa'ang de dang 'dra/ /lha yi bu mo dal gyis 'bab pa'i chu rgyun gyis/ /'phral thabs klong pa rnams dang lhan cig rtse myong
<p>51a</p>
<p>51a.1</p>nas/ /phyir yang chu bo rab med rba drag 'bogs pa yis/ /smas pa'i sdug bsngal mi bzad bstan par bya dgos so/ /lha tshal dpag bsam shing lo'i gding ba kun bkram par/ /lha yi bu mo dang bsten bde bar gnas nas kyang / /phyir yang mtshon rnon mang po
<p>51a.2</p>'bab pas lus dbad pa/ /lo ma ral gri lta bu'i nags tshal bgrod dgos so/ /rkang bzhag nems dang 'phar byed reg na bde ba yi/ /ri rab spo yi dkyil du yun ring gnas nas kyang / /phyir yang bye ma bsregs pa'i me ma mur gyi tshogs/ /brla dang rkang lag kun du zhig par
<p>51a.3</p>'khyam par 'gyur/ /dril bu mdzes khrol mu tig phreng tshogs lhag ge ba/ /gzhal med khang du zhugs te lha yul bgrod nas kyang / /mi bzad skyabs med mun nag thibs po dpag med pa/ /pha mtha' med pa'i nang du spyi tshugs ltung bar 'gyur/ /gang du lha klu mi'am ci yi mgo rgyan
<p>51a.4</p>gyi/ /'od kyi tshogs kyis rkang rten dmar ba'i brgya byin yang / /las kyi rlung 'khrugs 'gro ba ngan par 'gro 'gyur ba/ /de la skyes bu su zhig 'jigs pa bstan mi byed/ /me tog rab tu rnyings shing lus rngul thon pa dang / /gos rnying smre zhing nye du rnams la lta ba yis/ /lha rnams
<p>51a.5</p>'chi ba'i rab tu sdug bsngal gang yin de/ /'tsho ba chu bur lta bur g.yo ba'i mi la med/ /sdug bsngal me tshogs 'phung bas 'jigs pa'i 'jig rten 'dir/ /skye bo bde snyam mngon pa'i nga rgyal byed pa dang / /de ni gshin rje'i kha yangs 'byed par byed pa ste/ /de ni skye ba phyi
<p>51a.6</p>ma'i ljon shing sa bon yin/ /de ni gshin rjes srid mtshor rgyu ba'i sems can la/ /log par smon pa'i 'jigs pa dbyig pa nag po'i rtser/ /sred pa'i tha gu ring pos dam bzhag btags pa yi/ /mchil pas nya la bya ba bzhin du btab pa yin/ /dmyal rnams zangs chen lhag
<p>51a.7</p>lhag skol ba tsha ba'i shugs drag nas/ /skad cig tsam zhig mgo stod dbugs 'byin 'gyur ba rnams/ /lcags kyi tho ba rab tu mang po khros te gzas pa yis/ /brgyab na de nyid mchog tu bde ba yin par sems pa ltar/ /de bzhin sdug bsngal mi bzad pa yis dbang med rtag
<p>51b</p>
<p>51b.1</p>gzir cing / /re zhig tsam zhig ji zhig ltar te skye shi'i 'khrugs med nas/ /skad cig sdug bsngal gnyug mar bzod dka' me lce zhil gyur na/ /'jig rten thams cad bde ba kham 'ga' la yang sred par byed/ /ji lta ji ltar 'gro ba kun la bde ba'i 'du shes bskyed/ /de lta de
<p>51b.2</p>ltar gti mug mun pa shin tu stug por 'gyur/ /ji lta ji ltar 'gro ba kun la sdug bsngal 'du shes bskyed/ /de lta de ltar gti mug mun pa shin tu srab mor 'gyur/ /ji lta ji ltar sdug pa bsgom pa shin tu rnam 'phel ba/ /de lta de ltar 'dod chags me lce shin tu 'phro bar 'gyur/ /
<p>51b.3</p>ji lta ji ltar mi sdug bsgom pa shin tu 'phel 'gyur ba/ /de lta de ltar 'dod chags me lce shin tu rtse zhil 'gyur/ /bud med yan lag dri nga rul pa mi sdug dang / /pad ma'i 'dab ma ut+pal dag tu snyam byed pa/ /snyan dngags mkhan gyi brdzun de'i 'bras bu mi bzad pa/ /
<p>51b.4</p>de dag de yi mngal gnas 'jug pa de yin no/ /'gro bar lan brgyar ma son 'gro de gang zhig yod/ /sngon chad lan mang ma myong bde ba de gang zhig /rnga yab dkar mdzes lta bu'i dpal gang ma thob pa/ /de yang gang zhig yod na 'on kyang 'dod chags 'phel/ /gang gi gling bar ma
<p>51b.5</p>gnas chu bo de yong min/ /yul phyogs gang du gnas ma bcas pa'i gnas de med/ /gang du ma song nam mkha'i phyogs de'ang yod min na/ /'on kyang 'dod chags dgang dka' 'phel bar 'gyur ba nyid/ /sngon chad lan mang ma myong sdug bsngal de yod min/ /'gro bar gang
<p>51b.6</p>gis tshim gyur 'dod pa de dag med/ gang gi ltor ma nyal ba'i sems can de med na/ /'on kyang ji ltar 'khor ba can la chags bral med/ /skye ba yongs su 'dzin pa 'gro ba rgya chen 'dir/ /bde dang sdug bsngal dag tu lan mang 'gre ldog pa/ /'gro ba gnyen ma gyur pa'i
<p>51b.7</p>skye bo de gang med/ /'on kyang zhe sdang sbrul gyi rang bzhin 'jigs par gnas/ /gang dang lhan cig 'dus nas bgad cing rtses pa dang / /glu blangs dga' 'dun byas shing gcig tu zos 'thungs dang / /dus kyi rim pas me tog rna rgyan dengs byas dang / /gnas skabs ci zhig
<p>52a</p>
<p>52a.1</p>ltar mnyam mi mnyam byas pa yi/ /nye du 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho'i khongs su chud gyur pa/ /klong gi nang du lhung ba lta bu snang bzhin du/ /skye shis 'phos pas ngo ma shes pa de bor nas/ /gal te gcig thar byed na de las khrel bor med/ /byis pa bang na btsa' ba
<p>52a.2</p>ci yang mi nus par/ /gang gi nu zho byams pa'i shugs kyis gzags 'thungs pa/ /ngal ba mang bsten byams pa bsten pa de dag 'dir/ /shin tu ma rabs zhig na'ang spong bar su zhig spro/ /gang gi khong na 'di skabs rnyed nas gnas bcas shing / /gang gi rtse bag sems
<p>52a.3</p>kyis zon bcas 'di blangs pa/ /nyon mongs de dag sdug bsngal skyabs med der bor nas/ /'gro ba ma rabs tha shal zhig na'ang su zhig spro/ /'gro ba sdug bsngal mi bzad mang pos dbang med skyabs med 'dir/ /gzhan gyi don du sdug bsngal gang de bde zhes skyes mchog
<p>52a.4</p>gsungs/ /skad cig gzhan bkres skom dang tsha ngal bral bas rangs byas pa/ /des dga' gang yin de dang 'dra ba 'di na'ang gang zhig yod/ /gzhan phan bde ba skyed par brtson pas dga' ba rnyed pa gang / /de ni yul bde'i longs spyod lhur len rnams kyis ji ltar yang / /gzhon
<p>52a.5</p>bdes mi thob mi dbang 'byor pa'i yo byad rnams kyis min/ /chung mas ma yin gzhan min lha gnas lha min 'gro bas min/ /shin tu rnyed sla rtswa kham 'ga' lta phyugs kyang rang nyid za/ /shin tu skom pas gdungs pa'ang chu zhig rnyed na dga' mgur 'thung / /'di na skyes bu gzhan
<p>52a.6</p>don byed par brtson pa gang yin pa/ /de 'di'i brjid bag yin te de bde skyes bu'i rtsal de 'phags/ /nyi ma rlabs chen rta zhon rgyu ba snang byed gang yin dang / /khur la mi rtsegs sa yis 'jig rten 'degs pa gang yin de/ /rang don 'ga' med chen po rnams kyi rang bzhin de 'dra ste/ /
<p>52a.7</p>de dag 'jig rten phan dang bde ba'i rol gcig tu gzhol/ /'jig rten ma rig dud sprin 'khrigs pas 'gro ba 'khrugs gyur ba/ /sdug bsngal me rab 'bar ba'i nang du dbang med ltung mthong nas/ /thong la me lce 'bar ba lta bur yid brel brtson pa gang / /'di na de dag skyes
<p>52b</p>
<p>52b.1</p>bu yin te mkhas pa'ang de dag yin/ /gzhan gyi don du me lces gang ba'i mnar med dmyal bar yang / /gangs dang zla 'od bsil ba lta bur rab tu dga' bzhin 'jug /nyid kyi don du pad ma kha bye lhag ger 'dug pa yi/ /mtsho yang de la me lce'i tshogs bzhin rab tu gdungs
<p>52b.2</p>bar byed/ /gzhan la phan par byed par chas pa'i mkhas pa rnams/ /lo ma ral gri tshal na'ang bde blag gnas byed kyis/ /skad cig tsam yang lha yi bu mo dang 'grogs nas/ /dga' ba'i tshal gyi nang du skyid par byed mi 'gyur/ /rgal bar gyur pa skyabs med skye bo bsgral
<p>52b.3</p>ba'i phyir/ /phyir yang chu bo rab med nang du 'jug byed kyis/ /lha yi chu bo dba' rlabs chil chil 'dug pa yis/ /reg pa'i bde ba bdag nyid sten par byed ma yin/ /de ltar rgyan gyis brgyan gyur legs spyad rin po che/ /gsal ba'i nang na gsal ba zhi ba'i bdud rtsi
<p>52b.4</p>yangs/ /dga' ba'i dga' ba byas pa mi gzo rnyed dka' ba/ /bkra shis rnams kyi bkra shis zhi ba'i bde rgyun te/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung gi me tog rtag bsten bya/ /ljon shing me tog de las 'bras bu rgya chen 'byung / /bde gshegs me tog gsung las don tshogs
<p>52b.5</p>bsten bya ste/ /sbrang ma sbrang rtsi la mchog dga' bar byed la ltos/ /skad cig gcig la zad cing rtag tu 'khrug pa'i yul rnams spong / /zhi ba'i bde 'bras 'chi ba'i 'tsher med gcig pu dben pa sten/ /rnam thar sgo yi gtan pas gti mug 'khrugs pa'i rab rib sol/ /rta
<p>52b.6</p>mchog rte'u ni shin tu yun ring gnyid log 'gyur ma yin/ /khyod gcig gdung bas nyam thag rnams la srid pa'i mya ngam du/ /shing chen sdang brtan rgya chen kun gel bzod dang dul ba'i lo ma can/ /zhig nas me tog shes rab yal ga rab smin lo bran stug /smon lam rtse mo
<p>52b.7</p>tshul khrims dri ma rab zhi 'bras bcas kyis/ /khyod gcig gdung bas nyam thag rnams la srid pa'i mya ngam du/ /mtsho chen yangs gsal byin gzhol gting zab bsam pa rab tu dngas/ /rtag bsil sbrul gdug rnyi yis bag med 'jigs spangs rang bzhin gyis/ /rab tu
<p>53a</p>
<p>53a.1</p>gtsang zhing sred pa gcod byed rtul ba'i khur bzod kyis/ /khyod gcig gdung bas nyam thag rnams la srid pa'i mya ngam du/ /sprin chen skye bo mang phan mi 'jigs smra ba'i sgra chen sgrogs/ /drag pa rgya chen char gyi shugs drag snying rje'i rlung gis bskyod/ /rdul
<p>53a.2</p>bral zhi bas tshul khrims dri mas sa steng brgyan par gyis/ /bdag gis de skad brjod pas bsod nams cung zad bsgrubs pa gang / /de yis skye bo ma lus bde gshegs spyod la dang byed cing / /rtag bde longs spyod bzang ldan yid la re ba 'byor ba dang / /gzhan la phan dga' de nas rim
<p>53a.3</p>gyis kun mkhyen bgrod par shog /dmyal ba lag mthil ltar mnyam rnam bsal me rab zhi ba dang / /skam 'khrungs pad+ma'i lo mas khebs shing rtsa ba'i khye'u so 'thon/ /gtsang zhing dri zhim pad+ma kha byes sa rnams brgyan pa dang / /rgyas shing bzang la ser bu'i ngad bcas char zim 'bab pa
<p>53a.4</p>par shog /bdud dpung pham pa cho nges 'debs pas mi bsnyengs sgrogs pa po/ /lha chu'i rtse mo bas kyang dga' mdzad lha dang mi 'dul ba/ /skye shi nyon mongs sdug bsngal rgyun rnams 'joms pa'i sangs rgyas dag /phyogs dang phyogs su brnag pa bzhin du nam zhar 'byung bar
<p>53a.5</p>shog /'gro ba chos kyi kun dga' 'phel ba'i dga' ston che bar shog /'chi bdag re ba shin tu yun ring goms pa don med shog /thub pa'i skye bo gtam tshogs 'phel bas zhe ba bdud rtsi yi/ /char gyi zla ba'i snang ba rab bzang bsil bas don byas shog /slob ma la springs pa'i
<p>53a.6</p>phrin yig slob dpon chen po tsan dra go mis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po sarba dz+nya de ba dang / /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban de dpal brtsegs rak+Shi tas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ 
<p>53a.7</p>ma hA rA dza ka ni ska le kha/ /bod skad du/rgyal po chen po ka nis ka la springs pa'i spring yig /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bgrod par bgyi 'os khyod lags na/ /bkug kyang ma mchis gang lags de/ /ma gus ma lags brnyas ma lags/ /rga
<p>53b</p>
<p>53b.1</p>dang nad kyi bar chad bgyis/ /bdag ni sems can thams cad dang / /'dra bar khyod la brtse mod kyis/ /khyod kyi yon tan gyis khyod la/ /lhag par nye mgon khyad par bgyid/ /gdams bgyi phal cher mchis mod kyi/ /thams cad gdams par sus rngo thogs/ /khyod kyi yon
<p>53b.2</p>tan gang lags des/ /bdag ni spyi brtol skyes par gyur/ /bzlog pa med pa'i yon tan gyis/ /phyogs rnams kun du bsgos pas ni/ /mi mchog rnams kyang thugs thub par/ /mdza' bshes bzhin du 'dzem pa med/ /de ltas snyan bstod nyid kyi ched/ /bdag gis
<p>53b.3</p>gsol ba 'di gson te/ /bsgrub dang btang ba'i phyogs gnyis las/ /gang rigs de ni nyams su bzhes/ /dga' bar bgyid pa'i yul rnams dang / /rgya gas par bgyid pa'i lang tsho dang / /bdag nyid rang dgar spyod pa de/ /kun du don med bgyid pa'i sgo/ /phung bar byed pa
<p>53b.4</p>de gsum spang / /mkhas pas dam pa bsten pa dang / /dbang po dul dang shes rab kyi/ /stobs mthus nyams ni smad nas spyad/ /khyod gyi nyos pa'i gzhir gyur pa'i/ /cha ni gsum po de dag rnams/ /chos lugs dag dang 'dul ba yis/ /bcos nas yon tan nyid du mdzod/ /
<p>53b.5</p>ci ste rgyal po blon po dag /dkyel che snying rje'i bdag nyid ni/ /rtag tu nyon mongs med pa yi/ /las kyis rgyal srid bya bar rung / /'jig rten 'di na blo gros kyis/ /nyam chung gyur dang mgon med pa/ /bya ba ma yin byed pa la/ /gdon mi za bar 'jug par 'gyur/ /de bas ji srid
<p>53b.6</p>sa de las/ /myur du ma brgal bar du ni/ /blo mthu bskyed phyir mkhas pa dag /bsdu bar dgyes pa'i nan tan mdzod/ /chos kyi bstan bcos gdon bgyi zhing / /de yi don gyi tshul gson la/ /gsan pa'i chos rnams rnam dpyad de/ /dpyad pa la ni mkhas par mdzod/ /mya
<p>53b.7</p>ngan gyis ni ma gdungs shing / /na gzhon nad med longs pa yi/ /dngos po da ltar byung ba yi/ /blo gros la ni mi nus med/ /'dir ni skyes bu dam pa las/ /dus dus su yang nyung zad gson/ /nyung ngu bsags na'ang nges par ni/ /ring por mi thogs mang por 'gyur/ /
<p>54a</p>
<p>54a.1</p>rtag tu chu thigs re re'i rgyun/ /bar chad med par 'bab pa yis/ /gang zhig gang bar mi 'gyur ba'i/ /snod de ji lta bu zhig mchis/ /de ltar dpe gsal de lta bu/ /rgyal po tshad mar mdzad nas ni/ /dam pa'i chos ni gsan pa la/ /rtag tu dges pa
<p>54a.2</p>nyid du mdzod/ /yon tan nor ni gnyer la gnyen/ /mkhas shing snying rje'i bdag nyid can/ /byas gzo phongs chos mi bgyid pa/ /bzang po khyod kyi slad du zhog /khyod kyi blun dang phongs chos can/ /skams shing byas pa mi gzo dang / /kha gsag gtum po mi bzad pa/ /yul
<p>54a.3</p>na rang gnas su ma stsal cig /rtag tu so so'i skye bo yi/ /khyad par mkhyen par mdzod cig dang / /de yi khyad par mkhyen tsam la/ /phun sum tshogs pa rag las so/ /mi gang dka' ba spyod byed dang / /dor bar bya dka' 'dor ba dang / /bzod par dka' ba bzod byed dang / /bkur
<p>54a.4</p>dka' nyams su len pa dang / /gnas min las ni zlog byed dang / /gnas su 'jog par brtson pa dang / /de yi bsam pa mthun gus dang / /bde bar 'dod cing 'o byams pa/ /de dag rnams ni mdza' bshes te/ /gnyen 'dun grogs po'ang de dag lags/ /rang don tsam
<p>54a.5</p>phyir 'brang ba'i mi/ /gzhan dag skye bo phal par bas/ /grogs po phan par 'dod pa'i tshig /mi snyan yang ni phan pa dang / /'jam dang bde ba lags pa dag /thugs la bzhag par mdzad du gsol/ /tshig snyan phan pa ma lags dang / /'jam yang bden pa ma
<p>54a.6</p>lags pa/ /dam pa ma yin rnams kyi tshig /khyod kyi thugs la ma bzung shig /phan par smra ba khro yang ni/ /khyod kyis gnang chen dag tu mdzod/ /mi phan smra ba bstod bgyis kyang / /dgyes pa dag tu ma mdzad cig /rab dngas mtsho la dang pa yi/ /rgyal po dang ni chus
<p>54a.7</p>'jigs bzhin/ /dam pa rnams kyis bsnyen sla dang / /dam pa min pas bsnyen dka' mdzod/ /khyod kyis mkhas rnams tshim bgyis pas/ /'byor ba don du gnyer mi bgyi/ /yon tan dgyes phyir khyod kyis ni/ /yon tan rnams kyis mi ngoms mdzod/ /longs
<p>54b</p>
<p>54b.1</p>spyod byed dam bde ba dang / /sdug bsngal phrad pa'am spyod pa'am/ /spyod lam kun du spyod pa na/ /khyod kyis dam pa bsten pa dang / /dran pa'i grogs kyis bskor ba na/ /bag yod par ni gnas 'gyur te/ /sA la'i shing la 'khri shing bzhin/ /bzang po dpal gyis
<p>54b.2</p>'khyud par 'gyur/ /khyod kyis gzhom pa bden pa dang / /khyad par zhing la sbyin pa dang / /dran dang bral bas 'dod pa dbye/ /chad pas gang du'ang gcad mi bgyid/ /log pas 'thab gcugs byed pa dang / /bkren la dman par lta ba dang / /tshul khrims ldan rnams
<p>54b.3</p>mi dga' dang / /dka' thub sdom pa 'khrul byed pa/ /bzhi po 'di dag 'dod min te/ /rtsa ba 'joms par bgyid pa lags/ /rab brtson khyod kyi yul na ni/ /de dag gtan ma mchis par mdzod/ /stobs dang ldan pas stobs chung ba/ /gnang chen gyis ni mi
<p>54b.4</p>gnang dang / /mchod 'os rnams kyis mi mchod dang / /smos 'drin kyis ni mi shes pa/ /gang yang rung la gang gis kyang / /brnyas pa med par khyod kyis mdzod/ /tha snyad rnams ni dag pa yis/ /kun la 'dra bar gzigs su gsol/ /kun gyis rang gi chos thob
<p>54b.5</p>cing / /chos kyis thams cad 'tsho bar mdzod/ /mi sdug kyang ni nyes med na/ /thams cad bde bar mdzad du gsol/ /pha yis bu la ji lta bar/ /khyod kyis 'khor la byams bgyis na/ /bu yis pha la ji lta bar/ /khyod kyis zhabs 'bring dga' bar bgyid/ /phal
<p>54b.6</p>rnams rang bzhin bzang na ni/ /khyod kyi dgongs pa bzhin du 'gyur/ /phal rnams rang bzhin ngan na ni/ /khyod kyi dgongs pa bzhin mi 'gyur/ /gal te gzhung lugs bzang bzhes na/ /gong nas gong du 'phang bar 'gyur/ /ci ste ngan pa'i spyod mdzad na/ /'og nas
<p>54b.7</p>'og tu ltung bar 'gyur/ /dam pa'i las la gnas na ni/ /khyu mchog dang ni khyu lta bur/ /rjes su 'tsho ba'i skye bo'i tshogs/ /'di kun rjes su 'brang bar 'gyur/ /khyod ni gya gyu la zhugs na/ /gya gyu kho na'i rjes 'brangs pas/ /skyes dgu khyod mdzad rjes 'brang pa'i/ /
<p>55a</p>
<p>55a.1</p>skye dgu de ni nyams par 'gyur/ /de bas bdag gzhan bsrung slad du/ /thugs kyis rab tu bsgrims nas ni/ /gna' rgyal drang srong rnams kyi lugs/ /nyams pa sar par bcos su gsol/ /gna' yi rgyal po'i spyod pa las/ /gang dag bzang ba de
<p>55a.2</p>mdzod la/ /mi rigs pa ni gang lags de/ /smad par mdzod la spang du gsol/ /sngon gyi bka' khrims skyon chags pa/ /gna' nas mchis kyang rgyun chod la/ /rgyal po ka ni skas mtshan pa'i/ /khrims su bca' ba gsar pa mdzod/ /lha khyod yon tan don gnyer bas/ /
<p>55a.3</p>yon tan lha bzhin kho nar mdzod/ /lha khyod skyon rnams mkhyen pa yis/ /lha bzhin nyes med kho nar mdzod/ /zla ba mar gyi ngo bzhin du/ /nyes pa'i tshogs rnams 'grib pa dang / /zla ba yar gyi ngo bzhin du/ /rtag tu yon tan gyis brgyan mdzod/ /yab mes bzhin du bdag nyid
<p>55a.4</p>kyis/ /chos kyis sa steng bskyang ba dang / /yab mes bzhin du lha gang gi /dus ston 'phel bar mdzad du gsol/ /khyod kyis mtho ris byang grol gyi/ /them skas ma mnyam mnyam pa'i phyir/ /bsod nams las byung bzo rig che/ /rtag tu lha khang dag tu sogs/ /rga dang
<p>55a.5</p>'chi bas bsnyengs mdzod de/ /chos bzhin rgyal srid dpal spyad nas/ /bgres kar dgon par gshegs su gsol/ /dam chos bstan pas 'bras mchis mdzod/ /rang byung rnams kyi rjes bslabs pas/ /ku sha'i rigs su 'khrungs khyod kyis/ /yab mes 'phags
<p>55a.6</p>rigs nyi ma yi/ /gdung rgyud chos lugs ma nyams mdzod/ /skye ba can la nges par ni/ /rga dang 'chi dang na mchis na/ /ma bgres ma bsnyungs ma 'grongs zhes/ /legs smon gsol yang ci la sman/ /srid pa dag ni gang yang rung / /de nyid rgas dang 'chi ba lags/ /
<p>55a.7</p>yongs su bsgyur bas rga ba ste/ /skad cig 'jig pa 'chi ba yi/ /ma rgas ma na ma 'chi zhes/ /smra ba dag ni smra ba na/ /de ltar 'jig rten kun 'bar na/ /yang srid med las gzhan ci yod/ /gang na mi mthun yod ma yin/ /gang du 'du byed 'jig mi 'gyur/ /gang na
<p>55b</p>
<p>55b.1</p>gcig tu bde bar gnas/ /gang du song na 'chi mi 'gyur/ /srid pa kun nas nyon mongs dang / /sdug bsngal 'byung ba phyir mi mkho/ /de slad des pa srid pa rnams/ /med par bsgom pa rgyas par mdzod/ /'dir ni bgyi ba 'di nyid de/ /de las gzhan pa'i bgyi mi 'tshal/ /
<p>55b.2</p>bgyi ba de ni bgyis pa yis/ /mi bgyi ba yi tshar phyin to/ /bgrang phreng bzhin du 'khor ba ru/ /lan mang yongs su 'khor ba ni/ /lan brgya 'am yang na stong dag tu/ /'jig rten dag tu ci ma bgyis/ /'di ma bgyis slad byis pa yi/ /yang dang yang du bgyi 'tshal bas/ /
<p>55b.3</p>thog ma med pa'i dus can 'di/ /da dung bar du ma log go/ /'chi bdag su dang mi bshes pa/ /glo bur dag tu 'bab 'gyur bas/ /sang dag bya zhes ma bzhes par/ /dam pa'i chos la bsnyur te mdzod/ /'di sang deng 'di mi bya zhes/ /bya ba mi la bzang po min/ /nam
<p>55b.4</p>zhig khyod ni med 'gyur ba'i/ /sang de gdon mi za bar 'ong / /'chi bdag brtse ba med pa can/ /skyes rtsal don med gsod 'gyur ba/ /gsod pa sngon du 'ong bzhin du/ /mkhas pa su zhig bag rkyong spyod/ /de las dpag chen bzod med des/ /mda' ni mi bzad 'chor
<p>55b.5</p>med par/ /de ni ji srid ma 'phangs pa/ /de srid rang gi don la 'bod/ /rnam smin 'byin pa sngon las kyis/ /khyod ni yongs su btang gyur pa/ /gsar pa'i las dang rjes 'brel zhing / /'chi bdag gis ni drangs pa na/ /dge dang sdig pa ma gtogs par/ /'gro ba
<p>55b.6</p>thams cad phyir log nas/ /'ga' yang khyod rjes mi 'brang bar/ /mkhyen par mdzod la legs par spyod/ /bdag ni snying rjes zil gnon cing / /yid mi dga' ba'i rlan gyis ni/ /shin tu brlan pa'i smre sngags 'di/ /re zhig gsan par mdzad du gsol/ /'gro
<p>55b.7</p>ba dman pa log ltung ba/ /mgon med nyes med phal cher ni/ /rtswa dang chu dang 'bras bu ni/ /phal pas 'tsho ba sgrub bgyid pa/ /bya dang ri dgas phyugs dag la/ /rgyal pos gsod dam gsod 'jug pa/ /ci ga rigs sam mi rigs pa/ /bde la gnas pa khyod
<p>56a</p>
<p>56a.1</p>nyid gsungs/ /khyod ni chen por mi khro zhing / /gnod pa bgyid la'ang bzod ces gda'/ /khyod kyi thugs rje dud 'gro la/ /kye ma su yis dgag par bgyis/ /gnod pa bgyid la bzod mdzad cing / /gnod mi bgyid pa 'gums mdzad
<p>56a.2</p>pas/ /khyod la brtse dang mi brtse ba'i/ /rgyu mthun pa ni gnyis ka gda'/ /sngon chad bgyis pa'i sug las kyis/ /'di ltar 'ben du gyur pa la/ /khyod nyid gnod pa mdzad na go/ /su la skyabs su mchi ba gsungs/ /gzhan gyis gnod pa bgyis na yang / /nyid kyi
<p>56a.3</p>phyag gis bshug 'tshal na/ /khyod bzhengs mngon du gnod mdzad na/ /phyogs kun mun par ma gyur tam/ /kun la srog ni phangs pa ste/ /kun la gson pa sdug pa lags/ /thams cad 'chi ba'i chos can te/ /thams cad sdug bsngal rnams kyis gdungs/ /'di
<p>56a.4</p>ltar gang zhig mi 'tshal ba/ /de nyid kyis ni sdug bsngal te/ /mkhas pa su zhig mgar ba ltar/ /tshig pa la ni yang sreg bzhin/ /khyod ni srog gcod mi dgyis shing / /srog gcod dgyes las phyir log na/ /rgyal srid nyams par 'gyur ram ci/ /lugs 'di ci
<p>56a.5</p>zhig lags pa gsungs/ /mtshon cha'i thabs la mkhas khyod kyis/ /g.yul ngor srol btod mthong lags na/ /gzhan du khyod la ri dgas la/ /ci slad gnod pa'i las rnams mdzad/ /ri dgas gzhon nu'i spyan mnga' khyod/ /spyan dang 'dra ba'i ri dgas rnams/ /rtabs
<p>56a.6</p>nas rig rig lta ba las/ /ci yi slad du thugs mi rje/ /khyod kyi spyan dang mig 'dra'i phyir/ /khyod la dga' ba gang lags de/ /ri dgas la yang dga' bgyid na/ /khyod ni ji ltar dgyes mi mdzad/ /log par ltung dang spyan 'dra dang / /mgon med yul na gnas pa nyid/ /re
<p>56a.7</p>re yang ni ri dgas dag /mi 'gums pa yi rgyur rung ngo / /mi rnams la ni mdzad pa bas/ /sdug bsngal lhag par brtags pa yi/ /dud 'gro rnams la ches lhag par/ /khyod kyi thugs rjes mdzad du gsol/ /khyod nyid bsrung ba'i don 'di la/ /bdag gis thal mo
<p>56b</p>
<p>56b.1</p>sbyar mi 'tshal/ /rgyud gzhan gsal bas gus bgyis par/ /legs par thugs tshod mnga' lags grang / /co nas bzung ste bslab sbyang ba/ /dam pa rnams kyi lugs su grags/ /de ltar lags pas rgyal po la/ /bu sdug bzhin du gsol ba lags/ /gal te bdag gis mi
<p>56b.2</p>phan pa/ /gsol na bdag la chad pas khum/ /ci ste gcig tu phan gsol na/ /bdag gis gsol ba bzhin du mdzod/ /gal te mi dgyes mdzad par ma gyur na/ /bdag gis yang dang yang du gsol bar 'tshal/ /ci ste bdag tshig khyad du 'gums mdzad na/ /bka' mchid 'di
<p>56b.3</p>ni nges par btang bar bgyi/ /dgyes par gyur na slar rjes mi 'gums te/ /mi dgyes gyur na dog sa gzung bar 'tshal/ /gnod bgyid nyi ma ltar rngo mi thogs pas/ /sa bdag zla ba nya ba bzhin du mdzod/ /sa bdag tsher ma'i shing las sbrang rtsi ltar/ /dgra bo las kyang legs
<p>56b.4</p>par smras pa gzung / /gser gyi ri la dug rgyu na ji bzhin du/ /yid 'ong skye bo'i tshig ngan spang 'tshal lo/ /mi mchog gal te legs par mdzad pa'i sbyor bas bsgrubs gyur te/ /pha rol gnod pa sel ba'i dpal 'di yon tan rgyan rnams kyis/ /phyug par bgyid na legs spyad
<p>56b.5</p>brgya la chags phyir g.yo ba'i snying / /mi brten pa yang rang dbang med par yun ring khyod la chags/ /slob dpon ma ti tsi tras rgyal po chen po ka nis ka la springs pa'i spring yig rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po bid+yA ka ra pra b+hA dang / /zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba ban de rin chen
<p>56b.6</p>mchog gis bsgyur/ A tsAr+ya dpal brtsegs kyis zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ tsi t+ta rat+na bi sho d+ha na kra ma nA ma le kha/ /bod skad du/ sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i spring yig /sangs rgyas dang byang chub
<p>56b.7</p>sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sa gsum dbang phyug skye dgu chos kyis skyong mdzad pa/ /lha mi'i bla ma 'phags pa'i gang zag rnams kyi yab/ /rgol ba tshar gcod rang gi 'khor gyi dga' skyed pa/ /chos kyi rgyal po gcig pu de ni rgyal gyur cig /blo zhan bdag
<p>57a</p>
<p>57a.1</p>'dras gzhan la skul bar mi nus shing / /bskul bas phan par 'gyur ba'ang deng sang nyung mod kyi/ /'on kyang sa yi bdag po khyod kyis nongs pa yal bor nas/ /'gro mang de 'drar 'gyur 'di ma bzod khyod la bskul/ /mi skyong khyod kyi dbang phyug 'di ni sngon chad nyid kyi
<p>57a.2</p>thugs/ /gdul dka' legs par btul las brnyes kyi gzhan gyis byin pa dang / /sa yi rum nas 'thon dang gnam babs lta zhig ga la lags/ /sa bdag dpal 'di mi nyams bzhed na da dung thugs thul 'tshal/ /gang zhig phan na de ni brtags te dka' yang mdzad
<p>57a.3</p>rigs la/ /gang zhig mi phan de ni bsgrub par sla yang gtang ba'i rigs/ /de phyir sngon tshe thub chen rgyal bu zla bar gyur pa yis/ /rgyal po su ta sa yi bu la gdams pa smras pas kyang / /rgyal po gcig pus g.yul ngor dmag gi dpung las rgyal/ /sems tsam tshar gcad phyir
<p>57a.4</p>ni sngar ma ma mdzad cig /mi yi bdag po 'jig rten phyi ma'ang gzigs par rigs/ /de bas dgyes kyang phan pa ma yin bsten mi rigs/ /zhes so/ /de phyir gang gis dman pa'i rigs su ltung byed pa/ /nga rgyal dgra spangs bdag gi tshig 'di sad phyir yang / /ci nas mi bdag khyod
<p>57a.5</p>kyis gus pas gsan rigs te/ /legs smras byis las blangs zhes thub chen gsal bar gsungs/ /sa bdag tsher ma'i shing las sbrang rtsi bzhin/ /dgra bo las kyang legs smras gzung bar bya/ /gser gyi ri las dug gi chu rgyun bzhin/ /yid 'ong skye bo'i tshig ngan
<p>57a.6</p>spang 'tshal lo/ /zhes so/ /gang zhig ma btul mnar med sogs/ /sdug bsngal bzod dkar skyed byed cing / /de nyid btul bas lha mi dang / /'jig rten min pa'i bde ba'ang 'thob/ /rab tu mthu ldan sems 'di ni/ /mkhas pa su zhig 'dul mi byed/ /'dir sems
<p>57a.7</p>ni rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba rtag tu rnam par mi rtog pa'i rang bzhin yin mod kyi/ lus dang ngag bran lta bu dang bcas pa glo bur gyi nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa dag gis dkrugs pa ste/ de'i phyir 'di dag rnam par sbyangs te nor bu chu shel gyi 'od ltar rab tu
<p>57b</p>
<p>57b.1</p>'od gsal ba'i rang bzhin dkrug ma dang bral ba bskyed de/ /'di tsam ni mi gnas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'o/ /de la 'dir bsdu na sems de dkrugs pas rtog pa can du byed cing / /lus dang ngag bran ltar 'khol ba ni rnam pa bzhi ste/ thams cad kyi rgyu rnam par rtog pa mang ba
<p>57b.2</p>dang / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / /gti mug shas che ba'o/ /de la gang rnam par rtog pa mang pa des ni rlung gi ting nge 'dzin la dmigs pas de spang bar bya ste/ bgrang dang rjes 'gro 'jog pa dang / rtog pa dang ni bsgyur pa dang / /yongs dag rnam pa drug tu 'dod/ /de ni
<p>57b.3</p>bgrang ba dang / /rjes su 'gro ba dang / 'jog pa dang / nye bar rtog pa dang / sgyur ba dang / yongs su dag pa ste rgyu drug dang ldan na yongs su rdzogs pa yin no/ /de la bgrang ba zhes bya ba ni/ /dbugs rngub pa dang dbugs 'byung ba dag la sems gtad nas mngon par 'du bya ba
<p>57b.4</p>med par lus dang sems rnal du bzhag ste dran pa tsam gyis gcig dang gnyis nas bcu'i bar du bgrang bar byed pa'o/ /sems mngon par bsdus pa dang rnam par g.yeng bar dogs pas ha cang mang ba dang nyung ngur ni ma yin no/ /de la skyon ni gsum yod de/ gal te gcig la
<p>57b.5</p>gnyis su brtsis na lhag par bgrang ba'i skyon yod do/ /gal te gnyis la gcig tu 'dzin na ma tshang bar bgrang ba'i skyon no/ /gal te dbugs rngub pa la dbugs 'byin par 'dzin tam dbugs 'byin pa la dbugs rngub par 'dzin na 'chol bar 'dzin pa'i skyon no/ /de las
<p>57b.6</p>gzhan pa ni yang dag par bgrang ba yin no/ /bar skabs su sems rnam par g.yengs na/ /yang mgo nas ji srid du ting nge 'dzin ma thob kyi bar du bgrang bar bya'o/ /rjes su 'gro ba zhes bya ba ni 'di dag ji srid cig tu 'byung ngam 'jug /ci 'di dag lus thams cad la khyab
<p>57b.7</p>bdag gcig gam phyogs 'ga' zhig nas rgyu ba dag yin zhes mngon par 'du bya ba med par dbugs rngub pa dang / /dbugs 'byung ba'i rjes su 'gro ba ste/ de 'jug pa na lkog ma dang / snying ga dang / lte ba dang / rked pa dang / brla dang / byin par 'jug pa'i rim
<p>58a</p>
<p>58a.1</p>gyis rkang pa gnyis kyi bar du rjes su 'gro la/ 'byung ba na mtho gang dang 'dom gang gi bar du 'byung ngo / /gzhan dag na re rlung gi dkyil 'khor dang rnam par 'thor byed kyi rlung gi bar du'o zhes zer te/ 'di ni de kho na nyid yid la byed pa'i phyir rigs pa yin no/ /
<p>58a.2</p>'jog pa zhes bya ba ni nor bu'i thag pa bzhin du sna'i rtse mo nas rkang pa'i mthe bo'i bar du gnas par lta zhing ci 'di dag phan 'dogs par byed pa zhig gam/ gnod par byed pa zhig gam/ grang ngam dro ba zhig ces rtog pa'o/ /nye bar rtog pa zhes bya ba ni 'di dag ni rlung 'ba' zhig ma yin gyi
<p>58a.3</p>'byung ba chen po bzhi po dag dang 'byung ba dag las mngon par grub pa'i rgyur byas pa'i gzugs dang / de dag la brten pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyang yod do zhes phung po lnga nye bar rtog pa'o/ /sgyur ba zhes bya ba ni rlung la dmigs pa'i blo bsgyur te chos kyi mchog gi bar du
<p>58a.4</p>blo gong nas gong du dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la yang dag par sbyor ba'o/ /yongs su dag pa ni mthong ba'i lam la sogs pa la 'jug pa'o/ /gzhan dag na re sgyur ba ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa nas rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyi bar yin la/ rnam par dag pa ni zad pa shes pa la sogs pa yin
<p>58a.5</p>no zhes zer ro/ /'di lta bu ni slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyi zhal snga nas ji ltar bris pa kho bos 'dir yang bris par shes par bya'o/ /de ltar rim pa drug po de dag gi las ni/ ji skad du 'phags pa sa'i snying po 'khor lo bcu pa'i mdo las gsungs pa bzhin te/ de las ni ji ltar dran pa'i
<p>58a.6</p>dbang gis yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba la rtog ce na/ /yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du bgrang ba dang / rjes su 'gro ba dang / zhi gnas dang / lhag mthong dang / 'jug pa dang / yongs su dag pa la rtog go/ /de la bgrang bas ni bya ba'i las kyi dngos po rnam
<p>58a.7</p>pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ /rten du gyur pas rnam par rtog pa dang rnam par dpyod pa gnyis thul bas/ /dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba'i mtshan nyid 'dzin par nus pa'o/ /rjes su 'gro bas kyang bya ba'i las kyi dngos po rnam pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ yang dag par 'byung ba la brten
<p>58b</p>
<p>58b.1</p>cing / rnam par rtog pa dang rnam par dpyod pa dang bral ba dang / dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba'i 'jug pa'i mtshan nyid la mkhas par 'gyur ba'o/ /zhi gnas kyis ni bya ba'i las kyi dngos po rnam pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba 'bri bar mngon du ston pa dang / ting
<p>58b.2</p>nge 'dzin gyi mchog la gnas par nus pa'o/ /lhag mthong gis kyang bya ba'i las kyi dngos po rnam pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba zad par mngon du ston pa dang / sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos so sor rtog pa la gnas pa'o/ /'jug pas kyang bya ba'i
<p>58b.3</p>las kyi dngos po rnam pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ nye bar len pa'i phung po spong ba'i sbyor ba la mkhas pa dang / 'phags pa'i sar 'jug pa la sbyor ba'o/ /yongs su dag pas kyang bya ba'i las kyi dngos po rnam pa gnyis byed par 'gyur te/ kun nas nyon mongs pa spong ba dang / lta ba
<p>58b.4</p>yongs su dag pa'o zhes so/ /de ltar dbugs thung ngu rngubs na yang dbugs thung ngu rngubs so snyam du yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rab tu shes so zhes bya ba la sogs pa bcu drug kyang legs par rtogs par 'gyur ro/ /'dir rnam par rtog pa mang ba la bstan pa ni gtsor byas kyi yon tan ma
<p>58b.5</p>lus pa 'di la brten pas na thar pa'i grong khyer gyi sgo 'byed pa ni dbugs rngub pa dang 'byung ba dran pa yin te zhes gsungs so/ /ji ltar zhe na rab tu gdul dga' ba'i sems zhes brjod pa de ni rlung las gud du ma dmigs pa'i phyir te/ de bas na sems zhes bya ba de ni rlung du brjod do zhes
<p>58b.6</p>gsungs so/ /de ltar mi bdag khyod kyis rlung gi phra dang zab mkhyen nas/ /yun ring dus nas rnam rtog dgra yis rab tu gtses pas shin tu yang / /mnyel zhing skyo ba'i thugs ni deng nas ngal bsos rtog dgra bzlog pa dang / /lo yis ma yin gus par sbyor bas zhag gi rim pas rtog
<p>58b.7</p>bral mdzod/ /de nas rim gyis yongs su dag pa'i mthar yang khyod kyi thugs gzhol na/ /sa bdag khyod gyi skye ba 'bras bcas de nas chos kyi rgyal por 'gyur/ /de yi bar du lha mi'i bde ba tshad med rnams la dgyes bzhin du/ /thugs btul mthu yis spyod pa 'di la the tshom
<p>59a</p>
<p>59a.1</p>med par mngon sum gnas/ /rnam par rtog pa'i gnyen po bshad zin te/ /sems kyi rtog pa sbyang ba'i rim pa'o/ /mi skyong khyod kyi thugs ni gal te bud med kyis phrogs na/ /'di ni sa yi bdag po'i mthu rtsal rab tu dman pa ste/ /gang gi g.yul chen
<p>59a.2</p>'jigs su rung ba gzhom pa'i thabs mkhyen na/ /mi gtsang kun snod mngon gyur bud med mtshan nyid mi mkhyen 'di mtshar che/ /shin tu yid 'ong tsher ma'i gnod pa'ang mi bzod lus 'di ni/ /bud med bsten pa'i rgyu las 'di dang slad pa mgo gcod sogs/ /rab tu bzod dka'i sdug
<p>59a.3</p>bsngal 'byung 'di nyid kyis mngon sum na/ /'on kyang bla ma'i bka' yis 'dod chags zhi bar byed pa mdor brjod bgyi/ /chags pa can rnams kyi gnyen po ni rus gong yid la bya ba yin te/ keng rus chags can thams cad la zhes bshad pas so/ /ji ltar zhe na/ /rus pa rgya
<p>59a.4</p>mtsho'i bar du ni/ /spro zhing sdud pas las dang po/ /rkang rus dang ni thod phyed bar/ /btang bas sbyang ba byas par bshad/ /smin ma'i bar du sems 'dzin pas/ /yid la byed pa rdzogs pa yin/ /zhes bshad pa'i rim pas so/ /gzhan yang byis pa rnams ni phal cher kha dog dang / 
<p>59a.5</p>dbyibs dang / reg pa 'jam pa dang / bsnyen bkur la chags te/ de dag gi gnyen por ni rnam par bsngos pa dang / rnam par dmar ba dang / rnam par tshig pa dag yid la byed pas kha dog la chags pa dag sel to/ /rnam par rnags pa dang / rnam par zos pa dang / rnam par 'thor bdag
<p>59a.6</p>yid la byed pas ni dbyibs la chags pa sel bar byed do/ /rnam par dbus gzhig pa dang rus gong rgyus pas 'brel ba dag yid la byed pas ni reg bya 'jam pa la chags pa sel to/ /rnam par bam pa'i ro mi g.yo ba rkyal ba stong pa bus pa lta bu/ rdo ltar bsnyen bkur byed pa dang
<p>59a.7</p>bral ba yid la byed pas ni rkang pa bkru ba la sogs pa'i bsnyen bkur la chags pa sel bar byed do/ /gzhan yang rnam par phye ste brjod na/ sngo bsangs la sogs pa'i kha dog la chags pa zhig na rnam par bsngos par yid la bya'o/ /tsan+dan dang ga bur la sogs pa'i dris byugs pa'i
<p>59b</p>
<p>59b.1</p>lus la chags pa lta na rnam par rnags par yid la bya'o/ /mtshan sprad pa'i reg bya la chags pa zhig na rnam par 'bus gzhig par yid la bya'o/ /dbyibs phun sum tshogs pa la chags pa lta na rnam par bam par yid la bya'o/ /rgyan gyis mdzes pa'i lus la chags pa zhig na rnam
<p>59b.2</p>par dmar bar yid la bya'o/ /sha rgyas pa'i lus la chags pa zhig na rnam par zos par yid la bya'o/ /'khyud pa dang 'o byas pa la sogs pa'i rtse 'jo la chags pa'i dus na rnam par 'thor bar yid la bya'o/ /kha dog dang dbyibs phun sum tshogs pa la chags par gyur na rnam par
<p>59b.3</p>tshig par yid la bya'o/ /so rnams dkar ba la chags pa'i tshe na rus gong gi yid la byed pas zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /rab tu mi bzad nags bsregs me lce'i tshogs/ /char rgyun drag pos skad cig zhi byed ltar/ /byis pa'i nags tshal thal bar byed pa yi/ /'dod chags me chen
<p>59b.4</p>mi sdug char gyis 'joms/ /'jig rten gnod pa'i rtsa ba ji snyed pa/ /kun gyi phul byung 'khrig pa'i 'dod chags te/ /sa bdag 'di mkhyen 'dod las phyir ltos dang / /rab tu dgyes pa byis pas ma myong ba/ /bsam gtan bde bas lus la phan 'dogs shing / /kha na ma tho
<p>59b.5</p>med pa myong ba'i rigs/ /'dod chags dang bcas pa'i sems sbyang ba'i rim pa ste/ 'dod chags kyi gnyen po bshad zin to// //lha mi'i bla mas gang du 'bad pas bkag gyur pa/ /de ni 'gro la byams dang snying rje med pa ste/ /de phyir mi dbang khyod kyis thub la gus pa dang / nyid
<p>59b.6</p>kyi thugs kyang dam pa'i grangs su 'gyur ba'i phyir/ /gang la skra rtses gzung bya'i skye bo de la yang / /nyid kyi sras bzhin gces shing byams pas bskyang bar rigs/ /bshes gnyen dam pa'i lung gis goms par byas pa las/ /srin po sha za seng ge sogs kyang 'gro la byams/ /
<p>59b.7</p>de phyir mi dbang khyod kyis thugs ni 'jam pa dang / /'gro ba bskyang las nam yang phyir ldog ma mdzad cig /legs pa'i lam ni ji snyed bstan pa dag las kyang / /gtso bor gyur pa byams dang snying rjer dam pas gsungs/ /'di ji ltar bsgom par bya zhe na/ dang por rang gi ma'am
<p>60a</p>
<p>60a.1</p>pha'am bu 'am bu mo 'am/ 'brel pa gnyis sam/ gang yang rung ba cig bde ba ma lus pa dang phrad par gyur cig snyam pa dang / /bdag gis de dang phrad par bya'o zhes pa dang / nus pa lta na dngos su de bsgrub pa dang / phrad pa la phrag dog med pa nyi ma
<p>60a.2</p>'ga' zhig gus par bsgom mo/ /de nas ni de bas cung zad mi gcugs pa la'o/ /rim gyis par ma la'o/ /de nas dgra bo dman pa la'o/ /de nas de'i bar ma la'o/ /de nas de dgra bo rab tu ma rungs pa la'o/ /de la ma la sogs pa dang mnyam pa thob pa na grong dang grong khyer pa
<p>60a.3</p>la'o/ /de nas ni yul dang ljongs dang gling gcig dang gnyis la sogs pa nas stong spyi phud dang / stong gnyis bar ma dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po dang / phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA klung gi bye ma snyed la sogs par byams pas khyab par byas te/ de nas gzhung de
<p>60a.4</p>bzhin du sdug bsngal dang bral bar gyur cig ces pa dang / sdug bsngal dang bral ba la dga' ba dang / de dag 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam la dgod par bya'o zhes bya ba'i rim pas snying rje dang dga' ba dang btang snyoms rnams bsgom mo/ /dang po nyid du sdug cing yid du 'ong ba'i mtshan nyid
<p>60a.5</p>can gyi byams pa yid la ma byas par ni sdug bsngal dang bral ba'i snying rje ga la 'jug ste/ de ltar rim pa gzhan yang ngo / /gnod par sems pa'i yid tsam bor bas kyang / /'khor los sgyur nyid thob par thub pas gsungs/ /byams sogs goms las 'chi med ma brnyes kyang / /
<p>60a.6</p>tshangs pa'i 'jig rten bde ba rgya chen thob/ /de phyir mi rje khyod kyis gang spyod pa/ /tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi yis ni gnas par rigs/ /khyod kyis 'byor pa dug can zas bzhin du/ /bor nas gcig pu gzhan du gshegs 'tshal na/ /grogs bzang 'dod med dge ba de bkri'i phyir/ /
<p>60a.7</p>thugs ni rnam par sbyang bar cis mi mdzad/ /zhe sdang dang bcas pa'i sems sbyang ba'i rim pa ste/ zhe sdang gi gnyen po bshad zin to// //rang dang gzhan dang gnyis ka las skye dang / /rgyu med 'byung zhes smra ba gang lags pa/ /'di dag log par smra ba phung khrol ba/ /
<p>60b</p>
<p>60b.1</p>legs par spyad kyang 'bras bu mi 'dod 'byin/ /de phyir khyod kyis rten cing 'brel 'byung ba/ /lta ngan sel 'joms thub pa'i man ngag mchog /bdud rtsi'i mchog 'di myur du gsol ba yis/ /dkar phyogs ma lus rgyas shing brtan por mdzod/ /rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ji lta
<p>60b.2</p>bu zhe na/ 'di lta ste ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed/ 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa/ rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs/ ming dang gzugs kyi rkyen gyis skye mched drug /de'i rkyen gyis reg pa/ de'i rkyen gyis tshor ba/ de'i rkyen gyis sred pa/ de'i
<p>60b.3</p>rkyen gyis len pa/ de'i rkyen gyis srid pa/ de'i rkyen gyis skye ba/ de'i rkyen gyis rga shi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa rnams 'byung bar 'gyur te/ /de ltar na sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'di 'ba' zhig
<p>60b.4</p>'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes shes rab kyi mig gis lta bar byas te rgyu med pa la sogs pa bsal lo/ /don 'di ni 'phags pa byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod las/ gang du ma rig skye 'gyur ba/ /nyon mongs rgyu ni tshul bzhin min/ /de yi rkyen ni 'du byed de/ /sdug bsngal bar du skye bar
<p>60b.5</p>'gyur/ /zhes pa dang / gang gis sems can dag 'gyur ba/ /rgyu gnyis dang ni rkyen gnyis te/ /gzhan las rjes su mthun sgra dang / /nang du tshul bzhin lta ba'o/ /de bzhin rgyu ni zhi gnas te/ /lhag mthong yang ni rkyen yin no/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de ltar srid pa 'byung ba'i rim pa la
<p>60b.6</p>yid ches par byas nas/ yang ma rig pa 'gags pas 'du byed 'gag pa nas sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po 'di 'ba' zhig 'gag par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du yid la bya'o/ /de nas rtag par ma yin pa dang / chad par ma yin pa dang / 'pho bar ma yin pa dang / de dang
<p>60b.7</p>'dra ba'i rgyud du 'jug pa dang / rgyu chung ngu las 'bras bu chen po 'byung ba zhes nges par bzung ste/ phyi rol yang sa bon las myu gu dang de las 'dab ma dang / /de las sdong bu dang / de las me tog dang / de las 'bras bu 'byung zhing rgyu de dag dang rkyen 'brel bar 'byung ba khams bzhi
<p>61a</p>
<p>61a.1</p>dang nam mkha' dang dus kyi khams te/ rnam pa bcu gnyis po 'di dag tsam mo zhes 'byung ba dang / 'gag pa las rgyu med pa dang / mi mthun pa'i rgyu spangs te 'dir ni mdor bsdus nas rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yid la byas pas rig pa bskyed pa dang / ma rig
<p>61a.2</p>pa'i ngo bo'am de las 'byung ba'i log par lta ba spang ba'o/ /gal te rgyas par yid la byed pa lta zhig na rang rang gi mtshan nyid dang / ming gi don dang / las tha dad pa dang / yan lag lngas yang dag par bsdus pa dang / yan lag gsum gyis yang dag par bsdus pa dang / gsum las
<p>61a.3</p>gnyis 'byung ba dang / gnyis las bdun 'byung ba dang / bdun las gsum 'byung ba dang / dus gsum pa'i ngo bor gzhag pa dang / rkyen dang 'brel ba dag yid la bya'o/ /sa bdag rten cing 'brel 'byung mkhyen na snang bas mun pa bzhin/ /khyod kyi thugs la gnas pa'i gti mug go skabs
<p>61a.4</p>ga la mchis/ /'di mkhyen srid pa'i 'khor lo phra zhing zab pa gzigs pa'i phyir/ /shes rab ye shes spyan gnyis dri med lung gi sman byugs gzigs/ /ji skad du 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas kyang / /rten cing 'brel bar 'byung 'di rgyal ba yi/ /gsung gi mdzod gyi gces pa zab mo
<p>61a.5</p>ste/ /gang gis 'di ni yang dag mthong ba des/ /sangs rgyas de nyid rig pa rnam mchog mthong / /zhes bstan to/ /gti mug dang bcas pa'i sems sbyang ba'i rim pa ste/ rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba yid la byed pa bshad zin to// //mi yi bdag po gal te phra ba'i thugs kyi
<p>61a.6</p>go skabs su/ /thog ma'i rtsom med dus can sdig pa'i rtsa ba'i rtog dgra 'di/ /zhen pa gnas snyam zhum pa'i rtog pa mi bzad zhugs gyur na/ /de yi gnyen por brten cing skyes pa'i dngos pos rang bzhin gzigs/ /dri med me long ngos la skyes pa'i bzhin gyi gzugs brnyan gang / /gal te yang dag
<p>61a.7</p>gnas na rkyen la rag las mi 'gyur zhing / /slar 'di rnam par 'jig 'gyur go skabs can du ga la 'gyur/ /de phyir dngos med rkyen la rag las gcig pu rnam par spang / /ji ltar gnas pa'i rang bzhin 'di yang legs par rnam dpyad na/ /rab tu phra rdul bar du 'gyur
<p>61b</p>
<p>61b.1</p>zhes dam pas dang por gsungs/ /gal te dngos yod de dag shes rab cis mi 'bab/ /de phyir de yang phyogs cha'i bye brag dag gis ga la gnas/ /rin chen sems kyi khyad par 'ga' zhig sna tshogs snang zhe na/ /de bzhin 'di la'ang skad cig ces bya rab phra dam pas gsungs/ /skad cig skad
<p>61b.2</p>cig ces bya'i gang dag phra la rnam par rmongs/ /de yang ji ltar thog ma dbus mtha' dag tu blta mi nus/ /de'i phyir rin po che'i phreng ba las/ /skad cig ji ltar mtha' yod ltar/ /thog ma dang dbus de ltar brtag /skad cig rang bzhin gsum gyi phyir/ /'jig rten skad cig la mi
<p>61b.3</p>gnas/ /zhes bstan to/ /de ltar 'di dag phyi dang nang du bcas pa gcig min zhing / /de nyid phyir na de yi rang bzhin rnam bsags du ma'ang min/ /'di dag las dben dngos po shes rab mig gis 'ga' ma dmigs/ /des na 'di dag mtha' gnyis grol bar dam pas gsal bar gsungs/ /
<p>61b.4</p>de bzhin gcig gis gcig nyid skyes pa mngon sum 'gal mthong ste/ /rab tu phra ba'i 'bras bu rgyu ni gcig min la ltos par/ /'gro ba'i mngon sum nyid du ston pa bzhin du nges par gnas/ /de bzhin gcig gis gcig min skyed sogs thams cad gnod par bcas/ /dngos rnams
<p>61b.5</p>thug med ma lus slar skyed 'gyur 'di bzlog dka'i phyir/ /yod pa 'ga' zhig skye zhes 'di ni sus kyang smra mi nus/ /gang med 'ga' zhig skye na med pa'i tha snyad su zhig 'jog /de phyir bdag las skye sogs 'di dag mkhas pas rtsa nas bton/ de ltar khyod kyi shes rab spyan gsal
<p>61b.6</p>dri med rnam rgyas pas/ /rten cing 'brel 'byung mtshan nyid 'di la yun ring gzigs pa na/ /thog med sring rgyud bsags pa'i bsnyengs gnas rab tu phra ba yang / /gang na'ang gnas par 'gyur 'di gzigs min mi bdag gang gis zhum/ /de ltar ni 'phags pa mi pham pa'i zhal snga nas/ 'di
<p>61b.7</p>la bsal bya ci yang med/ /bsnan par bya ba cung zad med/ /yang dag nyid la yang dag lta/ /yang dag mthong na rnam par grol/ /zhes gsungs shing / 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas kyang / mthong ba'i chos la mya ngan 'das/ /bya ba byas pa'ang de nyid yin//zhes gsungs so/ /des na
<p>62a</p>
<p>62a.1</p>gang la dga' ba'am yang dag skrag nas 'di ci zhig /bskal pa bye bar bsgrubs kyang brtan gnas de ni su yis nus/ /gang zhig nam mkha' gzhom zhes 'bad pa'ang blun te rnam par ngal/ /ci'i phyir zhe na gdod nas ma skyes de la su yis dgag /de 'dra'i
<p>62a.2</p>gnas med 'dir gnas ye shes can te rtag bde ldan/ /gang la rnam rtog med 'di bde zhes thub pas gsal bar gsungs/ /'di spangs lha yul 'dod pas rab tu yid 'phrog byed pa dang / /'khor los sgyur ba'i 'byor ba'ang dam pas tsher ma'i gnod 'drar gsungs/ sa bdag
<p>62a.3</p>'on kyang gnas 'dir shin tu dgyes par ma gyur cig /ci phyir zhe na bdag gzhan phan pa mi bzod 'byor las khyod/ /rnam par ltung ba'i sgo mo mi mkhas rnams la 'di rab spang / /kha cig sgo 'dir rab dga' 'jug la snying brtse ring du spangs/ /gzhan dag gnas 'dir 'khrul
