<p>62a.4</p>phyir las 'bras thal ba bzhin du byed/ /gzhan dag shin tu med las sangs rgyas yon tan bsam yas 'dod/ /'di 'dra 'di dag sgo 'dir zhugs nas rang gzhan de las nyams/ /de phyir 'di ni yan lag ldan par bags kyis bsten par bgyi/ /de ltar ni 'phags pa dri ma med par
<p>62a.5</p>grags pas bstan pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo las kyang / ming yang yod dang yod ma yin par tshig gis gsungs/ /rgyu la brten te byung ba'i chos ni 'di kun te/ /'di la bdag med tshor ba po dang byed med kyang / /dge dang mi dge'i las rnams cung zad med mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs
<p>62a.6</p>so/ /rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i de bzhin nyid bsam gyis mi khyab par yid la bya'o/ /mi dbang yan lag bzhi po 'di tsam gyis/ /khyod kyi thugs kyi dri ma rags pa rnams/ /nges par bsal 'gyur 'di la dgos pa mdzad/ /de las gong du khyad par rnam bzhed na/ /dkyil 'khor
<p>62a.7</p>byug pa sngon du 'gro ba yis/ /skye ba gzhan du 'byor pa mi zad pa/ /da lta'i bzhed pa nyid kyi phyag gnas ltar/ /slu ba med par bdag gis brjod par bgyi/ /oM badzra re khe hUM/ gtsang spyod pa yi lci ba ni/ /chu dang 'o ma zho dang mar/ /thams cad de las byung ba dag /snod gtsang
<p>62b</p>
<p>62b.1</p>bskol te chu rnams dbo/ /tshigs ma dor te dbus kyi chas/ /dbyibs ci dga' ba'i maN+Dal ni/ /sa bdag khru gang yan chad par/ /gsang sngags don la gzhol bar byug /de nas de ni gus pa yis/ rgyal ba sras gsum bcas la 'bul/ /mjug tu thub pas gsungs pa yi/ /tshigs
<p>62b.2</p>bcad 'di dag brjod par bya/ /ba yi lci ba chur bcas sbyin pa ste/ /legs par byug par byed pa tshul khrims so/ /srin bu grog sbur bsal ba bzod pa yin/ /bya ba la ni nyer zhugs brtson 'grus te/ /de yi skad cig sems ni gcig byed pa/ /bsam gtan shes rab ri mo gsal
<p>62b.3</p>ba'o/ /thub pa'i maN+Dal byas pa yis/ /pha rol phyin pa 'di drug 'thob/ /gser gyi mdog tu 'gyur ba ste/ /nad rnams kun dang bral bar 'gyur/ /zla ba ltar mdzes gsal ba yi/ /lha dang mi ni dam par skye/ /nor dang gser ni 'byor ba yi/ /rgyal po'i rigs su skye bar
<p>62b.4</p>'gyur/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i pho brang mchog /maN+Dal gang zhig byed pa dang / /sdig pa thams cad mi byed cing / /dge ba phun sum tshogs pa dang / /rang gi sems ni yongs 'dul ba/ /'di dag sangs rgyas rnams kyis bsngags/ /zhes so/ /de nas dge ba de nyid rgyu mtshan
<p>62b.5</p>du byas la/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal zhing / /dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su mchi/ /bdag ni khyed la rnams kun dbul/ /sdig pa thams cad bshags par bgyi/ /'gro ba'i dge la rjes yi rang / /dam chos 'khor lo mchog bskor dang / /yongs su mya ngan
<p>62b.6</p>'das spang phyir/ /bdag ni khyod la gsol ba 'debs/ /'di sogs dge ba'i las rnams ni/ /byang chub bla na med par bsngo/ /'gro ba sdug bsngal khur chen bor ba'i phyir/ /bdag gi sems ni byang chub phyir bskyed de/ /ma bsgral bsgral dang ma grol dgrol ba dang / /
<p>62b.7</p>dbugs ma phyin pa bdag gis dbugs dbyung ste/ /mya ngan ma 'das bdag gis mya ngan bzla/ /de ltar byang chub kyi sems rab tu brtan par bskyed la ji ltar 'dod pa'i bya ba dge ba la 'jug par bya'o/ /mi dbang khyod thugs sbyangs pas dge ba rgya chen dag la dgyes bskyed na/ /
<p>63a</p>
<p>63a.1</p>sbyin dang tshul khrims bzod pa brtson 'grus bsam gtan shes rab pha rol phyin/ /rgya chen spel mdzad der yang khyod kyi thugs ni rma med 'bad 'tshal te/ /sems ma bsrungs pa'i skyes bu'i dge la 'jug pa bu chu'i rgyun khrus ltar/ /phan dang 'brel ba'i gnod
<p>63a.2</p>pa'ang rab tu ma rungs gyur pa'i gnas skabs mchis/ /gnas 'di mkhas pas gzigs nas mthu ldan nyid kyi thugs ni bsrung 'tshal lo/ /de ltar bsnyengs dang bral na mang du gsol ci 'tshal/ /phan pa'i man ngag don po 'di lags te/ /khyod kyi thugs thul mdzod cig bcom ldan
<p>63a.3</p>gyis/ /sems ni chos kyi rtsa ba lags zhes gsungs/ /tshigs su bcad pa gcig pu 'di 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas mkhar gyi rgyal po bde spyod la gdams pa bshes pa'i spring yig las bdag gis drangs pa'o/ /mi skyong khyod ni gal te gsang ba'i lam la dgyes pa na/ /
<p>63a.4</p>lam der rab tu rtogs dka' sems la rma 'byin tshig 'phros te/ /bud med 'khyud sogs tshul khrims ma yin yid la byed par ldan/ /kha cig mngon sum 'khrig dang drag shul spyod la 'jug pa ste/ /mi dbang thugs la gnod na thub pa'i bka' yang dug dang 'dra/ /de phyir khyod kyis
<p>63a.5</p>gsang ba'i lam du zhugs pa'i rgyu mtshan las/ /khyod thugs 'dod chags la sogs dri mas gos pa 'di ni spangs/ /gang gzhan skye bo de 'dra bzlog par khyod kyis rnam bsgrub rigs/ /don 'di ni/ zhu ba'i 'og tu za ba la/ /mar gyi nying khu ka ra dang / /sbrang rtsi dag ni bdud rtsi
<p>63a.6</p>bzhin/ /ma zhu za ba dug tu 'gyur/ /de bzhin rab rgyas bdud rtsi mchog /dgongs pa'i tshig la mi mkhas shing / /byis pa'i blo dang ldan rnams la/ /mi bzad pa yi dug tu 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs te/ 'di ni 'phags pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i
<p>63a.7</p>mdo las gsungs pa bdag gis 'dir bris pa'o/ /rin chen sems 'di rnam par sbyang ba'i phyir/ /thub pa'i bka' lung cung zad 'dir bris pas/ /sa yi bdag po thugs ni dri med pa/ /ston ka'i zla rgyas lta bur gsal gyur cig /'gro ba'ang rim gyis sems ni rnam sbyangs te/ /mu tig
<p>63b</p>
<p>63b.1</p>dri med 'bru ltar rnam dag shog /sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i rim pa zhes bya ba'i spring yig slob dpon byang chub sems dpa' chen po dgra las rgyal ba gsang bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po A tsAr+ya du lo pa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab
<p>63b.2</p>kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ gu ru le kha/ bod skad du/ bla ma la spring ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rgyal sras rnams kyi don du stug po bkod par sangs rgyas nas/ /dga' ldan skye bo'i don mdzad phyir ni dam pa tog
<p>63b.3</p>dkar gyur/ /de nas 'dir ni 'gro ba'i don du shAkya thub gyur gang / /kun mkhyen nyes bral ngo bo nyid med de ni rgyal gyur cig /bla ma mkhas pa blo gros rgya che la/ /'dod sred bag med nyon mongs spang ba'i thabs/ /thub pa'i gsung bzhin mdor bsdus brjod pa 'di/ /sman bzhin
<p>63b.4</p>phan par brtags nas gsan pa'i rigs/ /ji ltar rigs ngan lag nas rin chen mchog /blo ldan skye bos rab gus len pa ltar/ /kun rmongs bdag gis brtse bas gsol ba yi/ /spring yig 'di ni rab gus blang bar 'os/ /ston pa'i mdo sde zab cing rgya chen rnams/ /mkhan po
<p>63b.5</p>nyid kyi thugs su chud mod kyi/ /lus kyi don du gsod pa'i kha zas ltar/ /bdag gis brjod pa 'di yang bstan par mdzod/ /ri dgas glang po phye ma leb dang nya/ /sbrang ma lnga po lnga yis bcom gyur na/ /gcig gis bcom na gang gis lnga po kun/ /rtag tu bsten na ci phyir bcom mi
<p>63b.6</p>'gyur/ /'dod pa rnams ni kun nas 'bar ba ste/ /rab tu smad cing bsad dang dgra bo yin/ /phyir rgol ba dang rtswa yi sgron me dang / /ki ma pa ka yi 'bras bu ral gri'i so/ /me mdag spungs pa dug gi lo ma dang / /lcags kyu tsher ma mi gtsang rlubs lta bu/ /'dod pa'i rgyus ni sems can
<p>63b.7</p>dmyal bar ltung / /yi dgas rnams dang dud 'gror skye bar 'gyur/ /'dod la brkam pa bde 'gror mi skye zhing / /mya ngan 'das pa nam yang thob mi 'gyur/ /dal rnyed shes rab ldan gyur cing / /rgyal ba'i bstan la zhugs pa khyod/ /'dod dang sred pa bag med dang / /nyon mongs rnams
<p>64a</p>
<p>64a.1</p>ni spang bar mdzod/ /kun rtog las ni 'dod skye bas/ /'dod pa'i rtsa ba mkhyen nas ni/ /khyod ni kun rtog ma mdzad dang / /de ni khyod la 'byung mi 'gyur/ /'dod pa rnams las mya ngan skye/ /'dod pa rnams las 'jigs pa 'byung / /'dod pa dag ni rnam spangs
<p>64a.2</p>na/ /mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/ /'dod pa'i rnam smin sdug bsngal te/ /dang po mngar la 'bras bu tsha/ /me sgron lag nas ma bor na/ /mjug tu byis pa sreg byed bzhin/ /nor bu'i rna cha bu dang chung ma la/ /yongs su chags sems gang yin la ltos na/ /lcags
<p>64a.3</p>shing gres ma las byas chings ma gang / /de dag dam po min zhes 'phags pa gsungs/ /'dod pa'i chings ma gang yin de lhod kyang / /rab tu dgrol bar dka' zhes 'phags pas gsungs/ /brtan rnams 'dod pa'i bde la mi lta bar/ /de dag gtubs nas myur du 'gro bar
<p>64a.4</p>byed/ /'jig rten sna tshogs gang de 'dod min gyi/ /skyes bu'i kun rtog 'dod chags 'dod pa yin/ /'jig rten sna tshogs de la gnas kyang ni/ /'on kyang 'jig rten 'di na 'dun pa 'dul/ /mi rnams la ni brten pa'i 'dod pa med/ /'dod pa gang la chags te mi rtag pas/ /yang srid
<p>64a.5</p>med phyir sems kyis rab spangs la/ /'chi ba'i gnas mi 'gyur bar gyis zhes gsungs/ /'dun pa bskyed cing zag par mi byed dang / /sems la skyon med pa dang dran pa dang / /'dod pa rnams la so sor ma chags gang / /de ni gong du 'pho ba yin zhes gsungs/ /mgar ba yis ni
<p>64a.6</p>rdul bzhin du/ /blo gros ldan pas rim pa bzhin/ /skad cig thang cig cung zad tsam/ /rang gi dri ma bsal bar bya/ /lham mkhan gyis ni ko ba dag /yongs su sbyangs pa'i lham bde ltar/ /'dod pa gang dag gang spangs pa/ /de de bde ba phun sum ldan/ /gal te bde ba kun
<p>64a.7</p>'dod pa/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs su spongs/ /'dod pa thams cad yongs spangs pas/ /mchog tu bde ba thob par 'gyur/ /ji srid 'dod pa'i rjes 'brangs pa/ /de nyid rab tu ngoms mi 'gyur/ /de la gang dag shes rab kyis/ /zlog byed de dag tshim pa 'thob/ /'dod
<p>64b</p>
<p>64b.1</p>pas ngoms par mi 'gyur bas/ /shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa bde/ /shes rab kyis ni ngoms pa'i mi/ /srid pa'i dbang du mi 'gyur ro/ /'dod la chags pa'i mi gang yin/ /de dag kye ma chos min dga'//cung zad gson por 'dug pa na/ /bar chad mthong bar mi 'gyur ro/ /
<p>64b.2</p>blo ngan longs spyod kyis bcom pa/ /pha rol tshol bar mi byed cing / /bsam brlag 'dod la srid pa yis/ /bdag phung gzhan yang phung bar byed/ /lha yis 'dod pa'i char bab kyang / /'dod ldan rnams la ngoms mi 'gyur/ /brgya byin dang ni mnyam pa yi/ /lha yi 'dod pa yod
<p>64b.3</p>gyur kyang / /nga las nus bzhin mi ngoms par/ /rtogs par mdzod la legs par spyod/ /'dod pa mnog chung nyes mang bar/ /mkhas pa rnams kyi khong du chud/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyan thos rnams/ /lha yi 'dod pa rnams la yang / /lhag par dga' bar mi 'gyur
<p>64b.4</p>gyi/ /sred pa zad pas dgyes par 'gyur/ /gang dag sdug bsngal rgyu shes pa/ /de dag nam yang 'dod la dga' mi 'gyur/ /'jig rten dag na zug rngu'i rgyur mkhyen nas/ /'di dag gdul phyir bstan pa 'thob par mdzod/ /'dod pa spang ba'i le'u ste dang po'o// //lus
<p>64b.5</p>can rnam par rtog pas rab bcom pa/ /'dod chags mi bzad gtsang ma'i rjes lta bas/ /'dod chags phyir zhing rab tu 'phel 'gyur te/ /rang gi 'ching ba de yis dam por byed/ /gang dag rnam rtog nye bar zhi dga' zhing / /mi sdug bsgom pa rtag tu dran byed pa/ /de yi sred pa rab tu
<p>64b.6</p>spangs pa yin/ /rang gi 'ching ba de dag gtubs par 'gyur/ /'dod pa'i mun nag dra bas g.yogs/ /sred pa'i dgab pas bkab pa dang / /bag med 'ching bas bcings pa dag /tshod mar chud pas nya dang 'dra/ /skyes bu bag med rab tu spyod byed pa/ /'khri shing bzhin du sred pa
<p>64b.7</p>'phel 'gyur zhing / /skye rga na 'chi'i rjes su 'gro 'gyur te/ /ma drung nu zho 'dod pa'i bu dang 'dra/ /'dod pa'i bran dang mngon dga' chags byed dang / /yid bde ba la rtog par byed pa dag /de yis yang dang yang du 'khor bar 'khyams/ /tshal dang 'bras bu 'dod pa'i
<p>65a</p>
<p>65a.1</p>spre dang mtshungs/ /mi gang rtag tu bde ba 'dod byed pa/ /skye rga na 'chi'i dra bar chud 'gyur zhing / /ngan 'gro'i srid pa rnams kyis mdun du bdar/ /rgya nang ri bong yongs su rgyugs pa bzhin/ /srid pa'i zhags pas mdud pa'i sems can dag /srid dang longs spyod dag
<p>65a.2</p>la sems chags shing / /bu dang chung ma rnams la rab zhen pa/ /yang dang yang du sdug bsngal 'thob par 'gyur/ /skye bo grub dang bde rnams dang bral zhing / /bdud kyi sbyor ba dag dang ldan pa de/ /'jigs dang sdug bsngal rnams kyis 'joms 'gyur te/ /rtswa dang lo ma'i
<p>65a.3</p>mchog la me dang 'dra/ /'di na sred pa de 'dra spong byed pa/ /sred dang longs spyod dag la sred bral zhing / /dge slong srid pa zil gyis gnon byed pa/ /lhag ma med par yongs su mya ngan 'da'/ /gang zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/ /srid pa'i bud med 'dir bsten pa/ /de yi mya ngan
<p>65a.4</p>'phel 'gyur te/ /rtswa la char pa bab pa bzhin/ /gang zhig 'jig rten spang dka' ba'i/ /srid pa'i bud med 'di spong ba/ /de yi mya ngan ldog 'gyur te/ /pad+ma la ni chu thigs bzhin/ /u shi'i phyir ni rtswa bzhin du/ /srid pa'i rtsar bcas drung nas phyung / /skyes bu sred pa dang
<p>65a.5</p>'grogs na/ /yun ring dus su 'khyams 'gyur bas/ /sred pa drung nas phyur shig dang / /mya ngan med cing 'jigs pa med/ /yang dang yang du nyer len cing / /yang dang yang du mngal du 'jug /gnas skabs 'gyur dang gzhan 'gyur bas/ /sems can 'od dang 'gro bar
<p>65a.6</p>'gyur/ /'dir ni spang dka'i sred pa de/ /spongs la sa bon chod cig dang / /de yi sred pa med 'gyur zhing / /de ni yang du 'khor mi 'gyur/ /gang phyir srid mtsho'i rgyur gyur pa/ /yul la sred pa 'bras kyi gzhi/ /'khri shing dra bas khebs byed pa/ /gdung bar byed pa ma btul
<p>65a.7</p>na/ /sdug bsngal 'di ni yang dang yang / /rnam pa kun du ldog mi 'gyur/ /dper na ljon shing rtsa nas ma bton na/ /bcad kyang phyir zhing skye ba kho nar zad/ /de bzhin srid pa'i phra rgyas ma bton na/ /yang dang yang du sdug bsngal 'di mi ldog /dper na bdag nyid kyis ni
<p>65b</p>
<p>65b.1</p>byas pa'i mtshon/ /de yi rkun po'i mthu yis bdag gsod ltar/ /de bzhin nang gi sems las byung ba yi/ /srid pas lus can nye bar gsod par byed/ /de ltar srid las sdug bsngal dag /'byung ba'i nongs dmigs mkhyen nas ni/ /sred spang nye bar len med pa'i/ /don dam
<p>65b.2</p>dge slong mchog 'gyur mdzod/ /sred pa spang ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// //bag yod 'chi med gnas yin te/ /bag med pa ni 'chi ba'i gnas/ /bag med 'chi bar mi 'gyur ste/ /bag med pa ni rtag tu 'chi/ /de yi khyad par de rig pas/ /mkhas
<p>65b.3</p>pa rnams ni bag dang ldan/ /bag yod pa la rab dga' ba/ /'phags pa'i spyod yul dga' ba yin/ /brten pa grub bde bla med pa/ /mya ngan 'das la reg pa yin/ /gang tshe mkhas pa bag yod pas/ /bag med bcom pa de yi tshe/ /shes rab khang bzang steng
<p>65b.4</p>'dzegs nas/ /mya ngan med pas gdung bcad de/ /brten rnams ri bo'i rtse dag nas/ /sa steng byis pa rnams la blta/ /brtson 'grus dang ni bag yod dang / /yang dag sdom dang dul ba yis/ /mkhas pa'i gling du byas nas ni/ /chu bo chen po mngon du zlog /brtson
<p>65b.5</p>pa ldan zhing dran dang ldan pa dang / /spyod pa gtsang zhing brtags nas byed pa dang / /yang dag sdom dang chos kyis 'tsho ba dang / /bag yod rnams kyi grags pa mngon par 'phel/ /tshul khrims ting 'dzin shes rab mchog /thub pa'i bslab gzhi rnams la bslab/ /nyer zhi
<p>65b.6</p>rtag tu dran ldan pa'i/ /skyob pa mya ngan med pa yin/ /dman pa'i chos la mi brten cing / /bag med pa la brten mi bya/ /log par lta la 'dod med dang / /'jig rten 'phel bar mi bya'o/ /'jig rten pa yi yang dag lta/ /chen po su la yod gyur pa/ /de ni tshe rabs stong du
<p>65b.7</p>yang / /ngan 'gror 'gro bar mi 'gyur ro/ /bag med pa la sbyor byed pa'i/ /skye bo byis pa bsam brlag yin/ /tshong dpon nor rnams bsrung ba ltar/ /mkhas pa bag dang ldan par bya/ /bag med pa la mi sbyor zhing / /'dod pa rnams la rgyab phyogs nas/ /rtag tu
<p>66a</p>
<p>66a.1</p>bag yod sems byed pa/ /zag pa zad pa thob par 'gyur/ /zag pa zad pa ma thob par/ /mkhas pas bag med mi bya ste/ /ri dgas mo yis seng ge ltar/ /bag med pa dag gsod par byed/ /bag med pha rol bud med sten byed pa'i/ /mi gang yin la
<p>66a.2</p>gnas skabs 'di bzhi 'byung / /bsod nams min 'thob bde bar mi nyal dang / /dam pas smad cing lus zhig ngan 'gror skye/ /gang zhig bdag bde lta 'dod pa/ /de ni gong ma bzhin du sbyar/ /byis pa'i shing rta bzhin gyur pas/ /brtan pas brtson 'grus zhan mi bya/ /dper
<p>66a.3</p>na byis pa'i shing rta dag /lam chen bzang po bor nas ni/ /lam ngan dag tu 'gro byed pa/ /mig chag sems khong chud pa ltar/ /de bzhin chos ni spangs pas kyang / /chos min rjes su 'jug byed pa'i/ /byis pa 'chi bdag dbang 'gro zhing / /chos nyams bde ba bcom pa 'thob/ /gang
<p>66a.4</p>zhig bya ba rnam spangs nas/ /mi bya ba dag byed pa dang / /bag med pa yis rlom byed pa/ /de dag rnams kyi zag pa 'phel/ /gang zhig lus sogs dran pa dag /rtag tu legs par brtsams pa dang / /bya ba ma yin mi byed cing / /rgyun du bya ba byed pa dang / /dran dang shes bzhin ldan pa de'i/ /zag pa
<p>66a.5</p>rnams ni zad par 'gyur/ /ji tsam mang du smra byed pa/ /de dag dam chos 'dzin pa min/ /gang dag 'di na thos nyung yang / /yid kyi chos dag mngon sum byas/ /gang dag chos la bag byed pa/ /de dag dam chos 'dzin pa yin/ /gal te rigs bcas mang du smras kyang ni/ /bag med mi dag de
<p>66a.6</p>ltar byed mi 'gyur/ /dper na phyugs rdzis gzhan gyi phyugs bgrang ltar/ /de dag dge sbyong skal ba thob ma yin/ /gal te rigs bcas nyung ngu smra byed kyang / /chos kyi rjes su chos la spyod pa dang / /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug spong byed pa/ /de dag dge sbyong skal ba thob pa yin/ /bag
<p>66a.7</p>yod bsngags pa rjod byed cing / /rtag tu bag med la smod pas/ /bag med mchod sbyin rgyal ba yang / /lha rnams nang na gtso bor 'gyur/ /bag dang bcas pa'i mkhas pa yis/ /don gnyis rab tu len par byed/ /tshe 'di'i don ni gang yin dang / /phyi ma'i don ni gang yin pa'o/ /de
<p>66b</p>
<p>66b.1</p>dag brten pas rtogs pas na/ /mkhas pa zhes ni nges par brjod/ /dge slong bag yod la dga' zhing / /bag med pa la 'jigs lta bas/ /bdag nyid ngan 'gro las 'dren te/ /'dam rdzab las ni glang chen bzhin/ /sdig pa'i chos rnams sprug par byed/ /rlung gis ljon shing
<p>66b.2</p>lo ma bzhin/ /kun du sbyor ba phra rags dag /sreg ste me yis rtswa bzhin no/ /'du byed nyer zhi zhi ba yi/ /go 'phang mchog ni so sor rtogs/ /mya ngan 'das dang nye ba'i phyir/ /yongs su nyams 'gyur mi srid do/ /brtson 'grus ldan zhing bag yod dang / /chos spyod legs par spyod
<p>66b.3</p>byed pa/ /'jig rten 'di dang pha rol du/ /dga' dang bde ba rab tu 'thob/ /zhi phyir bslab pa la brten dang / /rtsol ba dang ni brtson 'grus skyed/ /mi dran pa dang bag med dang / /brtson 'grus chung dang kun sdom med/ /gnyid dang sdom pa g.yeng ba rnams/ /'di dag bslab pa'i
<p>66b.4</p>bar bcad pas/ /khyod kyis yan lag de mkhyen nas/ /dran pa chud ni mi gzan mdzod/ /mkhas khyod tshul khrims bzang ba dang / /bag yod pa la dgyes pa yis/ /kun rtog legs par mnyam zhog ste/ /nyid kyi thugs ni rjes su srungs/ /gang zhig chos 'dul 'di la ni/ /bag dang
<p>66b.5</p>ldan par spyod byed pa/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rab spangs nas/ /sdug bsngal tha mar byed par 'gyur/ /bag med pa spang ba'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// //nyon mongs rnams ni bdag 'joms sems can 'joms shing tshul khrims 'joms/ /nyams bcas rnyed pas
<p>66b.6</p>dman zhing srung dang de bzhin ston pas spangs/ /rtsod bcas mi snyan de ni gzhan du mi khom rnams su skye/ /thob dang ma thob nyams pas 'jigs dang sdug bsngal chen po 'thob/ /nyon mongs lhag pas thub la rma 'byin te/ /dam chos spong dang dge 'dun skur bar byed/ /pha ma gsod cing
<p>66b.7</p>chom rkun log g.yem spyod/ /rdzun dang phra ma tshig rtsub 'khyal ba smra/ /brnab sems gnod sems log lta yid byed cing / /dmyal ba yi dgas dud 'gro 'phel bar byed/ /'dir ni nyon mongs sa bon bzhin/ /klu bzhin rtswa bzhin ljon shing bzhin/ /de bzhin shun pa lta bu ste/ /
<p>67a</p>
<p>67a.1</p>las ni shun bcas 'bras dang 'dra/ /de bzhin sman dang me tog bzhin/ /skye ba bza' btung grub pa 'dra/ /kun sbyor 'ching ba bag la nyal/ /nye ba'i nyon mongs kun nas dkris/ /chu bo sbyor ba nyer len mdud/ /sgrib dang tha ba dri ma sdig /zug rngu ci
<p>67a.2</p>yang nye bar spyod/ /zag pa phongs pa yongs su mdud/ /'khrug dang 'thab pa rims nad dang / /nags sbyor dang ni gnas zhes bya/ /'dod chags khong khro gti mug dang / /nga rgyal lta ba the tshom dang / /khro dang khon du 'dzin pa dang / /'chab dang tshig dang phrag dog dang / /ser
<p>67a.3</p>sna dang ni sgyu bag dang / /g.yo rgyags rnam 'tshe ngo tsha med/ /khrel med rmugs dang rgod pa dang / /ma dad pa dang le lo dang / /bag med pa dang brjed ngas dang / /rnam g.yengs shes bzhin ma yin pa/ /rab mkhas khyed kyis spang bar mdzod/ /nyon mongs de dag spang slad du/ /zhi gnas
<p>67a.4</p>lhag mthong bsgom pa dang / /mi sdug byams khams rten 'brel dang / /dbugs rngub dbugs dbyung dran pa mdzod/ /dran pa nyer gzhag spang ba bzhi/ /de bzhin rdzu 'phrul rkang pa dang / /dbang stobs byang chub yan lag dang / /lam gyi yan lag bsgom par mdzod/ /de ltar
<p>67a.5</p>'dir ni mdor bsdus nas/ /mkhas pa khyod la springs pa yi/ /dge ba gang des 'gro ba kun/ /rnam grol zhi ba thob par shog /nyon mongs pa spong ba'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// //bla ma la spring ba dge slong dgon pa pas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan
<p>67a.6</p>po A tsAr+ya bi na ya tsAn dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ su taM le kha/ bod skad du/ bu la spring ba/ 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mtsho chen sa
<p>67a.7</p>gzhir gyur 'di dgra bcom bye ba'i yul/ /legs spyod mis gang dpe med dpal sgo rig gnas 'dir/ /mkhas pa rin chen rdo rje'i rgyud 'dzin bram ze'i rigs/ /gzugs stobs shes rab phun tshogs ma hA dzA nar 'gyur/ /mchog tu brtse ba'i pha ma mdza' bshes
<p>67b</p>
<p>67b.1</p>gnyen 'dun tshogs/ /mchil ma'i thal ba bzhin du ltos med yal dor nas/ /mtha' 'khob kla klo mun pa'i nang na gcig 'khyams pa/ /blo ldan bu de shes rab sgron mas snang gyur cig /shin tu brtse ba'i ded dpon bdag gis ni/ /legs bshad rgya mtsho'i gling nas blangs pa yi/ /
<p>67b.2</p>spring yig rin chen 'di ni bu la bskur/ /rab gus dga' zhing dad pas mnyan par gyis/ /dge ba'i yul dbus khang bzang longs spyod dang / /g.yo med sems kyis rgyun du brtse ba yi/ /pha ma mdza' bshes rtsa lag spangs nas ni/ /bu khyod mtha' 'khob rgyu ba shin tu smad/ /dam chos
<p>67b.3</p>phyir ni pha ma yal dor nas/ /nor bzang bzhin du yul gzhan rgyu 'os na/ /'dod pa'i don du pha ma yal dor nas/ /smad pa'i don du rgyu ba ga la rigs/ /bu khyod gzugs sdug mchog dang sgra snyan dang / /dri zhim ro mchog reg bya'i bde byed pa/ /'dod pa'i 'dam du 'gro ba 'di dag bying / /
<p>67b.4</p>dper na glang chen 'dam du chud pa bzhin/ /'dod pa las ni 'jigs dang sdug bsngal dang / /mya ngan dang ni 'tshe ba sna tshogs 'byung / /gsod dang bcing dang yan lag gcod pa dang / /me dang chu dang g.yang sar 'dor bar byed/ /'dod la brkam pas sems can dmyal ba dang / /yi dgas
<p>67b.5</p>dud 'gro rnams su sdug bsngal rnyed/ /mir gyur na yang sdug bsngal mi snyan dang / /dri mi zhim dang bkres skom nad kyis gzir/ /g.yen ba can la phrug na bde/ /de bzhin 'jig rten 'dod ldan bde/ /de bas 'dod pa med pa bde/ /ji ltar me long brag ca dang / /spos snod gzar bu
<p>67b.6</p>nam mkha' rnams/ /gzugs brnyan sgra grags spos dang ni/ /tshod ma'i ro dang rlung rnams kyis/ /nam yang ngoms par 'gyur ba med/ /de bzhin mig dang rna ba dang / /sna dang lce dang lus rnams dang / /gzugs mdzes sgra snyan dri zhim dang / /ro mchog reg bya bde ba yis/ /nam yang
<p>67b.7</p>ngoms par 'gyur ba med/ /de bas 'dod pa rnams spang zhing / /'phags pa'i chos rnams bsten par bya/ /tshul khrims ting 'dzin shes rab mchog /rnam grol bde bas ngoms par 'gyur/ /'dod la chags pa spang bar bya'o/ /nor la chags pas 'dir gdung phyi mar gdung / /
<p>68a</p>
<p>68a.1</p>gnyis kar gdung ste des na bdag nyid kyis/ /las rnam smin mthong de gdung rab tu gdung / /'gro ba dman par song bas phyir zhing gdung / /bsag dang bsrung dang brlag pa'i gdung ba yis/ /nor ni phung khrol mtha' yas shes par bya/ /nor la chags
<p>68a.2</p>pas g.yeng bar gyur pa rnams/ /srid pa'i sdug bsngal las grol skabs med do/ /nor gyi phyir ni rgyal bu dge don gyi/ /mig gnyis tsher ma rnon pos brtol bar gyur/ /bu mo mdza' bo rna ba bye ba ri/ /rgya mtshor shi 'phos 'khyam par gyur pa yin/ /'di na nor 'tshol kha cig gsal
<p>68a.3</p>shing btsugs/ /la la yan lag nying lag gcod par snang / /gzhan dag btson ra shin tu zab mor bcug /kha cig khong sgril su mi 'dod kyis bcings/ /nor bu len pa'i tshong pa lnga brgya dag /sing ga la yi gling du srin mos bzung / /rdzu 'phrul chen po'i rta rgyal ba la has/ /de dag
<p>68a.4</p>bsgral bar nus pa ma yin no/ /'di na gser dang dngul dang bai DUr+ya/ /mu tig byi ru asma gar+b+ha dang / /kAR+Sha pa Na la sogs char babs kyang / /nor 'tshol rnams ni ngoms par 'gyur ba med/ /gangs can 'bigs byed dang ni mnyam pa yi/ /nor gyi phung po la ni dbang bsgyur kyang / /nor
<p>68a.5</p>tshol gcig kyang ngoms par 'gyur ma yin/ /de phyir bu khyod nor la chags pa spongs/ /'di na nor mang skye bo sdug bsngal ba/ /'dod pa chung rnams de lta ma yin te/ /klu dbang rnams la mgo bo ji snyed pa/ /de las byung ba'i sdug bsngal de snyed do/ /lus srog yal bar dor nas nor
<p>68a.6</p>bsags kyang / /shi na skal ba nyams par 'gyur ba yi/ /nor de rmi lam sprin dang mtshungs pa yin/ /de bas 'dod pa chung zhing chog shes bya/ /nor mang bsags shing sba byas kyang / /cung zad cung zad spyad pa yis/ /'jungs pa'i nor ni 'dra ba ltar/ /sdug bsngal skyed pa kho nar zad/ /
<p>68a.7</p>bu khyod gal te nor 'tshol na/ /'phags pa'i nor bdun bsten par gyis/ /rgyal po rkun pos mi phrogs shing / /srid pa'i dbul ba sel bar 'gyur/ /rtag tu tshul khrims ldan pa la/ /sbyin pa bkur stis brgyan par gyis/ /nor rnams de ltar gter du sbos/ /rjes su 'brang zhing
<p>68b</p>
<p>68b.1</p>dbrog tu med/ /'di na nor slong dman pa ste/ /mi sbyin pa ni de bas dman/ /nor sbyin pa ni mchog yin te/ /mi 'dod pa ni de bas mchog /nor la chags pa spang ba'o/ /'dod pa'i phyir ni byis pa rnams/ /bud med rul pa sten byed pa/ /'gro ba rul par 'gro 'gyur zhing / /ngan song
<p>68b.2</p>rnams su ltung bar 'gyur/ /'jigs pa chen po'i 'ching ba ni/ /bud med zhags pa mi bzad pa/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis 'dod pa dang / /bud med bsten pa'ang ma bsngags so/ /lam 'dis byang chub bar bcad pas/ /sbrul gdug shin tu khro ba ltar/ /mkhas khyod bud med rnam par
<p>68b.3</p>spongs/ /mi gang dag ni bud med 'dod/ /de dag bde bar ga la 'gyur/ /bud med phung bar byed pa ste/ /'jig rten 'di dang pha rol phung / /rnam pa kun du nor 'jig dang / /ngan song rtsa ba bud med yin/ /bu khyod bdag la phan 'dod na/ /de bas bud med rtag tu spongs/ /bud med rnams
<p>68b.4</p>kyi rang bzhin ni/ /'dod can rnams kyis mi rig ste/ /skyes pa dang ni yid gcugs shing / /rtse dga' du ma byas nas kyang / /sbrul gyi lpags rnying 'dor ba ltar/ /bud med kyis ni blo bur 'dor/ /sbrang mas me tog rnying pa ltar/ /bud med kyis ni nor med pa'i/ /skyes pa rgan po 'dor byed
<p>68b.5</p>cing / /gzugs byad ngan pa'ang 'dor ba yin/ /rab tu brtse bas bud med dag /thams cad du ni yongs bskyangs kyang / /bud med shin tu mi bzad pa/ /bdag gir bya bar mi nus so/ /de yi rang bzhin 'di yin te/ /bud med rnams ni sems mi srun/ /byas pa drin du mi gzo bas/ /
<p>68b.6</p>rang gi skyes pa'ang gsod par byed/ /chu bo dang ni sder mo can/ /rwa can lag na mtshon thogs pa/ /rgyal po ngan dang bud med la/ /nam yang yid brtan mi bya'o/ /bud med kha zas nyis 'gyur te/ /g.yo sgyu dag ni bzhi 'gyur yin/ /phrag dog shas ni drug 'gyur te/ /'dod pa brgya
<p>68b.7</p>'gyur yin par bya/ /shing rnams kyis ni med dang ni/ /char gyis rgya mtsho chen po dang / /'byung po kun gyis gshin rje ltar/ /skyes pa bud med ngoms mi 'gyur/ /pu ka rtse yi kha chu yis/ /bye ma'i phung po ji ltar 'bang / /skyes pa gzhon nu thams cad kyis/ /bud med gcig ni
<p>69a</p>
<p>69a.1</p>ngoms mi 'gyur/ /byi bo byed pa'i ngang tshul can/ /ma bsdams mi bsrun 'dod la brkam/ /rang gi chung mas mi chog ste/ /'jig rten dag na smad 'os yin/ /'di dang pha rol sdug bsngal 'gyur/ /gsod dang chad pa drag po myong / /sems can dmyal
<p>69a.2</p>ba rnams su skye/ /de bas bu khyod de spongs shig /byi bo byed pa shal+ma li/ /lcags kyi tsher ma rtse mo 'bar/ /sor ni bcu drug yod pa la/ /ngu zhing stobs kyis 'dzegs par 'gyur/ /bud med shin tu 'jigs 'jigs lta/ /mche rno lus che 'bar ba yis/ /gzhan gyi bud med
<p>69a.3</p>'phrog pa la/ /ci nas za ba kho nar 'gyur/ /gal te chung mar brten na yang / /de yi nyes dmigs drug cu lnga/ /drag shul can gyi mdo las gsungs/ /de'i phyir bud med spang bar bya'o/ /bud med la chags pa spang ba'o// //gang zhig 'thungs nas ra ro glo nas gom tshugs dbang med
<p>69a.4</p>'dor/ /yul grong ma 'dris par yang 'khyam zhing brdeg 'chos 'gyur/ /bza' dang mi bza' spyad med dug dang 'dres pa za/ /de bas bu khyod myos 'gyur khu ba rtag tu spongs/ /gang 'thungs na ni bdag la brtan med blo nyams shing / /phyugs dang 'dra bar mdza' bos spong zhing dgra bos 'phya/ /
<p>69a.5</p>'dus pa bro gar byed cing glu len 'khar rnga rdung / /dge legs grags nyams rgyu de su zhig 'thung bar byed/ /de 'thungs ngo tsha khrel yod dor nas ni/ /gcer bur byung kyang 'dzem med smyon pa bzhin/ /rkun po gcan gzan rgyu ba'i lam du 'gro/ /lus srog nyams rgyu de ni khyod kyis spangs/ /de
<p>69a.6</p>'thungs skyugs pas gos shing 'gyel gyur nas/ /kha yang khyi yis dogs pa med par ldags/ /dran med lam po cher yang nyal gyur na/ /bag med rtsa ba rtag tu spang bar bya/ /gang zhig 'thungs nas myos par 'khrul 'gyur te/ /'bris na an d+ha dag kyang rme byung na/ /du chen 'thib ste
<p>69a.7</p>phan tshun thal mar byung / /phung khrol rtsa ba de ni su zhig 'thung / /gang zhig 'thungs na dpal gyi gzhir 'gyur rigs/ /je mtho je mtho gyur pa'ang rlag byed pa/ /nor gyi dbyig ldan khyim kyang phung 'gyur ba/ /nyes mang gzhi rtsa de ni su zhig 'thung / /glo bur ngu zhing re 'ga' dgod par byed/ /
<p>69b</p>
<p>69b.1</p>ma nges smra zhing gdon gyis zin pa bzhin/ /dam pas smad cing brnyas pa'i gnas gyur pa/ /'khrul slang rgyu de su zhig 'thung bar byed/ /bag yod rnams kyang de 'thungs sems nyams shing / /bdag la phan pa'i lam du mi 'jug pa/ /ma brtags mang du smra zhing tshig rtsub 'byin/ /sgo
<p>69b.2</p>gsum nyams byed de ni btung mi bya/ /gang gi nyes pas sngon gyi lha rnams myos/ /lha yi dbang po'i dpal ni nyams gyur nas/ /skyabs 'dod phyir na rgya mtsho'i nang du gab/ /lha yang nyams byed de ni btung mi bya/ /mi bya ba yang bya ba bzhin du byed/ /mi bden pa yang bden pa bzhin du smra/ /
<p>69b.3</p>zhum pa rnams kyang ma zhum bzhin du spyod/ /myos 'gyur rigs nyams sdug bsngal rgyur gyur pa/ /sdig pa'i srin mo byur ngan mngon sum bzhin/ /rtsod pa'i gzhi dang tha dad ma yin pa/ /snying gi mun pa mi bzad de su 'thung / /de 'thungs yid ni rab tu 'khrugs gyur nas/ /brtse
<p>69b.4</p>ba'i pha dang ma yang gsod 'gyur zhing / /nyes med dge sbyong bram ze drang srong gsod/ /chom rkun dang ni log g.yem smad pa byed/ /rdzun dang phra ma tshig rtsub 'khyal pa smra/ /brnab sems gnod sems log lta'i mun pa 'dzin/ /mi dge'i rtsa ba de ni btung mi bya/ /gang zhig btung na tshul
<p>69b.5</p>khrims ting 'dzin dang / /shes rab lta ba 'tsho ba cho ga dang / /dran pa shes bzhin dad pa brtson 'grus nyams/ /dge chos chud gzon de ni btung mi bya/ /de 'thungs sdig spyod rnams ni lus zhig nas/ /rab tu bzod dka'i sems can dmyal bar ltung / /yi dwags dud 'gro rnams kyang
<p>69b.6</p>smyon par 'gyur/ /sdug bsngal rtsa ba de ni btung mi bya/ /thub pas dga' ba can gyi mdo las ni/ /myos 'gyur nyes pa sum cu rtsa lnga gsungs/ /de phyir bu khyod bdag la phan 'dod na/ /nyes kun rtsa ba de ni btung mi bya/ /chang dga' dgos pa thams cad la/ /rtag tu bag med spyod par
<p>69b.7</p>'gyur/ /mkhas pa rnams kyi sman 'gyur zhing / /dkar po'i chos rnams 'grib par 'gyur/ /nyes kun rtsa ba bag med gnas/ /'di dang gzhan du rnam par rmongs/ /de bas skye bo chen po khyod/ /chang la dga' ba rtag tu spongs/ /phan par smra ba dkon pa ste/ /nyan par byed pa
<p>70a</p>
<p>70a.1</p>shin tu dkon/ /de dag bas kyang mi nyan yang / /phan pa'i rjes su byed pa dkon/ /phan par smra ba mchod pa ni/ /bsgo ba shin tu sgrub pa yin/ /bu khyod nga la mchod 'dod na/ /gdams pa bzhin du rjes su sgrubs/ /chang la dga' ba spang ba'o/ /bdag gi
<p>70a.2</p>spring yig rin chen 'di/ /bu la brjod pa las byung ba'i/ /dge ba gang des 'gro ba kun/ /thams cad mkhyen pa thob par shog /bu la spring ba paN+Di ta mkhas pa chen po sad dza na chen pos mdzad pa rdzogs so// //kha che'i mkhan po ma hA dza na dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba
<p>70a.3</p>mar ba chos kyi dbang phyugs gis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[  @##/ /rgya gar skad du/ bi ma la rat+na le kha nA ma/ bod skad du/ dri ma med pa rin po che'i spring yig ces bya ba/ /bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rje btsun ma sgrol ma la phyag
<p>70a.4</p>'tshal lo/ /ma hA g+ha tir sku bltams nas/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa 'phel mdzad cing / /rgyal srid chos kyis skyong mdzad pa/ /nir ya phal rgyal gyur cig /khyod kyis sngon chad sbyin pa dang / /dge ba bcu dang gso sbyong dang / /bzod dang brtson 'grus la goms pas/ /lha
<p>70a.5</p>khyod da lta phun sum tshogs/ /bla ma rnams kyi bka' lung dang / /mdo stsogs chos kyi rjes 'brang 'di/ /gus pas spyi bos blang mdzod dang / /bdag gzhan gnyis la phan par 'gyur/ /the tshom thams cad rnam spangs shing / /sgrub la nan tan che bar mdzod/ /gnyid rmugs le lo
<p>70a.6</p>rnam spangs shing / /rtag tu brtson 'grus 'bad par bya/ /dran dang shes bzhin bag yod pas/ /dbang po'i sgo rnams rtag tu bsrung / /nyin mtshan dus su yang dang yang / /sems kyi rgyud la brtag par bya/ /rang skyon rtog la mig bzhin bya/ /gzhan skyon rtog la long ba
<p>70a.7</p>bzhin/ /dran dang nga rgyal med pa dang / /stong nyid rtag tu bsgom par bya/ /bdag gi nyes pa bsgrag bya zhing / /gzhan gyi 'khrul pa btsal mi bya/ /gzhan gyi yon tan bsgrag par bya/ /bdag gi yon tan sba bar bya/ /rnyed dang bkur sti spang bya zhing / /khe grags rtag tu spang bar bya/ /
<p>70b</p>
<p>70b.1</p>byams dang snying rje bsgom bya zhing / /byang chub sems ni brtan par mdzod/ /mi dge bcu ni spang bya zhing / /rtag tu dad pa brtan par bya/ /'dod pa chung zhing chog shes dang / /byas la drin du gzo bar bya/ /khro dang nga rgyal spang bya zhing / /dman pa'i sems dang ldan par bya/ /log pa'i 'tsho
<p>70b.2</p>ba rnams spang zhing / /chos kyi 'tsho bas 'tsho bar bya/ /zang zing thams cad rnams spang zhing / /'phags pa'i nor gyis phyug por bya/ /rtag tu 'du 'dzi spang bya zhing / /dgon pa la ni gnas par bya/ /'khyal pa'i tshig rnams spang bya zhing / /rtag tu ngag ni bsdam par bya/ /bla ma
<p>70b.3</p>mkhan po mthong ba'i tshe/ /gus pas rim gro bskyed par bya/ /khyad par can gyi skyes bu dang / /gang zag chos kyi mig can dang / /las dang po yi sems can la/ /ston pa'i 'du shes bskyed par bya/ /sdug bsngal dag gis gdungs pa dang / /sems can thams cad mthong ba'i tshe/ /byang
<p>70b.4</p>chub sems ni bskyed bya ste/ /pha ma bu tsha'i 'du shes bskyed/ /'jig rten bya ba kun spangs te/ /rtag tu ting 'dzin bsgom par mdzod/ /sdig pa'i grogs po spang bya zhing / /dge ba'i bshes la sten par mdzod/ /tshul khrims 'chal ba'i dge slong dang / /chos kyis phongs pa gzhan dag
<p>70b.5</p>dang / sdig pa spyod pa mthong ba'i tshe/ /de dag yal bar dor mi bya/ /mi dge'i bshes gnyen thams cad dang / /sdig pa'i grogs po thams cad dang / /dkon mchog gsum dang bla ma dang / /mkhan po slob dpon mi gus dang / /byas la drin du mi gzo dang / /tshe 'di 'ba' zhig dran
<p>70b.6</p>pa dang / /gzhan yang dad pa chung ba dang / /zhag gsum 'das par gnas mi bya/ /sdang dang mi dge'i sa spangs shing / /gang du bde bar 'gro bar bya/ /gang la chags pa spang bya zhing / /chags pa med par gnas par bya/ /chags pas bde 'gro mi 'thob cing / /thar pa'i srog kyang gcod
<p>70b.7</p>par byed/ /gang du dge ba'i bshes gnas pa/ /der ni rtag tu gnas par bya/ /bla ma rtag tu bsten pa dang / /rtag tu mdo sde blta bar bya/ /thog mar brtsams pa gang yin pa/ /dang por de nyid bsgrub bya zhing / /gzhan du gnyis ka 'grub mi 'gyur/ /gzhan du sdig pa bshags pa dang / /
<p>71a</p>
<p>71a.1</p>bsod nams mchog la 'bad par bya/ /'jig rten spyod dang mthun pa dang / /rtag tu pha rol sems su mdzod/ /gang tshe mtho ba'i sems skyes tshe/ /de tshe nga rgyal bcag bya zhing / /gang du bag yod bral ba'i tshe/ /bla ma'i gdams ngag dran par bya/ zhum pa'i
<p>71a.2</p>sems ni byung ba'i tshe/ /sems kyi gzengs kyang bstod par bya/ /shes rab pha rol phyin dran te/ /spros pa ma lus zhi bar mdzod / /gang du chags sdong yul byung tshe/ /sgyu ma sprul pa bzhin du blta/ /mi snyan tshig rnams thos pa'i tshe/ /brag ca lta bur mkhyen par mdzod/ /lus la gnod
<p>71a.3</p>pa byung ba'i tshe/ /sngon gyi las su blta bar bya/ /bas mtha' dgon par rab gnas shing / /ri dgas shi ba'i ro bzhin du/ /gang du sus kyang mi shes par/ /bdag gis bdag nyid sba bar bya/ /rtag tu yi dam brtan par bya/ /'dod dang gnod sems gnyid dang rmugs/ /le lo snyom las
<p>71a.4</p>sems byung tshe/ /de tshe bdag la rngan bgrang zhing / /brtul zhugs snying po dran bya dang / /mi rtag pa dang 'chi ba bsam/ /gzhan gyi mdun du gnas pa'i tshe/ /zhi des gsong por smra bar bya/ /khro gnyer ngo 'dzum spang bya zhing / /rtag tu 'dzum zhing gnas par bya/ /rtag tu gzhan la dga' bya
<p>71a.5</p>zhing / /ser sna med cing gtang la dga'/ /rtag tu phrag dog spang bar bya/ /gzhan gyi sems ni bsrung bya zhing / /rtsod pa thams cad spang bar bya/ /ngo dga' med cing gsar 'grogs med/ /rtag tu zungs ni thub par bya/ /rtag tu bzod dang ldan pa dang / /'dod pa chung zhing chog shes bya / /
<p>71a.6</p>gdol pa bran gyi 'du shes so/ /ngo tsha shes dang khrel yod dang / /pha rol mgu bya de la brtson/ /rang gi sdom pa bsdam par mdzod/ /gzhan la brnyas pa spang bya zhing / /gus pa'i tshul gyis gnas par bya/ /gzhan la gdams ngag byed pa'i tshe/ /snying rje phan sems ldan par mdzod/ /sangs
<p>71a.7</p>rgyas chos la gus pa dang / /dam chos nam yang spang mi bya/ /rtag tu dkon mchog gus pa dang / /'khor gsum yongs su dag par mdzod/ /sngon du snying rje song ba yis/ /nyin dang mtshan mo lan gsum du/ /mchod pa bdun du rab grags pa'i/ /phung po gsum pa gdon par mdzod/ /
<p>71b</p>
<p>71b.1</p>'gro ba'i sdug bsngal bsal 'dod pas/ /smon lam rgya chen gdab pa dang / /sems can smon dang byang chub 'dod/ /thams cad byang chub chen por bsngo/ /dus ni ring por dam bcas nas/ /rtag tu brtson dang ldan par bya/ /de ltar mdzad na tshogs gnyis po/ /rdzogs 'gyur
<p>71b.2</p>sgrib gnyis zad par 'gyur/ /mi lus thob pa don yod cing / /mthong ba'i chos la mya ngan 'da'/ /bdag dang gzhan don rdzogs gyur nas/ /dam pa nyid ni thob par 'gyur/ /sos ka'i khu byug gzhon nu skad snyan sgrogs zhes te / /rma bya gzhon nu skad mi snyan pa mi sgrogs sam/ /mkhas
<p>71b.3</p>pa mang pos legs par gsungs pa yod mod kyis/ /rgyal po gdung ba bcad phyir bdag gis bris pa yin/ /phan sems ldan pa'i gtam de legs par dgongs mdzod la/ /rtogs dang ldan pa'i skye bo gzhan la'ang smra bar mdzod/ /rtag tu lha drug dran mdzod dam tshig gtsang mar 
<p>71b.4</p>mdzod/ /rgyal srid chos kyis skyong mdzod bdag la bzod par mdzod/ /dri ma med pa'i rin po che'i spring yig ces bya ba/ /gnas brtan mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra shrI dz+nyA nas/ rgyal po nir+ya pha la la brdzongs pa rdzogs so// //dus de nyid du bla ma de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dge slong
<p>71b.5</p>tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba/ sh+lo ka bzhi bcu pa'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ tsan+d+ra rAdza le kha ka/ bod skad du/ rgyal po zla ba la springs pa'i spring yig /'jig rten mgon po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sa gsum dbang phyug lha dang mi yi rje/ /yon tan rtul
<p>71b.6</p>bod 'phags pa'i bu stong mnga'/ /mnyam med chos kyi 'khor los sgyur mdzad pa/ /chos kyi rgyal pos rgyal po rgyal gyur cig /grogs po'i ming can rnal 'byor gyis/ /zla ba'i mtshan can sa bdag la/ /brtse bas rgyang nas nyid kyi drung / /rigs pa'i gdams ngag 'phrin du
<p>71b.7</p>gsol/ /sa bdag ji ltar 'byor pa'i dus/ /de nyid dus na spyad btang zhing / /yongs su bsngo bas gter du sba/ /tshe 'di gcig la gzhan dpag med/ /gang tshe phyi nas ser sna dang / /phongs pas bsregs na ci bgyir mchis/ /sa bdag ji ltar gang dang mdza'/ /de ltar snga
<p>72a</p>
<p>72a.1</p>nas 'brel rab spang / /des na gnod pa mang po'i rtsa/ /skal lan mi bgyid grags mi bgyid/ /gang tshe yud tsam rkyen stobs kyis/ /dbang bsgyur de tshe ci bgyir mchis/ /sa bdag ji ltar dgrar lta ba/ /de ltar sngon nas rtsod mi bgyi/ /ma la rkyen dbang gis
<p>72a.2</p>bskul lags/ /sgyu 'dra gnyis ka dngos med phyir/ /gang tshe nags la me shor ltar/ /'bar bar 'gyur tshe ci bgyir mchis/ /sa bdag ji ltar g.yar po'i lus/ /nad med rgud med bder gnas pa/ /de nyid tshe na snying po blang / /na 'chi rgud pas 'jigs med bgyi/ /gang tshe
<p>72a.3</p>na rgas rgud sogs na/ /dran yang de tshe ci bgyir mchis/ /longs spyod ci 'dra khyim gyi sbrang / /bshes pa ci 'dra tshong khang mi/ /sdang sde rmi lam gnod pa bzhin/ /rang lus ci 'dra sbrul gyi lpags/ /'du 'dzi ci 'dra nad gzhi bzhin/ /tshe srog ci 'dra ri gzar chu/ /gang tshe gang la sems
<p>72a.4</p>chags pa/ /de nyid dus na de btang bgyi/ /ci phyir chung yang gang la zhen/ /de nyid 'ching ba mi bzad phyir/ /gang tshe gang la sems sdang ba/ /de nyid dus na de bzhag bgyi/ /ci phyir chung yang blo 'khrug pa/ /de nyid phung khrol mi bzad phyir/ /gson cig 'di ltar khyod kyis sa/ /rgya mtsho'i
<p>72a.5</p>mthar thug dbang 'byor pa'ang / /nam zhig khyod nyid rnam 'gyur dus/ /de tshe ci 'dra legs par gsungs/ /re zhig khyod sku rdo rje ltar/ /'gro ba'i skyabs dang rin chen ni/ /brtan du mi rung g.yo bdag pas/ /nges par bskyed dus de mchis so/ /de ltar phun tshogs dpal gyi gseb/ /khyod
<p>72a.6</p>ni dgyes rol snyam bgyid na/ /thar pa rnams kyis rgyal srid bsdam/ /rgyal po bying ba lta bur gzigs/ /sdug bsngal rgya mtsho gting mtha' med/ /srid pa'i glong du bying gyur kyang / /skyo med 'jigs med dga' dang dgod/ /bdag cag snying la ci zhig mchis/ /phongs dang btsal dga'
<p>72a.7</p>bsrung dang brlag /'bral dang phrad dang na rgas rgud/ /rtag tu 'bar ba'i mer zhugs kyang / /bde rlom smyon pa lags pa snyam/ /gzugs sgra dri ro reg dang chos/ /gzugs brnyan dgra brnyan tshogs mtshungs phyir/ /rtag tu mi bsam chags mi bgyi/ /chags na'ang de nyid rnam spyod
<p>72b</p>
<p>72b.1</p>mdzod/ /thog med bag chags las dbang gis/ /sems ni bung bas rtsi bzhin no/ /rigs pa dang ni gdams ngag dang / /skyon dran pas ni slar bzlog bgyi/ /don med don log don dman don/ /'di 'dra'i don du 'dod nas dar/ /sgo gsum mi bzad sdug bsngal bgyis/ /mi mchog kyang ni
<p>72b.2</p>rnam dpyod rigs/ /ji ltar lus ngag de bzhin yid/ /rtse dang 'khyal dang rnam g.yeng dang / /srog gcod phra ma gnod sems sam/ /tshe 'dir chags pas dge bgyid pa/ /de lta de ltar don yod bzang / /don mchog bgyis na cis ma legs/ /ji ltar mi rtag srin po yi/ /khar chud ma
<p>72b.3</p>gyur de srid par/ /lha yi srid pa ru bzlog la/ /bsgrim par mdzod cig mi yi rje/ /gang tshe srin bu'i mgrin chud gyur/ /de tshe khyod kyi dmag dang dpung / /mthu dang 'byor pa btsun mo sras/ /rtsal bsnyems cir yang ma mchis so/ /kye ma sngon nas dub pa'i las/ /rtag tu bzod dka'i
<p>72b.4</p>sdug bsngal gyis/ /nyer rtsal da dung bsnyems med na/ /rgyal srid rgyal po ji ltar dregs/ /rgya mtshor bying bas rnyed pa'i gru/ /chu rgyun drag po'i rba dang ni/ /mngar skyur lo tog bya skrod shing / /rgyal po na rgas rgud dang 'chi/ /bzhi po 'di dag bsam par gyis/ /ji ltar phan
<p>72b.5</p>btags de ltar gnod/ /yod na skyo dang med na gdung / /'grogs na skyon mthong rtsod gyur pa/ /sems can rnams kyi mtshan nyid lags/ /gcig tu dge ba dkar po'i chos/ /des ni 'di phyi 'phral yun du/ /don yod don yod dgos mi dgos/ /na rgas rgud dang 'chi la dris/ /kyi hud
<p>72b.6</p>'jig rten mig bcas long / /mngon sum rtag tu nges mthong yang / /da dung cung zad mi sems pa/ /khyod snying rdo rjer gyur tam ci/ /tshe 'di bstod bde rnyed grags kyis/ /gzi brjid 'od kyis snying brid pa/ /'chal rnams de don gnyer ba yis/ /sems g.yengs nas ni dran ma mchis/ /
<p>72b.7</p>yun ring sngon nas da lta srid/ /na tshod gzhon dang gnyen dang rgan/ /'di tsam grangs kyis shi gyur kyang / /khyod ni rten dbang gis gnas na/ /ji srid skyes nas da lta'i bar/ /dus ni thung ngam ring yang rung / /yud tsam bsdad kyang mi snyam par/ /skad cig gcig gi chad par 'das/ /de bzhin da nas 'chi
<p>73a</p>
<p>73a.1</p>mtha' yas/ /cung zad 'dug pa'i lang med par/ /chad kyis 'das pa'i skad cig la/ /dran pa yud tsam byas te 'gro/ /btsun mo lha mo 'dra na yang / /mi bzad rul sungs brgyal ba nyid/ /sgo dgu mi gtsang rgyun rtag 'dzag /bshes gzugs ro
<p>73a.2</p>langs lags so rje/ /lha gcig ji ltar khyod 'byor kyang / /gshegs nas 'jig rten gzhan bzhud tshe/ /mya ngan thang la dgra bcom ltar/ /gcig pu sras med btsun mo min/ /na bza' ma mchis bshes ma mchis/ /rgyal srid ma mchis khab ma mchis/ /dpag med mthu
<p>73a.3</p>dpung mnga' lags kyang / /gzigs su ma mchis gsan ma mchis/ /gcig tsam nyid gcig phyi thag gi /rjes su 'brang ba'ang mi mnga'o/ /mdor na nyid kyi mtshan tsam yang / /de tshe med na gzhan ci smos/ /'jig rten bde ba sdug bsngal te/ /thar pa'i bde ba bde ba
<p>73a.4</p>nyid/ /de bas sdug bsngal mi bzhed na/ /nges par thar pa cis mi bzhed/ /thar pa zhes bya bcing grol phyir/ /'ching rgyu longs spyod sems can lus/ /bsdam phyir chags sdang zhe sdang yin/ /de phyir rgyal pos 'di nyid gzhom/ /gang yang mi yi gtso bo gson/ /'di na
<p>73a.5</p>gang dag 'dren pa yin/ /bshes gnyen ngan pas sems bslad dag /'jig rten snga phyi med smra ba/ /de ni sbrul gdug nag po'i lha/ /tshig tsam rigs pa la brten nas/ /zhib mo rnam dpyod ma mdzad par/ /lha yi thugs brten mi rung ngo / /'di ltar snga phyi yod min na/ /
<p>73a.6</p>da ltar srog sems gsal 'di gang / /rlan drod dus sad yal 'dab las/ /me tog 'bras bu ji bzhin no/ /nags dang sa las me tog dang / /sha mo rdol ba bzhin ce na/ /'o na ji lta de lta bur/ /shing sdong la yang srog sems min/ /gang de 'di 'dra dngos po'i rigs/ /
<p>73a.7</p>tha dad rigs pa'i mtshan nyid ni/ /de bas 'di dang 'di yi dpe/ /mtshungs par dpag par mi nus so/ /gzigs shig sems can srog lus dag /gcig dang cig shos rtag gi na/ /re zhig gcig na lus dang sems/ /shing dang nam mkha' 'dra ba'i phyir/ /de dag
<p>73b</p>
<p>73b.1</p>phan tshun de 'drar 'gyur/ /pha dang bu yi lus sems bzhin/ /de zad cig shos zad min pas/ /tha dad phyogs kyang mi rung ngo / /yun ring gnas skabs 'brel ba yis/ /rjes su 'gro ldog nges na ni/ /shing dang yal ga ri dang sdong / /thams cad da ltar thal bar 'gyur/ /
<p>73b.2</p>sems ni thogs med 'gags med bdag /mkha' ltar zhi dag stong pa'i phyir/ /gang du ji ltar chad par 'gyur/ /dul ba gzhan yang mu stegs can/ /bdag tu lta ba gtan ma mchis/ /'di la mgon po ma brtags par/ /nyid kyis bab col mi bgyi'o/ /'ching ba rnam
<p>73b.3</p>grol las gdams pa/ /gzigs nas brtan pos rnam dpyod mdzod/ /mi bzad lta ba 'di nyid las/ /gcig ni sreg byed me dpung ste/ /gnyis pa lcags sgrog 'ching ba lags/ /mkhas rnams nye bar mi bgyid do/ /de ltar lta ba'i dri ma las/ /log nas drang srong bstan zhugs
<p>73b.4</p>te/ /nyan thos rang sangs rgyas dang sras/ /theg gsum rim gyis bgrod par gsol/ /dpyod ldan bdag gis khyod gsol cig /gus dang mi gus tsam nyid kyis/ /blang bar mi bgyid dor mi bgyi/ /gser la mgar bas bsreg sogs bzhin/ /rnam brtags nges par gyur
<p>73b.5</p>nas gdod/ /mi rigs rgyang du 'phang du gsol/ /de ste rigs par gzigs na ni/ /nyid kyis spyi gtsug blang du gsol/ /rgyal po zla ba la springs pa'i spring yig /rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug shrI dzA ga ta mi tra A nan+das mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug
<p>73b.6</p>de nyid dang / bod kyi lo chung gnubs tshul khrims shes rab kyis bsgyur ba'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ byag ta pa da su hr-i da le kha TI kA/ bod skad du/ bshes pa'i spring yig gi rgya cher bshad pa tshig gsal ba/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur
<p>73b.7</p>gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdza' bo rgyal po bde spyod la spring yig yon tan can 'di bskur bas na bshes pa'i phrin yig ces bya ba'o/ /de la yon tan rang bzhin zhes bya ba ni bod pa ste/ sngon gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba las nges par skyed pa'i phyir/ /rang
<p>74a</p>
<p>74a.1</p>bzhin ni rgyu yin no/ /de nyid kyi phyir/ dge 'os zhes 'chad par 'gyur te/ gang zhig 'das pa'i dus na dge ba byed pa de ni/ da ltar byung ba'i dus na/dge ba'i skal ba can du 'gyur ro/ /'dis ni 'di dam pa'i chos mnyan pa'i 'os nyid yin par bshad de/ /de lta
<p>74a.2</p>bas na khyod kyis 'phags pa'i dbyangs 'di dag gsan pa'i rigs so zhes bya ba yin no/ /de dag sus ni byas/ ci'i phyir ni byas she na/ bdag gis ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung bsnyad las byung ba'i/ /bsod nams 'dun slad 'phags pa'i dbyangs 'di dag /cung zad cig
<p>74a.3</p>bsdebs zhes bya ba smos so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung bsnyad ces bya ba ni rab tu bstan pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste/ de las byung ba'i bsod nams gang yin pa de la 'dun pa'i phyir bdag gis/ 'phags pa'i dbyangs 'di dag bsdebs shing sbyar gyis/ gsan
<p>74a.4</p>pa'i rigs so zhes bya ba yin no/ /'phags pa'i dbyangs zhes bya ba ni tshigs su bcad pa'i ming ngo / /de dag kyang ci tsam zhig ce na/ cung zad cig ces bya ba smos te/ 'dis ni tshig mangs pa'i 'jigs pa spong bar byed do/ /rnam pa gzhan du na/ yon tan rang bzhin zhes bya
<p>74a.5</p>ba ni yon tan gyi ngo bo nyid ces bya ba'i tha tshig ste/ 'dis ni 'di dge ba'i mtshan nyid yin par bshad do/ /dge 'os zhes bya ba ni dge bar 'os pa nyid de/ dge ba'i bsam pa can gang yin pa de ni dge bar 'os pa yin no/ /de bas na dam pa'i chos mnyan pa'i rigs so zhes ston par byed
<p>74a.6</p>de/ dge ba ni de'i sngon du 'gro ba can yin pa'i phyir ro/ /lhag ma ni snga ma yin no/ /gal te khyod kyi snyan dngags bzang po ma yin pa 'di mi nyan no snyam du sems na de'i phyir/ ji ltar bde gshegs sku gzugs shing las kyang / /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ kyang zhes bya ba'i
<p>74a.7</p>sgras ni/ rdo ba dang 'jim pa la sogs pa bsdu'o/ /ci 'dra'ang rung zhes bya ba 'dis ni bzang po'am bzang po ma yin pa yang rung zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /ji ltar shing las de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs byas pa ci 'dra'ang rung ba ni bzhi po'i khyad par la mkhas pa rnams
<p>74b</p>
<p>74b.1</p>kyis mchod par bya ba yin pa de bzhin du bdag gi snyan dngags 'di yang ngan zhing bzang po ma yin yang / dam pa'i chos kyi gtam la brten pa'i phyir bsngags par bya ba yin no zhes ston par byed de/ bsngags par bya ba yin pa'i phyir/ mnyan par bya ba yang yin no snyam du dgongs pa
<p>74b.2</p>yin no/ /'on te ngas de bzhin gshegs pa'i bka' rnams shes zin pa nyid pas/ yang snyan dngags 'dis ji zhig bya snyam du sems na de'i phyir/ thub pa chen po'i bka' ni snyan dgu zhig /khyod kyi thugs su lta yang chud mod kyi/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ yang
<p>74b.3</p>zhes bya ba'i sgras ni thos pa dang rab tu bshad pa dang bsgom pa dag bsdu'o/ /'di skad du khyod kyi thub pa chen po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi bka' snyan pa dag lta thugs su chud mod kyi/ 'on kyang snyan dngags 'di smad par bya ba ma yin no zhes bshad pa yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 
<p>74b.4</p>rdo thal las bgyis dgung zla'i 'od kyis ni/ /ches dkar nyid du ci ste mi bgyid lags/ /zhes bya ba smos so/ /ni zhes bya ba ni 'di ltar zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste/ 'di ltar gzhal med khang rdo thal las byas pa rang bzhin gyis dkar ba yang zla ba'i 'od zer rnams kyis bzlas
<p>74b.5</p>pa bzhin du dkar po nyid du byed pas bka' stsal zin pa la yang bzlas na/ ches gsal ba nyid du 'gyur bas snyan dngags 'di smad par bya ba ma yin no/ /de la nyon mongs pa dang skye ba bag chags dang bcas pa de med pa'i phyir/ thub pa chen po ni de bzhin gshegs pa'o/ /legs
<p>74b.6</p>par gsungs pa'i phyir snyan pa yin no/ /'di man chad rgyal bas sangs rgyas chos dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni chos bstan pa yin no/ /sdig pa'i chos las rgyal ba'i phyir/ rgyal ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams te ji skad du/ sdig pa'i chos las nga rgyal
<p>74b.7</p>bas/ /de bas nyer 'gro nga rgyal ba'o/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /rjes su dran pa drug /rab tu bka' stsal zhes bya ba drug gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang / chos rjes su dran pa dang / dge 'dun rjes su dran pa dang / gtong ba rjes su dran pa dang / tshul
<p>75a</p>
<p>75a.1</p>khrims rjes su dran pa dang / lha rjes su dran pa'o/ /de la sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i dran pa nyid rjes su dran pa yin te/ de bzhin du thams cad la sbyar ro/ /yang rjes su dran pa de dag ji ltar bsgom par bya zhe na/ rang rang gi zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ sangs
<p>75a.2</p>rgyas la sogs pa so so'i yon tan rnams kyis rjes su dran pa de dag rjes su dran par bya zhing yid la bya'o zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /'dir ni sangs rgyas la sogs pa nyid rjes su dran pa dag yin par bshad de/ rjes su dran pa'i gnas yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir sangs rgyas la sogs pa de dag
<p>75a.3</p>rang rang gi yon tan gyi tshogs rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya'o zhes byas na legs par 'byor pa nyid do/ /yang sangs rgyas la sogs pa'i yon tan gang dag yin zhe na/ re zhig sangs rgyas kyi yon tan ni/ 'di ltar de ni bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
<p>75a.4</p>rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das zhes bya ba ste/ de lta bu la sogs pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon
<p>75a.5</p>tan yin no/ /'di ltar bcom ldan 'das zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten na snyan pa'i rnam par grags pa gang yin pa de ni/ 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa zhes tshig thams cad dang sbyar bar bya ste/ 'di lta bu yang yin/ 'di lta bu yang yin zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /
<p>75a.6</p>de la 'dod chags la sogs pa bcom pa nyid kyis bcom ldan 'das so/ /byang chub kyi snying po la bzhugs pa la/ bar chad bya bar brtson pa'i bdud bcom pa'i phyir yang bcom ldan 'das so/ /rnam pa gcig tu na 'di la skal ba yod pas na bcom ldan 'das de dbang phyug la sogs
<p>75a.7</p>pa dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/ /de bzhin gshegs pa zhes bya ba ni dngos po ji lta bar gnas pa de dag de bzhin du rtogs shing thugs su chud pas na de bzhin gshegs pa'o/ /ji skad gsungs pa de kho na ltar yin gyis gzhan du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir yang de bzhin gshegs pa'o/ /dgra bcom pa
<p>75b</p>
<p>75b.1</p>zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i dgra bcom pa'i phyir ro/ /'khor ba'i 'khor lo'i rtsibs bcom pas 'di'i phyir yang dgra bcom pa'o/ /rnyed pa dang bkur stis mchod par 'os pa'i phyir yang dgra bcom pa'o/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhes bya ba ni 'dis chos rnams yang dag par
<p>75b.2</p>phyin ci ma log par kun nas sangs rgyas pas na yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so/ /rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa zhes bya ba ni rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa ste/ mkhyen pa dang zhabs lta bu tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dag dang ldan pa'i phyir rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa'o/ /bde bar
<p>75b.3</p>gshegs pa zhes bya ba ni mdzes pa'i gnas su gshegs pa'i phyir bde bar gshegs pa zhes bya'o/ /phyir mi ldog par gshegs pa'i phyir yang bde bar gshegs pa ste/ rims nad legs par byang ba bzhin no/ /'jig rten mkhyen pa zhes bya ba ni 'jig pas na 'jig rten no/ /
<p>75b.4</p>de yang rnam pa gnyis te/ sems can gyi 'jig rten dang snod kyi 'jig rten no/ /de dag mkhyen pas na 'jig rten mkhyen pa ste sems can gyi 'jig rten gyi ni rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba'i yan lag bcu gnyis rnam par gzhag pa yongs su mkhyen pa'i phyir dang / snod kyi 'jig rten
<p>75b.5</p>gyi yang sa dang ri la sogs pa 'byung ba dang gnas pa dang tshad la sogs pa yongs su mkhyen pa'i phyir 'jig rten mkhyen pa zhes bya'o/ /rnam pa gcig tu na 'jig rten gyi tha snyad bzang po yongs su mkhyen pa'i phyir 'jig rten mkhyen pa zhes bya'o/ /skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na
<p>75b.6</p>med pa zhes bya ba la/ gdul bar rung ba ni gdul ba'o/ /de dag ni skyes bu yang yin la/ gdul ba yang yin pas skyes bu gdul ba'o/ /de dag gi kha lo sgyur ba ni skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba ste de dag gdul ba'i phyir ro/ /bla na med pa ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dag pas
<p>75b.7</p>khyad par du 'phags pa'i phyir te 'dul ba ni 'dir 'phags pa'i lam thob pa yin par rig par bya'o/ /des ni 'di 'dul bar 'gyur te/ yang dmu rgod kyi ngo bor mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/ /lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa zhes bya ba la lha dang mi zhes smos pa ni de dag mchog yin pa'i phyir ram/ 
<p>76a</p>
<p>76a.1</p>'phags pa'i lam gyi snod yin pa'i phyir ro/ /phyin ci ma log par ston pa'i phyir ston pa ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan 'di dag ni bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos ston pas rab tu phye ba bstan pa yin pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das zhes bya ba ni/ de kho na nyid
<p>76a.2</p>thugs su chud pa'i phyir sangs rgyas zhes bya ste/ tshig gi mjug mi mngon par byas pa'i phyir ro/ /rnam pa gcig tu na blo rgyas pa'i phyir te/ pad+ma rgyas pa bzhin no/ /yang na mi shes pa'i gnyid las sad pa'i phyir te skyes bu gnyid sad pa bzhin no/ /'di ni tshig 'di rnams kyi bsdus
<p>76a.3</p>pa'i don yin te/ rgyas par ni bstan bcos gzhan dag las khong du chud par bya'o/ /sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bshad zin to/ /chos kyi yon tan ni legs par gsungs pa la sogs pa yin te/ 'di lta ste bcom ldan 'das kyi chos ni legs par gsungs pa yang dag par mthong
<p>76a.4</p>ba dang nad med pa dus chad pa med pa/ 'di mthong ba la don yod pa/ nye bar gtod pa/ mkhas pa rnams kyi so sor rang gi rig par bya ba ste/ bstan pa'i chos dang rtogs pa'i chos zhes bya ba chos rnam pa gnyis bstan to/ /de la bsdus pa'i don ni legs par gsungs pa zhes bya ba 'dis ni
<p>76a.5</p>thog ma dang bar dang tha mar dge ba nyid kyis bstan pa'i chos bshad la/ lhag ma rnams kyis ni rtogs pa'i chos bshad do zhes bya ba yin te/ ha cang tshig mangs su dogs pas ma spros so/ /dge 'dun gyi yon tan ni legs par zhugs pa la sogs pa yin te/ 'di lta ste bcom ldan
<p>76a.6</p>'das kyi nyan thos kyi dge 'dun ni legs par zhugs pa/ drang por zhugs pa/ rigs par zhugs pa/ mthun par zhugs pa 'di lta ste/ skyes bu zung bzhi dang / skyes bu gang zag ya brgyad po dag yin no/ /bcom ldan 'das kyi nyan thos kyi dge 'dun 'di ni kun du sbyin pa'i 'os
<p>76a.7</p>su gyur pa/ rab tu sbyin pa'i 'os su gyur pa/ bskor bar bya ba'i 'os su gyur pa/ thal mo sbyar ba'i 'os su gyur pa/ 'jig rten gyi bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /'dir yang bsdus pa'i don ni 'phags pa'i dge 'dun slob pa dang mi slob pa'i yon tan
<p>76b</p>
<p>76b.1</p>rnams pa gnyis bstan te legs par zhugs pa la sogs pa tshig bzhis ni bsgrub pa'i yon tan bshad do/ /kun du sbyin pa'i 'os su gyur pa la sogs pas ni mchod par 'os pa nyid kyi yon tan bstan to zhes bshad pa yin no/ /gtong ba'i yon tan ni kye ma bdag skye bu'i yon tan
<p>76b.2</p>ni ser sna'i dri ma kun nas langs pa rnams kyi nang nas ser sna'i dri ma dang bral ba'i sems kyis gnas shing mchod sbyin khor mor byed pa dang / lag pa rkyong ba dang / rnam par gtong ba la dga' ba dang / sbyin pa la 'ged par dga' ba gang yin pa de ni bdag gis rnyed pa
<p>76b.3</p>legs par rnyed pa yin no zhes bya ba yin te/ 'dir yang rang gi rgyud du gtogs pa'i sbyin pa'i yon tan ser sna'i dri ma spangs pa dang / sbyin pa'i ngang tshul can dang / lus kyis brtson 'grus brtsams pa dang / dngos po yongs su gtong ba dang / de la mngon par dga' ba zhes bya ba
<p>76b.4</p>rnams bstan to/ /tshul khrims kyi yon tan ni bdag gi tshul khrims ni ma nyams pa/ skyon med pa/ ma 'dres pa/ ma gos pa/rang dbang yod pa/ mkhas pas bsngags pa/ ting nge 'dzin bsgrub pa dag yin no zhes bya ba yin no/ /'dir yang rang gi rgyud du gtogs pa'i tshul
<p>76b.5</p>khrims kho na'i yon tan rnams bstan te/ tshigs rnams kyi don ni 'og nas bstan par bya'o/ /lha'i yon tan ni rgyal chen ris bzhi pa'i lha dag dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa nas gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi bar dag yod do zhes bya ba yin te/ lha de rnams dang bdag nyid kyi yon tan
<p>76b.6</p>dag rjes su dran par byed pa yin no/ /de la skye ba'i lha rnams kyi skye ba'i rgyud du gyur pa'i yon tan dang / bdag nyid kyi tshul khrims dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / shes rab kyi yon tan rnams ni lha'i yon tan yin no zhes bshad do/ don du na 'dir rang gi yon tan rnams kho na lha'i yon tan dag dang
<p>76b.7</p>mtshungs par byas nas dran pa ni rjes su dran pa zhes bya bar bshad do/ /rjes su dran pa'i gnas drug ni sems dang bar byed pa'i phyir dang / bsod nams chen po rgyu yin pa'i phyir dang po nyid du bstan nas/ de la sems mngon par dad pas dge ba bya'o zhes bstan pa'i phyir/ dge ba'i
<p>77a</p>
<p>77a.1</p>las lam bcu po zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ 'bras bu yid du 'ong ba'i phyir dge ba'o/ /bya ba'i ngo bo nyid yin pa'i phyir las kyang yin la/ bde 'gro'i lam yang yin pas las kyi lam mo/ /las kyi lam bcu po de dag kyang gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ srog gcod
<p>77a.2</p>pa spong ba dang / /ma byin par len pa spong ba dang / 'dod pas log par g.yem pa spong ba dang / brdzun du smra ba spong ba dang / phra ma spong ba dang / tshig rtsub mo spong ba dang / tshig kyal pa spong ba dang / brnab sems med pa dang / gnod sems med pa dang / yang dag pa'i lta ba ste
<p>77a.3</p>dge ba'i las kyi lam bcu po 'di dag bsten par bya'o/ /yang de dag ji ltar bsten par bya zhe na/ /lus dang ni/ ngag dang yid kyis rtag tu zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ de la srog gcod pa spong ba la sogs pa gsum ni lus kyis rtag tu bstan par bya'o/ /brdzun du smra ba
<p>77a.4</p>spong ba la sogs pa bzhi ni/ ngag gis rtag tu bsten par bya'o/ /brnab sems med pa la sogs pa gsum ni yid kyis rtag tu bsten par bya'o/ /rtag tu zhes bya ba 'dis ni las kyis byas pa dang bsags pa ston par byed do/ /de la ji ltar srog gcod par 'gyur zhe na/ srog
<p>77a.5</p>chags pha rol yang yin srog chags yin par yang 'du shes/ gsad pa'i sems kyang nye bar gnas par gyur/ brtsal ba yang byas/ des kyang shi na srog bcad pa yin te/sdig pa'i khyad par ni gzhi dang bsam pa dang sbyor ba'i khyad par las rig par bya'o/ /ji ltar ma byin par
<p>77a.6</p>blangs par 'gyur zhe na/ gzhan gyis yongs su bzung ba yang yin/ gzhan gyis yongs su bzung ba yang 'du shes/ rku ba'i sems kyang nye bar gnas/ gnas nas kyang spags na ma byin par len pa yin te/ /'dir sdig pa'i khyad par ni rdzas de gang gi yin pa de'i khyad par dang sbyor
<p>77a.7</p>ba dang bsam pa'i khyad par las rig par bya'o/ /ji ltar 'dod pas log par g.yem par 'gyur zhe na/ bud med gzhan gyis bsrungs pa'am/ chos kyis bsrungs pa'am/ rang gi bud med la yang dus ma yin pa dang / gnas ma yin pa dang / yul ma yin pa dang / yan
<p>77b</p>
<p>77b.1</p>lag ma yin pa 'khrig pa'i chos bsten na 'dod pas log par g.yem pa yin te/ 'dir yang sdig pa'i khyad par ni gzhi dang bsam pa dang sbyor ba'i khyad par las rig par bya'o/ /de la ji ltar na brdzun du smras par 'gyur zhe na/ slu ba'i bsam pa dang lta ba yid la bzhag nas/ don
<p>77b.2</p>rnam par go ba la tshig tu smra ba'am/ lus kyis rnam par rig par byed pas kyang rung ste de lta na brdzun du smras pa yin te/ the tshom za ba'i dngos po la nges pa bzhin du smra ba yang brdzun du smra ba kho na yin no/ /'dir yang sdig pa'i khyad par ni bslu bar bya ba'i khyad par dang bsam pa'i
<p>77b.3</p>khyad par las rig par bya'o/ /ji ltar phra ma byas par 'gyur zhe na/ dga' bar 'dod pa'am dbye ba'i bsam pas 'ga' zhig las gzhan zhig la mi dga' ba thos nas de la bsnyad par gyur pa dang / de las thos nas 'di la bsnyad par gyur na yang dag pa yang rung / yang dag pa ma
<p>77b.4</p>yin pa yang rung ste/ de lta na phra ma byas pa yin no/ /yang dag pa ma yin pa smras na yang brdzun du smras pa yang ci'i phyir mi 'gyur zhe na/ kha cig na re 'gyur ba kho na yin no zhes zer ro/ /de ni de ltar gzung bar mi bya ste/ ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di dbye ba'i bsam pa can yin gyi/ bslu ba'i bsam
<p>77b.5</p>pa ni med pas so/ /de ltar byas na yang dag pa ma yin pa tshig rtsub mo smras na yang brdzun du smras par mi 'gyur te/ bsam pa gnyis cig car mi srid pa'i phyir ro/ /ji ltar tshig rtsub mo smras par 'gyur zhe na thos pa'i sems dang ldan pas/ pha rol po sdug bsngal bar bya bar
<p>77b.6</p>'dod pas/ don mngon par go ba la tshig tu smra na tshig rtsub mo smras pa yin no/ /don mngon par mi go ba la tshig 'khyal par 'gyur ro/ /ji ltar tshig 'khyal par smras par 'gyur zhe na/ brdzun du smra ba la sogs pa gsum ma gtogs pa tshig gzhan gang zhig nyon mongs pa can gyi
<p>77b.7</p>sems kyis brjod na/ de ltar na tshig rkyal pa smras pa yin no/ /las kyi lam gsum po 'di dag kyang brdzun du smra ba bzhin lus kyis kyang byed la sdig pa'i khyad par yang brdzun du smra ba dang 'dra ba kho nar rig par bya'o/ /ji ltar brnab sems su 'gyur zhe na/ gal te gzhan gyi bdog
<p>78a</p>
<p>78a.1</p>bdag la 'dod pa skyed par byed na de ltar na brnab sems su 'gyur ba yin no/ /ji ltar gnod sems yin zhe na/ gal te sems can gzhan la zhe sdang na de lta na gnod sems su gyur pa yin no/ /ji ltar log par lta bar 'gyur zhe na/ gal te las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams kyi
<p>78a.2</p>'bras bu med do snyam du nges par sems na de lta na log par lta bar 'gyur ro/ /las kyi lam gsum po 'di dag gi sdig pa'i khyad par ni bsam pa'i khyad par kho na las rig par bya la brnab sems kyis ni dmigs pa'i dbang gis kyang sdig pa'i khyad par du 'dod de/ mi dge ba'i las kyi lam
<p>78a.3</p>bcu po 'di dag spong ba'i dbang gis dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bsten par bya'o/ /chang rnams las ldog par mdzod cig ces bya ba la/ chang ni kha na ma tho ba chen po'i rgyu nyid yin mod kyang / spyad pa kho nas mi dge ba nyid ma yin pas las kyi lam rnams kyi nang du ma bshad de de lta bas na logs
<p>78a.4</p>shig tu dgag par ston to/ /mang po'i tshig ni chang ni myos par 'gyur ba nyid du khyad par med kyang rgyu'i khyad par las rig par bya ste/ bcos pa'i chang ni bu ram chang dang / 'bras phye'i chang dang / sbrang rtsi'i chang ste rnam pa gsum mo/ /sbyar ba'i chang ni me tog las mnan pa la sogs pa yin par
<p>78a.5</p>rig par bya'o/ /dge ba'i 'tsho ba la yang mngon par dgyes pa zhes bya ba ni mdzod ces bya bar sbyar te/ dge ba'i 'tsho ba ni gzhan la mi gnod par 'jug pa gang yin pa'o/ /de ltar dge ba'i las la rnam par gnas pas bdog pa ji lta ba bzhin du sbyin pa sbyin par bya'o zhes bstan pa'i phyir longs
<p>78a.6</p>spyod g.yo ba zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /spyad par bya ba yin pas/ longs spyod de 'di ni sbyin par bya ba'i dngos po zas dang skom la sogs pa'i tshig bla dgas so/ /longs spyod de dag kyang mi brtan pa'i phyir g.yo ba'o/ /ngoms mi shes pa'i phyir snying po med pa ste/ 'dis ni longs spyod
<p>78a.7</p>rnams la kun du 'dzin pa ldog par byed do/ /mkhyen nas zhes bya ba ni rtogs par byas nas so/ /dge slong zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni sbyin pa'i zhing rnam pa gsum po ston te/ /sbyin gnas kyi zhing ni dge sbyong dang bram ze rnams so/ /snying rje'i zhing ni bkren pa rnams so/ /phan 'dogs
<p>78b</p>
<p>78b.1</p>pa'i zhing ni bshes pa rnams so/ /tshul bzhin zhes bya ba 'dis ni gus par bya ba bstan to/ /de ni gcig tu rnam par smin pa yid du 'ong ba'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong dag bsod snyoms gus par byas pa rnams kyi rnam par smin pa ni 'dod pa sdug pa/ 
<p>78b.2</p>dga' ba yid dang 'thad pa so sor myong bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/ /sbyin las gzhan pa'i gnyen mchog ma mchis so/ /zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin pa phan chen po 'dogs pa yin pa nyid du ston te/ 'dis ni 'dir sbyin pa la brten par bya ba yin par rig par bya'o/ /longs spyod rnams la
<p>78b.3</p>mi lta bas tshul khrims yang dag par blangs nas bsrung bar bya'o zhes bstan pa'i phyir/ /khyod kyi tshul khrims ma nyams mod mi dma'/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de la ma nyams pa ni ji ltar yang dag par blangs pa las gcig las kyang ma 'das pa'i phyir ro/ /tshul khrims gcig
<p>78b.4</p>las 'das pas ni nyams par 'gyur ro/ /bslab pa mang po zhig las 'das pas ni skyon can du 'gyur ro/ /de gnyi ga med par bstan pa'i phyir/ /ma nyams mod mi dma' zhes bya ba smos te/ tshul khrims skyon can ni mod dma' ba yin no/ /ma 'dres zhes bya ba la tshul khrims 'dres
<p>78b.5</p>pa ni mi dge ba'o/ /'dren mar 'dug pa gang yin pa ste/ de med pa'i phyir ma 'dres pa'o/ /ma sbags pa ni srid pa dang longs spyod kyi don du yongs su ma bsngos pa'i phyir ro/ /tshul khrims 'di nyid rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ma gos pa zhes bya ste/ gos pa ni rnam pa gzhan du ston to/ /ma nyams
<p>78b.6</p>pa la sogs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa'i tshul khrims gang yin pa de ni rang dbang yod pa yang yin te/ sred pa'i bran nyid las thar pa'i phyir ro/ /de nyid kyi phyir tshul khrims de ni mkhas pa 'phags pa rnams kyis bsngags pa yin la/ ting nge 'dzin sgrub par byed pa yang yin te/ tshul khrims
<p>78b.7</p>dang ldan pa'i sems mnyam par 'jog pa'i phyir ro/ /tshul khrims de lta bu de khyod kyis brten par bya'o/ /ci'i phyir zhe na/ khrims ni rgyu dang mi rgyu'i sa bzhin du/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ ni zhes bya ba'i sgra ni 'di ltar zhes bya ba'i don to/ /ji ltar sa ni 'gro ba rgyu ba dang mi rgyu ba'i
<p>79a</p>
<p>79a.1</p>skye ba dang / gnas pa dang 'phel ba'i rgyur gyur ba de bzhin du tshul khrims kyang ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa yon tan thams cad kyi gzhi rten yin no/ /'dis ni gus pa bskyed pa'i phyir tshul khrims kyi skyes bu byed pa'i 'bras bu bstan te/ de ltar re zhig sbyin pa dang / tshul
<p>79a.2</p>khrims spyir bshad pa yin no/ /da ni theg pa chen po la gzud pa'i ched du sbyin pa la sogs pa pha rol tu phyin pas bsdus pa rnams bstan pa'i phyir/ sbyin dang tshul khrims zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de la byang chub tu sems bskyed pas/ sems can thams cad la phan par bya ba'i
<p>79a.3</p>phyir/ sbyin pa ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yin te tshul khrims la sogs pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yang de dang 'dra bar rig par bya'o/ /bzod pa ni 'dir gzhan gyis gnod pa byas pa la mi mjed pa'i bzod pa dang / sdug bsngal dang du len pa'i bzod pa zhes bya ba bzod pa rnam pa gnyis su bzhed do/ /brtson
<p>79a.4</p>'grus ni sems can gyi don du sangs rgyas kyi chos btsal bar spro ba'o/ /bsam gtan ni sems can gyi don byed pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin sgrub par byed pa'i bsam gtan bzhi pa'o/ /shes rab ni chos thams cad yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes par byed pa dang / sems
<p>79a.5</p>can rnams la don phyin ci ma log par rab tu ston par byed pa'i rab tu byed pa gang yin pa ste/ shes rab de lta bu ni/ nyan thos la sogs pa la med pa'i phyir gzhal du med pa zhes bya'o/ /pha rol phyin pa 'di dag rgyas mdzad ces bya ba ni pha rol tu phyin pa 'di rnams sgrubs shig ces bya ba'i tha tshig
<p>79a.6</p>go/ /ci'i phyir zhe na/ srid pa'i rgya mtsho'i pha rol phyin pa rgyal ba'i dbang po mdzod/ /ces bya ba smos so/ /de la pha rol tu phyin pa mdzod ces bya ba ni pha rol du son par gyis shig ces bya ba'i don to/ /gang gis she na srid pa'i rgya mtsho'o/ /nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dag kyang srid pa'i rgya mtsho'i pha
<p>79a.7</p>pha rol tu son pa yin pas/ rgyal ba'i dbang po zhes bya bas khyad par du byed de/ 'di skad du pha rol tu phyin pa drug rdzogs nas/ sangs rgyas nyid thob pas khyod kyis kyang pha rol du phyin pa rnams rdzogs par byos la/ sangs rgyas su gyis shig ces bshad pa yin no/ /de bzhin du sbyin pa la
<p>79b</p>
<p>79b.1</p>sogs pa dang ldan pa'i khyim pa dag kyang yod pas de dag gi dge ba'i las gzhan bstan pa'i phyir/ /gang la pha dang ma dag mchod pa yi/ /rigs de tshangs bcas zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de la rigs gang la pha dang ma dag mchod pa'i zhes bya ba 'dis ni/ rigs 'di la mi dang mi ma
<p>79b.2</p>yin pas byas pa'i gnod pa med par bstan to/ /tshangs pa dang bcas pa nyid kyis ni rigs de lhas byin gyis brlabs pa nyid du ston to/ /slob dpon dang bcas pa nyid kyis ni/ bla ma'i khyad par gyis byin gyis brlabs pa nyid du ston to/ /gzhan yang mthong ba'i chos dang / tshe phyi ma'i phan
<p>79b.3</p>yon bstan pa'i phyir/ de dag mchod ces bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ de gnyis la mchod pa ni de dag la mchod pa'o/ /pha dang ma dag la mchod pa ni mthong ba'i chos la yang dag par 'gyur la pha rol du yang mtho ris su 'gyur te/ /de lta bas na khyim na gnas pas bsgrims te pha dang ma
<p>79b.4</p>dag la mchod pa bya'o zhes bya ba yin no/ /khyim na gnas pa rnams la dus thams cad du tshangs par spyad pa dka' ba'i phyir na nyin zhag gcig pa'i tshangs par spyod pa la yang sbyar ba'i ched du gso sbyong yan lag brgyad pa bstan pa'i phyir/ 'tshe dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de la 'tshe ba
<p>79b.5</p>ni srog gcod pa'o/ /chom rkun ni ma byin par len pa'o/ /'khrig pa ni bshang ba dang gci ba dang kha'i lam du log par sgrub pa'o/ /brdzun ni brdzun du smra ba'o/ /chang ni bcos pa'i chang dang sbyar ba'i chang ngo / /dus min zas ni nyi ma phyed yol nas dus su rung ba'i dngos po spyod pa'o/ /mal
<p>79b.6</p>stan mthon po ni khri dang khri'u tshad las 'das pa'o/ /glu dag dang gar ni 'jig rten grags pa kho na'o/ /spos dang phreng ba spyod pa ni che ba'i don du bkag gi nad pa'i nad gso ba'i phyir ni ma yin no/ /brgyad po de dag ni gso sbyong gi yan lag yin no/ /yang 'di dag gang gi yan lag cha shas su
<p>79b.7</p>gyur pa yin pa/ 'di'i sdom pa gzhan gang zhig yod ce na/ 'ga' yang med de 'on kyang spyi'i yan lag ces bya ste/ phyi ma la yan lag lnga pa bzhin no/ /yang yan lag 'di dag nyid dgra bcom pa'i tshul khrims kyi rjes su byed pa yin nam zhe na/ gang gi phyir 'di skad du/ dgra bcom
<p>80a</p>
<p>80a.1</p>tshul khrims rjes su byed pa yi/ /yan lag brgyad po 'di dag dang ldan na/ /zhes bshad de 'di skad du yan lag dang po 'dis bdag 'phags pa dgra bcom pa de dag gi tshul khrims kyi rjes su slob po/ /rjes su bgyid do zhes bya ba la sogs pa 'byung ngo zhe na/ 'dir
<p>80a.2</p>dgra bcom pa'i tshul khrims ni yan lag rnams yin la/ dgra bcom pa'i tshul khrims kyi rjes su byed pa ni gang zag yin par snang ngo / /de lta yin dang 'dir rten gyis brtan pa bstan te/ dper na khre'u dag sgrogs so zhes bya ba lta bu yin pas nyes pa med do/ /da ni/ gso sbyong 'dod
<p>80a.3</p>spyod lha lus yid 'ong ba/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pas gso sbyong gi sdom pa 'di'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu ston par byed de/ 'di skad du/ nyin zhag gcig pa'i gso sbyong gi sdom pas ni 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha drug gi nang gar 'dod par skye bar 'gyur ro zhes bshad pa yin no/ /skyes
<p>80a.4</p>pa bud med dag la zhes bya ba ni skyes pa dag dang bud med dag la sbyin par byed kyis/ gzhan ma ning la sogs pa la ni ma yin te/ de dag la sdom pa skye ba med pa'i phyir ro/ /stsol bar bgyid ces bya ba ni sbyin par byed pa'o/ /khyim pa de dag nyid la bya ba ngan pa la chags pa'i nyes pas ser sna la
<p>80a.5</p>sogs pa 'byung la/ de dag kyang ngan song gi rgyu yin pas de las bzlog par/ ser sna zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de la ser sna ni sbyin pa dang mi mthun par rang gi phun sum tshogs pa la kun du 'dzin pa'o/ /g.yo ni sems gya gyu ba ste gang gis na rang gi bsam pa rab tu mi brtan pa'o/ /
<p>80a.6</p>sgyu ni gzhan slu ba ste gang gis na 'di ltar 'dis bsam pa shes nas glags rnyed par mi 'gyur bar gzhan rmongs par byed pa'o/ /chags pa ni bdag la sred pa dang longs spyod la sred pa'o/ /snyom las ni brtson 'grus kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs kyi chos te/ le lo zhes bya'o/ /mngon pa'i nga
<p>80a.7</p>rgyal ni khyad par thob par bya ba ma thob par bdag gis thob bo snyam du nga rgyal byed pa gang yin pa'o/ /'dod chags ni 'khrig pa la sred pa'o/ /zhe sdang ni sems can rnams la kun nas mnar sems pa ste/ chos brgyad po 'di dag dang / rigs kyis rgyags pa la sogs pa lnga dang mi dge ba'i
<p>80b</p>
<p>80b.1</p>chos bcu gsum la dgra bzhin du blta bar bya ste/ de rnams dang lhan cig 'grogs par mi bya'o zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /de la rgyags pa ni chos de rnams kyis sems gzengs rab tu mthos pa ste/ gang gis nar ro ba bzhin du chos dang chos ma yin pa sgrub par mi 'gyur ba'o/ /de nyid kyi
<p>80b.2</p>phyir rgyags pa ni rang gi chos la chags pa'i sems ni yongs su gtugs pa'o zhes 'byung ste/ rang gi chos la so so'i 'dod chags kyis de kho na la sems de yongs su gtugs shing yongs su zad par 'gyur gyi/ chos sam chos ma yin pa gzhan sgrub par mi 'gyur ba yin no zhes bya
<p>80b.3</p>ba'i tha tshig go/ /khyim pa rnams la yang bag dang bcas par bya ba yod pas de dag de la dgod par bzhed nas/ bag yod bdud rtsi'i gnas te zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ bag yod pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa bdud rtsi'i rten yin no zhes bya ba'i don to/ /bag med pa ni 'chi ba'i
<p>80b.4</p>gnas yin no/ /ji ltar shes she na/ thub pas bka' stsal to zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /de bzhin gshegs pas bka' stsal pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste/ bag yod bdud rtsi'i gnas yin te/ /bag med pa ni 'chi ba'i gnas/ /bag yod 'chi bar mi 'gyur te/ 
<p>80b.5</p>bag med pa ni rtag tu 'chi/ /zhes tshigs su bcad pa de bka' stsal pa'i phyir ro/ /de la bag yod pa ni dge ba'i chos bsgom pa'o/ /bzlog pa ni bag med pa yin par rig par bya'o/ /de bas khyod kyis dge chos spel slad du/ /zhes bya ba ni gang gi phyir de ltar bag yod pa phan yon
<p>80b.6</p>che ba de'i phyir khyod kyis dge ba'i chos spel bar bya ba'i phyir rtag tu bag yod par bya ste/ dge ba'i chos la goms pa dor bar mi bya'o zhes bya ba'i don to/ /'on te khyod kyis kho bo'i don zhig bya bar chad na/ dang po nyid nas ci ste ma smras kho bo sngar bag med par gyur zin pas/ bag yod pas
<p>80b.7</p>ci byar yod snyam du sems na de'i phyir/ gang zhig sngon chad bag med gyur pa las/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ /'di skad du/ gang zhig sngon chad bag med par gyur pa de yang gal te phyis bag yod pa la brten na de ni mdzes pa nyid de/ dper na zla ba sprin dang bral ba bzhin no
<p>81a</p>
<p>81a.1</p>zhes bshad pa yin no/ /ci sems can de lta bu 'ga' tsam mthong ngam zhe na/ /mthong ngo zhes bstan pa'i phyir/ dga' bo sor phreng zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /dga' bo zhes bya ba shAkya gzhon nu 'dod chags chen po zhig yod de/ de ni rang gi chung ma la shin tu lhag
<p>81a.2</p>par chags pas de med par thang cig tsam yang dga' ba mi myong ngo / /de 'dra ba de de bzhin gshegs pas khyim nas khrid de rab tu phyung ngo / /rab tu phyung yang nyin dang mtshan du de kho na la rjes su rtog par byed kyis chos la ni ma yin no/ /de lta bu la de bzhin gshegs pas dgra bcom pa nyid thob
<p>81a.3</p>pa'i dbang du mdzad do/ /sor mo'i phreng ba zhes bya ba ni bram ze'i bu zhig go/ /de ni blun po zhig ste 'di ltar des chos su 'gyur ro zhes bya ba bla ma'i lung mnyan nas mi dgu brgya dgu bcu rtsa dgu bsad do/ /de yang phyis de bzhin gshegs pas rab tu phyung nas/ khams gsum las 'dod chags
<p>81a.4</p>dang bral bar gyur to/ /mthong ldan ni ma skyes dgra'o/ /de ni zhe sdang can zhig ste/ 'di ltar des mi dge ba'i grogs po dang phrad pa dang / sngon gyi sha khon chags pas pha chos dang ldan pa'i rgyal po gsad do/ /de yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa kho na la brten
<p>81a.5</p>nas/ dmyal ba'i me'i bud shing las thar ro/ /rigs kyi bu bde byed yang tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa'i dbang gis gzhan gyi chung ma la nyal po bya ba'i le lan gyis ma bsad nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstan pa kho na la brten te/ pho long brdabs pa dang 'dra bar dmyal ba'i rdo rje
<p>81a.6</p>las thar te/ mtho ris kyi 'jig rten gyi bde ba nyams su myong bar gyur to zhes grags te/ de ltar dga' bo la sogs pa de dag kyang sngon bag med par gyur pa las phyis bag yod pa'i dbang gis sdug bsngal gyi khyad par de dang de las thar bas/ khyod kyang sngon bag med par gyur du zin kyang
<p>81a.7</p>phyis bag yod par bya dgos so zhes bya ba yin no/ /khyim pa rnams la mi 'dod pa du ma 'bab pa'i dbang gis khro ba mang ba'i phyir de la 'dun pa las bzlog pa'i ched du bzod pa bstan pa'i phyir/ 'di ltar bzod mtshungs thub dka' ma mchis pas/ /zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so/ /bzod
<p>81b</p>
<p>81b.1</p>pa dang 'dra ba'i dka' thub ni med kyi bzod pa kho na dka' thub thams cad kyi mchog yin te/ bzod pa dka' thub dam pa zhes tshigs su bcad pa de dag bka' stsal pa'i phyir ro/ /'di skad du bzod pa dang ldan pa kho na dka' thub can yin gyi/ sems khro bas nyams pa la rlung dang chu dang rtsa ba dang 'bras
<p>81b.2</p>bu za zhing lus skem pa dang / ral pa dang lo ma dang shing shun dang / /hral hrul gyon pa ni ma yin no zhes bshad pa yin no/ /'di ltar bzod pa dang ldan pas ni nyon mongs pa rnams gdung bar byed la/ cig shos kyis ni lus so/ /lus gdungs pa tsam gyis ni bde 'gro yang mi thob na thar pa
<p>81b.3</p>lta zhig smos kyang ci dgos/ gang gi phyir/ de ltar bzod pa phan yon che ba de yi phyir/ /khyod kyis khro ba'i go skabs dbye mi bgyi/ /bzod pa'i yon tan gzhan yang bstan pa'i phyir/ /khro ba spangs pas phyir mi ldog pa nyid/ /ces bya ba la sogs pa smos te/ khro ba spangs pa gang gi dbang
<p>81b.4</p>gis na 'dod pa'i khams sdug bsngal du ma dang 'brel bar 'ong bar mi 'gyur ba'i phyir mi ldog pa nyid kyang thob ste/ gnas 'di la ni sangs rgyas zhal gyis bzhes so/ /gnya' bo yin no zhes bya ba'i tha tshig ste/ ji skad du bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong dag 'di lta ste/ khro ba spongs shig dang / 
<p>81b.5</p>khyod phyir mi ldog pa'i gnya' bor gyur pa nga yin no zhes bya ba lta bu'o/ /de la bzod pa gang yin zhe na/ mi khro ba dang / khro ba skyes na yang de'i mod kho na la zhi bar byed kyis zhe la 'dzin par mi byed pa gang yin pa'o/ /da la khro ba gang zhe na/ sems can dang sems can ma yin pa dag las mi 'dod pa nye
<p>81b.6</p>bar 'bab pa da ltar byung ba la brten nas/ sems gtum pa gang yin pa ste/ tshig pa za ba zhes kyang bya'o/ /bdag ni 'dis spyos zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni bzod pa kho na ston to/ /kho na du 'dzin pa'i yul rnam pa bzhi ste/ 'dis bdag spyos so/ /'dis bdag gtags so/ /'dis bdag
<p>81b.7</p>pham par byas so/ /'dis bdag gi nor phrogs so zhes de ltar khon du 'dzin cing de ltar gzhan gyis gnod pa byas pa zhe la 'dzin na khro ba'i nyes rtsom 'khrug long rnams skyed do/ /gang gi sems la de lta bur 'dzin pa med cing khon du 'dzin pa rnam par spangs pa de ni sems kyi sdug bsngal med pa'i phyir/ /
<p>82a</p>
<p>82a.1</p>bde bar gnyid kyis log gi /cig shos ni sems sdug bsngal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir sdug bsngal zhing gnyid kyis log go/ /da ni sems can chu dang zhes bya ba la sogs pas/ sems can so so'i skye bo thams cad la yang ji skad bshad pa'i dge ba dang mi dge ba'i sems dag
