<p>123b.7</p>pa de bzhin du bstan pa yang ngo / /de la bstan pa ni gnyis las rtogs pa'i chos dang sbyar na bzang ba ni ting nge 'dzin no/ /'phan med pa ni tshul khrims te/ ji skad du/ rnam dag yon tan bzhi ldan no/ /'chal khrims de rgyus 'phan ma byung / /de yi gnyen po zhi la brten/ /zhes
<p>124a</p>
<p>124a.1</p>bshad pa lta bu'o/ /rnam par dag pa ni shes rab bo/ /lung gi chos dang sbyar na mdo sde dang / 'dul ba dang / mngon pa ste go rims bzhin no/ /chen po ni rigs can gsum mo/ /mnos pa ni thos pa la sogs pa byed pa'o/ /sa'i steng na gnas pa ni
<p>124a.2</p>bsam gtan dgu na spyod pa rnams kyi yid la gnas pa'o/ /rab rib ni mi shes pa gnyis pa'o/ /legs par sgrub pa ni chos kyi sprin de zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /char sprin ni nam mkha' la g.yos pa dang / char gyi rgyur gyur pa dang / char chu de yang ro gcig
<p>124a.3</p>pa dang / tsha ba'i gdung ba sel ba dang / snod kyi dbang gis ro du mar 'gyur ba ste/ chos lnga dang ldan pa bzhin du bstan pa yang ngo / /phan pa mdzad pa ni snga ma ltar ro/ /mya ngan ni 'khor ba pa'i/ /'das pa ni de las brgal bar ro/ /mchog ni nges pa don dam par dge ba yin pa'i
<p>124a.4</p>phyir ram/ 'dus ma byas pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i rgyu ni des de thob par byed pa'o/ /ro gcig pa ni chos thams cad bdag med pa/ tha mi dad pa'o/ /yang na theg pa gcig tu tha mi dad pa ste/ ji skad du/ shA ri'i bu nga la dad par gyis shig nges par zung shig /shA ri'i bu de
<p>124a.5</p>bzhin gshegs pa la ni brdzun gsung ba mi mnga' 'o/ /shA ri'i bu theg pa ni 'di gcig pu kho nar zad de/'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /gdung ba sel ba ni sdug bsngal ba dang nyon mongs pa spong ba'o/ /snod ni nyan po'i dbang po tha dad pa'am/ rigs tha
<p>124a.6</p>dad pa'o/ /ro rnams du mar 'gyur ba ni theg pa gnyis sam gsum mam bzhir 'gyur ba'o/ /de skad du yang / lha yi theg dang tshangs pa'i theg /bde gshegs nyan thos rang rgyal gyi/ /theg pa tha dad ngas bshad do/ /zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /'o na sngar ro gcig tu zhes theg pa
<p>124a.7</p>gcig tu bshad pa dang 'gal lo zhe na/ mi 'gal te/ go rims bzhin du nges pa'i don dang / drang ba'i don gyi dbang du byas pa'i phyir ro/ /de ltar chos la bstod nas/ dge 'dun la bstod pa'i bsam pa phun sum tshogs pa la bstod pa ni/ snod yangs zhes rkang pa phyed dang gnyis so/ /rgya
<p>124b</p>
<p>124b.1</p>mtsho chen po ni 'bab chu'i snod du gyur pa dang / rgya che ba dang / zab pa dang / dri ma med pa dang / bla 'og gsal ba dang / gru gzings la sogs pa 'debs pa na khur bzod pa dang / khrus dang btung ba la sogs pa nye bar spyad pa dang /nya dang rus sbal la sogs pa'i gnas su gyur pa ste/ chos
<p>124b.2</p>brgyad dang ldan pa bzhin du dge 'dun rnams kyang ngo / /de la dge 'dun ni rgyud yon tan gyi snod du gyur pa dang / yangs pa'i bsam pa ni tshad med pa bzhi yid la byed pa ste/ sems can thams cad la dmigs pa'i phyir ro/ /zab pa'i bsam pa ni bdag med pa gnyis yid la byed pa ste gting
<p>124b.3</p>dpag dka' ba'i phyir ro/ /dri ma med pa'i bsam pa ni dri ma drug dang bral ba'i phyir ro/ /ji skad du/ gzhan yang nyon mongs dri ma drug /sgyu dang g.yo dang rgyags pa dang / /de bzhin 'tshig dang khon 'dzin dang / /rnam 'tshe'o zhes bshad pa lta bu'o/ /gsal ba'i bsam pa ni nyon mongs
<p>124b.4</p>pa'i mun pa sel ba'i phyir ro/ /sbyor ba phun sum tshogs pa ni/ /khur kun bzod ba zhes rkang pa phyed dang gsum mo/ /de la khur bzod pa ni gzhan gyi don byed pa na skyo ba med pa'o/ /de skad du yang / dper na rab dul stobs ldan glang po che/ /khal rnams khyer kyang skyo bar 'gyur ba med/ /de
<p>124b.5</p>bzhin byang chub sems dpa' rab dul ba/ /sems can khur gyis skyo bar 'gyur ba med/ /ces pa dang / yang / sems can khur chen mgo la khyer ba yi/ /sems pa mchog ni dal gyis 'gro mi mdzes/ /bdag gzhan 'ching ba sna tshogs rab bcings pas/ /brtson pa brgya 'gyur
<p>124b.6</p>gyis ni bya bar rigs/ /zhes bshad pa lta bu'o/ /skye bo kun gyis dge 'dun la legs par sgrub pa thams cad do/ /nye bar spyad bya ni mtho ris dang thar pa'o/ /de gnas pa ni de thob pa'i rten byed pa'o/ /'o na dge 'dun ni 'gro ba gzhan gyi rten can yang ma yin nam/ mi'i gzugs can
<p>124b.7</p>kho nar brjod pa ji lta bu zhe na/ phal che ba'i phyir ro/ /de ltar mchod par brjod nas/ gdams ngag brjod pa'i dam pa'i chos mi 'dzin pa'i nyes pa ni/ gang dag ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /bstan pa 'dir mi 'jug pa gang dag skye ba ni mngal la sogs pa nas 'byung ba'o/ /
<p>125a</p>
<p>125a.1</p>rga ba ni na tshod gyur pa'o/ /shi ba ni srog gyur pa'o/ /bdud rtsi ni dam pa'i chos so/ /de thos pas thob par mi phyed/ bsam pas mi spyod/ sgom pas 'dzin par mi byed pa'o/ /yang na bslab pa gsum dang rim pa bzhin no/ /yang na theg pa gsum dang
<p>125a.2</p>ngo / /de la nyes pa ci yod ce na/ /de dag nyes mang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /bzung nas btang ba'i nyes pa ni/ /'gro ba kun gyi zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /mig ni chos te/ lam dang lam ma yin pa mthong bar byed pa'i phyir ro/ /dri ma med pa'i lung ni dri ma med pa'i
<p>125a.3</p>rjod byed yin la/ rtogs pa ni de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/ /sa gsum ni khams gsum mo/ /bzung nas ma btang ba'i phan yon ni/ byang chub ces rkang pa bzhi'o/ /bslab pa'i gzhi bcas pa ni sgrub pa dang spang bar khas blangs pa rnams so/ /rkang tshugs rton pa ni khas
<p>125a.4</p>blangs pa rnams mi nyams par byed pa'o/ /go 'phang chen po ni mtho ris so/ /go 'phong mtho ba ni thar pa'o/ /sa gnyug mar ltung ba ni mi khom par skye ba'o/ /tshul khrims ni srid pa'i rgya mtsho las rgal ba'i rten byed pa'i gzings su gyur pa'o/ /lag tu 'ong ba ni de thob pa'o/ /
<p>125a.5</p>spong ba ni de stong pa'am nyams par byed pa'o/ /sbong mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ 'phags pa'i zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /g.yang sa ni ngan 'gror 'gro ba ste/ bde 'gro nas thur du ltung ba'i phyir ro/ /de skad du yang / 'di 'og stong phrag nyi shu na/ mnar med pa'o/ /de tsam zhes pa
<p>125a.6</p>pa dang / yang dpag tshad stong du ltung ba yis/ /yun rings g.yang sa smos ci dgos/ /zhes bshad pa lta bu'o/ /ldang bar brtson pa ni g.yang sa dang mun pa nas thar par 'dod pa'o/ /tshul khrims la sogs pa'i yon tan rgyun mi 'chad par smyug ma'am/ nar mar bstan par bya ba'i
<p>125a.7</p>'dren pa ste/ dpyang thag gam zhags pa lta bu'o/ /bar ma dor 'dor ba ni de spong ba'o/ /dor mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ de dag ces rkang pa gcig go/ /lam ji ltar bsgrub pa'i thabs ston pa na tshul bzhin yid la byed pa ni/ gang dag ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /thar
<p>125b</p>
<p>125b.1</p>pa chol ba gang dag gcig pur gnas sam/ 'ang gi sgras mang po'i tshogs na gnas kyang rung / yid kyis rab brtags ni 'di snyam du bdag gi sgo gsum las gsum po gang la 'jug snyam du dpyod pa'o/ /de ltar dpyad pas sgo gsum dge ba la 'jug na de la sbyor zhing gnyis la 'jug na de dag las
<p>125b.2</p>bzlog par bya'o zhes ston pa ni yang dag las dang zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /yang dag pa'i las ni dge ba'o/ /lhan cig ni yul dang dus kun du'o/ /mnyam par 'grogs pa ni de lus dang srog gi phyir yang mi 'dor ba'o/ /yang na de la 'jug par slob pa'o/ /des phan yon ci
<p>125b.3</p>thob ce na/ /sa steng zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /sa steng dkyil na ste mi rnams kyi dbus na'o/ /gtso bor gyur pa ni dge ba sgrub pa'o/ /dam pa ni mi dge ba spong ba'o/ /yang na tshul khrims ni ma thob pa thob par byed pa dang / /thob pa mi nyams par byed pa ste tshig gnyis dang rim
<p>125b.4</p>pa bzhin no/ /slob ma mchog ni de len pa'o/ /bla ma ni de sbyin pa'o/ /bkur ba nyid du 'gyur te/ des de la sgrub pa'i mchod pa phul ba'i phyir ro/ /ngo tsha shes pa ni ngo tsha zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dper na ma ni bu'i lus skyed pa dang / rigs btsun pa dang / bu la
<p>125b.5</p>g.yo mi byed pa dang / bu la byams pa dang / bu'i rjes su 'brang ba dang / bu la bden par smra ba dang / bu la gzhung lugs che ba dang / bu skyong ba la dga' ba dang / bran mo la sogs pa zil gyis gnon pa'i gzi brjid che ba dang / rang gi srog gtong gi bu mi gtong ba ste/ chos bcu
<p>125b.6</p>dang ldan pa bzhin du ngo tsha shes pa yang ngo / /ngo tsha shes pa rnams ni rang gi srog bde blag tu gtong bar byed kyi dam bcas pa'i bslab pa rnams mi gtong ba yin te/ mdo las dge tshul pha la bu mos gsol ba btab pa na tshul khrims kyi don du rang gi srog dor ba'i gtam rgya cher gsungs
<p>125b.7</p>ba lta bu'o/ /khrel yod pa ni re zhig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dam bca' ba btang mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ re zhig skye bo kun gyi dpyas dang zhes smos te/ mdza' ba dang mi mdza' ba dang bar ma thams cad kyis nyes pa sgrogs pa'am/ sdig pa'i 'gro ba ni ngan
<p>126a</p>
<p>126a.1</p>song rnams te de dag ni mi dge ba las skyes pa'i phyir ro/ /rang bzhin rnal ma bor ba ni sngon gyi grol so dang chos dang zang zing gi longs spyod las nyams pa'o/ /mkhas la sa steng ni tshul khrims nyams pa de kho na sdug bsngal che'o/ /de las ma gtogs pa'i
<p>126a.2</p>sdug bsngal gzhan ci yod/ lam mi sgrub pa'i nyes pa ston pa'i sred pas slu bar 'gyur ba ni/ gang zhig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /chos kyi lam ni theg pa gsum ste/ rigs can gsum gyis bgrod par bya ba'i phyir ro/ /rgya chen po ni phan yon shin tu rgya che pa'o/ /
<p>126a.3</p>yang na theg pa chen po'o/ /dor mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /gar mkhan gyi lus kyi byed pa mi rtag pa dang 'dra bar ro/ /dga' ba ni rjes su chags pa'o/ bslus pa ni mtho ris dang thar pa las nyams pa'o/ /'khor bar 'khyams
<p>126a.4</p>par 'gyur ba ste/ gang zhig 'khor ba'i zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rtag tu 'gyur ba ni 'gro ba gcig nas gcig tu 'pho ba'o/ /bsti ba tsam ni 'dod pa'i yul lnga thob pa'o/ /mnyam pa ni lha dang mi rnams so/ /mi mnyam pa ni ngan 'gro rnams so/ /'khyams mod
<p>126a.5</p>nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ sdug bsngal gyis gzir bar 'gyur zhes ston pa na/ thog mar mi'i dbang du byas nas mngal gyi sdug bsngal ni/ shin tu mi bzod ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /skye ba'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i shin tu dog pa ni/ de ni zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /
<p>126a.6</p>srog mi spang ba ni/ 'on kyang zhes pa rkang pa gnyis so/ /mi gtsang bas gzir ba ni mi gtsang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /lus dang sems nyams par 'gyur ba ni gnod pa zhes pa rkang pa gnyis so/ /sngon gyi dran pa spong ba ni mngal gyi sdug bsngal rnams brjed pa'o/ /byis pa'i sdug
<p>126a.7</p>bsngal ni lus zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /nye bar spyod pa kun la mi 'bongs pa ni des sgo gsum gyi las yongs su rdzogs par mi nus pa'o/ /dar la bab pa'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i sbyor ba nyams pa ni dar la bab ces rkang pa gnyis so/ /sbrul gdug ni 'dod chags la sogs
<p>126b</p>
<p>126b.1</p>pa'o/ /gnas gyur ni rten byed pa'o/ /mu ni mtha' ste 'dod pa lnga'o/ /bag rkyong ba ni ngo tsha ba dang 'jigs pa med par ro/ /spyod mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ bsam pa nyams pa ni/ bsam brlag ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dge ba'i bsam pa brlag pa de ni
<p>126b.2</p>dar la bab pa de nas kyang rgan por lhung ngo / /mi gtsigs spyod pa mi 'dor ba ni sgo gsum zhi bar spyod pa'o/ /de mi 'dor ci'i phyir zhe na/ rga shi med par lta ba'i phyir zhes ston pa ni/ byis pa bdag lus zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /lam las nyams pa ni rmongs pa zhes tshigs
<p>126b.3</p>su bcad pa gcig go/ /de ltar sems pa med na nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ rmongs pa zhes smos te/ blang bya dang dor bya mi shes pa'o/ /lam bzang ni sbyin pa la sogs pa ste 'bras bu yid du 'ong ba 'byin pa'i phyir ro/ /lam min ni mi dge ba srog gcod pa la sogs pa ste 'bras bu
<p>126b.4</p>yid du mi 'ong ba 'byin pa'i phyir ro/ /bab dgu ni rtswa shing la sogs pa glang po'i lam du bab pa thams cad phye mar rlog cing 'gro ba bzhin du mtho ris dang thar pa phye mar rlog cing ngan song 'khor bar 'gro ba'o/ /rga ba'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i dga' bas lus dbang sgyur ba ni/ de nas de ni
<p>126b.5</p>zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dar la bab pa ni de nas mi gtsigs pa de ni'o/ /dge ba'i chos 'grib par 'gyur ba ni/ 'on kyang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /mi dge ba 'phel bar 'gyur ba ni/ rmongs pa zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /rang gi phun sum tshogs pa nyams par 'gyur ba ston
<p>126b.6</p>pa na skra nyams pa ni de nas de ni zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dgod pa bzhin du zhes pa ni skye bo rnams dgod pa'i tshe so dkar po snang ba bzhin du rgas pas skra dkar po snang ba'o/ /lus dang bsam pa nyams pa ni de nas de'i lhu tshigs zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /blo bslad
<p>126b.7</p>pa ni sems 'khrugs shing dran pa nyams pa'o/ /'gro ba nyams pa ni yul gzhan du 'gro ba na 'khar ba 'am bzhon pa med na 'gro mi nus pa'o/ /de skad du yang / kha lo sgyur ba mi rid nyam chung zhing / /sha khrag bskams shing rgyus lpags nyi tshes dkris/ /mgo dkar so rgal lus ni
<p>127a</p>
<p>127a.1</p>rab skem la/ /'khar bar brten cing mi bde khyogs 'gro su/ /zhes gsungs so/ /dengs pa ni mdangs yal ba'o/ /shig shig po ni tshigs rnams 'khrul pa'o/ /dbang po nyams pa ni dbang po zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /'dod pa bsten pa nyams pa ni/ 
<p>127a.2</p>yul la zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /'jigs pa skyed pa ni/ gnas skabs zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /rga ba'i gnas skabs gang du dar la bab pa 'di 'gro bar 'gyur ba'o/ /'chi ba'i sdug bsngal ston pa ni 'gyod pa'i sdug bsngal ba ni/ bdag gis zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig
<p>127a.3</p>go/ /'di ma byas ba ni dge ba ma byas pa'o/ /de la byas pa ni sdig pa de spyad pa'o/ /'gro ba nyams pa ni bde 'gro nas ltung ba'o/ /'phrigs par ma gyur pa ni de ltar ma shes pa'o/ /mya ngan gyis sdug bsngal ba ni mya ngan zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rdo rje bsnun pas lus
<p>127a.4</p>la gnod pa de lta bur mya ngan skye bas sems la gnod pa'o/ /gnad gcod pas sdug bsngal ba ni/ gnad kyi gshis su zhes pa'i tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /zas dang gos la sogs pas bde ba lhur byas nas bkres skom dang tsha grang la sogs pa bsrung bar byas pa'o/ /yid
<p>127a.5</p>du 'ong ba ni gces phangs su 'dzin pa'o/ /'dris pa ni thog ma med pa nas nga'i lus snyam du zhen pa'o/ /gshin rjes bzung bas sdug bsngal ba ni/ gshin rje'i zhags pas zhes tshigs su bcad pa gnyis so/ /cho nges 'debs na de nye du rnams kyis thos pas grogs byed
<p>127a.6</p>par 'gyur ro zhe na/ de yis zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /gshin rjes bzung mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ bgrod dka' zhes rkang pa bzhi'o/ /dus kyi zhags pa ni 'chi ba'i dus kyi che'o/ /de ltar mi'i sdug bsngal bstan nas/ ngan 'gro'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i yi dgas zas
<p>127a.7</p>la sgrib pa can gyi sdug bsngal ni/ mi bzad pa skom pas zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /phyi'i sgrib pa can gyi sdug bsngal ston pa'i ri bo phyin ci log tu snang ba ni/ dus rlabs zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rlung gis chu bskyod pa'i dus su rlabs chen po langs nas chu
<p>127b</p>
<p>127b.1</p>gyen du 'thor bas ri rtse bsel ba'o/ /chu bo phyin ci log tu snang ba ni/ /chu gter zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /chu gter ni rgya mtsho ste chu mi zad pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'i phyir ro/ /char sprin phyin ci log tu snang ba ni/ /'di ni zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /tsha grang phyin
<p>127b.2</p>ci log tu snang ba ni/ tsha bas nyen la zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /de ltar phyin ci log tu snang ba'i rgyu ni shin tu zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /nang gi sgrib pa can gyi sdug bsngal ni/ khab mig tsam zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de ltar yi dgas kyi sdug bsngal brjod nas/ dmyal
<p>127b.3</p>ba'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i khyis 'tshe ba ni ral pa'i zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /spu gris smas pa ni spu gri zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /khron par ltung ba ni/ rtse gsum zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /gshin rje'i kha bas thu ba ni/ /de bas das 'jigs pa'o/ /lo ma'i ral gris
<p>127b.4</p>gshags pa ni/ nyin mtshan zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de'i tshe dud mo khon bshes yin gyi de las gzhan pa'i bshes med pas de brlag par gnas so/ /bud med 'bar bas 'khyud pa ni/ bud med ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /'khrigs pa ni snga ma shi bar phyi
<p>127b.5</p>ma skye ba'o/ /lug gis 'joms pa ni ri dang zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /shal+ma li'i gnod pa'i yar 'dzegs pa'i tshe tsher mas gnod pa ni/ bse khyi zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /sbrul gyis gnod pa ni gshin rje'i zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /byas gnod pa ni/ 
<p>127b.6</p>gson por zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /mar 'bab pa'i tshe tsher mas gnod pa ni/ thur du zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /mtshon gyis gnod pa ni/ /de na zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /byas 'tshe ba ni/ de tshe zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /g.yang sar lhung ba ni/ kha cig ri bo'i
<p>127b.7</p>zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /zangs su btsos pa ni/ kha cig 'bru mar zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /sa gzhi 'bar bar ltung ba ni gzhan dag ces rkang pa gnyis so/ /'bu sbrang gis za ba ni/ kha cig 'bu sbrang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /'o na de ltar sdug bsngal chen pos
<p>128a</p>
<p>128a.1</p>bcom pa rnams 'chi 'pho bar mi 'gyur ba ci ste zhe na/ de dag gson pa'i rgyu ni/ las kyi zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /las ni mi dge ba'o/ /'tsho ba ni srog go/ /thogs pa ni des gzung ba'o/ /rang gi yan lag bskyod pa tsam yang ngo / /gson pa ni
<p>128a.2</p>bdag nyid 'chi bar smon kyang mi 'chi ba'o/ /de ltar tsha ba'i dmyal ba bstan nas/ grang ba'i dmyal ba ston pa'i chu bur can ni lhags pa zhes rkang pa phyed dang gsum mo/ /chu bur rdol ba ni/ rdol ba zhes rkang pa phyed dang gnyis so/ /so tham tham pa ni kos thag ces tshigs su
<p>128a.3</p>bcad pa gcig go/ /da ni rab tu tsha ba bye brag tu ston pa'i me'i gnod pa ni/ dmyal mes zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /dmyal ba'i srung mas 'tshe ba ni/ rus gong zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /mnar med pa'i sdug bsngal ston pa'i mdor bstan pa ni/ gnyis las phyi'i gnod
<p>128a.4</p>pa ni/ la lar zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /nang gi gnod pa ni brang gi zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /rgyas par bshad pa yang gnyis las nang gi gnod pa ni/ glo nas zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /phyi'i gnod pa ni/ sdug bsngal zhes tshigs su bcad pa gsum mo/ /de las gnas
<p>128a.5</p>khang gi gnod pa ni/ sdug bsngal zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ mda'i gnod pa ni/ mda' chen zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /dbyug pas gnod pa ni dmyal ba'i srung mas zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /khu ba 'bar ba'i gnod pa ni/ lcags zhun zhes rkang pa drug go/ /spyi'i don
<p>128a.6</p>bsdu ba ni/ skye bo zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de ltar dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal bstan nas/ dud 'gro'i sdug bsngal ston pa/ des ngal 'byor rnyed par dka' ba ni/ skye bo zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /'chal spyod pa ni mi dge ba byed pa'o/ /de nyes pa cir 'gyur
<p>128a.7</p>zhe na/ brgyal zhe na/ 'jig rten 'gro ba mtha' yas bye ba 'phyes rnams su dud 'gror skye'i/ mi'i dngos po shin tu rnyed par dka' ba nyid/ mi'i nang na yang smad par skye ba ni/ gal te zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /dud 'gro gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni/ dud 'gro zhes rkang pa
<p>128b</p>
<p>128b.1</p>byed dang gnyis so/ /de nas dmyal bar ltung ba ni/ gang gis zhes rkang pa phyed dang gnyis so/ /de ltar theg pa thun mong gi lam sgrub pa gdams nas theg pa chen po'i lam sgrub pa la gdams pa brjod pa na sgrub pa'i rten ni gang zhig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /gang zhig ni
<p>128b.2</p>dal 'byor ro/ /skye ba ni sems can rnams der bying ba dang de las brgal dka' bas rgya mtsho'o/ /byang chub mchog gi sa bon dge ba ni de skyed pa ste/ /ji skad du/ rigs kyi bu byang chub kyi sems ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi sa bon lta bu'o zhes gsungs pa lta bu'o/ /
<p>128b.3</p>dge ba ni de ma bskyed pa skyed cing mi nyams par byed pa'o/ /bsgrub par bya ba'i lam ston pa ni/ bde gshegs zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /mi ma yin pas bsgrub par mi nus pa ni/ lam de zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /mi rnams lam bsgrub pa la sbyar ba ni/ mi'i dngos po
<p>128b.4</p>zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /lam la 'jug pa'i sgo mi rtag pa yid la byed pa na skad cig gi mi rtag pa ni/ mar me zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /glo bur gyi mi rtag pa ni/ 'di ni zhes pa'i tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rgyun gyi mi rtag pa ni/ so ga zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig
<p>128b.5</p>go/ /sgrub pa'i gnas ni/ zla ba'i zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /sgrub pa'i grogs ni/ nags mthongs zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dga' ba'i nags tshal ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams la yod pa'o/ /sgrub pa'i cha rkyen chu phun sum tshogs pa ston pa ni
<p>128b.6</p>nags rlung zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /chu gtsang ni dri rnyog pa dang / srog chags med pa'o/ /dogs bde ba ni 'gram gnyis kyang ngo / /dben pa ni 'du 'dzi nyung ba'o/ /de na skyid pa gang yin pa de ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha'i bu mo'i lus lha'i spos dang sman dri zhim
<p>128b.7</p>pos byugs pa'i mgo bo'i lan bu'i rgyan du thogs pa me tog gi tshogs mdzes pa zil gyis gnon pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa lha'i chu la'ang yod par 'gyur ram/ rgyun dang ldan pa'i lha'i chu ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i mtshe'u dal gyis 'bab pa yin no/ /shing phun sum tshogs pa
<p>129a</p>
<p>129a.1</p>rtsa ba 'bras bu zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /nyams dga' ni yid du 'ong ba'o/ /bas mtha' ni grong zad pa'i mur thug pa'o/ /gcig pu ni grogs med par ro/ /dmyal sdong ni khyim gyi grong 'dab bam chung ma ste 'bras bu'i ming rgyu la
<p>129a.2</p>btags pa'i/ /bslus med gnas pa ni nges brid par mi nus pa'o/ /de dag gi don bsdus pa ni ri sul zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de la gnas kyi don bsdu ba ni ri sul zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /shing gi don bsdu ba ni/ nyer spyod ces rkang pa gcig go/ /chu'i don
<p>129a.3</p>bsdu ba ni chu ngogs zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /ri sul yangs pa ni gcong rong dang ngam grog la sogs pa med pa'o/ /nyer spyod rgya che ba ni der 'chag pa dang 'dug pa la sogs pa bag yangs su spyod pa'o/ /nyan pa ni thos pa'i tshe rna bar 'phrod pa'o/ /ji ltar snyan zhe na rnga ltar ro/ /phu
<p>129a.4</p>chu bdag cag skom pas nyon mongs shing sdug bsngal ba'i yul min te/ 'thungs na ngoms pas bde zhing skyid pa'i yul yin zhes 'gron la sgrogs pa bzhin chu sgra 'byin pa'o/ /sgrub pa'i bar chad spong ba na/ 'dod pa'i nyes pa yid la byed pa ni/ 'dod pa rnams zhes bya ba la
<p>129a.5</p>sogs pa'o/ /de la 'dod pa rnams snang la rang bzhin med pa ni/ 'dod pa rnams 'byor dang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /'dod pa'i 'bras bu yid du mi 'ong ba ni rmi lam lta bu zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /ngan spyod 'khrul pa ni mi dge ba bcu byed pa'o/ /de la chags pa ni 'dod pa
<p>129a.6</p>la sred pa'o/ /'dod pa'i bde ba yid du mi 'ong ba ni/ yul dang zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dug pas 'dod pa nyes dmigs che ba ni dug dang zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /de'i gtan tshigs ni dug ni zhes rkang pa drug go/ /de ltar 'dod pa dang yul gyi nyes pa brjod nas/ 
<p>129a.7</p>'dod byed yul can gyi nyes pa ston pa ni/ ji ltar zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rnyed pa grub pa med pa ni rtswa lo ma zos pa'o/ /de dang 'dra bar bde 'gror grub pa med par ngan 'gror ltung ba'o/ /de ltar 'dod pa spyi'i nyes pa bstan nas khyad par du lha'i 'dod pa'i
<p>129b</p>
<p>129b.1</p>nyes dmigs ston pa'i mtshe'u la chags pa'i nyes pa ni lha'i bu mo zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /'phral thabs glong ba ni rang gi phun sum tshogs pas dregs pa'o/ /ljon shing la chags pa'i nyes pa ni dga' tshal zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dpag bsam
<p>129b.2</p>gyi shing ni bzhi ste/ bza' btung dang / gos dang / rgyan dang / rol mo'i dpag bsam gyi shing ngo / /sa la chags pa'i nyes pa ni/ /rkang gzhag ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de la rkang pa gzhag nems zhes sor bzhis dma' bar 'gyur zhing bteg na par zhes
<p>129b.3</p>sor bzhis mtho bar 'gyur ba'o/ /reg na bde ba ni lus la phan 'dogs pa'o/ /khang bzangs la chags pa'i nyes pa ni/ dril bu zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /khang pa de'i steng g.yogs nas dril bu mdzes pa 'khrol zhing mu tig gi phreng ba'i tshogs 'phyang ba 'od lhag
<p>129b.4</p>ge ba'i gzhal med khang du zhugs te/ /lha yul der 'dod pa lnga bgrod nas te longs spyod byas nas kyang ngo / /pha mtha' ste thar thabs med pa'i nang du'o/ /dbang phyug la chags pa'i nyes pa ni/ gang du zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rnam par rgyal byed kyi khang
<p>129b.5</p>bzangs gang du rgyal chen ris bzhi dang / /sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha dang / klu dang / mi'am ci'i spyi bos brgya byin gyi rkang pa la gtugs nas/ de dag gi mgo bo'i rgyan gtsug gi nor bu mar gad kyi 'od kyi tshogs kyis rkang rten te gdan khri dmar por gyur pa'o/ /de yang
<p>129b.6</p>'gro ba ngan par 'gro bar 'gyur ba ni ngan song du lhung ba ste/ ji skad du/ brgya byin 'jig rten mchod 'os gyur nas ni/ /las kyi dbang gis phyir yang sa stengs ltung / /zhes bshad pa lta bu'o/ /srog la chags pa'i nyes pa ni me tog ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /
<p>129b.7</p>'tsho ba ni srog go/ /de ma 'gags bar du sems can gson por 'tsho ba'o/ /sdug bsngal ba la bde bar rlom pa'i nyes pa ni sdug bsngal zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /nga rgyal byed mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ de ni zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /'khor ba la chags
<p>130a</p>
<p>130a.1</p>pa'i nyes pa ni/ de na gshin rjes zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /log par smon pa ni srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad thob par 'dod pa'o/ /de nyid 'jig pa'i rgyu yin pas 'jig pa zhes bya'o/ /sdug bsngal ba la bde bar rlom pa'i dpe dgod pa
<p>130a.2</p>ni dmyal rnams zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dmyal ba de nyid shin ci ma rung snyam pas tho ba bsnun pas mchog tu bde ba yin par sems so/ /don de dang 'dra bar sbyar ba ni/ de bzhin zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /rtag tu ni mya ngan las 'das pa ma thob kyi bar
<p>130a.3</p>du'o/ /re zhig tsam zhig ni lha dang mir skyes pa na'o/ /ji zhig ltar bsod nams bsags pa'i dbang gis ngan 'gro'i skye shi'i 'khrul 'khor med nas skad cig ste/ bde 'gro nas ma lhung bar du ngan 'gro'i sdug bsngal gnyug mar bzod dka' me lce lta bu zhi 'gyur na/ lha dang
<p>130a.4</p>mi'i 'jig rten thams cad bde ba kham 'ga' ste/ lha dang mi'i 'dod pa lnga la yang sred par byed do/ /lam sgrub pa'i rang bzhin gnyen po sgom pa na 'khor ba sdug bsngal du yid la byed pa ni/ ji lta ji ltar 'gro ba kun na zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /stug po ni shas che
<p>130a.5</p>ba'o/ /srab mo ni shas chung ba'o/ /mi sdug par yid la bya ba ni ji lta ji ltar sdug pa zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /mched pa ni 'phel ba'o/ /zhil ba ni 'grib pa'o/ /zhar la bud med sdug par smra ba'i 'bras bu ni/ bud med ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig
<p>130a.6</p>go/ /lus ni pad+ma ltar 'jam/ byad bzhin zla ba ltar mdzes/ mig ni ut+pal ltar dkar gnag phyed ces mgo snyoms pa'o/ /snyoms mod nyes pa cir 'gyur zhe na/ snyan dngags mkhan gyi brdzun de'i zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /mi bzad pa de gang zhig ce na/ de dag ces rkang
<p>130a.7</p>pa gcig go/ /mi rtag par yid la byed pa ni sems can mi rtag pa ni/ 'gro ba zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /snod mi rtag pa ni gang gi zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /longs spyod mi rtag pa ni sdug bsngal ba dang / bde ba dang / skye gnas la longs spyod
<p>130b</p>
<p>130b.1</p>pa ste/ rim pa bzhin sngon chad ces pa rkang pa gcig dang gcig dang gnyis so/ /byams pa dang snying rje yid la byed pas nye du la byams pa sgom pa ni/ skye ba zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /grogs la byams pa sgom pa ni/ gang dag ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig
<p>130b.2</p>go/ /dus kyi rim pa ni so ga la sogs pa'o/ /mnyam pa ni rigs la sogs pas mtshungs pa dang 'grogs pa'o/ /mi mnyam pa ni mtho ba'am dma' pa dang 'grogs pa'o/ /gnyen bshes la snying rje bsgom pa ni/ nye du zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /sems can thams
<p>130b.3</p>cad nye du yin na dgra dang bar ma la nye dur ngo ma shes pa ji lta bu zhe na/ skye shis zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /ma la byams pa sgom pa ni/ byis pa zhes tshigs su bcad pa gnyis so/ /bu'i ched du las kyi mtha' sna tshogs la 'bad pas ngal ba mang po bsten kyang bu la byams pa
<p>130b.4</p>bsten pa de dag rang bzhin gyi don byed pa'i skabs 'dir bu shin tu ma rabs shig yod du zin na'ang ma de spong zhing 'dor bar su zhig spro ste spro bar mi bya'o/ /de ltar byams pa dang snying rje sgom pa'i thabs bstan nas/ goms pa'i phan yon ston pa'i snying rje'i phan yon ni/ 'gro
<p>130b.5</p>ba sdug bsngal zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /sdug bsngal mi bzad pa mang po ni sdug bsngal chen po gsum mam/ brgyad dam/ brgya rtsa bcu la sogs pa'o/ /dbang med pa ni mi 'dod bzhin du 'byung ba'o/ /skyabs med pa ni sdug bsngal sel ba'i grogs
<p>130b.6</p>med pa'o/ /gzhan sdug bsngal ba'i don du bdag gi sdug bsngal bzod pa gang yin pa de bde ba'i rgyu la gnas pas bde zhes skyes mchog gsung ngo / /tha na skad cig tsam yang gzhan la bza' btung byin pas des bkres skom dang bral ba dang / gos byin pas tsha
<p>130b.7</p>grang dang bral bas de mgu zhing rangs par byas pa des bdag dga' ba gang yin pa de dang 'dra bar snying rje goms pa 'di na gang zhig yod de med do/ /byams pa'i phan yon ni gzhan phan zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /gzhan la mya ngan las 'das pa'i phan yon
<p>131a</p>
<p>131a.1</p>dang / lha mi'i bde ba bskyed par brtson pas bdag dga' ba rnyed pa gang yin pa de ni ste/de dang mnyam pa yul lnga'i bde ba'i longs spyod lhur len pa rnams kyis ji ltar thob ces 'og ma dang sbyar ro/ /de ltar phan yon bstan nas/ spyod pa
<p>131a.2</p>ston pa'i byams pa'i spyod pa gzhan bde ba sgrub pa la brtson pa ni shin tu rnyed sla zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /byam pa'i spyod pa byed pa 'di kho na'o/ /'phags pa ni rang gi don lhur len pa rnams pas de mchog tu gyur pa'o/ /gzhan bde ba sgrub pa la gzhol ba ni/ 
<p>131a.3</p>nyi ma rlabs chen zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de 'dra zhes bya ba ni nyi ma dngas dang mtshungs pa'o/ /gcig tu gzhol ba ni rang don dang 'dren mas ma yin pa'o/ /yang na gcig pu gzhol te grogs la mi ltos par ro/ /snying rje'i spyod pa ston pa'i gzhan gyi sdug bsngal
<p>131a.4</p>sel ba la brtson pa ni/ 'jig rten zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /gzhan gyi sdug bsngal sel bar dga' ba ni/ gzhan gyi don du tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /gzhan gyi sdug bsngal sel ba na bde ba ni/ gzhan la phan par zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig
<p>131a.5</p>go/ /rang smin nas gzhan smin par byed pa ni/ rgal bar 'gyur zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de ltar byams pa dang snying rje yid la byed pa bshad nas/ bslab pa gsum brtan par byed pa 'chad pa ni de ltar zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o/ /tshul khrims bsngags pa ni/ 
<p>131a.6</p>de ltar zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /rwa dang / ba so la sogs pa'i rgyan pas gser dang / dngul la sogs pa'i rin po che'i rgyan mchog tu gyur pa ltar legs spyad de/ tshul khrims ni rgyan gyi mchog go/ /de skad du yang / tshul khrims ldan pa rgyan rnams kun gyi mchog/ /
<p>131a.7</p>ces gsungs so/ /shes rab bsngags pa ni/ gsal ba'i zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /nor bu dang mar me la sogs pa'i gsal ba'i nang na nyi zla'i gsal ba mchog yin pa ltar shes rab ni shes bya gsal bar byed pas mchog go/ /de la phan yon ci yod ce na/ zhi ba
<p>131b</p>
<p>131b.1</p>bdud rtsi yangs zhes smos te/ mya ngan las 'das pa chen po 'thob ces bya ba'i tha tshig go/ /de skad du yang / thub pa khyed kyi ye shes kyis/ /snang bas mi shes rab rib dag /'joms pa'i tha na nyi ma yang / /me khyer tsam yang mi po da do/ /zhes bshad do/ /ting 'dzin
<p>131b.2</p>bsngags pa ni/ dga' ba'i zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /mi rnams kyi dga' ba'i nang na 'khor los sgyur ba'i dga' ba mchog yin pa ltar/ /ting nge 'dzin ni shin tu sbyangs pa'i dga' ba dang ldan pas mchog go/ /'o na de sus rnyed par 'gyur zhe na/ byas pa gzo ba rnams kyis rnyed par sla'i/ byas pa mi gzo bas rnyed
<p>131b.3</p>par dka' ba'o/ /de gsum gyis 'bras bu mya ngan las 'das pa'i bsngags pa ni/ bkra shis zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /gza' dang rgyu skar dang tshes grangs bzang po la sogs pa bkra shis pa rnams kyi nang na gang gis 'dod pa'i don grub
<p>131b.4</p>pa'i bkra shis mchog yin pa ltar zhi ba ste mya ngan las 'das pa ni sdug bsngal dang / nyon mongs pa dang bral bas mchog go/ /'on te sdug bsngal dang bral ba tsam yin gyi bde ba ma yin nam zhe na/ bde rgyun sten zhes smos te bde ba'i rgyun mi 'chad pas so/ /de ltar rtogs
<p>131b.5</p>pa'i chos bsngags nas/ lung gi chos bsngags pa ni/ bde bar gshegs pa'i zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /de la brten na phan yon ci yod ce na/ ljon shing zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /'bras bu rgya chen ni mtho ris dang thar pa'o/ /'o na gsung gi don nam tshig
<p>131b.6</p>gang bsten zhe na/ bde gshegs zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /sbrang ma me tog bzhag nas sbrang rtsi len pa ltar ro/ /de ltar gdams ngag rgyas par brjod nas/ mdor bsdus te bshad pa'i 'gro ba spyil gdams pa ni/ skad cig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /skad
<p>131b.7</p>cig la lus 'jig longs spyod zad cing rtag tu ste/ gnyen po skyes kyi bar du sems g.yeng zhing 'khrugs par byed pa'i yul lnga po rnams spongs/ zhi ba'i bde 'bras thob par byed cing 'ching ba'i 'tshe ba med par byed pa gcig pu grogs la mi ltos par dben pa ste 'du
<p>132a</p>
<p>132a.1</p>'dzi med pa bsten/ bdag dang gzhan 'khor ba las rnam par thar pa mya ngan las 'das pa'i sgo mo dbye ba'i gegs bstan pa lta bu'i gti mug ste rmongs pa dang / 'khrugs pa ste ldongs pa dang / rab rib ste chags pa sol te spongs/ spyir rta rnams rang bzhin gyis gnyid
<p>132a.2</p>che yang rta'i mchog cang shes ni rte'u ste phru gu nas bag zon che bas shin tu yun ring por gnyid log par 'gyur ba ma yin te/ cung zad gnyid log nas rtswa chu la spyod do/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi slob ma rnams kyang 'dod pa la yun ring por sten par mi byed de/ cung zad bsten kyang des skyo
<p>132a.3</p>bar byas nas dge ba spyod do/ /de ltar skye dgu spyi la gdams nas slob ma la bye brag tu 'doms pa ni shing chen po lta bur chos dgu dang ldan par gyis shig ces brjod pa ni/ khyod gcig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dper na shing chen po sdong po lta bu ni brtan pa'o/ /gel pa lta bu
<p>132a.4</p>bzod pa'o/ /dul ba ni lo ma lta bu'o/ /zhi gnas ni me tog lta bu'o/ /shes rab ni yal ga lta bu'o/ /rgyu rab tu smin pa ni lo bran myu gu lta bu'o/ /smon lam ni rtse mo lta bu'o/ /tshul khrims ni grib ma lta bu'o/ /rab zhi ste mya ngan las 'das pa ni 'bras bu lta bu'o/ /mtsho chen lta bur
<p>132a.5</p>chos bcu gcig dang ldan par gyis shig ces brjod pa ni/ khyod gcig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dper na mtsho chen po yangs pa ltar shes rab rgya che ba dang / gsal ba ltar shes bya gsal ba dang / byin gyis gzhol ba ltar dge ba la gzhol ba dang / gting
<p>132a.6</p>zab pa ltar chos zab mo rtogs pa dang / rab tu dang ba ltar dang ba'i dad pa dang ldan pa dang / rtag tu bsil ba ltar nyon mongs pa'i gdung ba las bsil ba dang /sbrul gdug pa'i rnyi yis bag zhad med pa ltar dug gsum med pa dang / me'i 'jigs pa spangs pa ltar ngan 'gro'i
<p>132a.7</p>'jigs pa spangs pa dang / rang bzhin gyis rab tu gtsang ba ltar tshul khrims kyi sa gtsang ba dang / skom pa gcod pa ltar sred pa gcod pa dang / gru gzings 'degs pa'i khur bzod pa ltar gzhan don byed pa'i khur bzod pa'o/ /char sprin chen po lta bur chos drug dang ldan par gyis
<p>132b</p>
<p>132b.1</p>shig ces brjod pa ni/ khyod gcig ces tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dper na char sprin chen po des me tog la sogs pa la phan 'dogs pa ltar skye bo mang po sdig pa las bzlog ste/ dge ba la bkod nas phan 'dogs pa dang / 'brug gi sgra sgrogs pa ltar 'khor ba'i
<p>132b.2</p>sdug bsngal gyis mi 'jigs pa dam pa'i chos smra ba'i sgra chen sgrogs pa dang / char chen po 'bab pa ltar grags pa rgya chen pos khyab pa dang / char de rlung gi shugs drag pos bskyod pa ltar sems snying rje'i rlung gis bskyod pa dang / sa'i rdul ldang ba zhi ba ltar nyon mongs pa'i
<p>132b.3</p>rdul rab tu zhi bar byed pa dang / grib mas sa stengs brgyan pa ltar tshul khrims kyis sgo gsum brgyan pa'o/ /de ltar gdams ngag brjod nas/ de las byung ba'i dge ba bsngo ba'i legs pa grub par bsngo ba ni/ bdag gis zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /bde gshegs
<p>132b.4</p>spyod pa ni dang po sems bskyed pa nas tha ma mya ngan las 'das pa'i bar ro/ /rtag tu bde ba ni ji srid 'tsho'i bar du nad med pa'o/ /longs spyod bzang po ni log par 'tsho ba med pa'o/ /yid la re ba 'byor pa ni 'dod pa'i don thams cad grub pa'o/ /gzhan la phan par dga' ba ni/ 
<p>132b.5</p>sems can thams cad sdug bsngal las bsgral nas bde ba la 'god par spro ba'o/ /kun mkhyen ni shes bya thams cad thugs su chud pa'o/ /bgrod par shog ces pa ni de thob par smon pa'o/ /nyes pa zhi bar bsngo ba ni dmyal ba zhes tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /dmyal
<p>132b.6</p>ba'i ngam grog dang g.yang sa lag mthil ltar mnyam mun nag rnam bsal lus la me 'bar ba rab tu zhi ba dang / ro myags btsog pa'i 'dam rdzab bskams nas der 'khrungs shing skyes pa'i pad+ma'i lo mas khebs shing rtsa ba'i khye'u so thon pa dang / ro myags kyi 'dam de
<p>132b.7</p>gtsang zhing dri zhim gyur nas/ phyogs der pad+ma kha bye bas sa rnams rnam par brgyan pa dang / dmyal ba rnams bde ba rgyas shing bsam pa bzang la rlung ser bu'i ngad bcas char zim 'bab pas tsha ba'i gdung ba zhi bar shog /ston pa 'byung bar bsngo ba ni/ bdud dpung zhes
<p>133a</p>
<p>133a.1</p>tshigs su bcad pa gcig go/ /sgrogs pa ni dam pa'i chos ston pa'o/ /lha'i chu ni mtshe'u dal gyis 'bab pa'i/ /rtse mo ni der lha dang lha mo rnams rtse bas nang phan tshun dga' ba byed pa bas kyang gdul bya rnams dga' bar mdzad pa'o/ /gdul bya de dag kyang
<p>133a.2</p>gang zhe na/ lha dang mi 'dul ba zhes smos so/ /gang gi phyir gdul zhe na/ skye shi zhes rkang pa phyed do/ /gang gis 'dul zhe na/ sangs rgyas dag ces rkang pa phyed dang gnyis so/ /brnag pa bzhin du zhes bya ba ni gdul bya rnams gang la mos pa'i skur ro/ /nam zhar zhes bya ba ni rtag
<p>133a.3</p>tu'o/ /bstan pa rgyas par bsngo ba ni/ 'gro ba zhes rkang pa gcig go/ /de'i 'gal rkyen med par bsngo ba ni/ /'chi bdag ces rkang pa gcig go/ /mthun rkyen tshogs par bsngo ba ni 'phags pa'i zhes rkang pa gnyis so/ /'phags pa'i skye bo ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems
<p>133a.4</p>dpa' dang / nyan thos rnams so/ /'o na rang sangs rgyas 'phags pa'i skye bo ma yin nam zhe na/ yin mod kyi/ de ni lus kyis chos ston gyi ngag gis mi ston pas gtam tshogs med do/ /gtam tshogs ni theg pa gsum mo/ /spel ba ni gong nas gong du rgyas pa'o/ /de la phan yon
<p>133a.5</p>ci yod ce na/ zhi ba'i bdud rtsi zhes bya'o/ /zhi ba'i bdud rtsi'i char gyis bsil bas don byas shog /zhi ba'i bdud rtsi'i zla ba'i snang ba rab bzang don byas shog /ces tshig rnam par sbyar ro/ /bdag gis slob ma'i spring yig 'di/ /rtogs shing cung zad bshad pa las/ /dge ba dri med
<p>133a.6</p>gang thob des/ /'gro kun rnam par grol bar shog /slob ma la spring ba'i 'grel pa/ /slob dpon mkhas pa chen po shes rab 'byung gnas blo gros kyis rang gi slob ma rnams la phan pa'i don du mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po bi nA ya tsan dra dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong
<p>133a.7</p>chos kyi shes rab kyis sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o//[ ]@/ /lho za mo tshangs dbyangs la sdug bsngal gyi bye brag bstan pa bzhugs so// @##/ /slom ma lho za tshangs ba'i dbyangs zhes bya ba zhig gis me tog gtor/ gung skyems drangs
<p>133b</p>
<p>133b.1</p>gus pa bgyis nas/ rje lha gcig lags 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal gyi mtshan nyid 'di kho na yong ji lta bu lags/ bka' stsal par zhu zhes gsol bas/ slob dpon gyis cung zad tsam zhig btud de dgongs nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to/ /thog ma med pa'i
<p>133b.2</p>dus ni bgrangs pa nas/ /rang sems 'khrul ba'i lus la chags pa yis/ /skye gnas mang po brgyud cing skye shi mang po myong / /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal 'di la bzod pa'i glags med do/ /dmyal ba yi dgas byol song sdug bsngal mi bzad pa/ /gsum dang brgyad kyi sdug
<p>133b.3</p>bsngal 'dam rdzab yin/ /skol cag kun kyang 'dam rdzab 'di la gnas/ /regs par ldan pa'i skyes bu'i shes rab kyis/ /bka' dang bstan nas nan tan bstan pa 'di/ /mi khom gnas brgyad skyes tshe ma nyan dbang med/ /khom ldan mi lus thob pa gsan du gsol/ /
<p>133b.4</p>bskal par bsags pa'i bsod nams rgya mtsho yis/ /rab tu dkon pa'i khom ldan mi lus thob/ /lho yi 'dzam bu'i gling du skye ba dkon/ /shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa'i chos bslab 'tshal/ /phung po 'di ni sems dang gnang gzhes 'bral/ /sdig dang bsngos nas ci bsnyod
<p>133b.5</p>ci bskon yang / /ro stod ro smad chags pa'i gzugs phung 'di/ /sdug bsngal rtsa gzhi chen por shes par gyis/ /de yi phyir na gzugs la ma chags shing / /rnam shes ma rig mun la chags pa ni/ /shes rab me ltar 'bar ba'i sgron ma yis/ /ma rig mun rum gting nas
<p>133b.6</p>thar bar 'gyur/ /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dbang po ches/ /btsog pa'i mngal gnas sdug bsngal sna tshogs myong / /ma yi drag dal tsha grang 'grangs bkres kyis/ /'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal der che phyis mi smos/ /'byung ba'i dus na sog mig drangs pa snyam/ /
<p>133b.7</p>dbugs chad brgyal nas ngan song sgo ru byung / /byung bas tsher ma'i nang du bsgyur ba snyam/ /blangs pas bye'u chung khri yis khyer ba snyam/ /ba spu'i gu gar lhags pa'i mda' re byung / /nyams su tshor ba'i sdug bsngal sna tshogs myong / /skye ba'i sdug bsngal 'di la bzod pa'i
<p>134a</p>
<p>134a.1</p>glags med do/ /phung po 'di la rgas pa yongs kyis 'ong / /mgo la skra med kha nas so yang med/ /mig kyang mi mthong rna ba'ang mi thos la/ /rtag tu nad pa ji bzhin mal na nyal/ /ldang yang mi nus sgur ram gog ci 'gro/ /zas 'dod skom 'dod kun gyis 'bod cing
<p>134a.2</p>slong / /rgas pas nyam thag gzugs kyi phung po de/ /me long grib ma mthong na 'dre bas 'jigs/ /gnod pa ma byas mi byed byed mi 'gyur/ /khyim mtshes byis pa kun kyang shi na dga'/ /rgyas pa'i sdug bsngal 'di la bzod pa'i glags med do/ /phung po 'di la na ba yongs kyis 'ong / /
<p>134a.3</p>ci na yang mi bzod pa'i glags med de/ /shi ru dogs nas sdug bsngal nyam thag pas/ /sha la mes sreg gtar ka dbug dral byed/ /snum gyi rang bzhin kha la btung dka' yang / /shi dogs phan re dbang med brnag cing 'thung / /blo log mi yis bsgyur kyang slongs te/ /nad
<p>134a.4</p>gram sems rten snying la kun 'dus nas/ /gnad gcod na ba'i sdug bsngal bzod pa'i glags med/ /phung po 'di la shi ba yongs kyis 'ong / /phyogs bzhi'i ngos nas ri rdib ji bzhin du/ /de la zhur med de la gsol du med/ /dang po 'chi ba'i nad de bzod glags med/ /
<p>134a.5</p>tshig kyang 'chol nas mig kyang khur bur bros/ /re gdung bred do 'o byas snying gtugs nas/ /dus shing gdungs nas sme sngags mang po bton/ /'jus shing 'phyangs kyang phan pa ci yang med/ /gshes ma 'chi bdag srog gcod snying bcu pa'i/ sdug bsngal nang na shi ba mi phod de/ /shi
<p>134a.6</p>las thar pa'i sems can gcig kyang med/ /med pa btsal gyis mi rnyed sdug bsngal ni/ /yul dang gnas spangs gnyen por phyogs bzir brgyugs/ /sgyu dang zol gyis bslus nas 'dod pa btsal/ /lam gyis dub dang bkres skom sdug bsngal khyad bsad nas/ /sha rus bye ba
<p>134a.7</p>tsam du nyon mongs than bskol te/ /khyim du nam phyin snyam pa'i yid kyis gdung bas myos/ /gal te rnyed pa grub nas khyim du phyin na yang / /'di bas lhag btsal snyan nas yang ni tshol khro'i lam du zhugs/ /btsal ba grub pa dgra dang phrad de kun phyogs sgron mor btang / /rang
<p>134b</p>
<p>134b.1</p>yang ma bsad brdegs nas btang ba 'on kyang rigs pa che/ /khyim du phyin nas bu smad dang phrad na yang ngo 'dzum gnag/ /chom rkun la sgugs byed pa'ang sdug bsngal lhag par che/ /tshong ba sgyu zol bre srang sgyur zhing slu byed dang / /ma byin len dang 'phrog rlom byed dang 'jab bu dang / /mthus
<p>134b.2</p>'phrog khrel dang bral ba ci dgos yi dgas skye/ /med pa btsal ba 'di yang bzod pa'i glags med do/ /yod pa btsal bas mi thub sdug bsngal chen po ni/ /bdag shi gzhan gyi dbang du gyur gyis dogs pa'i sdug bsngal dang / /bu tsha gnyen bshes shi ru ngogs pa'i sdug
<p>134b.3</p>bsngal dang / /ci nas pha rol mthos kyis dogs pa'i sdug bsngal dang / /nor phyugs shor gyis dogs pa'i sdug bsngal dang / /nye drung shi nas phrad 'dod mi phrad 'di yang sdug bsngal glags med do/ /sdang ba'i dgra dang phrad kyis dogs pa'i sdug bsngal ni/ /be rga mtshon gyis
<p>134b.4</p>mgo lus med par brdegs/ /ci yod phrogs nas ral gri rno rtul sad/ /snying rje ye med dgra dang phrad pa yi/ /sdug bsngal 'di yang bzod pa'i glags med do/ /byams sdug gnyen dang bral gyis dogs pa'i sdug bsngal ni/ /pha ma bu tsha gnyen bshes phangs pa rnams/ /dbang
<p>134b.5</p>med las kyis shi nas bral ba'i tshe/ /dus skabs med par mi bskyud sems la dran/ /gdung sems mya ngan 'di ltar bskyud mtha' med/ /phung po zhig pa tsam du mya ngan cher byas te/ /yod dam snyam nas brtags na gal yod de med/ /sra chas dam du bcings nas sa 'og
<p>134b.6</p>sbas pa ste/ /rul myags bskams nas thal ba'ang dengs pa la/ /brgya bos stong bos rnams ni mi thos na/ /dko byams sdug gnyen dang bdag tu phrad par ga la 'gyur/ /byams sdug gnyen dang bral du dogs pa'i sdug bsngal 'di la'ang bzod pa'i glags med do/ /
<p>134b.7</p>sdug bsngal 'di brgyad lon pa'i phung po yin/ /lnga phung 'grub par byed pa'i rtsa ba dug lnga yin/ /dug lnga rang dgar spyod pa'i sems can ni/ /sems can lus ni sna tshogs tshang bar blangs/ /de yi nang nas gzugs rab 'phags pa'i rgyu/ /mi lus rin chen bzang sdug mdzes
<p>135a</p>
<p>135a.1</p>thob ldan/ /btsan phyug ba de skyid thob pa'i skyes bu yang / /mi tshe 'di la dge ba ma spyad na/ /dmyal ba yi dgas ngan song gnas su lhung / /rang la rang sdang rang sdug btson rang chud/ /sdug bsngal sde brgyad nang na rtag tu 'khor zhing 'khyam/ /'phags
<p>135a.2</p>pa nyan thos yon tan smon pa yis/ /phung po sdug bsngal dgrar mthong skyon rnams spong / /bsrung ba'i tshul khrims dag cing gtsang bar gyis/ /gsung rab rgya mtsho zhal thon par ma bcad/ /sdig pa byang bar 'dod na rtag tu mthol bshags gyis/ /dgra bcom mos pas spyod
<p>135a.3</p>pa grub pa dang / /bden gnyis don rtogs theg pa chen po yi/ /chos dang gang zag bdag med rtogs par gyis/ /mkhyen bzhi sku gsum grub la phyag 'tshol mchod/ /sdug bsngal brgyad spangs bde la rtag gnas 'gyur/ /slob dpon ka ma la shI las
<p>135a.4</p>lho za mo tshangs pa'i dbyangs la sdug bsngal brgyad kyi bre brag bstan pa rdzogs so//[ ]#/ /rje 'bangs dang bod btsun rnams la spring yig bzhugs so// @##/ /'phags pa 'jam dpal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bod kyi spu rgyal mgo nag yongs kyi rje/ /
<p>135a.5</p>khri srong lde'u btsan ag tshom mes kyi sras/ /rlung nam 'phrul gyi rgyal po'i dbon po yi/ /srong btsan sgam po spyan ras gzigs kyi sku/ /byang chub sems dpa'i sku rgyud gdung ma chad/ /'gro drug nang na shes rig che ba'i mi/ /dug lnga sdong po rgyud drug kun gyi gzhi/ /khri rje thog btsan
<p>135a.6</p>man chad brgyud ma yi/ /dge bcu thang khrims btsugs nas dul bar mdzad/ /rigs kyi sprul pa khri srong lde'u btsan gyis/ /'gro ba'i mun pa'i skar khung dbye slad du/ /rgya gar yul gyi rdo rje gdan stengs su/ /sde snod gsum po shAkya thub pas gsungs/ /kun dga' bo la
<p>135a.7</p>sogs pa'i 'khor rnams smin/ /'dzam bu'i gling gi snying po'i dbus su gyur/ /bsod nams che ba'i mkhas pa grangs kyis smin/ /de gsan thugs kyi rus pa bcas nas ni/ /bsod nams chung ba'i rgyal khams smin bya'i phyir/ /'phags pa'i rigs can ma lus kun btsal
<p>135b</p>
<p>135b.1</p>te/ bai ro tsa na ska ba dpal brtsegs dang / /klu yi rgyal mtshan ye shes sde dang ni/ /e ra a ro many+dzu la sogs la/ /nor gyi dam pa gser dngul dbyig bskur nas/ /rgya gar yul gyi dam chos len du brdzangs/ /bod kyi mun rum nag po'i skar khung phye/ srid kyi chab srid
<p>135b.2</p>mnga' thang dgung la reg /bud+ha gu h+ya bdag dngos glo ba dga'/ /chab srid yo ba kun gyi gzhung srong zhing / /sprul pa'i rgyud ma chad pa'i nang na lde/ /khri srong lde'u btsan mnga' bdag zhal snga nas/ /mi chos lha chos mnga' thang rtse ru chibs/ /rin chen 'bar ba'i sku yi phung po
<p>135b.3</p>la/ /rlung mkhris bad kan 'dus pa'i nad chen dang / /stong phrag brgyad cu'i bgegs kyis ma btsal bar/ /'jam dpal dang ni mu ri ta la khums/ yas kyi sa nas bdag 'dra spyan 'dren pa/ /sku mnyel lags te bdag la dbang ma mchis/ /'phags pa 'jam
<p>135b.4</p>dpal zhal nas bod yul du/ /khyod kyis phyin na srog dang 'bral bar gsungs/ /bdag la dbang med khri lan skyes lan du/ /man ngag yo ga a ba ta ra brdzangs/ /bang chen mi gnyis po yi rtsed lan du/ /mngon par byang chub pa yi tan tra bshad/ /phyi nang gnyis kyi lag
<p>135b.5</p>len mang po kun/ /gcig kyang ma lus dgos pa thams cad brdzangs/ /gzigs rtog mdzad la gzhan du shor ra re/ /bod kyi mi ni sgrin la tshor skyen te/ /mthong ba thams cad la 'ur byed par 'gyur/ /nyes dmigs cha med dam chos stong bar byed/ /dmyal rgyu mang zhing 'bras
<p>135b.6</p>bu brlag par 'chi'o/ /phyi nang gnyis kyi lag len sba bar mdzod/ /rtsed la skyes lan gnyis kyis 'gro don mdzod/ /khri srong lde'u btsan yas kyi yang dbon gyi/ /rak+sha gnyis kyi bu gnyis phyogs rigs gcod/ /bod kyi rgyal khams srid kyi mkhar bu yang / /zhe dbon
<p>135b.7</p>man chad srid mkhar zhig par mchi'o/ /zhabs 'degs nyung zhing dmangs mo chung mar len/ /mtha' yi kha bzhi kun du grong slong byed/ /rgyal po'i dbyar ni bus pa'i rtse 'jo 'bul/ /dmangs mo tshol zhing grong zan slong bar mchi/ /yar 'gro mar 'gro 'gron po mtha' dag
<p>136a</p>
<p>136a.1</p>dang / /btsan po 'jal yang rgyal khams mi bzhin du/ /ngo mtshar mi che zhes ni mi phyogs par/ /'gron po ji bzhin rgyal nyal byed par mchi'o/ /phyogs bzhir sgyur ba'i mkhas pas bsgyur ba'i chos/ /rgyal po smos shing yon tan brjod pa'i phyir/ /
<p>136a.2</p>sde snod gsum po'i bka' rgyud ma lus pa/ /mnga' bdag phyir smos dpon sras drin du mchi'o/ /sku shugs phyung la bka' rgyud ma lus pa/ /lnga bcu rtsa dgu'i bar du bsgyur ba mdzod/ /drug cu na ni 'jig rten 'das nas ni/ /rgyal khams gzhan du skye ba bzhes par
<p>136a.3</p>mchi'o/ /'gro ba ris drug mtho dman gar skye ba/ /rang byung rig pa'i rgyal po rang dbang che/ /rdzas kyi shes pa shes pa'i nang na dbul/ /sems kyi mtshan nyid shes pa phyug ces mchi'o/ /de phyir sems kyi mtshan nyid legs par rtogs/ /sems ni khang spre'u glog ste ris
<p>136a.4</p>drug rgyu/ /mtho dman gar 'gro rang sems nyid dbang che/ /le lo ma mdzad rang sems ltas zhes mchi'o/ /gros kyi gdams ngag man ngag bstan pa ni/ /rgyal po nyung na brin phyir khab gzhis skyungs/ /btsun mo gcig la dang du bzhes pa ni/ /'phra mig g.yus spras
<p>136a.5</p>brgyan cing mdzes pa dang / gcig sems gcig la chags shing sha tsha mchi'o/ /srin bu gdong dmar bod kyi rgyal khams mi/ /dam tshig nyams shing mna' la mi 'dzem la/ /shes pa rags shing khong brnags chung ba yis/ /sngar byas khyad du gsod par 'os zhes
<p>136a.6</p>mchi'o/ /bsod nams che bar dpag bsam shing bu 'khrungs/ /bsod nams chung ba'i bod kyi rgyal khams su/ /shing bu ta la phyis mi skye ba 'khrungs/ /shing la gnod kyis 'chad pa shol cig mchi'o/ /gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten khang bzangs rnams/ /sdig pa
<p>136a.7</p>kun la gnod de las rmang yin/ /dam chos bsgyur ba zhu thug dag tu mdzod/ /lan cig dus su tshad mar byed par mchi'o/ /rgyal po'i rang bzhin gzhan dang smra mi bya/ /zugs thub gzobs la rab tu brtan par mdzod/ /thugs chen nang blon dpa' ba'i mi rnams
<p>136b</p>
<p>136b.1</p>la/ /dgos don gces spras lhug par smros shes mchi'o/ /srid la gnod pa'i gros ni mi snyan bor/ /khengs par mi bya zhi dul bskyar zhing smra/ /gtsigs dang bya dga' blon po rnams la ni/ /ha cang ma che ran tsam bya zhes mchi'o/ /blon po'i 'dod pa chu bzhin mi
<p>136b.2</p>bzad pas/ /srid kyi mkhar ni 'jig pa'i nyes mchis te/ srid kyis gal la bab pa'i dus na ni/ /sras la mi phangs sdig la mi 'dzem mchi'o/ /bsgyur ba mi bla snyan khung bskyed pa dang / /phyed tsam khyad du khums la rna la bzod/ /srid kyi chu mtha' rtog cing zad mi
<p>136b.3</p>shes/ /dkon mchog gsum ni spyan ltar mdzod ces mchi'o/ /theg pa kun la 'jug sgo re re ste/ /kun gyi sgo nas 'bras bu thob mod kyi/ /gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa dang du bzhes/ /bkri ba'i don du kun la'ang spyad tshul bstan/ /rdo rje theg pa dang du bzhes mchi'o/ /
<p>136b.4</p>mtha' lho bal rigs shes pa yod pa la/ /yid ches ma mdzad bong so bzhugs gnas rnams/ /kun du ma spong phung ba'i nyen mchis te/ /cal col ma mdzad co ge bzhugs zhes mchi'o/ /btsun mo rnams dang bud med gzhan dag la/ /'dod chags rang bzhin phyi phyir
<p>136b.5</p>'dod pa'i phyir/ /thugs kyis khug la ha cang spyad mi bya/ /nga khyod sre zhing mtho dman med par mchi'o/ /yid ches med par dgos don bsgrub mi bya/ /zas kyi sbyor shom zhim pos dgos mi bsten/ /zhe sas phyogs pa'i 'bangs la nye ring med/ /gzhan gyis mthong bar ma yin grong gzhan
<p>136b.6</p>du/ /gnyen pos bdag kyang 'gro bar mi mchi'o/ /rgyal po'i rang bzhin rgya mtsho'i chu lta bu/ /zha lag phyogs bzhir rgyas nas slar yang 'du/ /rgyal po'i rang bzhin de bzhin yongs kyis bsgrub/ /rgya mtshos kun sangs chos kyis 'gro drug spongs/ /zha lag phyogs bzhir don byed
<p>136b.7</p>sku gdung rnyed/ /so so snang yang slar la 'dus bzhin du/ /rlan gyis myu gu skyed bzhin gros rgya bskyed/ /chu yis 'bras bu bsgrub ltar dam chos bsgrub/ /rgya mtsho ma g.yos bzhin du g.yo mi bya/ /chu ni mnyen pa bzhin du khong mnyen bya/ /rgya mtsho gting dpag dka'
<p>137a</p>
<p>137a.1</p>bzhin tshod mi gzung / /chu chen bzlog thabs med bzhin srid la bya/ /rgya mtsho kun la khyab bzhin dang lag bskyed/ /chu 'thungs ngoms pa bzhin du gzhan ngoms bya/ /rgya mtshos chu rnams sdud bzhin 'khor rnams bsdu/ /chur ni gzugs brnyen gsal bzhin
<p>137a.2</p>gsal bar bya/ /rgya mtsho yon tan ji ltar ldan pa bzhin/ /rgyal po gcig gi sku la ldan gyur na/ /spu rgyal bod kyi rgyal po'i mnga' bdag rgyud/ /mgo nag yongs kyi rje ru bskos zhes mchi'o/ /'ol byung gdams ngag spyan sngar brdzangs pa 'di/ /mnga' bdag rgyal po'i mun pa'i
<p>137a.3</p>skar khung mdzod/ /dus min rtag tu thugs la gdags par zhu// //blon po rnams la brdzangs pa/ /khong dal smras pa btsan na blon pos rab tu chud/ /bud srid khye 'byin mi yi khong brna yis/ /so nams rgya yis chod na kun kyang drag par 'gyur/ /drang 'jam mig thag
<p>137a.4</p>byed na srid mtha' yin/ /mkhas btsun sngags pa khyad du mi gsod bu tsha'i gter/ /khong gdug kha 'jam byed pa'i blon po 'jigs/ /'o byams ban de 'khur ba'i blon po chos dang ldan/ /kun la snyoms par zas kyis bsten pa gzhan la byams/ /dul zhing gtang ba thub pa'i mi ni
<p>137a.5</p>grogs por btsal/ /'phral du khros pa lan mi ldon pa dgrar mi bya/ /dgra thabs zab mo dgra la byas pa rang la'o/ /nye dpung ma bshig gcig tu bsdus na dgra yang 'jigs/ /blo gtad mi la bu bzhin brtan par byed pa'i mi ni brling po yin/ /kha tshags dam la zas sgo
<p>137a.6</p>yangs na yul mis rtsi/ /phur ma'i mi la spyi ched dang du blangs na smras pa nyan/ /yon tan can gyi mi la bkur sti byas na bsod nams che/ /shes rab can gyi mi la bslab sbyang byas na mkhas par 'gyur/ /dga' ba'i mi la gcam par phab nas smras na khong blo gtod/ /chung
<p>137a.7</p>ma ji ltar mdzangs kyang gros blo gting mi gtad/ /skyes bu kun du grags pa tha shal che na nyams/ /ci la 'ang tshod zin sgrin khar mi 'dor rang lugs byed pa bzang / /sngar byas 'gyod pa med par shes na mi yi blon po yin/ /dgra thabs mkhas la ral ka byed pa blon po
<p>137b</p>
<p>137b.1</p>dpa' bo yin/ /kha 'jam che la khang ba rna chung ba'i mi la blo mi gtad/ /bskon thos rna gzod g.yos pa med na gdeng po che/ /pha ma dkon mchog phud du khur na rang gi ltang / /ngan pa rnams la zhe sas phyogs na dman pa'i gzhi/ /dgra la sran du 'dzugs na phyis dgra 'jigs/ /
<p>137b.2</p>khong ba rna chung ba'i mi la gnyer mi gtad/ /chung ma mdog sdug pho dad che ba blang mi bya/ /sge'u sres gud du byed pa'i chung ma gshin pa'i rtags/ /ngag 'jam khong yangs smra ba btsan de zhi na mdzangs/ /dpa' zhing phyogs che blo gtad thub pa pho zhes bya/ /tshig mkhas dgra la gnag na
<p>137b.3</p>gnyen gyi rag 'jigs che/ /mi don byed pa rang don bzhin du 'bad na g.yo sgyu chung / /rang don bzhag nas mi don byed pa ngo mi rtag /ngo dga' rma zhing kha rngam ngo mi rtag na khyo ga'i mo/ /'jam la gros gal gcod zhi btsan na gros zla bya/ /dpa' la gnyid chung lag pa gtsang bas lam
<p>137b.4</p>grogs bya/ /nye ring gang du 'gro yang grogs dang 'grogs/ /spro ring kha tshags dam pa'i 'khor re skyid/ /pha khu bzang po'i bu tsha ngan pa phos tshig che/ /'phral du khong gyod nga ro che ba'i mi dang 'grogs pa byur/ /pha tshan bzang po'i gseb tu skyes pa'i ngan pa rang mthong che/ /kha dman
<p>137b.5</p>khyim mtshes kun la sdang ba'i mi ni glang / /mna' ma rnams dang 'khon par byed pa'i bshal thag yin/ /ngan las bu phos byas na gros re khug pa re/ /phar ngan bu ru ngan na gros mjug 'thab mos byed/ /sngon du dpa' bo thod rgal byas na skyes bur 'gyur te dgra yang rtsi/ /mi btsan brdzun du
<p>137b.6</p>smras pa'i tshig mi btsun/ /smra mi nyan pa'i nang du smra ba blun pa ma yin nam/ /rang shes chung ba yon tan can la smod pa ngan pa yin/ /pha mes yon tan smos shing rang spu ngan pa lo nyes yin/ /khong gyod gnyen la sdang ba bu lon ngan pa byol song yin/ /byas pa med par rang mthong che ba
<p>137b.7</p>glen pa yin/ /bcol ba med pa'i las la 'jug pa smyon ba yin/ /zas ngor 'khrug ldan byed pa phung ba yin// //sgom chen rnams la brdzangs pa/ /tshul chos mi bya shes pa'i sa mi gzung / /sde snod gsum po kun la lta rtog bya/ /bltas pa'i tshig la mi brtag don la
<p>138a</p>
<p>138a.1</p>dpyad/ /lung la mkhas pa'i slob dpon rnams dang 'grogs/ /sgom chen yin zhes phug tu yong mi 'dug /yid ches med par bsgom par tshul mi bcos/ /the tshom bcad cing mkhas pa'i zhal yang lta/ /the tshom chod cing blo la snang ba dang / /sgom pa'i gol
<p>138a.2</p>sgrib chod cing don shes shing / /rus sbal kho gor nang na 'dug pa de/ /brkyang bskum 'dug 'gro gzhan gyis ma mthong ltar/ /'khor gyis slebs par ma yin dben par 'dug /snying po don las nyin mtshan 'byung mi bya/ /chung ma gshin yang bsgom g.yog bya ba min/ /'du
<p>138a.3</p>long ngan par 'khor du bsten mi rung / /rang sems dpang du btsugs la yengs mi bya/ /g.yeng dang bying rmugs yod zhig yod gyur na/ /tshul 'chos mi bya bla ma rnams la dri/ /thams cad mnyam pa'i snying por gyur pa'i rtags/ /ci la'ang chags thogs mi mnga' mnyam par
<p>138a.4</p>'gyur/ /de 'dra'i sgom chen sangs rgyas rnams dang mtshungs/ /dus min rtag tu sems la gdams ngag 'di/ /sgom chen rnams kyi sems la shar bar smon// //spyi'i ban de rnams la brdzangs pa/ /mi dge bcu spangs dge ba bcu las ni/ /lus ngag
<p>138a.5</p>yid gsum dus bzhir g.yo mi bya/ /dam chos zab mo'i phyir ni srog gis bor/ /mkhas su re zhes shes pa'i sa mi gzung / /bdag gis shes kyang the tshom gzhan la dri/ /chos kyi srid pa sa gsum sems pa bzhin/ /ngoms par mi bya shes rab gsum gyis bslab/ nges
<p>138a.6</p>pa rang la med par gzhan mi bslab/ /bsrung ba rnam gsum zhing tshigs bzhin du bsrung / /rdo rje slob dpon yi dam lha ltar bkur/ /man ngag zab mo mig gi 'bras ltar btsa'/ /theg pa kun la mkhas kyang gsang theg la/ /gzhan shes de la ma 'byor ban de ni/ /theg gzhan
<p>138a.7</p>shes kyang gsang theg ma 'byor na/ /gser 'dod bong ba rnyed pa ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po skye rgyud ma chod par/ /btsun par skye rgyud gcod pa snying re rje/ /nyon mongs ma spangs btsun pa gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /sa bon rul ba'i 'bras bu ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po
<p>138b</p>
<p>138b.1</p>dug sdong ma bsgyel bar/ /sgur nas lha phyag 'tshal ba snying re rje/ dug sdong ma bsgyel zab srung gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /skyer tsher dar gyis phur pa ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po dbyings su ma bskor bar/ /mchod rten bskor ba byed par snying re rje/ /chos dbyings ma mthong bskor
<p>138b.2</p>ba gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /mar 'dod lha khang khyis bskor ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po rnam par ma dag par/ /gdong bkrus lag pa bsnyal ba snying re rje/ /rnam par ma dag 'khru ba gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /bre ka nas kyis bcad pa ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po zhi bar ma byas
<p>138b.3</p>par/ /chos nyid zhi bar lta bar snying re rje/ /zhi bar ma byas lta ba gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /char ma gnam sdong ljong bu ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po mgo bo ma bregs par/ /mgo zlum dpung zlum byed pa snying re rje/ /nyon mongs ma bregs mgo zlum gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /mun
<p>138b.4</p>gnag nang na rdzas tshol ji bzhin no/ /nyon mongs lnga po dul bar ma byas par/ /pha rol dgra dpung 'joms pa snying re rje/ /dul bar ma byas dgra 'joms gnyis mi 'phrugs/ /ri gzar rbab shor 'dzin pa ji bzhin no/ /chos nyid zab mo lta bas klong du bya/ /spyod pas 'gro don
<p>138b.5</p>bsam gtan rgyun mi bcad/ /ye shes ral gris skye rgyud gcad par rigs/ /nyon mongs lnga pos ldang ba gnas su bstim/ /yang ldang yang ldang byed na chos nyid bsam/ /mnyam pa'i don la bsam ba'i gtan la gzhug /rang dbang med par gzhan dbang bskur mi bya/ /dus
<p>138b.6</p>gsum chos kyi mtshan nyid blo la gzhag /gsang sngags zab mo grong yul mi la ni/ /bstan par mi bya rnga dril yang mi brdung / /yas ra yas lug mkhas zhes gsad mi bya/ /pho mo mang po'i nang du sgrub pa byed par khrel/ /zas nor gsang sngags zab mo yon du 'tshong ba smyos/ /
<p>138b.7</p>gsang sngags bsam gtan yi dam nyid du nyo tshong byed pa med/ /ban de'i rang bzhin grong gi dbus mi 'dug /tshong la mi bza' sdig pa'i rmang gzhir 'gro/ /pho bla mi byang chub ma'i dad kyang skyungs/ /be'u mang po mi bsrel sdig pa'i rgyu/ /nyin mtshan med par 'gro don byed 'dod
<p>139a</p>
<p>139a.1</p>pas/ /rang sems dag na 'dod pa'i don la sgrub/ /mi nag skye bo mang po'i 'gro don yang / /tshod yod mi bya bsam gtan nyid du bya/ /'di rnams ma nor shes pa ban de yin/ /nyin re bzlas pa mi gcad skyo dub kyang mi bya/ /rtse gcig dang du blangs la bya ba yin/ /mkhas
<p>139a.2</p>pa'i rang bzhin don la mkhas pa yin/ /tshig la mkhas pa ne tsho tshig zlos mkhas/ /rtse gcig yang dag bden pa'i rlung las ni/ /rang sems dpang du btsugs la nyams mi bya/ /nyin mtshan med par chos kyi don la ni/ /dus gsum 'du 'bral med par ting 'dzin bya/ /shes pa che
<p>139a.3</p>yang mkhas pa'i sa mi gzung / /rdo rje slob dpon yi dam lha bzhin du/ /khur zhing rtse gcig yi dam nyid du bya/ /de dang mi 'brel brtse gdung tshe mar 'grogs/ /bden pa ston pa'i rdo rje slob dpon ni/ /mig gi 'bras ltar bkur ba'i rang bzhin la/ /g.yog 'khor ngan pa slob dpon
<p>139a.4</p>spong byed pa/ /nyan byed mi de blun po spre'u zhes bya/ /'di rnams bdag gis mdo tsam bstan pa 'di/ /bod kyi rgyal khams phan bde'i sems la ni/ /gdams ngag 'di ni kun la shar bar smon// //slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas gsang bas bod kyi rgyal po khri srong
<p>139a.5</p>lde'u btsan rje 'bangs dang / bod btsun rnams la brdzangs pa'i spring yig go//[ ]@/ /dad skyed sgron ma bzhugs so// @##/ /sems can dam pa'i chos la dad pa skyed mdzad pa'i/ /dad pa skyed mdzad bla ma dam pa dang / /mos pas yon tan 'byung
<p>139a.6</p>ba'i dkon mchog la/ /bdag nyid gus pas de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhe sdang me yis rang gi rgyud bsregs shing / /gti mug mun pas shes rab dmigs bu ljongs/ /'khor ba'i g.yang sar lhung bas sdug bsngal rgyun mi 'chad/ /'khor ba'i btson rar bzung zhing lcags
<p>139a.7</p>bcug pa'i/ /ma 'ongs skye bo'i don du bdag gis brtsam par bya/ /bdag gi rgyud la legs par tshur bltas bas/ /mi lus 'di ni shin tu thob par dka'/ /gyang ngos sran ma gtor ba gcig chags srid/ /thams cad sa la ltung nas song ba ltar/ /mi lus thob dka'
<p>139b</p>
<p>139b.1</p>sems can grangs la ltos/ /rgya mtsho gcig nas gnya' shing bug pa dang / /rus sbal phrad pa bas kyang dud 'gro nas/ /mi nyid ches thob dka' bas mi dbang gis/ /dam chos spyad pas de 'bras mchis par mdzod/ /sbyin nor 'dra ba'i mi lus 'di thob tshe/ /'di la phan pa'i
<p>139b.2</p>thar pa ma bsgrubs par/ /phyis ni dal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa 'di/ /thob par dka' ba'i tshe 'di chung ma gsan/ /'jig rten spyod pa dag la phar bltas pas/ /thar la mi mos sdig la dga' ba skye / /mtho la phrag dog mnyam la 'gran sems byed/ /dma' la
<p>139b.3</p>nga rgyal bstod na dregs pa skye / /mi snyan brjod na khong nas 'khrug par 'gyur/ /rang don thar pa rgyab tu bor byas nas/ /'khrul don bu dang nor la bdag tu 'dzin/ /skyabs pa'i chos bzhag thar pa'i lam sna bor/ /sdug pa'i mi chos glen pa'i bu nor sog /ji tsam sdig pa
<p>139b.4</p>bsdos nas nor bsags kyang / /sdig pa'i rnam smin rmongs pa bdag nyid 'khur/ /bsags pa'i nor ni kho bdag bu tsha khyer/ /ro dang mtshungs kyang bdag nyid bzang por 'dzin/ /'khor ba'i btson rar tshud kyang 'bros bsam med/ /phyi na rten med zas nor bu la chags/ /
<p>139b.5</p>dad ldan pha ma'i gdung sems rtsad nas bral/ /bdag ni stobs bzad gzhan ni dregs pa 'joms/ /gzhan gyi nor dang rdzas la chags pa skye/ /ma bcol gzhan la gnod pa'i kha gtogs zer/ /nyan bshad dus na bsam pa logs su gtong / /dkon mchog mthong na skyon med
<p>139b.6</p>gshe tshig smra/ /sems can mthong na zhe sdang gsod sems skye/ /'di la skyid na phyi ma sdug mod zer/ /de dang ldan pa'i sems can skye bo de/ /mi lus chud gsan ad tsa snying re rje/ /gling mchog bzhi na 'dzam gling 'dir skye dka'/ /'di na sems can grangs mang gnas pa la/ /
<p>139b.7</p>mi lus 'di ni shin tu thob dka' na/ /'on long zha bor gyur kyang chos spyod dka'/ /sgro skur med pa'i lus thob gzhon pa'i tshe/ /dam chos mi spyod mi lus chud re gsan/ /gang zhig gser snod rin chen spras pa yis/ /ngan skyugs 'phyag par byed pa de bas kyang / /gang zhig mi ru
<p>140a</p>
<p>140a.1</p>skyes nas sdig pa dag /byed pa de dag rab tu blun pa lags/ /na dang rga dang 'chi ba'i dus byung na/ /mi lus chud gsan 'gyod kyang phan pa med/ /dper na zon med dgra phyogs phyin pa'i tshe/ /dgra yis zin nas 'gyod pa'i 'bras sems skye / /skyes kyang phan
<p>140a.2</p>med bdag gis mi thar na/ /de 'dra de bas chos la 'bad par rigs/ /phyis 'jigs dogs nas sngon du mkhar dpe rtsig /phyi ma ngan song 'jigs nas sngon du spyod/ /lo dus su ni dar cig mi sdod na/ /nam la yod de tshe la long med do/ /lo zlas 'das shing 'chi dang phar phar nye/ /rang
<p>140a.3</p>gi tshe ni gad kha'i shing pu 'dra/ /'chi bdag bdud ni gad rtsi'i chu bo 'dra/ /skye rga na 'chi rang thag re mos 'dra/ /mi rtag 'gyur ba dbyar dgun ston dpyid 'dra/ /snga ma shi ba'i mi rnams kun gyis kyang / /rtag tu re zhing bu dang nor bsags kyang / /bu nor phyir lus bdag la phan pa med/ 
<p>140a.4</p>rang nyid dge sdig gnyis dang sbrags nas 'gro/ /nor dang rdzas ni shing ga'i bye'u chung 'dra/ /mi rtag nges kyis chags sems gnyen pos chod/ /skyid sdug mi rtag kha song di ring 'dra/ /chos la 'gro bar chas tshe gnyen 'dun tshogs/ /yon tan brjod cing mi chos bya dgos zer/ /nor
<p>140a.5</p>gyis brid cing de yi bar du gcod/ /dug bum thogs nas gtor du 'ongs dang mtshungs/ /bdag la bya snyam gnyen 'dun smra ba nyan/ /bde ba bkag nas g.yang sar gtong dang mtshungs/ /'khor ba'i bu tsha dug gi me tog 'dra/ /mthong na dga' ste ngan song rgyu sogs yin/ /bdag
<p>140a.6</p>nyid 'chi bdag bdud kyis bslus pa'i tshe/ /mal gyi tha mar nyal nas lus gdungs te/ /zas kyi tha ma skyug kyang dur brgyags snyod / /pha ma gnyen 'dun rnams kyis mtha' bskor te/ /de tshe rang la ci yis phan sems dang / /shags kyis mi lo dpa' bos 'thab tu med/ /mkhar
<p>140a.7</p>gyis mi thub nor gyis slu ru med/ /gnyen gyis mi phan sdar ma 'bros su med/ /zug gzer che yang gnyen 'dun bskor mi btub/ /gson tshe byams kyang shi nas 'jigs nas 'bros/ /yul mkhar bor nas rang shong gcig tu skyel/ /gnyen 'dun bor nas bdag rang gcig
<p>140b</p>
<p>140b.1</p>pu 'khyam / /bdag la byams kyang phyi nas 'ong ba med/ /de 'dra'i gnyen rtsa dgos kyi rdul bzhin spongs/ /byang sems myu gus rtsad nas ma bsregs par/ /byang chub mchog gi sems de rtag tu zung / /byang chub sems bskyed gyur na skad cig gis/ /'khor ba'i btson rar bsdams
<p>140b.2</p>pa'i nyam thag rnams/ /bde gshegs sras su dgongs te byin gyis rlobs/ /sems can mi bde bsal bar 'dod pa dang / /'khor bar gnas dang bral bar 'dod pa rnams/ /byang chub mchog gi sems 'di rtag tu bskyed/ /'phags pa'i gdams dag don chen 'di lags te/ /
<p>140b.3</p>khyod kyis thugs dul mdzod cig bcom ldan gyis/ /byang sems chos kyi rtsa ba lags par gsungs/ /khengs grags dge ba bsod nams 'bras bu bzhin/ /bden par spyad kyang zad par 'gyur ba yin/ /sems bskyed pa yi yon tan rtag par yang / /'bras bu 'byin cing mi zad
<p>140b.4</p>'phel ba yin/ /sdig pa'i phung po ri rab tsam yod kyang / /sems bskyed tsam gyis de dag zhi nus na/ /de la bag can rnams kyis cis mi rten / /des ni dus mtha'i me bzhin sdig chen rnams/ /skad cig gcig gis de dag bsreg par nus/ /de phyir bdag gis sems bskyed g.yo ba dang / /
<p>140b.5</p>smon dang 'jug pa gnyis kyis sems bskyed de/ /mi ldog rtse gcig pa yi dad pa yis/ /byang chub sems de rtag tu gzung bar bya/ /de nas le lo gnyid kyi dbang song bas/ /sems bskyed brjed kyang bsod nams shugs la 'phel/ /rgyun mi 'chad pa'i chu bo'i gzhung dang mtshungs/ /nam
<p>140b.6</p>yang 'byung ste yon tan brjod mi lang / /sems bskyed dad pas dam chos sgor zhugs pa'i/ /skyes bu dam pas man ngag 'di ltar zung / /mi khom gnas su skyes na chos spyad dka'/ /rang la dbang yod bzhin du dbang med zer/ /bdud kyis mngon bslus rang nyid phung bar 'gyur/ /thar pa bdag la
<p>140b.7</p>rag las 'di la ni/ /gzhan gyis ci yang grogs bgyir ma mchis kyis/ /mi lus thob tshe dal gyis spyad par rigs/ /bde sdug zin pa med kyis dam chos spyod/ /'jig rten longs spyod sus za cha med kyis/ /sngun na sdod kyi son ma 'bad par rigs/ /gal te mi lus thob nas gzhon
<p>141a</p>
<p>141a.1</p>pa'i tshe/ /'jig rten dga' ba'i ca co sogs bor la/ /gzhon pa'i tshe ni dam chos dang du long / /bu tsha snying sdug 'khor ba'i rtod phur yin/ /bu tsha bden par 'dzin pa'i rmongs pa 'ga'/ /lus la shig za bya ra mig gis byas/ /sor mo'i rgya ba bkye nas
<p>141a.2</p>gshed mas gsad / /rnam smin gdong na sdod de phyi mar smin/ /sdug bsngal myong tshe bu yis bdag mi phan/ /khyod kyis dge slong bram ze lha dang ni/ /mgron dang yab yum sras dang btsun mo dang / /'khor gyi slad du sdig pa mi bgyi ste / /dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal bskal 'dod 'ga' ma
<p>141a.3</p>mchis// de phyir bu la ma chags chos la 'bod/ /gzhon tshe dam pa'i chos la ma 'bad na/ /rgas nas nyan 'dod rna bas sgra mi thos/ /shes rab bying bas blo la rtogs pa dka'/ /chos la 'gro 'dod lus la nus pa med/ /chos la dga' yang bdag gis spyod mi nus/ /gzhon pa'i tshe
<p>141a.4</p>na dam chos cis mi spyad/ /dam pa'i chos la bden par ngo yis zung / /'jig rten bde ba sprin bzhin 'gyur ldog che/ /chos la spyod na phyug por mkhyen par mdzod/ /'jig rten nor gyis phyug pas phung bar nges/ /sdig bcu spangs nas dge bcu dang len pa/ /mdzangs pa lags te
<p>141a.5</p>skyes bu phyi mar bde/ /mi 'khyag tsam du dag dug gon byas shing / /mi ltogs tsam du zas ngan zos byas la/ /longs spyod bla med byang chub bsngo bar bya/ /nor rnams kun gyi nang na chog shes pa/ /rab mchog lags par lha mi'i ston pas gsungs/ /kun du chog shes mdzod cig
<p>141a.6</p>chog shes na/ /nor mi bdog kyang yang dag 'byor pa lags/ /bdag ni khyod la byams pa'i zhal ta zer/ /bdag la zas nor skyabs kyi re ba med/ /ngan song 'khor ba'i gnas dang bral phyir gdams/ /bka' ltar mi byed gti mug smad pa'i gnas/ /g.yang sar 'gro yang dogs
<p>141a.7</p>zon bya dgos na/ /bskal pa'i gting lhung g.yang sa smos ci dgos/ /di ring sang la 'chi bar mi 'gyur zhes/ /bde bar 'dug pa bdag gis ga la rigs/ /chos spyad gzhon yang shi ba bde ba ste/ /zhing khams dag par 'gro zhing sdug bsngal med/ /chos med rgan rgon shi ba
<p>141b</p>
<p>141b.1</p>skyid ces smra/ /shi sdug lags te ngan song gnas su 'gro/ /skyid sdug gnyis kyi bye brag mkhyen par mdzod/ /chos dang ldan na dman yang bkur sti thob/ /chos kyi dag byung mkhas pas bshad kyi nyon/ /'jig rten nor dang ldan zhing dam chos rdzas kyis spyod/ /chos la ma thongs rdzas kyi
<p>141b.2</p>mngon zhen gyis/ /longs spyod rnams ni skar ma'i rang bzhin la/ /yongs su ma btang de dag nges par 'gyur/ /dgra dang chom rkun dag dang rgyal pos 'joms/ /mi bsad stong du 'gro srid rkun pos rku yang srid/ /chos la btong ba'i brtson 'grus spyad par rigs/ /longs spyod g.yo
<p>141b.3</p>ba snying po med mkhyen nas/ /dge slong bram ze gnyen dang bshes rnams la/ /sbyin pa tshul bzhin stsal bgyi pha rol du/ /sbyin las gzhan pa'i gnyen mchog ma mchis so/ /'gron po yun rings rgyags su sbyin pa rme/ /rdzas rnams myur du thod cig skyes bu dad pa can/ /byin rlabs
<p>141b.4</p>'dir 'byung phyi ma gdong na sdod/ /bde skyid 'dod dang sdug bsngal spong 'dod dang / /rigs mtho bzhin legs bde ba'i gnas thob dang / /bde mthong mos shing sdug bsngal spong 'dod pas/ /dam chos 'di ni rtag tu spyad par bya/ /lha dang mi yi bde ba thob 'dod pas/ /dge bcu spyod de lus
<p>141b.5</p>kha bsrung ba ni/ /'dod log g.yem dang srog gcod rku ba dang / /brdzun dang phra ma tshig rtsub 'khyal pa dang / /brnab sems gnod sems log par lta ba dang / /rang don lags kyis sdig bcu rgyab tu bor/ /rang la byams shing brtse bas 'bad par bya/ /rngon pa mi rgod rkun po jag pa
<p>141b.6</p>sogs/ /sdig pa'i rkyen sogs grogs po 'dug pa spong / /kun du dge ba'i slob dpon sman bzhin bsten/ /'on long zhar sgur lus thob rgud pa dang / /dbul phongs bzhin dan las las nad mang rnams/ /rnam smin lags kyis gzhan la yus ma ches / /mtho ris ngan song
<p>141b.7</p>gnyis la gang mos pa/ /rang dbang yod kyis skyid sdug khyad par nyon/ /gal te mtho ris thar pa mngon zhe na/ /yang dag lta ba goms pa dag tu mdzod/ /rnam rtog ri bos mnan pa'i sems can rnams/ /sdug bsngal 'di la bzod pa'i glags med de/ /'khor bas 'khor te zo
<p>142a</p>
<p>142a.1</p>chu khyud mo 'dra/ /rnam rtog rlung gis khyer te rtsi shing lo 'dab 'dra/ /rnam rtog rgyud la skyes te rtswa la me mched 'dra/ /ye shes skad cig mi gnas dbyar kha'i she mun 'dra/ /phyi yi sdug bsngal bzhi ni rang sems myong / /yod na mi thub med na btsal mi rnyed/ /byams dang
<p>142a.2</p>bral dogs sdang dang phrad kyi dogs/ /nang gi sdug bsngal bzhis ni rang lus 'joms/ /ma lus 'byung tshe brag bar btsir ba 'dra/ /ma yis mchod sa tshe g.yang la phyin pa snyam/ /lhung tshe tsher ma'i dang du bsgyur ba snyam/ /blangs na bye chung khra yis khyer ba snyam/ /skye ba'i sdug bsngal rang
<p>142a.3</p>lus rdul bzhin rlog /lo zla 'das shing rgas pa shugs kyis 'od/ /rgas tshe mgo la skra dkar so yang med/ /rna bas mi thos mig gis rang mi mthong / /'dug na rang lus sa rdo chad pa 'dra/ /langs na spang las phur pa 'byin dang mtshungs/ /phyi sgor 'gro yang sgur nas gog cing 'gro/ /zas skom
<p>142a.4</p>'dod na gzhan la rag las slong / /bu tshas mthong yang mi mos yid mi 'ong / /dug po bskon zhing sgo rtsa srung du gtod/ /gzhan dag 'ong nas ngo tsha phar zur zer/ /khyim mtshes byis pa gshe zhing 'tshe ru 'ong / /'tshogs par phyin na skyugs bro phar song zer/ /shi skal chad de rgan rgon yi dgas
<p>142a.5</p>skye/ /ngo tsha khrel 'dzem shor de gzhan gyis skyur / /bu smad kun yang shi na rung zhes smras / /rkang lag 'dar zhing kha mig chu yis khengs/ /lus kyi stobs shor ber ga grogs su tshol/ /legs par smras kyang gzhan gyi rnar mi snyan/ /bde bar nyal kyang lus tshigs khol zhing na/ /gzhan
<p>142a.6</p>la gtam smras rgas pa'i ngag mi snyan/ /rgas pa'i sdug bsngal bshad na kun la'ang / /lus la nad med bde sdug re ba rnams/ /nges pa 'dod pas nongs dang 'chi ba dang / /na rga la sogs sdug bsngal du ma yi / /'byung gnas 'khor ba la ni skyo mdzod cig /de yi nyes pa'i shas kyang
<p>142a.7</p>mkhyen par mdzod/ /khams gsum 'khor ba'i lam la bde ba med/ /rigs drug sems can nad la grangs re mang / /dug lnga dug gsum nad kyi dbal re cha/ /thog mtha' med pa nad kyi yun re ring / /de ltar lags te ma rig bde ru med/ /'chi bdag bdud kyi zhags pas zin pa'i tshe/ /lus
<p>142b</p>
<p>142b.1</p>ngag yid gsum nad kyis thebs pa'i tshe/ /ngag gi sdug bsngal rnga mo bu stor 'dra/ /lhang lhang tser tser cis kyang nad kyi dbang / /lus kyi sdug bsngal skam la nya skyur 'dra/ /rgal bu stod stod 'phar yang nyams stobs med/ /'bros par bsams kyang thar ba'i dus mtha' med/ /gzer gyis
<p>142b.2</p>lus btab ngo tsha khrel 'dzem shor/ /gnyen 'dun bskor yang sdug bsngal rang gis myong / /zas skom kha ru bcug kyang bro brlag med/ /nye bas bos kyang kha nas skad mi thon/ /ji ltar nyal kyang bde ba'i bar skabs med/ /sdig la 'gyod pa skyes kyang bshags long med/ /na ba'i sdug
<p>142b.3</p>bsngal lags te kun la 'ong / /des na mi ni yang dag nyid du mi bde zhing / /mi gtsang bdag med pa ru rig par bgyi/ /'chi ba'i tshe na dge sdig las kyis 'byed / /dge ba can ni 'chi tshe bde ba mthong / /mun pa'i khams nas bde ba byung ba dang / /lus la chags pa med cing lus sems bral nas
<p>142b.4\] dga'/ /bde gshegs bskor ba byed cing chos bshad mthong / /bde ba'i zhing khams byung bas mos pa 'byung / /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan mchod pa'i rdzas 'bul dang / /'gro drug gnas mthong snying rje'i sems 'byung ste/ /de dang ldan na bde ba'i gnas su skye/ /sdig can dag ni 'chi tshe nyes
<p>142b.5</p>skyon mthong / /snang ba'i khams ni mun pa nam sros bzhin/ /mtho na spyi tshugs thur la song ba mthong / /lag na 'dug pa gdug pa'i mtshon char mthong / /sgra skad thams cad gdug rtog sgra ru thos/ /sdig pa byas na ngan song lam du ston/ /'chi bdag gshin rjes rgyab nas phul zhing brdeg /
<p>142b.6</p>srog gcod bdud kyis gdong nas brtson bzhin khrid/ /gcan gzan gdug pa'i 'brug sgra bzhin du sgrogs/ /mtshon cha gdug pa'i dbal ni rtsang bzhin 'dzugs/ /'khor ba'i g.yang sar ri gzar rbab bzhin 'dril/ /yi dgas gnas na sdug bsngal dpag tu med/ /bkres skom grang ngo
<p>142b.7\] ngal dang 'jigs pa yis/ /skyed pa shin tu mi bzad sten 'tshal lo/ /mgo lus skom par mi mthun rgyu las byung / /skom skyugs bro zer sna yi rgyu las byung / /sdug bsngal che ste las la zad dus med/ /gal te tshe zad dmyal ba'i gnas 'gro ste/ /skad cig yud kyis gnas der myur par
<p>143a</p>
<p>143a.1</p>phyin/ /dmyal ba'i sdug bsngal rig na mchi ma 'ong / /btsong khu rgyal po 'phrang du bsdad nas ni/ /gson po pags pa bshus shing yan lag 'don/ /de ltar byas kyang rnams smin 'chir mi 'dod/ /bye ba phrag brgya nyams su myong yang ni/ /ji srid mi dge de zad ma
<p>143a.2</p>gyur pa/ /de srid sdog dang 'bral bar mi 'gyur ro/ /dmyal ba'i lcags khad mthong na dga' snyam sems/ /las kyi sgo phye nang du dbang med 'gro/ /las rlung phug nas sgo gcod mun pa 'thibs/ /phyogs mtshams kun nas me 'byung 'bros sa med/ /sha rus tshig kyang 'chi ru las kyis 'tsho/ /
<p>143a.3</p>rang nyid zangs su 'tshod cing sha rus bral/ /phur bzhi rgyang shing steng 'og lcags kyis btab/ /lcags gzer steng 'og lus la gang bar 'debs/ /gal te 'gul na lhu tshigs rus pa 'bral/ /lcags kyi bya phra mkha' la lding zhing 'debs/ /mtshon cha'i 'khor los lus la dum bur
<p>143a.4</p>gcod/ /lcags kyi tho chen mkha' la lding zhing brdeg /sog les spyi bo'i gtsug nas rkang mthil gshog/ /spu gris gtams pa'i ri la dbang med 'dzeg /rnag khrag bshul ba'i dri ma dpag tshad khyab/ /rang gis rang bsregs skye bo rang gis len/ /'chongs pa de ltar lags te lha mi dang / /
<p>143a.5</p>dmyal ba yi dgas dud 'gro rnam dag tu/ /skye ba [(]bzad [,]bzang [)]po ma lags skye ba ni/ /gnod pa du ma'i snod gyur lags pas mkhyen par mdzod/ /des na 'jig rten bde nus ci la phan/ /de phyir bdag gis bshad pa'i man ngag nyon/ /'gro ba'i don mdzad bla ma dam pa yis/ /ma 'ongs sems can skye
<p>143a.6</p>pa'i don dag tu/ /man ngag dad skyed sgron ma 'di brtsams pas/ /'gro ba kun gyis sangs rgyas thob par shog/ /slob dpon ka ma la shI las mdzad pa//dad skyes sgron ma rdzogs so//[# ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ dr-iSh+TA na ta mA l+ya/ bod skad du/ dpe'i phreng ba/ 
<p>143a.7</p>'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dang por smra ba rnams kyi rab mchog ston pa dang / /srid pa gsum gyi 'dod chags rnams 'joms chos dang ni/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i bstan pa bdud rtsi'i snod gyur pa/ /gang zag mchog brgyad kyis brgyan dge 'dun rab brtul zhing / /bsam
<p>143b</p>
<p>143b.1</p>rdzogs rtsib logs 'tsher la sogs pa de dang de/ /thams cad yod smra'i khyu mchog dad pas mchod byas te/ /dpe yi phreng ba 'di ni bdag gis bshad par bya/ /rab blo'i legs sbyar ma sbas 'di na de bstan gyis/ /yon tan dang skyon gyi mtshan nyid khong du chud pa las mchod bar bya ba dang / 
<p>143b.2</p>mchod par bya ba ma yin pa rtogs par 'gyur bas yon tan dang skyon gyi mtshan nyid khong du chud pa la rab tu 'bad par bya'o/ /de yang 'di ltar rjes su thos te/ yul gan d+ha ra nas tshong pa kha cig bcom brlag tu song ba dang / de de na mchod rten rnams la yang dang yang du phyag 'tshal zhing dge sbyong rnams
<p>143b.3</p>la yang bsnyen bkur dang bcas pas phyag byed par gyur pa dang / de la 'di ni dge bsnyen yin no snyam du shes nas bram ze rnams kyis bzhad gad byas par gyur to zhes grag go/ /de nas re zhig gcig na de so ga'i dus kyi phyi dro'i tshe bram ze zhig gis lam srang na 'dug go/ /der yang bram
<p>143b.4</p>ze kha cig khrus byas shing dris byugs pa dang zas la spyad pas dbang po tshim pa dang khang pa sgo'i phyogs na lag na rnga yab thogs shing mchod phyir dkar po thogs la/ gcig tu shas cher bgad de gtam la rjes su chags shing dga' bas kun du 'khod par gyur ba dang / de rnams kyis dge
<p>143b.5</p>bsnyen de bltas nas rab tu bgad do/ /bram ze gzhan zhig gis kyang smras pa/ /sangs rgyas kyi dge bsnyen khyod tshur shog stan yod par 'dug shig /de der 'dug pa dang / bram ze zhig gis dris pa/ gang lha chen po dang khyab 'jug la sogs pa'i lha rnams spangs nas sangs rgyas la
<p>143b.6</p>mchod pa byed par gan d+ha ra ba rnams kyi rang bzhin 'di ci zhig yin/ des bgad de smras pa/ bdag cag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi yon tan rnams kyi phyogs gcig shes kyi lha chen po la sogs pa'i lha rnams kyi yon tan ni mi shes te/ rgyu des na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa byed pa
<p>143b.7</p>yin no/ /des de'i tshig de thos pa dang / /bram ze kha cig gis smras pa/ legs ldan lha chen po'i yon tan mi shes pa 'di ni/ khyod glen pa yin te gang gi phyir/ 'di na lha min grong khyer mkha' la rgyu/ /skyes pa bud med rgan dang gzhon bcas pa/ /gzhu chen blangs nas 'bar ba'i mda' yis ni/ /me
<p>144a</p>
<p>144a.1</p>yis rtswa bzhin skad cig dag gis bsregs/ /dge snyen gyis smras pa/ gang rang bzhin gyis 'chi ba'i chos can gyi srog chags rnams la gsad pa'i phyir 'bad pa dang ldan pa'i sems can gyi khyad par de 'dra ba la ni kho bo mi dga'o/ /su zhig zil pa'i thigs pa ni/ /rtswa yi rtse la
<p>144a.2</p>chags pa dag /ngang gis 'jig pa'i chos can la/ /gzhig pa'i phyir ni 'bad par byed/ /re zhig gzhan thams cad lta zhog gis/ ci khyed rnams pha rol la gnod pa byed pa yon tan yin par shes sam/ /de nas bram ze de dag thams cad kyis dus gcig tu smras pa/ lha ma yin gsod pa ni yon tan
