<p>144a.3</p>yin par rab tu shes pa'o/ /dge snyen gyis dbugs phyung ste smras pa/ las gang las ni dam pa rnams/ /ngo tshar gyur pa de nyid la/ /dam pa min pa dregs gyur pa/ /kye ma 'jig rten ngo mtshar che/ /zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten las legs par smras pa yin no/ /mdor na/ yon tan skyon stsogs brtags la bya ba dang / /
<p>144a.4</p>bya min sad pas rgyal ba'i yon tan ni/ /rgya chen rjes la yon tan nges dga' rnams/ /mchod pa'i 'bras bu 'dod pa rgya chen yin/ /skyon la yon tan dag tu 'du shes shing / /skyon dang ldan pa dam par shes pas mchod/ /'bras bu rgya chen thob par mi 'gyur gyi/ /lta ba ngan pa dag kyang 'phel bar 'gyur/ /
<p>144a.5</p>tshig de bram ze rgan po kha cig gis thos pa dang / khro bas 'bar ba'i mig gis dge bsnyen de la lta zhing brnyas pa dang bcas lag pa g.yon pas ston cing smras pa/ gan d+har ba rmongs pa rnams de skad ma smra shig /gal te lha ma yin gsod par dga' ba'i lha chen po la sogs pa'i lha rnams mchod par
<p>144a.6</p>bya ba ma yin na mchod par bya bar su zhig 'gyur/ dge snyen gyis smras pa/ /gang yon tan yang dag pa dang ldan par 'gyur ba ste/ bram ze chen po ltos shig /gang zhig stobs ldan 'tshe ba rnams/ /gal te mchod byar de gyur na/ /dred dang gzig dang stag la yang / /'gro ba rtag tu mchod par 'gyur/ /
<p>144a.7</p>yon tan skyon mkhas dam pa ni/ /su la yang ni 'dod mi byed/ /dred la sogs pa'i gdug pa rnams/ /yon tan med la mchod mi byed/ /mi 'tshe la sogs yon tan yin/ /'tshe sogs skyon du shes par bya/ /yon tan skyon rnams mi shes pas/ /skyon ni yon tan dag tu shes/ /gang gis shin tu drag po'i las/ /
<p>144b</p>
<p>144b.1</p>'jig rten byis pas mthong nas su/ /mchod pa'i yul las mi mkhas pas/ /de nyid lan ni mchod byar shes/ /gan d+ha ra ba ni nges par yang / /skyon dang yon tan rtog dang ldan/ /des na sangs rgyas bcom ldan la/ /dad kyi lha chen sogs la min/ /bram zes smras pa/ kye gan d+ha ra ba re zhig sangs
<p>144b.2</p>rgyas zhes bya ba 'di su zhig yin dge bsnyen gyis smras pa/ /shAkya'i rigs su legs 'khrungs pa/ /kun mkhyen nyes pa kun las rgyal/ /sems can kun la phan bzhed pa/ /drang srong chen po sangs rgyas yin/ /bram zes smras pa/ gal te sangs rgyas drang srong chen po yin par shes na/ 
<p>144b.3</p>gzhan la gnod pa byed pa de mchod par bya ba ma yin par smra 'am/ 'di la 'pho ba dang / me 'bar ba dang / rgyas pa dang / gnas 'jog dang / rgyun shes dang / phur bu gsum pa dang / rgyun shes kyi bu la sogs pa drang srong chen po rnams kyis dmod pa 'debs so zhes 'jig rten na grags so/ /gal
<p>144b.4</p>te sangs rgyas de drang srong chen por gyur na nges par des kyang dmod pa 'debs par byed par 'gyur ro/ /dge bsnyen gyis rna ba bkag nas smras pa/ sdig par ma gyur cig /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni dmod pa 'debs par mi mdzad do/ /bram zes smras pa/ sdig pa zhi bar gyur cig ces 'dir
<p>144b.5</p>ci'i phyir smra/ gal te sangs rgyas dmod pa 'debs par mdzad na ni/ de yang dag par 'tshe ba can du 'gyur ro/ 'on te su la yang dmod pa mi 'debs na sangs rgyas 'di la mthu ci yang med do/ /de nas bram ze de dag rnams kyis gnyis ka ltar 'gal ba'i tshig gis gan d+ha ra ba khyad par du
<p>144b.6</p>bsad nas gsang mthon pos brgyad par brtsams so/ /dge bsnyen des ma 'khrul pa nyid du smras pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mthu chen po mi mnga' ba yang ma yin mod kyi 'on kyang dmod pa'i rgyu dang bral bas gang la yang dmod pa mi mdzad do/ /bram ze chen po ltos shig /chags can gang la
<p>144b.7</p>kun du chags/ /de dang bral na de khros te/ /bya dang bya min rnam rmongs pa/ /phyi nas dmod pa gtong bar 'gyur/ /de bzhin gshegs pa 'dod chags bral/ /rmongs pa dang bral khro las rgyal/ sems can thams cad phan mdzad na/ /de ni dmod pa ji ltar mdzad/ /de nas bram ze de rnams yid la
<p>145a</p>
<p>145a.1</p>bzung ba'i rgyu rnams rjes su dpog cing dge bsnyen de la smras pa/ kye gan d+ha rab gal te sangs rgyas dmod pa mi byed na/ nges par phan 'dogs par yang mi byed do/ /dmod pa dang phan 'dogs pa'i nus pa dang bral na ni/ drang srong chen por yang mi 'gyur ro/ /dge bsnyen gyis
<p>145a.2</p>smras pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dmod pa'i nus pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni de ltar bden mod kyi/ 'on kyang phan 'dogs par ni spyod pa nyid yin te/ /khyed rnams kyang ltos shig /gzhan gyi sdug bsngal la sdar bas/ /de ni dmod pa mi mdzad kyi/ /'jig rten phan 'dogs brtson pas na/ /phan par
<p>145a.3</p>yang ni mdzad pa yin/ /rga nad 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal gyis/ /dang gis 'jig rten sdug bsngal na/ /rma la lan tshwa ji bzhin du/ /mkhas pa su zhig dmod pa 'debs/ /de yang byams pa la gnas shing / /rtag tu snying rje'i bdag nyid can/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung bsil ba'i/ /chu yis
<p>145a.4</p>'jig rten tshim par mdzad/ /de nas bram ze de rnams yud tsam zhig mgo thur du smad nas bsams te/ dge bsnyan de la rjes dang bcas pa'i mig gdangs pas bltas te/ smras pa kye gan d+ha rab shin tu brtags pa'i gnas rnyed nas khyod kyis rab tu dad pas bdag cag ngo mtshar du byas so/ /mang du smrang
<p>145a.5</p>pas ci zhig bya ste/ gan d+ha ra zhes bya ba'i yi ge ni don phyin ci ma log par grags pa yin te/ ci'i phyir zhe na/ go zhes bya ba sa ru bshad/ /sa de gang zhig yang dag 'dzin/ /skyes bu dam pa de rnams ni/ dam pa sa 'dzin zhes bshad do/ /ci'i phyir na sa 'di ni/ /khyed cag rnams kyis 'dzin mi byed/ /
<p>145a.6</p>gang phyir khyed kyi yon tan bsngags/ /mgon po sangs rgyas la brten yin/ /de nas dge bsnyen des bram ze rnams kyi sems snod du rung bar byas par shes te/ da ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bshad pa'i dus yin no snyam nas/ yang dag par dga' ba'i bzhin gyis gzengs bstod de smras pa/ gang
<p>145a.7</p>khyed rnams sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la dad pa skyes par gyur pas bdag ni mchog tu yang dga' ba skyes par gyur mod kyi/ 'on kyang dad pa 'di nyid 'phel bar bya ba'i phyir yon tan dang skyon gyi mtshan nyid rjes su dran par bya ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang tshe 'gro ba yon tan rab rtog tshe/ /rgyal ba yon
<p>145b</p>
<p>145b.1</p>tan rgya mtsho gcig pur mthong / /zhi dang dga' ba skyes par gyur mod kyi/ /tshul khrims ting 'dzin shes rab kyis/ /sangs rgyas dang mnyam gang na'ang yod ma yin/ /dper na ri rab mnyam pa'i ri ni med/ /rgya mtsho mnyam pa'i mtsho ni yod ma yin/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas dang mnyam sa stengs sam/ /mkha'
<p>145b.2</p>la lus can mchog de yod ma yin/ /shAkya'i khyu mchog des ni gang phyir dal bas dka' bar ma zhugs ci zhig yod/ /thub pas phan pa'i don du lan mang dgongs te ma gzigs de ni gang zhig yod/ /de la skyabs song drang srong des ni phan gdags ma byas de ni gang zhig yod/ /'di nas des
<p>145b.3</p>gsungs lam la rab gnas nyon mongs dgra bcom de ni su zhig yod/ /mu stegs kun las rgyal de bde bar gshegs zhes yon tan rnams rgyas dri med grags pa'i kha bye gzhan su yod/ /phug na seng ge lta bur lha yul sa stengs dag na 'jigs med rang gi gsung mchog sgrogs pa gzhan su
<p>145b.4</p>yod/ /rtag tu yid 'ong gsung gis las dang nyon mongs dag gi gnas skabs rjes su ston pa mdzad pa'ang gzhan su yod/ /gang gis mchod rten mkha' la sprin dkar lta bur 'gro ba yang dag brgyan pa 'ga' yang 'di na yod ma yin/ /de nas bram ze de rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan gyi
<p>145b.5</p>bsngags pa thos pa dang / sangs rgyas la mngon par dad par gyur to/ /'dis ci zhig ston pa yin zhe na/ de ltar sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thos pas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par dang par shes pas/ dad pa la ni gzhan rnams kyang yang dag par gzhug par bya'o zhes nye bar ston pa'i mdo brtsams
<p>145b.6</p>pa yin no/ /de yang dge slong dag khyed rnams kyis gang rjes su brtse ba dang / gang snying brtse bar bya'o zhes rgya cher gsungs pa'i phyir te/ sangs rgyas mchog la gsungs pa'i yon tan gyi phan yon gyi mdo sde dag la yang nye bar sbyar bar bya'o/ /gus par byas te chos nyan pa la yang brjod par bya'o/ /
<p>145b.7</p>yang 'dis ci zhig ston ce na/ de ltar sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thos pa don gzhan la mngon par zhen pa'i bram ze rnams kyang bcom ldan 'das la mngon par dad par 'gyur na/ sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thos pas rna dkrugs pa lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ khyed rnams sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thos pas dad
<p>146a</p>
<p>146a.1</p>pa rnam par 'phel bar ci'i phyir mi 'gyur te/ de bas na sangs rgyas dang / sangs rgyas kyi bka' dag gi bsngags pa mnyan par shin tu 'dod pa'i khyim na gnas pa dang / rab tu byung ba khyed rnams kyis ma yengs par mnyan par bya'o zhes 'di ni yang dag par skul bar byed pa yin no/ /
<p>146a.2</p>sangs rgyas mchog gi dpe ste dang po'o/ /rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po d+harma shrI b+ha dra dang / lo tsA ba ban de tshul khrims yon tan gyis bsgyur cing / dge slong rin chen bzang pos bcos nas zhus te gtan la phab pa//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ a sho ka mu kha nA
<p>146a.3</p>ga bi na ya pa ri ts+tshi daH/ bod skad du/ mya ngan med pa'i sgo nas klu btul ba'i le'u'o/ /'di ltar rjes su thos te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mya ngan las 'das nas lo brgya lon pa na/ grong khyer pa ta li pu trar rgyal po mya ngan med ces bya ba 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i bzhi cha la dbang
<p>146a.4</p>byed pa zhig byung bar gyur to/ /des nor gyi don du tshong pa lnga brgya bkug nas smras pa/ shes ldan dag khyed song la rgya mtsho chen po nas rin po che sna tshogs pa long la shog shig /gang gi tshe de dag rim gyis song ste rgya mtsho chen por phyin nas/ rin po che dang / gser dang / dngul dang / rdo rje dang / bai DUr+ya
<p>146a.5</p>dang / shang ka shi la dang / bye ru la sogs pa rin po che'i tshogs du mas de dag gi gru yongs su bkang ste 'dzam bu'i gling du phyogs te chas so/ /de dag log nas 'ongs pa na rgya mtsho'i dkyil du klus gru bcom nas/ de nas tshong pa de dag srog gi lhag ma 'ba' zhig dang grus 'ongs te/ gang gi tshe rim
<p>146a.6</p>gyis grong khyer pa ta li pu trar phyin pa dang / rgyal po mya ngan med kyis tshong pa rnams 'ongs so zhes thos so/ /de skad ces bya ste/ rtswa yis me ni ngoms med sreg /rgya mtsho chu yis ngoms pa med/ /'dir ni lha yul yid 'ong bas/ /'gro rnams dbang drug ngoms pa med/ /ces bya ba yin pas de
<p>146a.7</p>'dod pa'i rgyus sems bskyed cing nor du ma dgram pa'i gnas bya'o snyam du bsams te/ de nas de'i rdzing bu dang bcas pa'i skyed mos tshal du gnas rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan pa/ ba dan dang rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba bla re dang gos kyis spras par yid du 'ong ba'i spos rnams ni gtul/ gangs ltar
<p>146b</p>
<p>146b.1</p>bsal ba'i chus gang ba'i rdzing bu na shel lta bu'i phye ma dang ldan pa ut+pa la dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu ta dang / puN+Da rI ka rnams kyis khebs pa/ ngang pa dang /khu byug dang / rma bya dang / ne tso dang / ri skegs dang /ngur ba dang / ka la ping ka dang / shang shang te'u dag bya skad snyan pa sgrogs pas
<p>146b.2</p>nyams dga' ba/ pi wang dang / gling bu dang / rdza rnga dang / sgra bzangs dang / 'khar rnga dang / pa Ta ha dang / rnga bo che dang / dung rnams rgyun du rdung ba/ blon po dang / grong mi dang / ljongs kyi mi dang / skye bo rnams ni 'dus/ dge sbyong dang / bram ze dang / kun du rgyu dang / gcer bu pa dang / kun du 'tsho

<p>146b.5</p>pos smras pa/ gang gis gru bcom par gyur/ tshong pa rnams kyis smras pa ba tshwa can gyi rgya mtsho na gnas pa'i klus bcom lags so/ /rgyal pos smras pa/ bdag gis dus 'dir ji ltar bsgrub par bya/ tshong pa rnams kyis smras pa/ lha 'di yongs su btsal du gsol/ /gal

<p>147a</p>
<p>147a.1</p>ngan med/ /rab tu drag cing btsan pa yis/ /nor khyer mtshor gnas gang yin pa/ /de dag 'dir ni myur ba ru/ /nga yi drung du bskyal bar gyis/ /zhes yi ger bris te/ zangs ma'i byang bu de rgya mtshor bskyur ro/ /de nas klu ma rangs nas/ rgya mtsho nas slar 'dzam bu'i gling du
<p>147a.2</p>bskyur ro/ /de nas rgyal po'i pho nyas zangs ma'i byang bu de blangs nas slar pa ta li pu trar 'ongs te/ rgyal po la skabs de bsnyad pa dang / de nas rgyal po mya ngan med sems khong du chud nas mtshan mo stan gyi steng du nyal te/ ji ltar 'di la bsgrub par bya snyam du sems so/ /de nas nam mkha'i dkyil
<p>147a.3</p>na gnas pa'i lhas rgyal po la smras pa/ rgyal po chen po sdug bsngal ma byed cig /'jig rten gsum mchog lha mi'i mchod/ /stobs phyug chu srin rgyal mtshan can/ /mthar byed bde gshegs sku gdung la/ /mchod pa rnams kyis rab mchod gyis/ /de rjes khyod kyi dgos 'grub 'gyur/ /lha
<p>147a.4</p>gnyis pas smras pa/ gang zhig bya min rgyal chen mya ngan ma mdzad par/ /sngags dang rig sngags sman sbyor mi bgyid par/ /mi dbang dbang du bya bar nus 'gyur ba/ /bde gshegs bstan la lhag par gus pa yis/ /de yis klu rgyal gang yin dbang du 'gyur/ /de nas zhag gnyis pa la rgyal po mya
<p>147a.5</p>ngan med skra bkrus te/ gos dkar po bgos nas dri dang / me tog dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa rnams thogs nas tshig 'di skad ces smras so/ /phyogs mtshams mkha' bzhugs rdzu 'phrul ldan/ /shar gyi phyogs dang gzhan bzhugs la/ /bdag ni gsol 'debs spyan 'dren gyis/ /bdag la
<p>147a.6</p>thugs rjes gzung du gsol/ /rgyal pos de skad ces smras ma thag tu shar phyogs dang lho phyogs dang nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs rnams nas dgra bcom pa stong phrag drug cu byon zhing 'dus par gyur to/ /rgyal pos me tog dang / spos dang / dri dang / byug pa rnams thogs nas/ de bzhin gshegs
<p>147a.7</p>pa'i sku gdung la mchod pa byas te/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la mngon par bstod pa/ na ba dang ni rgas dang sdug phongs gzhan yang 'chi gzigs nas/ /rgyal bas yul dang 'byor pa btsun mo'i 'khor dang nye du spangs/ /sa bdag zas gtsang drung gshegs bskrad nas rgyal po'i dpal spangs pa/ /bcom ldan de la
<p>147b</p>
<p>147b.1</p>bdag gus dang bas de yi sku gdung mchod/ /gang gi stobs kyis bdud ni shin tu stobs ldan blta bar dka' rnams bcom/ gang gis bA ra NA sIr 'khor lo legs bskor srid spangs zhi bar mdzad/ /gang gis lnga sde skye ba'i sdug bsngal gyis gdungs 'chi ba bkrol/ /shAkya thub de'i sku gdung dpe
<p>147b.2</p>med 'di la bdag gis yang dag mchod/ /gang zhig gang du mya ngan 'das gshegs 'dir ni mar me 'gags pa bzhin/ /glang po stong stobs las lhag de ni mi rtag stobs kyis phye mar brlags/ /sa bdag mchog gis cha brgyad mnyam bgos sku gdung yang dag mchod gyur pa/ /de yis sku gdung dpe med
<p>147b.3</p>'di ni 'jig rten mkhas pas yang dag mchod/ /de nas dge slong gi dge 'dun la gdugs tshod drangs nas mchod do/ /de nas rgyal pos tshe dang ldan pa dbang po la smras pa/ 'phags pa ci zhig mchog tu bsgrub par bgyi/ tshe dang ldan pa dbang pos smras pa/ rgyal po chen po dang po ni khyod kyi gzugs/ 
<p>147b.4</p>gnyis pa klu'i gzugs te/ sku gzugs legs pa gnyis mdzod la gser gyi snod chen po byas pa'i nang du de gnyis stsol cig dang de las mngon sum du gzigs par 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du byas te phyis rgyal pos bltas pa dang / klu'i gzugs 'dug pa la rgyal po'i gzugs phyag byed
<p>147b.5</p>pa rgyal pos mthong ngo / /rgyal po yid la gcags par gyur pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa dbang pos smras pa/ rgyal po chen po dus 'dir yang dang yang du nyi ma re re la khyad par gzigs par 'gyur ro/ /ji lta ji ltar rgyal pos de bzhin gshegs pa la me tog dang / phreng ba dang / dri dang / spos dang / 
<p>147b.6</p>byug pa rnams kyis mchod cing dge slong gi dge 'dun la yang rang gi lag nas bza' ba dang bca' ba rnams tshim par bstabs shing rgya cher mchod par byas te/ chos kyang gus par mnyan pa de lta de ltar rgyal po'i gzugs langs pa la klu'i gzugs phyag 'tshal bar gyur to/ /yang de'i rjes la
<p>147b.7</p>klu'i gzugs de yan lag thams cad kyis rgyal po'i gzugs la phyag 'tshal bar gyur pa mthong bas des rgyal po yid rab tu dga' bar gyur te/ tshe dang ldan pa dbang po la smras pa/ kye ma dkon mchog gsum mchod pa'i/ /'bras bu ci 'dra 'di la gzigs/ /rgya mtsho'i nang na gnas pa'i
<p>148a</p>
<p>148a.1</p>klu/ /bdag gis btul zhing 'di dbang bgyis/ /blo gros chung ba'i mi rnams kyang / /su zhig sangs rgyas mchod mi bgyid/ /gang zhig 'bras bu 'phral bskyed la/ /su zhig yid kyis sems mi bgyid/ /bdag nyid che ba thob 'dod pa'i/ /lha rnams dang ni mi rnams kyis/ /

<p>148a.3</p>pos yi ge de spyi bos blangs so/ /de nas des rgyal po la lan mang du lha tshong pa de dag 'dir rdzongs shig /so so'i rin po che gang lags pa bskur la slar brdzong ngo zhes smras pa dang / de nas rgyal po'i pho nya slar 'ongs nas rgyal po la phrin de smras pa dang / de nas rgyal pos tshong pa rnams bos nas smras pa khyed
<p>148a.4</p>cag song la so so'i rin po che gang yin pa long la slar shog shig /de nas gnas brtan dbang pos rgyal po la brgyad pa/ chos kyi rgyal po las rdul ngan pa 'bul bar byed pa yin mod/ de nas rgyal pos gnas brtan dbang po la smras pa/ slob dpon 'o na ji ltar bsgrub par bgyi/ gnas brtan dbang

<p>148a.7</p>khyad par dang / rgyal po'i rnam par 'phrul pa mthong bar 'dod pa dag zhag bdun pa la rgyal po'i pho brang du shog shig /de nas rgyal pos zhag bdun pa la grong khyer pa rnams dang / blon po dang / grong rdal dang / ljongs kyi mis yongs su gang bar bskor te/ rgyal po'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang / mthu
<p>148b</p>
<p>148b.1</p>chen po dang / 'byor pa chen pos 'khor gyi khyams su song nas seng ge'i khri la 'dug go /de nas klu'i rgyal po klu du mas yongs su bskor nas mi'i cha byad du sprul te/ rang rang gi phrag pa la rin po che'i khur thogs nas rgyal po chen po mya ngan med ga la ba der song ste phyin nas khur rnams phog nas rkang pa gnyis la
<p>148b.2</p>phyag byas so/ /skye bo'i tshogs chen po de ngo mtshar du gyur te/ sngon ma mthong ba mthong ngo zhes ca co'i sgra bsgrags te 'di skad ces smras so/ /'di 'dra'i bsod nams stobs kyis ni/ /rgyal po yongs su gzung bar gyur/ /skye bo rnams ni ngo mtshar skyes/ /lha rnams dang ni 'di ru yang / /phun sum
<p>148b.3</p>tshogs pa 'dod pa yis/ /bsod nams gang yin zhes bya ba/ /'di lta'i bye brag su mi sgrub/ /bsam du med pa'ang gang bsams pa/ /don de 'bad pa med pa ru/ /mi rnams la ni 'bras bur smin/ /rkang thang glang chen myos pa dang / /rta dang shing rtas rgya mtshon/ /gnas pa'i klu dang lhan cig g.yul/ /
<p>148b.4</p>stobs chen sna tshogs mtshon chas min/ /sdug bsngal mgo bo'i gdengs ka can/ /bsod nams rang bzhin 'di 'dra ba'i/ /zhags pa yi ni nges bcings nas/ /mya ngan med rgyal zhal mthong ba/ /bka' drin bsams pas rjes mthun 'jug /des kyang de dag sna tshogs pa'i dka'
<p>148b.5</p>bas 'ongs pa mthong nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bka'i yon tan rjes su brjod pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad gsungs/ /bsod nams me yis mi 'tshig ste/ /rlung gis 'jig par mi 'gyur ro/ /bsod nams chu yis 'ju mi 'gyur/ /sa bzhin du ni khyer mi 'gyur/ /rgyal po dang ni
<p>148b.6</p>chom rkun gyis/ /dbrog tu med par bsod nams gnas/ /skyes pa dang ni bud med kyis/ /dbrog par nus pa ma yin no/ /bsod nams bde ba skyed pa'i gter/ /'dir ni lus par mi 'gyur te/ /gang dang gang du skyes pa ru/ /de dang der ni rjes su 'brang / /de nas blon po gzhan zhig ngo mtshar
<p>148b.7</p>skyes nas 'di skad ces smras so/ /yongs su bskor ba'i 'khor dbus na/ /bsod nams rgyan gyis rgyal po mdzes/ /skar ma'i tshogs kyis yongs bskor pa'i/ /ston ka yi ni zla ba bzhin/ /chu dang mkha' la 'gro ba'i klu/ /bsod nams kyis ni nges pham byas/ /sa la gnas pa'i dgra yi
<p>149a</p>
<p>149a.1</p>tshogs/ /bsod nams kyis ni zad par byed/ /ji ltar yid la bsams pa yi/ /bde ba bsod nams kyis thob byed/ /bsod nams 'di ni bsags pa ru/ /sems dang ldan pa su mi byed/ /sbas pas grub ces bya ba'i blon pos smras pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'di skad
<p>149a.2</p>gsungs/ /bsod nams 'di ni dag byed yin/ /bsod nams nges par 'bab stegs te/ /mtho ris su ni 'gro ba'i lam/ /mi rnams bdes rol bsod nams yin/ /bsod nams rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi/ /mya ngan 'das par 'gro ba'i lam/ /yang blon po gsum pa gzhan zhig gis smras pa/ 
<p>149a.3</p>bsod nams kyis ni khyod kyi bzhin/ /zla ba dang ba shar dang mtshungs/ /rgya mtsho'i nang du zhugs pa yang / /bsod nams kyis ni stor ma mchis/ /yid du 'ong ba thob byed pas/ /bsod nams 'gro bas phyag byar 'os/ /bsod nams yang dag bsags pa la/ /'bad par mi rnams su byed pa/ /bsod
<p>149a.4</p>nams kyis rgyal skyes bu ni/ /rta yis ma yin glang pos min/ /shing rtas bsod nams las rgyal min/ /mda' dang ral gris ma yin no/ /nor rnams dang ni yul dang ni/ /g.yul gyis bsod nams las rgyal min/ /bsod nams kyis ni rgyal ba la/ /rigs dang stobs dang gzugs kyis min/ /bsod
<p>149a.5</p>nams kyis 'phags mi rnams ni/ /sa rnams gsum gyi steng na gnas/ /bsod nams mi rnams gnas yin te/ /bsod nams thar pa thob byed mchog /bsod nams 'jig rten grags byed yin/ /de phyir bla med bsod nams btsal/ /mtho ris thob byed ngan song spong / /mi yis rtag tu bsten
<p>149a.6</p>bya ste/ /mkhas pas bsod nams bya ba yin/ /de nas rgyal pos tshong pa de dag rnams la smras pa/ khyed rang rang gi rin po che rnams khyer cig /de nas de dag gis blangs nas rgyal po la rab tu bstabs te/ gzhan yang lha'i sbyor bas lags kyi/ /lha'i de dag legs par snoms shig /rgyal pos
<p>149a.7</p>smras pa/ bdag la cung zad kyang dgos pa med kyis khyer la song la the tshom med par longs spyod cig /de nas rgyal pos rab tu dga' ba'i yid kyis dkon mchog la bstod pa 'di skad ces smras so/ /e ma sangs rgyas e ma'o chos/ /e ma'o bstan pa phun sum tshogs/ /sa rdul snyim gang phul
<p>149b</p>
<p>149b.1</p>ba yi/ /rnam par smin pa 'di 'dra thob/ /de nas rgyal pos yang smras pa/ /ding 'dir klu ni bdag dbang gyur/ /thub chen khyod kyi bka' drin las/ /legs spyod rgyal po bdag bgyid pa/ /bdag gi skye ba 'bras bcas lags/ /yon tan mchog ldan thub pa yi/ /bstan mchog 'di la su
<p>149b.2</p>mi 'jug /dper na sa bon rdul btab pas/ /'bras bu chen po skyed byed na/ /rin chen phul ba smos ci 'tshal/ /de nas klu chos la sbyar nas slar song ngo / /mya ngan med pa'i sgo nas klu btul ba'i le'u rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po gnas brtan a dzi ta shrI b+ha dra dang / dge slong
<p>149b.3</p>shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur ba'o//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ saM g+ha man+t+ra/ bod skad du/ dge 'dun spyan drang ba/ sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mgon po kun mkhyen rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /dri ma med pa zab mo'i chos/ /yon tan che ldan dge 'dun te/ /dkon mchog
<p>149b.4</p>gsum la bdag phyag 'tshal/ /dpal shAkya'i rigs chen po dam pa gtsang ma dpal shAkya'i mgon po thub pa sangs rgyas nyid/ sa la mdzad pa mtha' dag rdzogs te/ 'jig rten du yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa na/ dpal dga' ba'i bshes gnyen zhes bya ba'i sdom brtson rnam par thar pa
<p>149b.5</p>brgyad la bsam gtan pa mngon par shes pa drug pa 'jig rten las 'das pa zhig byung bar gyur to/ /de yang 'di ltar thos te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas lo brgyad brgya 'das pa de'i tshe de'i dus na yul shi bi'i grong du/ rgyal po rnam par rgyal ba'i sde'i dus su/ dga' ba'i
<p>149b.6</p>bshes gnyen zhes bya ba'i dge slong byung ste/ dge slong de yang dgra bcom pa/ rnam par thar pa brgyad la bsam gtan pa/ mngon par shes pa drug dang ldan pa rdzu 'phrul chen po can/ mthu chen po dang ldan pa ste/ de yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i dus su dge slong gi dge 'dun 'dus pa la/ 
<p>149b.7</p>ma 'ongs pa'i don lung bstan pa dge slong rnams kyis ma shes te/ gnas brtan dga' ba'i bshes gnyen la yongs su dris pa/ gnas brtan bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa yun ji srid cig gnas zhes so/ /de nyid la smras pa mar 'bri ba'i tshe lo bcu pa nas/ yar 'phel ba'i
<p>150a</p>
<p>150a.1</p>tshe lo drug khri pa'i bar de srid du gnas so/ /de'i 'og tu lo stong phrag bcur dbu skra sha la sogs pa'i ring bsrel gnas par 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu lo stong phrag bcur rang sangs rgyas rnams 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas lo brgyad khri pa la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
<p>150a.2</p>chen po byams pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /bcom ldan 'das byams pa de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de'i bstan pa la/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa la sangs rgyas la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun
<p>150a.3</p>pa'am/ chos la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun pa 'am/ dge 'dun la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun pa de thams cad sangs rgyas byams pa'i bstan pa la 'dus pa gsum par yongs su mya ngan las 'das par 'gyur ro/ /de la sangs rgyas la dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun pa gang zhe na/ tha na nas tsam gyi sangs rgyas ri mor bris
<p>150a.4</p>pa dang / glegs bam bris pa dang / 'tsho ba'i rgyu bsgrubs pa'o/ /chos la bskrun pa gang zhe na/ nyan thos kyis bshad pa 'am/ byang chub sems dpas bshad pa'am/ sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa'ang rung ste/ tha na tshigs su bcad pa gcig tsam bzung ba'o/ /dge 'dun la bskrun pa gang zhe na/ 
<p>150a.5</p>phyogs pa la sogs pa spyan drangs pa dang / tha na a ru ra gcig tsam phul ba'o/ /de skad thos nas dge slong de rnams ngus pa dang / gnas brtan gyis dbugs phyung ba/ dge slong rnams ma ngu shig /smre sngags ma 'don shig /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das kyis yongs su mya ngan las 'das
<p>150a.6</p>pa'i dus kyi tshe/ /nyan thos chen po bcu drug po rnams kyi phyag tu dam pa'i chos gtad par gyur te/ sbyin pa po rnams dang sbyin bdag rnams la rjes su brtse ba'i phyir dang / yon yongs su sbyong ba'i phyir du'o/ /de skad ces smras pa dang / dge slong de rnams kyis gnas brtan dga' ba'i bshes
<p>150a.7</p>gnyen la 'di skad ces smras so/ /gnas brtan bdag cag rnams kyis gnas brtan chen po bcu drug po de dag rnams kyi mtshan dang / de dag gang du bzhugs pa mi shes so/ /gnas brtan gyis smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa rnams dang po re zhig gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza piN+Di la b+ha ra d+h+wa dza/bsod
<p>150b</p>
<p>150b.1</p>snyoms len zhes bya ba/ dgra bcom pa stong dang thabs cig tu nub [(]gyi [,]kyi [)]ba lang spyod na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan gser be'u zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa lnga brgya dang thabs cig tu byang phyogs kha che'i yul na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa drug brgya dang thabs
<p>150b.2</p>cig tu shar gyi lus 'phags gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan mi phyed pa zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa bdun brgya dang / ka na ka bat+sa thabs cig tu byang gi sgra mi snyan gyi gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan ba ku la zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa brgyad brgya dang thabs cig tu dzam+bu'i gling na bzhugs so/ /
<p>150b.3</p>gnas brtan bzang po zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa dgu brgya dang thabs cig tu a b+he d+ya zangs gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan nag po 'char ka zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa stong dang thabs cig tu sing ha la'i gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan bklI pu tra zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa brgya phrag bcu gcig dang / 
<p>150b.4</p>thabs cig tu b+ha dra pa Na ba'i gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan sbed byed ces bya ba dgra bcom pa stong phrag bcu gnyis dang kA lo da yI thabs cig tu ri spos kyi ngad ldang na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan lam bsten zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa brgya phrag bcu gsum dang thabs cig tu sum cu rtsa gsum na
<p>150b.5</p>bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan sgra gcan 'dzin ma grags 'dzin dang / go pa ka lhan cig dgra bcom pa stong phrag bcu bzhi dang thabs cig tu pri yad+gu'i gling na bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan nags na gnas pAn+tha ka zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa brgya phrag bcu dang thabs cig tu ri skya bo la bzhugs so/ /gnas
<p>150b.6</p>brtan yan lag 'byung zhes bya ba rA hu la dgra bcom pa brgya phrag bcu gsum dang thabs cig tu ri ngos yangs la bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan klu'i sde zhes bya ba dgra bcom pa brgya phrag bcu bzhi pa na gA pI dang thabs cig tu lus 'phags ri la bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan ma pham pa zhes bya ba dgra
<p>150b.7</p>bcom ang gi ta pa lnga brgya dang thabs cig tu bya rgod phung po'i ri la bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan lam phran tsU DA paN+Tha bsten zhes bya ba dgra nA ga sen bcom pa brgya phrag bcu drug dang thabs cig tu ri gshol mda' 'dzin la bzhugs so/ /gnas brtan bcu drug a dzi ta po de rnams la shin
<p>151a</p>
<p>151a.1</p>tu chung ba'i yon phul yang 'bras bu chen por 'gyur ro/ /de ltar yang / sems can gang zhig bdag bstan la/ /skra tsam rab tu sbyin byed pa/ /bskal pa stong phrag brgyad cur ni/ /longs spyod chen po'i 'bras chen dang / /gzugs dang nad med bde spyod cing / /de bzhin 'dod
<p>151a.2</p>pa'i dbang phyug dang / /mthar yang bla med byang chub kyi/ /'bras bu mngon du thob par 'gyur/ /de lta'i 'bras bu che thos nas/ /su zhig bsod nams byed mi 'gyur/ /gaN+Di'i dus ston chags bral dus ston dang / /phyogs pa spyan drang la sogs dag kyang bya/ /da ni chags bral rnams kyi
<p>151a.3</p>mchod pa'i cho ga brjod par bya ste/ dang po re zhig nyi ma dang po la/ rje btsun sangs rgyas kyi sku khri mtho ba la bzhugs su gsol te/ nyi ma 'char ka'i dus su me tog la sogs pa rnams kyis yang dag par mchod de/ de'i spyan sngar maN+Dal gsum dang / na mo bud+d+hA ya/ na mo d+harmA ya/ na maH
<p>151a.4</p>saM g+hA ya zhes bya ste gnas lngar me tog la sogs pa rnams dbul bar bya'o/ /de nas rang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po dang / 'phrog ma la oM yig sngon du 'gro ba'i bzhi ba'i mtha' can gyis me tog la sogs pa dbul bar bya'o/ /sangs rgyas la sogs pa'i maN+Dal
<p>151a.5</p>gsum gyi de ma thag tu/ chu tshod bdun pa'i don du spyan drang bar bya ste/ tshig 'di sngon du 'gro bas so/ /nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling na bzhugs pa'i gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza bsod snyoms len thub pa dge slong stong phrag gis yongs su bskor ba rnams/ sbyin pa'i bdag po ming 'di zhes bya bas sang zhal
<p>151a.6</p>zas la chu tshod bdun pa'i don du spyan drang bar bgyi'o/ /zhabs la mchod yon dang zhabs kyi chu sngon du 'gro bas so/ gnas brtan gser be'u zhes bya ba dge slong lnga brgyas yongs su bskor ba de/ bdag dang sbyin pa'i bdag po ming 'di zhes bya bas song chu tshod bdun pa'i don du zhabs la mchod yon la
<p>151a.7</p>sogs pa sngon du 'gro bas spyan drang par bgyi'o/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun dang rang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po dang / /'phrog ma la yang mchod yon sngon du 'gro bas/ bdag dang sbyin pa'i bdag pos sang zhal zas la spyan drang bar bgyi'o/ /nyi
<p>151b</p>
<p>151b.1</p>ma phyi ma la snga bar chu klung gi 'gram dang skyed mos tshal dang mchod rten gyi gnas dang nye ba 'am/ gzhan du yang rung ste phyogs gtsang mar so so'i rnam pa sngon du 'gro ba la dbul ba la sogs pa bya ba'o/ /'di ltar bya ste/ nub kyi ba lang spyod kyi gling na bzhugs pa'i gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza bsod
<p>151b.2</p>snyoms len thub pa dgra bcom dge slong stong gis bskor ba de/ bdag che ge mo zhes bya ba dang sbyin pa'i bdag pos chu tshod bdun pa'i don du gzung lags kyi stan 'di la bdag rjes su gzung ba'i slad du bzhugs su gsol/ zhabs bsil 'di dang zhabs la mchod yon 'di dag zhabs dag la
<p>151b.3</p>dbul bar bgyi'o/ /dUrba ma nyams pa dang dri dang me tog dang bcas pa'i rung ba'i chu yis zhabs dag bkru bar bgyi'o/ /de nas so so la gdan phul te ji lta bar bzhugs pa la zhal zas la sogs pa dang yid las byung ba'i 'byor pa lha rdzas kyi dri dang me tog dang bdug pa dang sgron me dang gos dang
<p>151b.4</p>gdugs dang ba dan la sogs pa ji ltar 'byor pa dbul bar bya ste/ tshig 'di yis so/ /gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza bsod snyoms len thub pa dgra bcom pa stong gis bskor ba la zhal zas la sogs pa sna tshogs pa'i tshod ma dang khur ba dang bshos dang zho la sogs pa dang bcas pa rung ba'i dri
<p>151b.5</p>bzang po'i chus gang ba'i bum pa dang lha rdzas gya nom pa me tog dang bdug pa la sogs pa phul ba 'di bdag che ge mo dang sbyin pa'i bdag po dang sems can thams cad kyis thams cad gzigs pa bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thob par 'dod pas dbul bar bgyi'o/ /
<p>151b.6</p>gnas brtan gnyis pa gser be'u zhes bya ba dge slong lnga brgyas yongs su bskor ba de/ bdag ming 'di zhes bya ba dang / sbyin pa'i bdag pos chu tshod bdun pa'i don du gzung lags kyi/ stan phul ba la bdag rjes su gzung ba'i slad du bzhugs su gsol/ zhabs bsil dang zhabs
<p>151b.7</p>kyi mchod yon 'di zhabs dag la dbul bar bgyi'o/ /dUrba ma nyams pa dang / dri dang / me tog dang bcas pa'i rung ba'i chu yis zhabs dag bkru bar bgyi'o/ /de nas stan gnyis pa phul te/ ji lta bar bzhugs pa la zhal zas la sogs pa yid dang mthun pa'i lha rdzas kyi dri dang me tog
<p>152a</p>
<p>152a.1</p>dang bdug pa dang sgron me dang gos dang gdugs dang ba dan dang rgyal mtshan dang dril bu la sogs pa ji ltar 'byor pa tshig 'dis dbul bar bya'o/ /gnas brtan gser be'u thub pa lnga brgyas bskor ba la zhal zas la sogs pa sna tshogs pa'i tshod ma dang khur ba dang
<p>152a.2</p>bshos dang zho la sogs pa dang bcas pa'i lha rdzas gya nom pa dri bzang po'i rung ba'i chus gang ba'i bum pa dang me tog la sogs pas bdag ming 'di zhes bya ba dang sbyin pa'i bdag po dang sems can thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub thams cad gzigs pa nyid thob cing rab
<p>152a.3</p>tu dgod par 'dod pas dbul bar bgyi'o/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun dang rang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun chen po dang / gnod sbyin mo chen mo 'phrog ma la yang bza' ba la sogs pa sna tshogs pa'i tshod ma dang zho la sogs pa dang khur ba dang bshos dang lha
<p>152a.4</p>rdzas gya nom pa dri zhim po rung ba'i chus gang ba'i bum pa dang me tog la sogs pa 'di yang bdag ming 'di zhes bya ba dang sbyin pa'i bdag pos sems can thams cad bsgral ba'i phyir de rnams la dbul bar bgyi'o/ /bzhes pa yongs su rdzogs pan zhal bsil dang / tsan+dan dang tAm+bu la yang 'bul zhing
<p>152a.5</p>bzod pa gsol bar bya ste/ de skad brjod do/ /gang 'dir bdag gis ma rnyed dang /ma shes pa dang ma tshang ba/ /de yang dgongs chen bzod par gsol/ /zhing dang bsam pa rnam dag las/ /nyung ngu phul yang mi nyung 'gyur/ /bden pa yi ni tshig 'di yis/ /phra mo yang ni rgya cher 'gyur/ /phyag
<p>152a.6</p>'tshal ba yang bya ste/ ston pa'i bstan pa skyong mdzad ri mchog gling dang ning+gi dza lar bzhugs/ /sangs rgyas mnyes pa lhur mdzad nyon mongs ltos 'gro 'joms/ /sems can don ni mchog tu rgyas mdzad sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung / /gnas brtan bcu drug slob mar bcas pa'i zhabs la
<p>152a.7</p>mchog tu phyag 'tshal lo/ /bsod nams yongs su bsngo ba yang bya ste/ bsod nams 'di yis thams cad gzigs pa nyid/ /thob nas nyes pa'i dgra rnams pham byas te/ rga nad 'chi ba'i rlabs chen 'khrugs pa yi/ /srid pa'i mtsho las 'gro ba 'don par shog /ces so/ /
<p>152b</p>
<p>152b.1</p>lcogs brgyad rang bzhin ri bo ni/ /gling dang nye gling yang dag ldan/ /rin chen bdun gyis yang dag dkrigs/ /bla med yon 'di dbul bar bgyi/ /bla ma byang chub sems rnams la/ /'gro bas kun mkhyen thob bya'i phyir/ /rin chen maN+Dal yang dag rdzogs/ /dngos po kun gyis dbul bar bgyi/ /
<p>152b.2</p>de ltar smon lam brjod nas gshegs su gsol te/ /khyed kyis sems can don kun mdzad/ /rjes su mthun pa'i dngos grub stsol/ /sangs rgyas yul du gshegs nas kyang / /slar yang 'byon par mdzad du gsol/ /oM badzra mu swAhA zhes pas gshegs su gsol/ /dge 'dun
<p>152b.3</p>spyan drang ba zhes bya ba 'di dpal 'byor rab brtan gyi phyag dpe rgya dpe las zha lu lo tsA bas sgyur cing zhus so//[ ]@##/ /rgya gar skad du/ s+tha bI ro pa ni man+t+ra NaM/ bod skad du/ gnas brtan spyan drang ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /btsun pa rnams
<p>152b.4</p>dgongs su gsol/ dgongs nas kyang / shel dang / nor bu dang / dngul dang / ku mu ta dang / kha ba'i phung po dang / zla ba'i 'od zer dang / ston gyi chu dang / nam thang ba dang / pad+ma'i rtsa lag ltar dri ma med par mdzod la/ rlung gi stobs kyis shing gi lcug phran bskyod pa dang / smig rgyu dang / 
<p>152b.5</p>sgyu ma dang / rmi lam dang / glog dang / rta'i shing rta'i rdul dang / ba glang gi phru gu'i rna mchog dang / sbrul gyi lce dang / zil pa dang / rgya mtsho bskyod pa'i rlabs ltar g.yo ba'i yid/ skad cig re re la yang mi sdod par 'gro ba rtse gcig pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs kyis yud tsam zhig rgyu ba nang
<p>152b.6</p>du dgag tu gsol/ smras pa/ ri gzar 'bab pa'i dba' rlabs gyur pas kyang / /gang gi dba' rlabs 'gyur la bsgrun med par/ /'jig pa thogs med g.yo ba'i yid de ni/ /yud tsam rtse gcig mdzod cig btsun pa rnams/ /lha yi bu mo yi chad shugs phyung skad cig zim mar byas pa'i
<p>152b.7</p>mig /ring zhing rdzir ldan bkra la 'od 'tsher mig chags lta ba'i g.yo ba yis/ /gang gi thugs ni skye rgyun gcod pa las 'khrungs g.yos par ma gyur pa/ bdud kyi dpung 'joms mkhas gcig thams cad mkhyen pa de la phyag mdzod cig /skye ldan gang zhig bsten na dud 'gro'i skye
<p>153a</p>
<p>153a.1</p>gnas sems can dmyal zhi dang / /yi dgas 'jig rten gnas su 'gro bar mi 'gyur sdug bsngal 'jig byed pa/ /'khor bdag na 'gro ba chen po rnams kyi grogs gyur 'phags gcig po/ /zhi bde 'gro de'i sgor gzhol chos de la ni gus pas brten par mdzod/ /zhi ba'i
<p>153a.2</p>bdag nyid gang zhig bde gshegs gsung rab mthar phyin 'byung smra zhing / /gang la gus par cung zad tsam zhig byin yang sbyin pa 'phel 'gyur la/ ye shes snang bas mun pa zad byas dge slong dge 'dun de la ni/ /nyon mongs gcad pa'i ched du thams cad kyis kyang gus par phyag mdzod
<p>153a.3</p>cig /lcang lo chun po'i skra mang mgo la thogs shing dpung mgo gnyis g.yogs la/ /rang gi 'od zer phyogs mthar 'phro ba rnams kyis 'jig rten kun 'gengs pa/ lha dbang brgya byin cod pan btud de tshangs la phyag byas gang yin de/ /byin nas dga' byas sems kyi ting 'dzin shin tu chen po'i
<p>153a.4</p>'bras bu yin/ /rdo rje 'od 'phro'i phreng bas dpung rgyan 'dres nas mdzes gyur cing / /lha la bka' stsol dbang po mtho ris skyong ba gang yin pa/ /de dag dge ba dag 'byung rnam smin 'gyur dus nyams dga' zhing / /mngon par 'dod pa'i 'bras bu phun sum tshogs pa'i rgyu rnams yin/ /kha nas rgyags
<p>153a.5</p>'gyur dri zhim 'byung zhing mig gi mtha' dmar la/ /dbugs 'byung do shal g.yos pas nu ma 'bur la 'drud byed pa/ /sdu gu lhan cig nor bdag dga' tshal 'dug pa gang yin pa/ /de yang 'gro ba nyams dga' sbyin pa'i bdag nyid chen po yin/ /'brug sgra sgrogs shing sprin rnams chu ni kun du len byed pa/ /
<p>153a.6</p>rlabs 'byung dus na nor bu byi ru dung dang nya phyis 'byung / /rin chen gnas nang chu lha nyid kyi 'byor pas gang bsrung ba/ /der yang rgyu ni sbyin pa mchog ces thub pas bka' stsal to/ /gang yang 'od zer rnams kyis mkha' la skar ma'i 'khor lo zil mnan cing / /ku mu ta yi rdzing yangs rnams su dpal
<p>153a.7</p>ni rab tu rnam phye nas/ /glang po'i mche ba'i dpal dang ldan zhing mtshan mo shin tu rab mdzes pa/ /de yang nges par sbyin pa nyid kyi 'bras bu ro bro mang po yin/ /ri rab rtse la shing rtas lam kha 'dug pa'i rin chen rdo gcog cing / /rta yi rkang lag rnams kyis dgu tshigs chu bo'i rlabs ni gcod byed la/ /
<p>153b</p>
<p>153b.1</p>mun pa bsal phyir nyi mas skar ma zil mnan lham me gang yin pa/ /de rgyu yid kyi ting nge 'dzin gyis bskyed pa'i sbyin par thub pas gsungs/ /rgyal mtshan rtse btags rin chen 'od zer snang bas nam mkha' dmar gyur cing / /rta rmig 'dor bas mkha' la sprin gyi phreng ba dag kyang 'dral byed
<p>153b.2</p>la/ /rnga yab dkar pos g.yabs shing 'khor los sgyur ba song ba gang yin pa/ /'dod pa'i 'bras bu de yang sbyin pas bsgrubs zhes thub pas bka' stsal to/ /gser gyi pad+ma'i rdul gyi bye mas dmar bris mtshor ni khrus byas te/ /de ni nags 'dab bung ba sgra 'byin rnams su nyal ba'i bde rnyed
<p>153b.3</p>nas/ /rig 'dzin chung ma lhan cig 'jigs med mkha' las 'gro ba gang yin pa/ /de yang ser sna 'jil zhing skyon med dga' ba'i sbyin pa'i gzi brjid yin/ /ma la ya yi ri rtser tsan+dan grib mas bsil ba yangs pa dang / /'bigs byed ri dang gangs dang lhun po'i ri dang man da ra ba'i ri bo
<p>153b.4</p>la/ /grub pa'i tshogs chen chung ma lhan cig 'jigs bral dga' ba gang yin pa/ /'dod pa'i 'bras bu tshe 'di'i snying po 'byor pa de yang gtong bas yin/ /bud med rkang gdub 'khrol bas 'grogs nas 'phur ba'i [(]phu [,]phug [)]ron gnas pa yin/ /khang pa mthon po rnams dang 'bigs byed ri rtse
<p>153b.5</p>'gran pa'i ban glang dang / /gdugs dang rnga yab bud med g.yog 'khor rin chen gser dang rta rnams dang / bzang mdzes de dag kun kyang sngon gyi sbyin pa'i dge ba'i rnam smin yin/ ban+du ka ltar rtsa dmar rgun chang gser snod bzang por legs blugs pa/ yongs dag a mra smin gas lta bur
<p>153b.6</p>dri zhim ut+pal 'gying zhing ldem/ /na chung gshin ma nam dgos dus kyis stobs shing yams grangs mang 'drim pa/ /mchog tu dge ba de rgyu sbyin pa yin zhes blo gros dag pas gsungs/ /gser gyi phag skas rked bcings snyan smra 'jam zhing smin ma ya gcig bskyod/ /mig yangs rnar thug
<p>153b.7</p>dkar nag 'byes la skra bkab me tog phreng dkris pa'i/ /na chung bzang mo brla rgyas bdag nyid legs byas rnams kyi bran ltar byed/ /tshogs bsags 'bras de sbyin pa'i che ba nyid ces zas gtsang sras pos gsungs/ /de lta lags pas bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag thugs
<p>154a</p>
<p>154a.1</p>su chud pa shin tu rgyas pa'i chu ltar gyur pa snying po dri ma med pa dang / lha'i skye bo dang klu'i gnas su gyur pa/ tshul khrims 'dren ma ma yin zhing rgya che ba'i chu dang ldan pa/ dge ba la rnam par rtog pa'i zla ba shar ba'i dbang gis/ /ting nge 'dzin sna tshogs rgyas pa'i dus kyi rlabs gyis
<p>154a.2</p>byang chub kyi yan lag skyon med pa'i nor bu mang po kun du g.yengs pa/ sems kyi 'og gzhi la 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'i ri bo chen po brtan pa/ 'bras bu'i bye brag thob pa gang zag chen po'i chu srin rgyu ba/ 'phags pa'i bden pa dang / yang dag par spong ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi
<p>154a.3</p>rkang pa'i shing ljon pas mdzes par byas pa/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i ngogs dang ldan pa/ sgrib pa'i ro mi gnas pa/ sbyangs pa'i yon tan goms pa dag pa'i mu tig gi nya phyis kyi khog lus dang ldan pa/ mngon par rtogs pa'i chos nyid gting mi dpogs shing zab pa/ rgyun mi 'chad par
<p>154a.4</p>klog pa dang kha ton byed pa'i sgra rgya cher 'byung ba/ 'phags pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi rgya mtsho chen po la bdag gsol ba 'tshal lo/ /'di lta ste/ srid pa'i 'gro ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa dum nas dge ba'i sa bon btab pa/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa gzhal med khang gis
<p>154a.5</p>gzhi gcig pur gyur pa/ bzod pa dang des pa dang byams pa dang / tshul khrims dang thos pa dang zhi ba'i gnas/ bdag dang gzhan gyi gzhung gi don gyi de kho na ma lus par rtogs pa/ yongs su shes pas bsgoms pas dran pa nye bar gnas pa yang dag pa'i ye shes mthong bas log
<p>154a.6</p>par lta ba'i rab rib bsal ba/ legs par brjod cing shis la rgya che ba'i mig dang ldan pa skye bo bla ma la bsnyen bkur byed pa dang mngon du smra ba dang / phyag 'tshal ba la sogs pa'i tshul bzang po dang ldan zhing mdongs gsol che bas snyan pa rnams bskyed pa ston gyi zla ba nya ba'i 'od zer dag pa
<p>154a.7</p>lta bu'i yid 'byung ba/ sbyin bdag chen po che ba'i bdag nyid can ming 'di zhes bya ba 'di ni khyim bdag legs sbyin dang / bzang ldan dang / btsun mo'i 'khor gyi bla dang / mu shi la dang / tra du sa dang / go shi la dang / ta pa kar+Ni ka dang / mgon med zas sbyin dang / drag po dang / nag pa dang /
<p>154b</p>
<p>154b.1</p>nam gru la sogs pa dang / gzhan yang bcom ldan 'das la yid mngon par dad pas/ rgyal po gsal rgyal dang / tshangs pas byin dang / rgyal po 'char ka'i bu dang / gtum po rab snang la sogs pa sa'i steng la dbang ba'i sbyin pa las byung ba'i legs par spyad pa'i rjes
<p>154b.2</p>su slob ste/ lus dang / longs spyod dang / srog la sgyu ma dang / smig rgyu dang / dri za'i grong khyer dang / mgal me skor ba dang / rmi lam dang / ri'i 'bab chu ltar g.yo bar ri gnas/ stobs bcu mnga' bas gsungs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa dang / chos dang mngon pa dang / 'dul ba dang / mdo
<p>154b.3</p>sde 'dzin cing dge ba'i las kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa yod do zhes bsod nams kyi sa bon skyed pa'i rgyu 'khor ba'i bde ba phun sum tshogs pa'i gzhi/ skye bo ngan pas rnyed par dka' ba ser sna can gyi yid 'joms pa sgrub pa ni ston ka'i zla ba dri ma med pa ltar dang ba'i thugs mnga' ba/ srid pa'i
<p>154b.4</p>sa bon nyon mongs pa gcod pa/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa mkhyen pa/ grags pa 'jig rten gsum du khyab pas bdud kyi bu mo steg pa rgyun gcod pa'i rgyu/ skyabs su 'os pa/ chos ston pa/ 'gro ba la dge ba'i phyir bya dka' ba'i phrin las rnams kyis/ chos thams cad thugs su chud pas
<p>154b.5</p>rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas nyi ma'i 'od zer gyi snang ba gsal bas reg nas/ pad+ma'i 'dab ma rgyas pa ltar ring zhing rdzi ma legs pa'i spyan dang ldan pa/ gnod sbyin gye bdag po'i gtsug gi nor bu chen pos zhabs kyi sor mo kun du bskor ba gser gyi mchod sdong ltar gsal ba/ sku la rdo rje
<p>154b.6</p>dang / lcags kyu dang / pad+ma dang / nya dang / rgyal mtshan dang / gdugs dang / 'khor lo la sogs pa'i mtshan rnams kyi mtshan mnga' ba/ pad+ma'i 'byung gnas rnams la snang ba mdzad pa'i 'od kyi phreng ba bye brag med par khyab pa rgyas par 'gengs pa/ bung ba'i tshogs ltar sngo ba'i gtsug
<p>154b.7</p>tor gyi nang nas kun du 'byung ba'i 'od kyi dra bas phyogs kyi dkyil 'khor ma lus par bkra bar byas pa/ kha na ma tho ba med par zhugs pa/ 'phags pa'i bden pa ston pa/ zhi bar gzhol ba'i lam du 'dren pa/ 'jig rten sgrol ba/ mnyes gshin pa'i gnyen gcig pu/ mu stegs can ngan
<p>155a</p>
<p>155a.1</p>pa'i rgol ba rnams kyis gsung dang thugs dang dpal dang / mthu la mi gnod pa/ zas gtsang ma'i sras/ yul rnams kun la sred pa 'byung ba'i rgyun rnams skems pa'i rgyu/ /skye bo mkhas pa rnams ni sad par bya phyir shar gyur pa/ /bag la nyal gyi rab rib sel
<p>155a.2</p>ba ye shes snang ba'i mchog /sa rnams mtha' dag snang bas phyogs rnams thams cad snang mdzad pa/ /phyag dang zhabs dang dbu ni rab tu byin zhing tshul khrims dang / /smon lam dag gis byang chub lam bzang yang dag bsgrubs gyur pa/ /srid pa'i 'gro ba'i dug gi snye ma'i steng du lhung ba'o/ /skye
<p>155a.3</p>dgu rnams la kha na ma tho ba med pa ston par mdzad pa/ srid pa rnam pa gsum 'jig pa/ bcom ldan 'das stobs bcu'i stobs dang ldan pa/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi mnga' ba/ dpa' ba dang mthu kha na ma tho ba med pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos brgyan pas sku brjid pa/ pha rol tu phyin
<p>155a.4</p>pa drug dang dka' ba brgya phrag du mas dam pa'i chos dkon mchog bsgrubs pa/ brtsal ba tsam gyis sems can mtha' dag gi bsam pa thugs su chud pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'phags pa nyan thos kyi dge 'dun rab tu zhi ba dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / bzod pa
<p>155a.5</p>dang / byams pa dang / sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa/ nyon mongs pa'i rab rib dang ling tog ma lus par bsal ba/ 'khor ba'i rang bzhin rig pa dang phyogs dang phyogs kyi gtsug lag khang dang / kun dga' ra ba dang / ri dang / nags 'dab dang / khrad khrod dang / chu dang / ri sul
<p>155a.6</p>dang / gsher sa dang / ne'u gseng dang / shing gi grib ma rnam pa sna tshogs la dgyes pa/ yul dang ljongs du ma la phan gdags par rtsol ba mdzad pa/ yang dag pa'i dran pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / dga' ba thob pa las ma nyams pa/ phung po lnga'i phyir skad cig yang dag par so
<p>155a.7</p>sor rtog pa'i yid la byed pa bskyed pa/ mdo dang / 'dul ba dang / chos mngon pa dang / skyes pa'i rabs dang / gleng gzhi dang / tshigs su bcad pa dang / rtogs pa brjod pa dang / de lta bu byung ba dang / gtan la dbab pa'i gtam gyis sems sbyangs pa/ rang gi lus dang /
<p>155b</p>
<p>155b.1</p>ngag dang / yid kyi 'jug pa dran pa nye bar gnas par rgyu ba/ /dbang po dang / stobs dang / byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bden pa dang / 'phags pa'i lam dang / dran pa nye bar gzhag pa sgom pa goms pas dad pa thob pa la tshe rabs gzhan dang gzhan nas bsags pa'i dge ba'i rnam par smin
<p>155b.2</p>pas grub pa/ ji ltar 'byor pas nus pa dang mthun pa'i rtsom pas tshogs bsags pa/ phan yon lnga'i rgyu sems can thams cad gnas par byed pa/ 'jig rten pha rol du bde ba thob par byed pa/ kha dog dang dri dang ro dang reg pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba/ gya nom pa'i bza' ba dang / bca' ba dang / 
<p>155b.3</p>ldag pa dang / rngub pa dang / gzhibs pa la sogs pa zhal zas bsham par bya ba rnam pa sna tshogs zhal zas khyad par can gyis spyan 'dren to/ /de la thog mar bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa yongs su mya ngan las ma 'das pa'i tshe/ gang dag ye shes kyi mes nyon mongs pa'i bud shing thams cad ma lus
<p>155b.4</p>par bsregs pa/ gtong ba'i ngang tshul can gyis sbyin pa'i sa bon 'phel ba'i rgyur gyur pa/ phra ba gzigs pa/ mkhas pa/ de kho na la bsgoms pa 'di lta ste/ gnas brtan b+ha ra d+h+wa dza bsod snyoms len dang / 'phags pa sgra gcan zin dang / sbyin byed dang / lam bsten dang / skyed byed
<p>155b.5</p>dang gser be'u dang / rtogs byed dang / rdo rje can gyi bu dang / 'phags pa bsrung ba'i klu dang / klu sde la sogs pa slob ma bstan pa gnas par bya ba'i phyir gnod par gyur kyang lus kyi khur khyer ba rnams dang / gzhan yang gang dag sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i skye bo la phan pa'i phyir/ gser
<p>155b.6</p>gyi rdo leb chen po'i steng na 'dug pa'i rig sngags 'chang du ma glu len pas glang po che yur ba/ bung ba'i mchus pad+ma la 'jib cing 'khod pa'i man+da ka'i rdzing gi chu dang ldan zhing yal ga gsal ba'i steng na rin po che'i me tog gi phreng ba bres pa'i shing yongs 'dus kun du mdzes par byas pa'i ri'i lhun
<p>155b.7</p>po 'bab chu 'bab pa'i sa gzhi la 'khod pa rnams dang / yang na gang dag /gser ri'i dkyil nas bsil ba'i chu 'bab la/ /chu la zla ba'i gzugs brnyan 'byung 'gyur zhing / /zla ba'i 'od kyis ku mud kha phye ste/ /ku mud tshal na skad snyan dang pa gnas/ /ngang mo mtshe'u na sgra skad snyan pa 'byin/ /mtshe
<p>156a</p>
<p>156a.1</p>ngogs rma bya dgar bcas rgyags par gnas/ /rma bya rgyags sgras ri sul snyan par grags/ /ri sul yal ga lhags pas ri rtse 'khrigs/ /ri rtse stod rnams na ni sprin chags la/ /lang ling sprin gyi sman ljongs khra khro snang / /sman ljongs skyes pa'i nor bu ldum bu gsal/ /ldum
<p>156a.2</p>bu las brul lhung ba'i me tog ldan/ /me tog rgyas pa'i dpag bsam shing tshal mdzes/ /mdzes pa'i lha mo gser gyi phag skad drung / /gser gyi phag skad sgras ni bya 'drogs shing / /byas 'chos shing thog rtsa las chad cing brul/ /rtsa 'phyang khu ba zags pa spos kyi dri/ /spos glang dbang po dregs
<p>156a.3</p>brag dri rab zhim/ /dri rab zhim pa'i li shi ri 'khor mang / /ban glang mo rgyags drag 'gro lang long gyur/ /bung ba'i khyu yis me tog zegs gyur cing / /yal ga me tog rgyas pas gad pa dkar/ /gad pa chad pas nor bu'i ldum bu snad/ /me tog mgo lcogs bral bas rnam par bkra/ /nor bu
<p>156a.4</p>sil ma mod pos ri gzhol spras/ /me tog zegs pa'i shing gi yal gar gnas pa'i bung ba dga' bas 'phur rnams dang / /zla ba'i 'od zer dkar po ngang pa lta bus nye 'khor rdo ba chag chag btab/ /lhun po mtho ba'i ri la thub pa gang dag rab tu zhi ba'i thugs kyis bzhugs/ /de dag dri med zla 'dra'i
<p>156a.5</p>grags ldan 'di yi sbyin pa'i gnas la brten du gsol/ /rgya mtsho'i nye ba'i chu 'gram ri bo ma la ya'i/ /ri ngos ta mal sbal mig 'thon pa'i phreng ba can/ /sbrul mang 'khris pa'i tsan+dan shing gi nags tshal na/ /brten pa gang dag bzhugs par gyur pa de dag dang / /nyi ma'i rta yi rmig pas
<p>156a.6</p>rdo bcag cing / /mi'am ci yi bu mo phrugs kyis nyams dga' la/ /ri sul mthon po dpag bsam nags mang dang / /ri 'gab rnams na gang dag bzhugs pa dang / /shing gi me tog 'phrul pas dri zhim byas pa'i ser bu dad ldang zhing / /nags na glang po dregs pa zag pas bsgos pa'i rin
<p>156a.7</p>chen 'khri shing khyim/ /khyim la chags pa med pa'i lha yis bstan pa'i bsod nams chu gling gi /gnya' shing 'dzin khri bya rgyal khyung gnas pa na gang dag bzhugs pa dang / /bal glang mos bsnyogs snang ba rtsub 'gyur tshal/ /me tog ldan zhing ser bu dad ldan pa/ /sa h+ya ri bo
<p>156b</p>
<p>156b.1</p>ngos rab yangs pa la/ /yang dag thugs mnga' thub pa bzhugs dgu dang / /pad+ma ut+pal rgyas pa 'byung ba'i gnas/ /nyin re nyi ma'i shing rtas rdo snad can/ /srid pa'i 'jigs bral rab tu yid 'ong ba/ /'char ba'i ri stengs gang dag bzhugs pa dang / /ri yi rtse mos sngo bsangs sprin thal
<p>156b.2</p>sman ljongs can/ /ngogs ldan chu bo man da ras ni ri sul bkrus/ /glang chen myos pas bsnyogs pas sa phyogs rlog pa'i ri/ /'bigs byed rma bya rgyags gnas pa na bzhugs dgu dang / /sna tshogs 'byung khung tshon gyis kha bsgyur phug dang ldan zhing sprin kyang chags gyur la/ /ko lpags ldan pa
<p>156b.3</p>gtsang ma'i chu yis ngogs kyi rdo ba mang po bkrus gyur cing / /ngos la ba lang mjug ma mong po dag gis 'phyang zhing glog 'gyus snang byas pa/ /yongs 'dus ri rtse phrag na gcig pu sred dang bral ba gang dag bzhugs pa dang / yang / gang dag shing dang 'khri shing rnam pa mang po 'dab chags par gnas pa/ 
<p>156b.4</p>ne'u gseng 'jam la sngo ba'i steng na rma bya'i khyu gar byed cing sgra snyan pa 'byin pa/ ri dgas kyi tshogs bag yangs gnas pa'i sos bcad pa'i rtswa'i myu gu yod pa/ me tog dri zhim pos bsgom pa'i ser bu 'jam zhing bsil ba'i ngad ldang ba'i nags 'dab rnams su gnas bcas te bzhugs pa rnams dang / yang / 
<p>156b.5</p>gang dag dus su rlabs 'byung ba'i chu'i dba' rlabs kyis g.yengs pa'i na le sham dang li shi dang la ba kha'i 'bras bu sngon po mang po 'khrigs pa'i tshal dang / a ka ru'i shing khrod na gnas pa'i sbrul mgo'i gdengs ka gdengs shing 'jigs su rung ba yod pa/ glang po che dregs pa dang bcas pa'i
<p>156b.6</p>gnas byu ru'i sdong bu bsgyel ba dang ldan zhing / nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis reg pa'i dbang gis mu tig yod pa'i nya phyis kha bye ba'i khog pas rnam par spras pa nye bar 'bul ba dang ldan pa/ nor bu mchog gi rdo las grub pa'i chung ma'i skye bo gnas shing bya'i khyu dga' ste sgra 'byin pas glu len pa lta bu yod
<p>156b.7</p>pa'i rgya mtsho'i gling dag na/ klu'i bdag po'i lus chen pos sku dkris te/ gdengs ka'i gdugs kyis nyi ma'i 'od zer bsgribs shing bsam gtan mdzad pa rnams dang / sman ljongs dag na phyogs kyi glang chen brang gis rdo ba khebs pa'i khyu 'khod cing / khyor bcas lan cig ma yin ra
<p>157a</p>
<p>157a.1</p>ror gyur pa'i gnod sbyin mo dag gnas gyur la/ /klu yi rgyal po mgo bo stong de kha nas me 'bar 'byung bas shing sreg cing / /gangs ri ti se la ni blo gtsang gang dag zhal ton mdzad cing bzhugs pa dang / /rgya mtsho'i rlabs kyis bshal ba'i ri bo 'gab ldan ma smad pa/ /ri bo man da
<p>157a.2</p>ra la nyin phyed tshun chad bzhugs bzhugs shing / /nyi ma phyed par gyur nas gang dag gzhan du bzhugs pa'i phyir/ /nor bu'i rtse mo bkram pa'i 'khor yug ri la brten pa dang / /gang dag 'khri shing gzhon nus rdo ba khebs gyur pa'i/ /dbang chen rtse mo yid du 'ong bar bder gnas te/ /mkha' lding
<p>157a.3</p>shugs kyis nang du klu rnams dkrugs pa yi/ /rgya mtsho rin chen gnas la rnam par gzigs pa dang / /ngang pa'i tshogs can shin tu gtsang ba drag 'bab char gyi chu yis ri 'gab bkrus gyur cing / /phyogs kyi glang pos bsgyel ba'i sa la ki yis rdo ba chen po mang po khebs gyur la/ /gcan gzan dbang po
<p>157a.4</p>ral pa 'khyil zhing gsal bas dpung pa'i phyogs 'bar nyal bas gang gyur cing / /sbal mig mthon pa'i lcug mas 'khor bas grub pa ngal sos ri bo kron dzar gang gshegs dang / /gang dag mun bsal khyad par can gyi blos/ /shing ljon sna tshogs me tog rgyas gyur cing / /ri dgas rgyu bas ne'u
<p>157a.5</p>gseng gzhon snang ba/ /gzi rdo nags rnams mi spong bzhugs pa dang / /yang gang dag nub kyi ba lang spyod dang / shar gyi lus 'phags po dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan dang gling gzhan dag na skyes pa'i lcug phran mdog snum zhing sngo la 'jam pa mang pos sa gzhi kun du khebs pa/ shing gi grib ma'i dkyil
<p>157a.6</p>'khor bsil ba dang / khri shing gis 'khor zhing ri dgas mang po gnas pa'i nags tshal de dang de dag na bzhugs pa rnams dang / yang gang dag da ra dang /gan d+ha ra dang / gu zan dang / li dang / shi ring dang / ba le dang / bri sha dang / kha che'i yul dang / rgya yul dang / grong khyer zas 'dra dang / 
<p>157a.7</p>rdo 'jog zas 'dra dang / skyes pa'i grong khyer dang / phyogs mtshams dang / kun ti ma la ba dang / srung byed dang / grong khyer dang / tsha du ka dang / tsha ta dang / b+ha ru kad tsha dang / kau shAm+bI dang / ser skya'i gnas dang / mnyan yod dang / mi thub pa dang / grong khyer me tog dang / ti ra dang / bcom rlag
<p>157b</p>
<p>157b.1</p>dang / grong khyer longs spyod dang / tsam pa ka dang rgyal po'i khab dang / dbang po'i brag phug dang / 'brog dang / ko na'i grong dang / kun dga'i grong dang / mchod rten gyi grong dang / 'khrur bcug gi grong dang / rnam par rgyal ba'i grong dang / yangs pa can dang / li khar shing 'phel
<p>157b.2</p>ba dang / 'phel byed dang / zangs kyis g.yogs pa dang / rdo snyigs 'dzin dang / ko sa la dang / an dra dang / ka ling ga dang /ba rba dang / ya ba na'i gling dang / sing ga la'i gling dang / ka la sha'i grong khyer dang / gser gyi sa dang / ha ri ke la dang / ba ro sha ka ta ha dang / na ri ke la dang / 
<p>157b.3</p>pa na sa'i gling dang / shu sa ra dang / nim+ba'i grong khyer dang / dpal gyi zhing dang / dngul chu'i gnas la sogs pa yul dang / cha byad dang / skad dang / gnas pa dang / cho ga dang /rigs dang / rus dang / tshul khrims dang / tshul khrims can du ma'i yul/ mi gnas pa'i yul gzhan dag na
<p>157b.4</p>bzhugs pa rnams dang / /gang dag sngon chad nyi zla'i 'od kyis ma phog cing / /she sha sbrul gyi lus kyi 'obs gnas ri yi drung / /de yi gtsug gi rin chen 'od kyis mun bsal ba'i/ /sa 'og tu ni ring por ma thogs gshegs gyur dang / /gang dag chu ltar sa la thogs med bye'u 'dzul mdzad pa dang / /gang
<p>157b.5</p>dag sar gnas phyag gi rtse mos zla ba reg mdzad dang / /gang dag bya ltar nam mkha' la ni shugs kyis rgyu mdzad cing / /na bza'i tha mas sprin mthar reg pas sprin ling 'jig mdzad dang / /gang dag lha dang / klu dang / grub pa dang / 'khor ba dang / tshogs rnams kyis rtag tu mchod pa'i ri 'jigs med
<p>157b.6</p>dang bung ba'i ri dang / rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal dang / shar gyi ri bo dang / nub kyi ri bo dang / shi ri kun pa ta dang / kun du so ma dang / ta ma sa'i tshal dang / bsil ba'i tshal dang / lhas sprul dang / 'jigs med pa ri dang / nags tshal chen po dang / tsher ma can gyi tshal dang / byams pa'i ri dang / 
<p>157b.7</p>chu srin byis pa bsod kyi ri dang / ri nag po dang / gnas kyi ri dang / ser skya'i ri dang / me tog gi ri dang / klu'i ri bo dang / tsan+dan gyi ri bo dang /tsher ma'i ri bo dang / lha yul babs pa dang / a sa sim+ba dang / kun dga' ston ldan dang / ri bo'i rgyal mtshan dang / gzhi bkrus dang / rang gi mchod rten dang /
<p>158a</p>
<p>158a.1</p>sA lu spungs ldan dang / pho brang 'khor dpal yon can dang / bya rgod kyi phung po dang / ri dgas kyi nags dang / ka sho dang / gtsug lag khang gser ka ni Sh+ka sha hi/ la sogs pa cho 'phrul rmad du byung ba sna tshogs dang ldan pa rnams dang / d+harma rA dzi ka mchod rten du ma dang / 
<p>158a.2</p>sangs rgyas bzhi'i gdan khri yod pa bsod nams su gyur pa'i sa phyogs rgyun mi 'chad par klog pa dang / kha ton dang / bsam gtan dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par zhugs pa dang / tshul bzhin yid la byed pas 'jug pa dag pa'i sgra bcom pa rnams bzhugs bzhugs pa/ chos gos dang bsod
<p>158a.3</p>snyoms dang mal cha dang / na ba'i gso sman dang / yo byad dang 'tshog chas rnams kyis legs par byas pas mtha' mtha' na chu'i gnas yod pa la nye bar spyod pas nyams dga' ba/ bde bar gshegs pa'i zhabs kyis bcags pas gtsang bar gyur pa'i sa gzhi can/ zhi ba thub pa'i skye bo
<p>158a.4</p>gnas pa rnams na/ de kho na bsgoms pa'i yid kyis ting nge 'dzin bskyed pa/ tshe'i lhag ma gnas par mdzad pa rnams dang / gang dag glog 'gyu bya gag dag gis sku lus bkra byas sprin snum 'dra gyur nas/ /bkres pa'i sdug bsngal snod gyur mda' rtse rnon po lta bu'i spu yis rab gang zhing / /bsgoms
<p>158a.5</p>pas mig zha me stag bcas pa'i me rnams kyis ni kun nas lus bskor ba'i/ /yi dgas gnam du lta ba rnams la thugs rjes steng nas char gyi rgyun 'bebs dang / /rin chen bye ma'i phreng bas gya gyur dkrigs mtho la/ /dang khyu bag yangs gnas shing lang long nyal gyur cing / /chu dang nye bas
<p>158a.6</p>chu yi zer mas bsil gyur pa/ /ma na ya yi mtsho gling bsam gtan mdzad dgu dang / /gang dag mi ro mang po'i sha dang khrag gi ro bro bas dga' bar gyur pa'i bya khwa'i tshogs kyis gang bar gyur pa'i sa phyogs mgo'i thod pa gas nas tshil thigs zags pa'i snum gyis mched pa'i mes tshig cing / rang
<p>158a.7</p>gi me lces shing bcer ba bskams shing rnyings pa'i lag pa dang / rkang pa dang / so dang / skra'i dum grugs kyis gang zhing / zla ba dri ma med pa'i 'od lta bu'i keng rus kyi phung po yod la/ skabs shig tu ro langs byung nas/ a la la a la la zhes sgra 'byin cing / me stag dang bcas pa'i
<p>158b</p>
<p>158b.1</p>gad mo drag pos 'byung ba 'khrugs shing skrag par gyur pa ce spyang mi bzad pa'i kha nas du ba dang bcas pa'i me lce 'byung ba'i dur khrod chen po dag na bud med kyi ro sbos shing lto sgang nger gyur pa'i steng na 'dug cing / dga' ba'i bya rgod kyi mchu dang / sder mos lto 'brang cing lto'i nang na srin bu'i rigs
<p>158b.2</p>rnams gnas pa/ ce spyang gi stobs kyi shugs kyis drangs pa'i nang grol dri mi zhim pa'i dum bus 'khor la/ bya khwa bkres pas mig gi sha brus pa dag la gzigs shing / rtag tu mi sdug pa bsgoms te/ gang dag kha cig ro'i gnas mal dong nas ni/ /khrag dang sa chags dmar
<p>158b.3</p>zhing rtsub pa'i skra 'khyil dang / /bya yi mchu dang sder mos mig rkong brus pa yang / /mi ro bor ba'i lus la gzigs par gyur pa dang / /sgo dang srang bar la lar me 'bar me lce'i rtse mo mang pos mgo rmongs shing / /ral gri gtun dang rdo bas bsnun cing brdungs nas skye bo ku co 'don gyur la/ /gshin
<p>158b.4</p>rje'i pho nya snying rje med pa sdod cig zer ba'i bzod glag sgras gang ba'i/ /sems can dmyal ba rnams su'ang srogs chags don phyir gang dag skad cig 'jug pa dang / /gzhan yang sha ri'i mi'i dug mangs glang po che 'khrug pa'i mdun logs na yal ga bregs pa'i sdong bu yod pa phyogs kyi bar nas rlung
<p>158b.5</p>chen po langs pas 'od ma'i tshal bskyod nas 'khri shing gi dra ba dang drud pa las me byung ba'i me lces shing mchog sna tshogs tshig nas/ ri dgas dang / phag rgod mchog mgyogs pa brgya phrag dag skrag cing mgo rmongs pa yod pa/ shing lo mang po lhags la shing rnyings pa can bsil ba'i grib ma sang sid med
<p>158b.6</p>pa/ nyams dga' ba'i longs spyod yod pa/ nags kyi ma he dang phag rgod kyis me tog ut+pal dang / pad+ma dang / sa ha ka ra bskyod pas chu dri zhim por gyur pa'i mtshe'u 'gram na shing la spre'u 'i khyu gnas pa nye 'khor gyi ri las chu rlabs mi drag par 'bab pas 'khor nas ne'u gseng mong pa'i sa gzhi yod
<p>158b.7</p>pa'i 'brog dag na zhi ba'i bdag nyid can 'chag pa dang klog pa dang kha ton dang / bsam gtan la mngon par brtson pa/ gang dag bag med pa'i gnas dar la bab pa yol bar mdzad pa rnams dang / ri bo rdo leb che zhing yangs la rab tu snum pa 'dra gyur cing / /glog gi phreng bar me tog yod la 'ja'
<p>159a</p>
<p>159a.1</p>yis bkra ba'i bdag nyid can/ /chu bsil sprin chags rnams la chu 'bab zer phran chags pa'i rdzing ldan can/ /ser bus na bza' g.yo ba gang dag nyi ma'i gung la bzhugs pa dang / /de bzhin du rtag tu goms pa'i lam nas 'dong ba'i glang po'i khyu'i rmig rjes yod la/ /nags kyi ma he
<p>159a.2</p>'khrugs pa'i rwas grog mkhar chen po bshig pa'i shul gyi khung bu nas sbrul gyi lus phyed phyung ste/ nags kyi rlung 'gam pa yod pa/ sa tshal stug po dang 'dam bu dang / shing ka sha stug po'i khrod na stag zung du gnas pa can/ phag rgod kyi snas rlog pa'i gla sgong gi rtsa ba 'dzings pa ral pa ltar
<p>159a.3</p>'dug pa yod pa shing ni tsu la'i me tog brul bas rdo ba rtsa dmar bar gyur pa yod pa/ shing gi phyogs su ri dgas kyi khyu 'dam rdzab la thogs pa yod pa/ shing lo sngon po stug por skyes pa'i dri bsung mang po yod pa'i gsher ba'i chu rgyun dag tu mngon par dgyes shing dge ba'i phyogs ston pa rnams
<p>159a.4</p>dang / rin po che'i 'od zer gyis chu'i rtsa dmar bar gyur la/ thugs bsam gtan la zhen pas dpag bsam gyi shing gi lcug ma'i rtse mos reg pa'i ri spos kyi ngad ldang gi sul na rtsol ba med pa gang dag bzhugs pa dang / gang dag seng ge bsgyings pa yod pa ri dgas rgyu ba dang ldan pa/ chu 'dus te 'bab pa
<p>159a.5</p>yod pa g.yos pas steng gi rtse mo ldem pa'i sngags kyis skar ma'i tshogs 'phangs pa/ sa'i steng na lci ba lhun po yang lcug phran la bya ba bzhin du sgrim mi dgos par zhabs kyi sor mos sa'i 'og gi rmang dang bcas pa gsal bar 'phen pa dag dang / ting nge 'dzin thob pa gang dag char pa'i chus
<p>159a.6</p>rdol ba'i bu ga du ma nas nyi ma'i 'od zer byung ba zla ba lta bu yod cing / rmang rdo dang rtsig ngos shag shig tu gyur pa'i mtshams su ba rgya chags pa/ sbrul gsob rlung gis gang ste sgang der 'dug pa'i phreng ba rtag tu yod cing / nags kyi ri dgas kyi lces tsha sgo rdul can rtsub po bldags pas/ shing rtsa
<p>159a.7</p>sed sed por gyur pa yod pa/ rtsig rmang du srin bu go da'i tshogs ring nas gnas par gyur cing / sre mo mgo bstod de phyogs su blta bas byi ba skrag pa yod la/ nang du rtsa sngon po stug po skyes pa'i 'jag ma'i drung gi gseb na phye ma leb rgyu ba yod cing / 'ug pa mang po sgra 'byin cing glu len pa lta bu
<p>159b</p>
<p>159b.1</p>yod pa'i grong stong sus kyang ting nge 'dzin ma byas pa rnams na/ ston pa'i bka' nan tan gyis bsgrub pa rnams dang / gzhan yang / gang dag g.yag gi rmig pas rdo bcag yod cing sprin ldings ldan gyur la/ /mtha' mar sA la thang shing skyes la chu bsil mi khebs 'bab yod cing / /bsam gtan
<p>159b.2</p>zhen pa'i blos ni kha ba bab pas chos gos lci zhing zag gyur kyang / /gangs ri dag gi ltong na 'gro ba shing gi drung du bzhugs par dgyes pa dang / /nang na chu srin 'khrugs te g.yos pas nya rnams kun 'byer zhing / /skam pas nyam chung gyur pa'i sprin btung kha yis chu 'thungs la/ /gshong du 'khyil
<p>159b.3</p>bar sbrul dbugs phyung bas rba rlabs rgyun 'chad pa'i/ /rgya mtsho la yang mtshan mo brtan pa gang dag 'chag mdzad pa/ /snod gyur bdag nyid thugs ldan gtsang ma'i lhung bzed phyag bsnams shing / /bsod nams ldan pa'i sku lus na bza' chos gos rab g.yo ba/ /de dag sang gi gdugs
<p>159b.4</p>ni nam gyi gung du phyin pa na/ /gaN+DI brdungs pa'i sgra snyan skad gsang grags par gyur pa'i tshe/ /bstan bcos sna tshogs kyi de kho na goms pa'i chu blugs pas mi shes pa'i sems kyi dri ma bkrus pa'i mkhas pa'i tshogs 'dus pa/ nyi ma shin tu mang po nas 'dris pa'i srid pa'i spros pa bcad pa/ bde
<p>159b.5</p>bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab rin po che'i sgrom du gyur pa/ dge ba'i tshogs bdud rtsi'i btung ba'i gzhi bro ba/ ye shes kyi gser ma gtogs pa brdar ba'i brdar rdo sngon por gyur pa/ legs par spyad pa stong gi tshogs bsags pas grags pa rgya che ba dang ldan pa/ sbyin bdag chen po bdag nyid
<p>159b.6</p>can ston gyi nam thang lta bu'i yid dang ldan pa ming 'di zhes bya ba 'di'i gan du/ ma he'i rwa ltar sngo zhing dri med mkha' las 'phur/ /gzi brjid kyis ni nyi ma'i 'od zer stong 'thor zhing / /mngon du phyogs nas 'ong ba'i sprin ni dral nas su/ /skye bo phan phyir thub rnams song 'dir gshegs su gsol/ /rgyun
<p>159b.7</p>mi 'chad par ting nge 'dzin dang / klog pa dang / 'chag pa dang / skye bo bla ma la brten par mngon du dga' ba'i blo gros dang ldan pa/mya ngan las 'das pa'i lam gyi rjes su mthun pa/ kha na ma thob med pa'i rig pa gsum rab tu sgrub pa/ nyon mongs pa las grol bar 'dod pa'i dge slong gang dag
<p>160a</p>
<p>160a.1</p>'di na gnas pa 'dul ba'i cho ga la goms pa/ lus dang ngag dang yid kyi 'jug pa zhi ba dang ldan pa de dag kyang ma lus par ci bder do mod kyi mtshan mo zad par mdzod la/ 'di nyid du gnas par mdzod cig /thub pa'i sras mo shes rab zhi dang dul bas brgyan pa'i dge slong ma/ 
<p>160a.2</p>tha dad gling dang klu dang nags dang ri dgas spros pa'i bsam bral zhing / /'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dri bral zhi 'os 'gro ba'i ma lta bu/ /de dag dgyes par mdzod la sbyin bdag phan par bzhed pas sang 'dir spyon/ /phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa dang gnod sbyin gtso bo dang / /grub pa rnams dang
<p>160a.3</p>gang dag lha ma yin dang klu rnams dang / /sangs rgyas la ni rab tu dad pa'i lha mchog gang yin pa/ /de dag rnams kyang sbyin bdag 'di la phan phyir sang 'dir spyon/ /lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / rig sngags 'chang dang / grub pa dang / mi 'am ci dang / nam mkha' lding la sogs pa 'byung
<p>160a.4</p>po rnams dang / stobs bcu mnga' ba'i bstan pa'i yon tan bsgrub pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis kyang / dam pa'i chos gnas par bya ba dang / sbyin bdag chen po bdag nyid che ba 'di/ snod bzang po la sbyar ba dang / sbyin bdag chen po 'di la grogs bgyi bas nyid kyis dge ba'i yon tan skyed pa
<p>160a.5</p>la dge 'dun nan tan mdzod cig /rgyun mi 'chad par bsrung ba dang / bskyab pa dang / bskyang ba la brtson par mdzod cig /yang dul ba dang / tshul khrims dang / thos pas shin tu che ba'i 'phags pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun 'dus pa la gsol ba 'tshal lo/ /lhun po las byung sbrul
<p>160a.6</p>mgo lnga 'dra rdo rje ka na ka /nya dang gdugs dang 'khor lo dag dang lcags kyu'i mtshan mnga' ba/ /pad+ma gser gyi dpal ldan phyag sor dra ba srab mos 'brel/ /sen mo'i 'od kyis khyab pa rgyal ba'i phyag gis bskyab par shog /srid pa'i 'dod chags nyon mongs zhags pa bsal zhing sred
<p>160a.7</p>med pa/ /chu yi chu gter lta bur yon tan rnams kyi gnas gcig pu/ /thub pa'i sras mchog dge 'dun bdag gis gus par spyan drangs pas/ /de ring dge ba gang bsags de ni byang chub thob gyur cig /ji srid mkha' la 'od 'phro 'od kyis gsal bas rnam par snang byed cing / /ri dgas
<p>160b</p>
<p>160b.1</p>rtags can 'od kyi ral pa'i dkyil 'khor ldan la 'char ba dang / /rgya mtsho rgyas par gnas pa de srid lha dang lha min phyag byas pa'i/ /bde bar gshegs kyi bstan pa thogs pa med par gnas par shog /gnas brtan spyan drang ba slob dpon b+hA ba skan+da pa zhes bya bas mdzad pa rdzogs
<p>160b.2</p>so// //A tsAr+ya dzi na mi tra dang / ban de ye shes sdes sgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /[ ]@/ /bstan pa'i gtad rabs bzhugs so// @##/ /sangs rgyas la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas 'phags pa nyi ma gung pas kha cher gshegs te rdzu 'phrul
<p>160b.3</p>gyi cho 'phrul gyis 'phags nas klu'i rgyal po au duSh+Ta btul lo/ /bA rA Na sI'i ljongs kyi skye bo'i tshogs rnams la rtsed mos mdzad nas kha cher gshegs pa yin no/ /rdzu 'phrul gyis skye bo'i tshogs dang lhan cig tu ri bo spos kyi ngad ldang du gshegs nas klu rnams btul lo/ /gur gum
<p>160b.4</p>blangs nas kha che rnams bstan pa la btsud nas grong dang grong khyer dang ljongs rnams dang rgyal po'i pho brang gis brgyan nas thams cad la phan btags shing kha che ba de dag dga' bar mdzad nas bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa rgyas par mdzad de/ bstan pa yongs su bskyangs nas sems can rnams
<p>160b.5</p>la phan pa mdzad de 'phags pa shA na'i gos can la bstan pa gtad cing / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul bstan nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /'phags pa shA na'i gos can gyis kyang gar gyi rje zhes bya ba'i tshong dpon gyi bu ru mgo bo'i ri bo la gtsug lag khang mdzad nas 'phags pa nyer sbas rab tu phyung zhing
<p>160b.6</p>bsnyen par rdzogs nas dgra bcom par gyur te/ gnas pa las de la bstan pa gtad de yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /'phags pa nye bar sbas kyis kyang bdud sdig can btul te/ phug srid du khru bco brgyad pa rgyar khru bcu gnyis par gnas nas/ de'i gdams ngag bdun gyis dge slong rnams
<p>160b.7</p>kyis dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du byas pa'i thur ma rnams kyis bkang ngo / /bar skabs der mya ngan med ces bya ba stobs kyis 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po byung ste/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa la dad pa phyi phyir thob nas 'phags pa grags pas dge ba'i bshes gnyen byas pas
<p>161a</p>
<p>161a.1</p>bcom ldan 'das kyi mchod rten gang yin pa rnams dang nyan thos kyi yang ste/ de rnams la so so so sor gser gyi rgyan phul lo/ /byang chub kyi shing la yang de bas ches lhag par rab tu dang ba skyes nas bkur ste chen po byas te/ gser dang dngul dang baiDUrla dang shel gyi
<p>161a.2</p>rang bzhin gyi bum pa sna tshogs pa dri'i chus yongs su bsgos pa rnams kyis de la khrus gsol to/ /der 'ongs nas lo lnga'i bar du dge slong 'bum phrag gsum la ston mo byas te/ dang po la 'phags pa la bsod snyoms rgyas pa dang / rgyal mtshan la sogs pas mchod do/ /gnyis
<p>161a.3</p>pa la slob pa rnams la'o/ /gsum pa so so'i skye bo dge ba can rnams la chos gos gsum rnams kyis g.yogs so/ /ji tsam du rim gyis dbyig dang gser bye ba dgu bcu rtsa drug phul te/ kha cher yang dge 'dun rnams la de dag nyid phul lo/ /de ltar 'phags pa nyer sbas kyis sems
<p>161a.4</p>can la phan pa mdzad cing bstan pa yongs su bskyangs nas 'phags pa d+hI ti ka rab tu phyung zhing bsnyen par rdzogs nas dgra bcom pa nyid la bkod/ de la bstan pa gtad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /'phags pa d+hI ti kas kyang bstan pa yongs su bskyangs shing sems can la phan pa
<p>161a.5</p>mdzad nas/ 'phags pa nag po la bstan pa gtad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /'phags pa nag pos kyang bstan pa yongs su bskyangs shing sems can la phan pa mdzad nas 'phags pa legs mthong la bstan pa gtad de yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /'phags pa
<p>161a.6</p>legs mthong gis kyang bstan pa yongs su bskyangs shing sems can la phan pa mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'das so/ /ji tsam du yangs pa can du yangs pa can pa'i dge slong rnams kyis rung ba ma yin pa'i gzhi bcu byung ste/ de dag thams cad 'dod la sogs pa'i dgra bcom pa
<p>161a.7</p>bdun brgya rnams kyis nye bar zhi bar bya ba'i phyir bdun brgyas bsdu ba mdzad do/ /bar skabs der bcom ldan 'das yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas lo sum brgya lon te/ mya ngan med ces bya ba'i rgyal po nyid shi nas kha cher legs mthong byung ste ma dang pha dag las de la seng ge zhes bya ba'i
<p>161b</p>
<p>161b.1</p>ming du grub pa bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa la rab tu byung ste dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du byas so/ /ji tsam na byang gi lam nas rgyal po ka niSh+ka zhes bya ba 'phags pa seng ge blta pa'i phyir kha cher zhugs so/ /de la 'phags pa seng ges chos bstan to/ /des de las chos
<p>161b.2</p>thos nas byang gi lam du song ste ka niSh+ka'i mchod rten la rab tu gnas pa dang de rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa la sbyin pa dag sbyin/ bsod nams dag byas so/ /dge slong rnams la yang bstan nas kha cher rna rgyan gyi nags kyi gtsug lag khang du 'phags pa rtsi ba logs
<p>161b.3</p>la sogs pa'i dgra bcom pa lnga brgya dang / ba su mi tra la sogs pa'i btsun pa bzhi brgya rnams dang / byang chub sems pa lnga brgya rnams kyis kyang chos mngon pa rnam par bshad pa mdzad cing kha cher yang de rnams dge 'dun la phul lo/ /'di rgya dpe shog gcig ma cig lag tu byung ba/ 
<p>161b.4</p>bstan pa'i gtad rabs su 'dug pas mgo mjug ma tshang na yang / tshong 'dus kyi pho brang du 'gos lo tsA ba gzhon nu dpal gyis bsgyur ba yin no/[ ]#dgra bcom dge 'dun 'phel gyis lung bstan pa bzhugs so// @##/ /dgra bcom pa dge 'dun 'phel gyis lung bstan
<p>161b.5</p>pa/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'di skad bdag gis slob dpon gyis bshad pa thos pa na/ /yul 'di'i gtsug lag khang bru nya zhes bya ba'i dgra bcom pa dge 'dun 'phel zhes bya ba gsum rig pa mngon par shes pa thob pa/ rnam par thar pa brgyad la
<p>161b.6</p>bsam gtan pa zhig dus gzhan zhig na slob ma zhig dang thabs cig tu dbyar zla ba gsum 'jig tshogs kyi ri zhes bya ba la bzhugs te/ slob ma ban+de chos 'dul ba la slob pa zhig lags na/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas lo nyis stong lon pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rgya
<p>161b.7</p>gar gyi yul kau shAm+bI zhes bya bar nub par 'gyur ro zhes thos nas 'di snyam du rgya gar yul gyi chos dus de tsam zhig na/ yul kau shAm+bIr nub par 'gyur ba lta zhig na/ li yul la sogs pa gzhan gyi chos yun ji srid cig tu gnas par 'gyur/ nam 'jig rkyen ni gang gis 'jig par
<p>162a</p>
<p>162a.1</p>'gyur snyam du the tshom skyes so/ /de nas dgra bcom pa de phyi 'phred kyi dus kyi tshe nang du yang dag 'jog pa las bzhengs pa dang / slob ma des mkhan po'i zhabs la yan lag lngas phyag 'tshal nas 'di skad ces the tshom zhus so/ /slob dpon ston pa bcom ldan 'das shAkya
<p>162a.2</p>thub pa'i bstan pa lo nyis stong nas 'jig par lung bstan na/ li yul 'di la sogs pa yul gzhan gyi bstan pa ji srid du gnas par 'gyur/ nam 'jig rkyen gang gis 'jig par 'gyur ba lags/ de nas mkhan pos bka' stsal pa/ bu khyod kyis li yul la sogs pa'i skye bo mang po'i
<p>162a.3</p>don dang / bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa yun ring du gnas par bya ba'i phyir the tshom dris pa legs kyis/ legs par nyon la yid la zung shig dang / li yul la sogs pa'i bstan pa ji srid du gnas par 'gyur/ nam 'jig pa dang rkyen gang gis 'jig par 'gyur ba ngas so sor lung
<p>162a.4</p>bstan par bya'o/ /bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i bstan pa ni bcom ldan 'das mya ngan las 'das nas lo stong lnga brgya lon pa dang yul du dad pa med pa rnams 'byung zhing dam pa'i chos 'jig tu rgol lo/ /de'i tshe li yul 'dir dad pa med pa'i rgyal po yang 'byung bar 'gyur zhing / yul yang
<p>162a.5</p>rgyal pos phan tshun rtod cing 'phrog par 'gyur ro/ /de phyin chad ni yul yang nyin gcig bzhin du nyams par 'gyur/ grong dang gtsug lag khang la sogs pa yang phal cher stongs par 'gyur/ mi rnams kyang nyin gcig bzhin du phyir yang dkon mchog gsum la dad pa 'bri bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyu des
<p>162a.6</p>na dkon mchog gsum dang / chos smra ba dang / bsam gtan pa kun kyang mchod gnas su mi byed cing / mu stegs kyi rgyal po dang / blon po dang / yul 'dzin pa dang / khyim bdag rnams kyang chos dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs 'dzin cing dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam yal bar 'dor bar 'gyur
<p>162a.7</p>ro/ /chos dang mthun pa ma yin pa dang / ma brtags pa dang / bab chol gyi longs spyod kyang sogs par byed par 'gyur ro/ /de nas de'i 'og tu dge slong dang / dge slong ma rnams 'tsho ba'i yo byad kyi phyir g.yem spyo bar gyur te/ chos 'dul ba las 'byung ba dge sbyong gi tshul dang / spyod pa
<p>162b</p>
<p>162b.1</p>zhi ba dang / dul ba dang / ngo tsha shes pa dang / khrel yod pa la sogs pa yal bar 'gyur zhing / zhing dang / ldum ra dang / nyo tshong dang / skyi brnya dang / slong mo ba rnams kyis 'tsho bar byed do/ /khyim pas bslab par bya ba'i bzo dang / khyim gyi so nams dang / 'thab rtsod dang / sgo gsol
<p>162b.2</p>rngam po che yang byed par 'gyur/ pho nyar yang 'gro bar byed/ las kyi go 'phang dang / rtsa 'jing yang tshol bar byed par 'gyur te/ de'i tshe gtsug lag khang dang / dgon pa la mi gnas shing bde bar gshegs pa'i gdams ngag yal bar bor te/ yang dang yang du mkhar dang / grong dang / 
<p>162b.3</p>tshong dus dang / srang dang / sum mdo na gnas par sems dga' bar 'gyur/ bran dang / bran mo dang / rkang 'gros kyang tshol bar byed do/ /rgyu des na khyim bdag dang / yul 'dzin pa dang / blon po la sogs pas kyang de dag la rim gro mi byed cing / dad pa phyir log nas dkon mchog
<p>162b.4</p>dang dge 'dun gyi dkor la yang 'phrog par byed do/ /khyim pa de dag gis kyang nor rdzas de dag la brten cing spyad pas bsod nams 'bri bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyu des na li yul la sogs par gnod pa sna tshogs 'byung zhing lo re bzhin dma' bar 'gyur te/ rtsod pa dang / nad dang / dus ma
<p>162b.5</p>yin pa'i char dang / rlung dang / dgra mang po yang 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /dus ma yin pa'i sad dang / srin bu dang / bye ba dang / byi ba yang 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe na sems can rnams nang mi mthun par 'gyur zhing dus tshigs kyang 'chol bar 'gyur te/ de ltar na yul gang dang gang du
<p>162b.6</p>chos lugs log pa byed pa de dang der ni gnod pa de dag 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe li yul la sogs par rgyal po dang / blon po la sogs pa ya rabs las kyang dkon mchog la snying thag pa nas dad pa 'ga' las mi 'byung na/ phal pa lta smos kyang ci dgos te/ rgyu de lta bus
<p>162b.7</p>li yul la sogs pa'i dkon mchog gsum gyi mchod gnas thams cad kyi thams cad du rmegs med par 'gyur ro/ /de nas li yul la sogs par dge slong gi gnas sngon rgyal po la sogs pa dad pa can gyis byas pa yang blon po la sogs pa dad pa med pa rnams kyis btsan
<p>163a</p>
<p>163a.1</p>'phrogs su 'phrogs nas bdag nyid gnas par byed do/ /dge slong rnams kyang 'khyams nas 'tsho ba dang / chos gos dang / gnas kyis phongs par 'gyur ro/ /blon po la sogs pa de dag gis dge slong gi zhing chu dang / ldum ra la sogs pa yo byad rnams kyang
<p>163a.2</p>btsan thab su 'phrog par byed/ lha 'bangs dang / nang gi g.yog rnams kyang dge slong gi ngag mi nyan cing gnya' rengs su byed par 'gyur ro/ /de nas dge slong rnams kyis kyang de lta bur gyur par shes nas yi mug ste/ li yul gyi dge slong rnams phan tshun du gcig la gcig
<p>163a.3</p>'di skad du yu bu cag rnams gtsug lag khang tshar ma zhes bya ba dang po chos 'byung ba'i gnas der 'du'o zhes sbran nas gtsug lag khang der 'dus te/ dpyid zla tha chungs tshes bco lnga'i nub mo gso sbyong byas nas gcig la gcig 'di skad du yu bu cag rnams sngon bag med par gyur
<p>163a.4</p>nas mkhas pa chos dang mthun pa rnams la dbang zos pa'i rgyus de ltar khyim pa rnams kyis kyang rtsis med par byas te/ da ni 'tsho ba yang mi 'byor na deng phyin chad gang du 'dong / thabs ni gang gis 'tsho bar bya zhes smras te/ de'i tshe thams cad kyis cho de chen po 'debs par 'gyur ro/ /
<p>163a.5</p>de nas de'i tshe bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa srung ba'i lha/ bcom ldan 'das kyi byas pa gzo ba thams cad kyang gtsug lag khang der 'dus te gcig la gcig lta zhing 'di skad du bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa ni yun ring por mi gnas so/ /yul 'di yang stongs par 'gyur ro zhes mya
<p>163a.6</p>ngan byed cing du bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe dge slong de dag 'di snyam du yul 'dir ni 'tsho ba mi 'byor na 'di bor te yul gzhan du 'gro bar bya'o snyam du sems mthun par gyur pa gang du 'dod par bya zhes gros byas te/ yul nye ba gzhan dang gzhan na ni dad pa med pa dag gis gang / 
<p>163a.7</p>rgya gar yul du 'dong du ni lam mi thar bas bod kyi yul na/ dkon mchog gsum la mchod gnas su byed ces grags pas der 'gro bar byas nas nyi ma 'di la 'dong ngo zhes dus btab nas de'i nub mo gtsug lag khang tshar mar gzhag go/ /nam langs pa dang bud med dad pa can
<p>163b</p>
<p>163b.1</p>zhig gis gdan chud la spyan drangs te/ de nas gaN+DI brdungs nas dge 'dun spyi'i gtsug lag khang bskor te mchod pa byas pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi gzugs brnyan gyi gdan khri zhig gas pa'i gseb nas sgrom bu thar ma can zhig snang bar gyur te/ de nas sgrom bu de phye ba dang / de'i nang
