<p>163b.2</p>nas gser las byas pa'i kha zas kyi sder cha bdun byung ste/ dge slong kun gyis de blangs te/ 'brur bsgyur nas de dge 'dun kun dbyar zla ba gsum gtsug lag khang tshar mar tshul du 'jug pa'i 'tsho ba sbyar nas zong lhag ma las yul nas byung ste/ 'gro ba'i lam brgyags dang khur khal sbyar re/ /
<p>163b.3</p>dbyar zla ba gsum 'das nas 'di skad du yu bu rnams byin gyis brlabs pa'i yul 'di bltas la 'gro bar bya'o zhes smras te song nas/ 'phags pa sa'i snying po'i gnas gtsug lag khang ye shes ri zhes bya ba'i drung du phyin pa dang / de'i tshe de na brag la mchod rten gyi 'og gzhi rnyed pa zhig
<p>163b.4</p>yod pa rdib pa'i nang nas/ gser phor chen po mu tig gis gang ba zhig byung ba dang de yang blangs te 'brur bsgyur nas phyogs der rgun zla ba gsum gnas pa'i 'tsho ba sbyar te/ de nas dpyid byung ste 'gro ba'i dus la bab nas song ste/ shel chu 'og ma brgal ba dang / yul mi stod pa
<p>163b.5</p>rnams kyis sa lam yogs su gdugs tshod sbyar nas/ nyi ma re re zhing gtsug lag khang dag tu gdugs tshod gsol bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe yul mi smad pa rnams kyis kyang dge slong rnams yul byung ste 'gro zhes thos nas dge 'dun de dag gtsug lag khang cong zhes bya bar spyan
<p>163b.6</p>drangs nas/ zhag bdun gyi bar du bshos sbyor bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe li yul na gnas pa'i klu thams cad 'di snyam du bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa ni rmegs med par 'gyur la thug go snyam du mya ngan byed cing bstan pa gnas par bya ba'i phyir char chen po phab ste/ char pa des
<p>163b.7</p>gtsug lag khang cong zhes bya ba'i nang nas mchod rten gyi gzhi zhig yod pa nas gser phor gser phyes gang ba zhig byung ba dang / de yang dge 'dun gyis btsongs nas dpyid kyi 'tsho ba'i yo byad rnams sbyor bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas yang yul mi smad pa rnams kyis gtsug lag khang
<p>164a</p>
<p>164a.1</p>sA la'i tshal zhes bya bar dge 'dun rnams spyan drangs nas zhag bdun gyi bar gyi gdugs tshod gsol nas zhag bdun lon pa'i nyin par yul stod smad kyi mi thams cad gtsug lag khang sa na bar 'dus nas dge 'dun la rdzongs dang khur khal 'bul lo/ /de'i tshe
<p>164a.2</p>mi rgan rgon rnams ni bslab pa 'dzin par byed/ gzhon nu rnams ni rgyang nas lta zhing gad mos 'debs pa dang grogs byed par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe mkhar dge ba can gyi nang nas kyang mi rgan rgon kha cig gis gos kha dog bsgyur ba dang / lam du 'jug pa'i yo byad so so nas thogs nas
<p>164a.3</p>so so'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen dge slong de dag gi mdun du lhags nas 'phags pa rnams bzod par bzhes shig ces smra zhing mchis te/ phyag 'tshal bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe mchod pa de ni dper na ku sha'i grong khyer gyi mi rnams bcom ldan 'das mya ngan las 'das par shes nas mya ngan
<p>164a.4</p>byed pa bzhin du mchod pa byed pa dang 'dra bar/ li yul du dkon mchog gsum mchod pa'i tha ma yin no/ /de'i 'og tu dge slong rnams gtsug lag khang de nas bod yul ngos su chas pa dang lam kha na mchod rten rnying pa zhig gi drung du dpal lha mo chen mos dge 'dun gyi ched du gser gyi dang tse
<p>164a.5</p>phu dung gang bzhag pa rnyed nas dge 'dun gyis de bgos te lam gyi chas rdzas sbyor bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe li yul gyi mkhar gtsug lag khang ka sa ra zhes bya bar rgyal rigs las skyes pa'i yon bdag cig 'byung bar 'gyur te/ yon bdag des dge 'dun rnams zhag bdun du mchod ston
<p>164a.6</p>gsol bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe mchod ston gsol ba de ni li yul du dge 'dun gyi mchod ston gsol ba'i tha ma yin no/ /de nas dge slong rnams me skar gyi lam du zhugs te song ba dang / de'i tshe dge slong pho mo gsar bu las phal cher rang rang gi slob dpon dang / mkhan po la chos
<p>164a.7</p>gos phul te bzod par gsol nas slar yul du ldog par 'gyur dge slong pho mo gsar bu kha cig ni rab tu byung ba'i dngos po mi gtong zhing pha ma la sogs pa'i gnyen skyel du 'ongs pa rnams la mya ngan gyi tshig smra zhing dus nas gnyen rnams phyir bzlog ste/ dge 'dun dang lhan cig tu
<p>164b</p>
<p>164b.1</p>mi dga' ba'i yid kyis phyir byin gyis brlabs pa'i yul dang / gnyen gyi rjes bzhin du lta bzhin par me skar gyi lam du zhugs te 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar song ba dang de'i tshe rnam thos kyi bu dang / dpal lha mo chen mo gnyis mchog tu snying rje skyes te/ 'brog mi pho mo gnyis kyi lus
<p>164b.2</p>su bsgyur te/ dge 'dun rnams spyan drangs nas yul me skar du zla ba gsum gyi bar du gdugs tshod gsol te/ lam du 'jug pa'i yo byad ci dgos pa yang rdzong bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas dge slong de dag mdo lo'i lam du zhugs nas ri dang lung pa'i sul gtugs te song ba dang / 'brog dgon
<p>164b.3</p>par lam stor nas ngu zhing phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan dang li yul gyi lha thams cad kyi ming nas 'bod par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe rnam thos kyi bu snying rje skyas nas g.yag dkar po sgal pa dang / snal chu can cig tu sprul nas dge slong de dag gi drung du 'ongs pa dang dge slong rnams kyis
<p>164b.4</p>de mthong nas g.yag 'di ni mi'i khal g.yag cig yin te/ 'di'i phyi bzhin song na gdon mi za bar mi rnams dang phrad par 'gyur bas da ni mi 'chi'o snyam du yid sos te/ g.yag des kyang lam drangs nas gseb lam du byung ste/ tshal byir bskyal nas g.yag nyid mi snang bar gyur
<p>164b.5</p>to/ /de'i tshe dge slong rgan rgon mang po zhig ni lam kar 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas yul tshal byi'i bod rnams kyis dge slong de dag mthong nas bsu te/ /'phral du yo byad rnams sbyar nas bod yul 'dir li yul gyi dge slong mang po lhags na ji ltar bgyi zhes pho nyar gtong bar 'gyur
<p>164b.6</p>ro/ /de'i tshe na rgya rje'i bu mo byang chub sems dpa'i rigs can cig btsas pa bod kyi rgyal po'i khab tu len cing btsun mo dam pa byed par 'gyur te/ /de ni dad pa shin tu che ba/ snying rje dang ldan pa skad snyan pa dang des pa/ bslab pa'i yan lag lnga bzung ba zhig 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /
<p>164b.7</p>btsun mo des nyi 'og gzhan nas dge slong mang po bod kyi yul du lhags par mthong nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ni ring du mi gnas so snyam nas mya ngan chen pos non nas rang gi 'khor bud med nyis brgya dang / skyes pa sum brgya dang / ru rum dang / gzo bo dang gnang chen rnams drung du
<p>165a</p>
<p>165a.1</p>bos te ngus nas 'di skad ces/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa ni de'u re 'jig par gyur gyis khyed rnams myur du bsod nams ma byas/ tshul khrims ma bsrungs na 'phyis par 'ong ngo zhes smras par 'gyur ro/ /de nas btsun mo des rgyal po la 'di skad du dge 'dun de
<p>165a.2</p>rnams bdag gis bzhon pa dang gos la sogs pa'i yo byad sbyar nas 'dir spyan drang bar ci gnang zhes gsol pas rgyal pos kyang gnang bar 'gyur te/ tshul de lta bus dge slong de dag bod yul du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe bod yul gyi rgyal po dang blon po rnams kyis dge slong
<p>165a.3</p>de dag mthong nas dad pa chen po skye zhing gtsug lag khang chen po bdun yang brtsig par 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du dge slong an rtse pa dang gus tig pa dang / par wan pa dang / shu lag pa rnams kyang sdug bsngal chen pos non nas bru sha'i yul du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /tho kar
<p>165a.4</p>yul dang / kha che'i yul gyi dge slong rnams kyang dad pa med pa'i mi rnams kyis gtses te/ ma chags nas bru sha'i yul du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /dge slong de dag thams cad kyis bru sha'i yul du phyin nas/ bod yul na gtsug lag khang mang po brtsigs pa dang / rgyal po byang chub
<p>165a.5</p>sems dpa' zhig gnas pas dkon mchog gsum la mchod pa dang ri mo cher byed pa thos nas yid dga' ste/ thams cad bod yul du 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /bod yul du lhags nas lo gsum gyi bar du ni mchod pa chen po la sogs pa skyid pa nyams su myong bar 'gyur ro/ /lo gsum
<p>165a.6</p>lon pa dang bod kyi yul du bdud kyi ris kyi lha dang / lha ma yin dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za rnams kyis nad chen po 'bras dang / phol mig dang / 'brum bu gdug pa dag gtong bar 'gyur te/ nad des zhang blon dang dmag du ma dag 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe rgyal
<p>165a.7</p>mo de'i snying gar 'bras gsug pa byung ste/ shi nas lha yul du skye bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe bod kyi zhang blon rnams khros 'khrugs te 'di skad ces bdag cag gi yul 'di sngon gya nom pa las phyis mi bkra mi shis pa 'khyams pa sha stag 'dir lhags nas da ni yul du yang 'di lta
<p>165b</p>
<p>165b.1</p>bu gnod pa rnam pa sna tshogs byung bar 'gyur gyis/ rdzas lhag ma 'di rnams kyang yul 'dir mi gzhag cing sa mtshams 'das te bskrad par bya'o zhes gros byas nas dge slong gcig kyang bod yul du gnas su mi gnang ngo zhes glo bur du bsgo bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyal mo de nad kyis thebs
<p>165b.2</p>pa'i tshe bdag nyid mi 'tsho bar tshor nas rgyal po la kha chems su bdag gum na bdag gi nor rdzas ril gyis dge 'dun la 'bul bar ci gnang zhes gsol nas rgyal pos kyang gnang ste/ btsun mo'i rdzas thams cad dge 'dun la 'bul zhing des rgya gar gyi yul gan d+ha ra zhes bya bar 'gro
<p>165b.3</p>ba'i rdzas byas nas 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe bod yul gyi dge slong rnams kyang yi chad nas nyi 'og gi dge slong rnams dang gros gcig tu byas nas lhan cig tu 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /skye bo dang rtsod pa'i dus de'i tshe rgya yul gyi dge slong rnams kyang shin tu sdug bsngal bas gzir nas
<p>165b.4</p>yul gan d+ha rar 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar dong ba dang dge slong de dag thams cad yul gan d+ha rar 'gro ba'i lam kar phrad par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe bod kyi dmag gis rjes bzhin bsnyags nas lam kar bran g.yog dang / nor phyugs dag phrogs te dge slong dag kyang gsod par
<p>165b.5</p>'gyur ro/ /de ltar dge slong de dag bod kyi dmag gis bdas nas klu'i rgyal po e la'i 'dab kyi gnas drung du phyin pa dang / klu'i rgyal po e la'i 'dab kyis mi rgan zhig gi gzugs su bsgyur te dge 'dun gyi mdun du 'ongs nas phyag 'tshal te/ skyes bu dam pa khyed rnams gar
<p>165b.6</p>gshegs zhes dris pa dang / dge slong rnams kyis 'di skad du bdag cag gi yul na dad pa med pa sha stag gis gang bas 'tsho ba'i yo byad la sogs pas phongs te/ da yul gan d+ha rar 'tsho ba'i yo byad tsam zhig ci rnyed snyam nas lhags so zhes smras pa dang / de nas de'i
<p>165b.7</p>tshe klu'i rgyal po de bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa 'jig pa'i mtshan ma rtogs nas mchi ma khrag tu 'dzag cing dus nas/ dge 'dun rnams la yul der gshegs nas shul brgyags ji tsam mnga' zhes rmed par 'gyur ro/ /dge 'dun kun gyis kyang zhib tu brtsis
<p>166a</p>
<p>166a.1</p>nas zhag bco lnga'i brgyags yod do zhes smra bar 'gyur ro/ /klu'i rgyal pos 'di skad du 'di nas yul gan d+ha rar mtsho 'di'i g.yas g.yon du bskor na zhag bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i shul mchis na/ dgung bco lnga'i brgyags 'tshal lam/ gzhan yang shul ka nas la ka
<p>166a.2</p>mthon po dang nags tshal stug po dang / gcan gzan gdug pa dang / sbrul gdug pa dang / sdig sbrul la sogs pa dang / chom rkun pa yang mchis pas phyi nas tshur yang dmag gis bsnyegs pa dang / mtsho 'di'i nang na yang bdag gi 'khor gtum po dad pa ma mchis pa du ma zhig
<p>166a.3</p>mchis pas bdag gis phyir bzlog par mi nus te/ bdag ni de'i shul du bzhud par mi dga' zhing mchis so/ /de'i tshe dge slong pho mo mang po de dag thams cad 'di snyam du bdag cag rnams 'chi ba'i dus la bab pa 'dra snyam nas ngu zhing mya ngan byed par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe klu'i rgyal po e
<p>166a.4</p>la'i 'dab kyis dge 'dun rnams kyi mdun du pus mo btsugs nas dge 'dun ma bshums shig /bdag gis dge 'dun rnams kyi slad du srog kyang yongs su btang zhing bdag nyid kyi lus mtsho 'di'i steng du zam par bgyid lags so/ /bdag gis sngon bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa thog mar
<p>166a.5</p>legs par ma bsrungs par chad par srog gis god pa zhig gcod par 'tshal lo zhes smras par 'gyur ro/ /de nas klu'i rgyal po des rang gi lus sbrul chen po zhig gi gzugs su bsgyur nas/ bod yul ngos kyi ri'i rtse mo la ni mgos 'khyud/ yul gan d+ha ra'i ri'i rtse mo la ni
<p>166a.6</p>mjug mas 'khyud de lus kyi zheng du ni shing rta lnga'i khyon tsam gyi zam par btags so/ /de'i tshe dge slong de dag gis sbrul chen po de'i gzugs de mthong nas sngangs skrag ste/ phyogs su 'byer par 'gyur ro/ /de nas klu'i rgyal po des mi skad phyung ste/ dge 'dun dag ma sngangs shig / 
<p>166a.7</p>bdag gi lus 'di khyed kyi slad du zam par btags pa lags kyis/ ma bsnyengs par rjes dgra choms su dogs pa ni 'bangs dang phyag rjed dang khur rnams sngon la dgyer du gsol de'i 'og tu dge 'dun gzhon rims gshegs su gsol/ /bgres po rnams ni slad kyis gshegs su
<p>166b</p>
<p>166b.1</p>gsol zhes smra bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe klu'i rgyal po de'i rgyab kyi pags pa phyugs kyi rmig pa dang mi'i rkang pas bshus te rma chen po byung ste mtsho'i nang du rnag khrag kyang 'dzag par 'gyur ro/ /mi phyugs phal yang mtsho'i nang du ltung zhing 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /tha mar dge 'dun
<p>166b.2</p>rgan rabs rgal ba'i 'og tu klu'i rgyal po nyid kyang 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /mtsho de yang skams par 'gyur te/ mtsho bskams pa'i nang du klu'i rgyal po shi ba'i rus pa ri lta bur 'dug par 'gyur ro/ /ma 'ongs pa'i dus na sangs rgyas byams pa 'khor lnga brgya dang thabs cig tu klu'i
<p>166b.3</p>rgyal po e la'i 'dab kyi rus pa'i drung du gshegs te klu'i rgyal po e la'i 'dab kyi skyes pa'i rabs brjod pas byams pa'i 'khor dge slong lnga brgya po de dag thams cad kyis dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ro/ /de nas dge slong de dag yul gan d+ha rar phyin nas lo gnyis kyi
<p>166b.4</p>par du gnas so/ /lo gsum pa'i tshe yul de'i rgyal po dad pa can zhig yod pas 'chi bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po de shi ba'i 'og tu rgyal po de'i bu dad pa can zhig dang dad pa med pa zhig rgyal srid la brtod nas dmag gi g.yul bkye nas/ phyogs gnyis su chad par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe
<p>166b.5</p>na dge slong de dag gi nang na dge slong dpa' ba brtul phod pa tsham tshom med pa stong zhig yod pas rgyal bu dad pa med pa de dmag gis btab ste pham par byas nas rgyal bu dad pa can de la rgyal srid 'bul bar 'gyur ro/ /rgyal bu dad pa can des zla ba lnga rgyal po byas nas yang dge slong stong
<p>166b.6</p>po de dag gis bsad nas dge slong gcig rgyal po la bcug ste lo gnyis kyi bar du rgyal po byed par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe yul gan d+ha ra'i blon po dang yul mi thams cad 'dus te gsangs nas ci'i phyir nyi 'og gi mi bdag cag gi yul du bros pa/ ngan pa 'dis bdag cag gi rgyal
<p>166b.7</p>po gsad do zhes gros byas nas 'phral la dmag drangs te rgyal po gtubs par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe yul gan d+ha ra na gnas pa'i dge slong thams cad mthong dgu bsad de dge slong gang zhig yul dbus su bros te thar pa de 'ba' zhig gson par 'gyur ro/ /de'i 'og tu yul dbus ma
<p>167a</p>
<p>167a.1</p>gtogs par 'dzam bu'i gling 'di na dad pa med pa gsum 'byung bar 'gyur te/ sig ni la sogs pa mang po zhig gis rgyal po ni ta zig gi rgyal po byed par 'gyur ro/ /dru gu rus sna tshogs du mi'i rgyal po ni dru gus byed par 'gyur ro/ /gzhan mang po zhig gi rgyal
<p>167a.2</p>po ni bod kyi rgyal po byed par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po de gsum ka ni yang sems mthun par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po de gsum la dmag dpa' ba/ brtul bod pa sum 'bum zhig yod pas yul dbus ma gtogs pa/gzhan yang dag pa'i lta ba 'dzin pa'i yul thams cad bcom nas mi
<p>167a.3</p>mang po kha btags nas grong la sogs pa yang stongs par 'gyur ro/ /de nas rgyal po de gsum 'dus nas yul dbus su dmag drangs zhes gros byed par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe na yul dbus kau shAm+bI zhes bya bar rgyal po bzod dka' zhes bya ba zhig 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de btsas pa'i tshe khrag gi
<p>167a.4</p>char pa yang 'bab lag pa gnyis kyang gru mo man chad khrag gis bskus pa lta bur dmar ba zhig yin no de'i blon po yan lag mchog dang ldan pa lnga brgya dang dmag mi g.yul ngor dpa' ba nyis 'bum byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe ta zig gi rgyal po la sogs pa gsum yul dbus kau
<p>167a.5</p>shAm+bIr sod nas rgyal po bzod dka' tshol bar byed do/ /de nas rgyal po bzod dkas de skad thos nas dmag dang chas te rgyal po de dag gi mdun du bsgugs nas zla ba gsum gyi bar du rgyun du g.yul chen po sprad pa dang / rgyal po dad pa med pa de gsum dmag dang bcas te gtan med
<p>167a.6</p>par brlag par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po bzod dka' dmag dang bcas pa slar yul du 'khor nas rgyal po de 'di snyam du bdag gis mi mang po kha btags na/ bdag gi 'gro ba ni ji lta bu zhig tu skye bar 'gyur/ nam zhig ngan song gsum las thar par 'gyur snyam du 'gyod pa skye bar 'gyur ro/ /
<p>167a.7</p>de nas rgyal po de la blon po rnams kyis gsol ba/ ma bsnyengs par dmar bu can gyi yul na dge slong shir sha ka zhes bgyi ba sde snod gsum la mkhas pa zhig bzhugs pas de spyan drongs dang / des lha khyod kyi las ngan pa de bshags par 'gyur ro zhes smra bar 'gyur la/ rgyal pos
<p>167b</p>
<p>167b.1</p>kyang dge slong de spyan drangs nas/ de'i mdun du las ngan pa ji ltar byas pa thams cad lo rgyus smra bar 'gyur ro/ /dge slong des kyang 'di skad du rgyal po khyod kyis shin tu ma legs pa byas kyi che thang du 'gyod la/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi dge slong thams cad 'dir spyan drongs la rtag tu yo byad lnga phul
<p>167b.2</p>te/ skyabs su 'gro ba dang nyin gcig bzhin du dge 'dun gyi mdun du sdig pa shogs shig /khyod kyis mi mang po kha btags pa'i las bsrabs par 'gyur ro zhes smra bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas de'i tshe rgyal po des yul yul gyi dge slong rnams spyan 'dren pa gtong bar 'gyur ro/ /dge slong rnams
<p>167b.3</p>kyis kyang yul kau shAm+bI zhes bya ba na rgyal po bzod dka' zhes bya ba dge 'dun la yo byad lnga 'bul ba zhig yod do zhes thos nas yi rangs te/ yul kau shAm+bI zhes bya bar 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe yul kau shAm+bIr dge slong 'bum 'du bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas tshes bco lnga'i nub mo dge slong
<p>167b.4</p>rnams gso sbyong la 'dus te dge slong shir sha ka bos nas khyed kyis so sor thar pa'i mdo thon cig ces smra bar 'gyur ro/ /dge slong shir sha kas kyang 'di skad du khyed rnams la so sor thar pas ci zhig bya/ mi sna dang rna ba gcad pa la me long gis ci zhig bya zhes smra bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas de'i
<p>167b.5</p>tshe dge slong de dag gi nang na dgra bcom pa su ta ra zhes bya ba langs nas seng ge lta bu'i skad kyis dge slong shir sha ka la 'di skad ces khyod ci'i phyir de skad ces smra kho bo ni bde bar gshegs pas bka' stsal pa bzhin bslab pa cig kyang ma nyams so zhes smras pa dang / dge slong shir sha ka
<p>167b.6</p>shin tu skyengs par 'gyur ro/ /de nas dge slong shir sha ka'i slob ma a kan bi zhes bya bas dgra bcom pa de la 'di skad du khyod ci'i phyir nga'i slob dpon la mi mad sngar de skad smra zhes khros nas lag pa gnyis kyis sgo gtan blangs nas dgra bcom pa de gsod par 'gyur ro/ /de
<p>167b.7</p>nas dgra bcom pa de'i slob ma dge slong ka ra ta zhes bya bas kyang rang gi slob dpon gsad par mthong nas shin tu khros te dbyug pa blangs nas dge slong shir sha ka gsod par 'gyur ro/ /de'i tshe dge slong dag rim gyis khros nas phyog gnyis su chad nas gcig gis gcig gsod
<p>168a</p>
<p>168a.1</p>par 'gyur ro/ /de nas sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha thams cad der lhags te/ dge slong shi ba'i ro de dag mthong nas ngud mos 'debs shing mchod pa byed par 'gyur ro/ /dge slong de dag gis gos kha dog bsgyur ba dang skra dang sen mo yang lha'i gnas su khyer bar 'gyur
<p>168a.2</p>ro/ /de'i tshe yul der rlung dmar nag po dang / ser po dang 'dres pa ldang zhing dus dus su me'i char pa 'bab pa dang sa g.yo ba dang / 'ur sgra dang tug com dag kyang 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas rgyal po des skya rengs shar ba'i tshe 'di ltar dge slong thams cad kha btags pa
<p>168a.3</p>mthong nas/ mya ngan gyis gdungs pa'i rgyus mig gis res 'ga' ni mthong res 'ga' ni mi mthong bar 'gyur ba bzhin du myong la/ gtsug lag khang du brgyugs nas cho nges btab ste/ dgra bcom pa dang dge slong sde snod gsum pa'i ming nas 'bod cing de gnyis kyi ro pang
<p>168a.4</p>gis 'khyud de/ 'di skad du kye sde snod gsum pa khyod ni bde bar gshegs pa'i dam pa'i chos kyi mdzod 'dzin pa lags/ kye dgra bcom pa khyod ni bde bar gshegs pa'i bslab pa'i gzhi 'dzin pa lags na/ da khyed gnyis nongs pas 'jig rten 'di stongs par gyur to zhes smra
<p>168a.5</p>bar 'gyur ro/ /dam pa'i chos nub pa'i nub mo sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams kyang lha ma yin gyis pham par byas nas 'bros par 'gyur ro/ /de nyid kyi nub mo lha rtag tu myos pa'i nang nas lha 'di ni zhes bya ba 'chi 'pho bar 'gyur ro/ /de nas 'dzam bu'i gling de'i bu ram shing dang / rgun
<p>168a.6</p>dang sbrang rtsi thams cad kyang nub par 'gyur ro/ /bdud dbang sgyur zhes bya ba yang 'chi bar 'gyur te/ de nas nas dang gro dang 'bras thams cad nub par 'gyur te/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams kyi zas su sred dang khre rgod dang rtswa'i 'bras bu sna tshogs za bar 'gyur ro/ /dar dang za 'og dang man
<p>168a.7</p>tri dang / ras bzang po la sogs pa yang nub nas gos su gso ras dang / re phyar la sogs pa gyon par 'gyur ro/ /gser la sogs pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyan rnams kyang nub nas rgyan du rtswa las byas pa la sogs pa thogs par 'gyur ro/ /tshon bzang po dang ro zhim po rnams kyang
<p>168b</p>
<p>168b.1</p>nub par 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs rnams kyang klu'i gnas su 'khyer bar 'gyur ro/ /li yul gyi mkhan po rnams 'dus nas li rje btsun legs kyi ring la yos bu'i lo la brtsis nas de nas lo brgya rtsa gnyis na dam pa'i chos nub par 'gyur ro/ /dgra bcom pa dge
<p>168b.2</p>'dun 'phel gyis lung bstan pa rdzogs so//[ ]#/ /li yul lung bstan pa bzhugs so// @##/ /li'i yul lung bstan pa/ dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /li yul byung nas li'i rgyal po rabs drug ni 'das/ rabs bdun gyi rgyal
<p>168b.3</p>po bi dza ya kIrti zhes bya ba'i tshe na/ sad ka ya pra ha Na ya'i gtsug lag khang dang nye ba'i lung pa sa ka ya byi ri zhes bya ba na/ sang g+ha bar+d+ha na zhes bya ba'i dgra bcom pa zhig bzhugs te/ /de'i slob ma ban de zhig 'dul ba la slob pa las ban des tsan+d+ra gar+b+ha dang / 'dul ba'i dar ma
<p>168b.4</p>sangs rgyas kyi lung mthong nas dgra bcom pa la zhus pa/ li yul dang / shu lig dang / an se 'di gsum na sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og tu dam pa'i chos kyi gzugs brnyan dang / mchod rten bzhugs pa rnams dus ji tsam zhig na nub/ sus ni bshig /mthar ji ltar
<p>168b.5</p>'chi ba bshad cing lung bstan par gsol pa las/ dgra bcom pas bka' stsal pa/ 'di lta bu'i the tshom zhus pa ni dge'o/ /sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og tu chos kyi gzugs brnyan dang ring bsrel lo nyis stong du gnas nas nub par 'gyur ro/ /yul
<p>168b.6</p>'di gsum du rgya dang / gdong dmar dang / so byi dang / drug gu dang / hor la sogs pa dgra phal cher g.yos nas rtsod cing 'khrug par 'ong ste/ de bas na sangs rgyas kyis chos nyams shing mchod rten yang phal cher re'u rul du 'gyur ba bshig cing zhig ste/ dge 'dun gyi 'tsho ba'i
<p>168b.7</p>yo byad kyang 'chad par 'ong ngo / /yul 'di gsum la yang an se dang / shu lig ni chos mi byed pa'i dgra mang pos dkrugs te/ phal cher ni bsregs bshig ste stongs par 'gyur ro/ /gtsug lag khang 'di rnams kyi ban de yang phal cher li yul du 'ong ngo / /li yul gyi gtsug lag khang
<p>169a</p>
<p>169a.1</p>dang mchod rten la sogs pa na byang chub sems dpa' lnga brgya bzhugs te/ nyis brgya lnga bcu ni rab tu byung ba'i tshul du bzhugs/ nyis brgya lnga bcu ni khyim pa'i nang du skye ba blangs te bzhugs/ 'ge'u to shan gyi gtsug lag khang mi bskal pa bzang po'i sangs
<p>169a.2</p>rgyas stong rtsa lnga'i zhabs kyis bcags shing rgyun mi 'chad par gnas pa'i pho brang du 'gyur ro/ /'phags pa 'di rnams kyi che ba dang / thugs rje dang / byin gyi rlabs kyis li yul gyi mchod rten dang / dam pa'i chos spyod pa dang / yang yul gzhan las rgyas shing yun ring du gnas
<p>169a.3</p>so/ /rgyal po phal po che li yul 'dod pa'i phyir rtsod cing 'thabs te/ gang gis thob pa'i rgyal po de yang li yul gyi yon bdag chen por 'gyur te/ mi bshig mi 'bri bar byed cing mchod par 'ong ngo / /de'i dus na gdong dmar gyi rgyal po zhes bya ba dbang thang dang mthu skyes nas yul
<p>169a.4</p>khams gzhan mang du phrogs bzung ngo / /de'i tshe na byang chub sems dpa' gcig gdong dmar gyi rgyal po'i skye ba blangs te/ bod khams su dam pa'i chos 'byung ngo / /yul khams gzhan nas kyang chos kyi mkhan po dang / gsung rab mdo sde la sogs pa spyan drangs so/ /gdong dmar gyi
<p>169a.5</p>yul du gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten mang du brtsigs/ dge 'dun sde gnyis btsugs/ rgyal po dang blon po la sogs pa dkor ril gyis dam pa'i chos la spyod/ rgyal po gdong dmar de'i tshe li yul yang rgyal po de'i rigs su dbang bar 'gyur ro/ /dam pa'i chos dang / mchod
<p>169a.6</p>rten la sogs pa'i dkon mchog gsum gyi mnga' ris mi 'bri/ rgyas par btsugs shing mchod do/ /rgyal po gdong dmar gyi rgyud rabs bdun du dam pa'i chos spyod par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po 'di'i rabs bdun du yul khams gzhan na dkon mchog gsum gyi mchod rten bzhugs pa la ngan
<p>169a.7</p>sems dang gnod pa mi byed do/ /de'i dus na li yul gyi dge 'dun yang tsan dra gar+b+ha'i lung bstan pa las 'byung ba bzhin du dad pa bri/ chos khrims dang mi ldan/ 'jig rten gyi khe dang grags pa tshol/ rgyal po dang blon po'i dku gtsang gi nang du 'jug cing dam pa'i chos dman par byed pa
<p>169b</p>
<p>169b.1</p>dag kyang mang du 'byung ste/ de'i tshe zhang blon dang / zhang blon gyi bu tsha yang dad pa 'bri bar 'gyur ro/ /dkon mchog gsum gyi mnga' ris kyang ban des spyad pas li yul gyi mchod rten dang / dam pa'i chos la sogs pa dkon mchog gsum gyi mnga' ris kyang mngon pas 'brir 'ong ngo / /rgyal po
<p>169b.2</p>dang / blon po yang ban de de la mi dga'o/ /de'i rjes la byang chub sems dpa' cig gdong dmar gyi rgyal po byas pa'i rgyud rabs bdun gyi tha ma la rgyal po de'i chung ma rgya yul nas rgya rje'i bu mo kong co byang chub sems dpa' yin pa zhig 'khor drug brgya dang gdong dmar gyi yul du 'ongs so/ /
<p>169b.3</p>kong co de 'phags par chos la dad dbang thang che bas gdong dmar gyi rgyal po yang dad pa che ste/ sngon bas kyang dam pa'i chos rgyas par 'gyur ro/ /de'i dus na li yul gyi rgyal po gzhon zhing chos mi spyod pa zhig gis li yul gyi dge slong rnams la bsgo ba/ yang na ni skye bor bo pas shig /
<p>169b.4</p>yang na ni gar dga' bar dengs shig ces bskrad nas dge 'dun ril gyis tsar ma zhes bya ba'i lha khang du 'dus nas gros byed pa'i tshe/ lha khang gi nang 'khor 'dus pa'i dkyil nas gser gyi zan dang gser gyi 'khur ba cha bdun byung nas dge slong lnga stong rgyal pos 'tsho ba bcad de/ mi
<p>169b.5</p>'byor ba'i zla ba gsum du 'tsho ba'i zong du 'gyur/ de'i tshe de'i dus na la la ni skye por babs/ ma babs pa gung du 'gro ba rnams kyang pha ma dang / gnyen 'dun dang / yul sa dang 'bral ba mi dga' ste/ ngud mo chen po 'byung ngo / /dge 'dun phal mang po lam du zhugs te/ /song
<p>169b.6</p>ba las 'bong zhes bya ba'i lha khang du phyin pa dang / de na mchod rten chen po zhig bzhugs pa rlung gi rgyal po dad pa can gyis dral te/ nang nas gser gyi phor pa mu tig gis bkang ba zhig byung nas dge 'dun spyi la phul lo/ /gzhan yon bdag dang pa can gyis 'tsho ba'i yo byad sna sna nas
<p>169b.7</p>phul lo/ /de nas dge 'dun rnams mdo le me skar gyi yul du phyin te/ mu tig gis zla ba phyed kyi 'tsho ba'i yo byad sbyar ro/ /me skar nas song te/ rkong nya zhes bya ba'i lha khang na dge 'dun bzhugs pa'i tshe bai shra ma Na dang / dpal gyi lha mo mi khyo shug tu sprul nas yul de na 'dug ste/ 
<p>170a</p>
<p>170a.1</p>dge 'dun thams cad la bdag cag bsod nams bgyid do zhes gsol nas/ /zla ba phyed kyi bar du dge 'dun la mchod ston gsol nas dpal gyi lha mos phu rung gang gi gser gyi dong rtse dge 'dun spyir phul te/ dge 'dun ril gyis gdong dmar gyi yul du kha
<p>170a.2</p>bltas te song ba las/ yul pha shan gyi rong du gcan pa dang phrad de ma bkye'o/ /lam gzhan yod na song zhig ces zer to/ /de'i tshe bai shra ma Na g.yag dkar po rgal ba can snal chu yod pa zhig tu sprul pa dge 'dun gyis mthong ste/ g.yag rgal can 'di ni mi'i phyugs
<p>170a.3</p>yin pas 'di gar 'gro ba'i phyi bzhin du 'deng zhes zer ro/ /de'i tshe g.yag des nye lam du drangs te/ zhag bzhi lngas ban de ril gyis gdong dmar gyi yul tshal byi zhes bya bar phyin to/ /de'i tshe yul de'i dbang pos dge 'dun mang po zhig stod phyogs nas byon to zhes gdong dmar gyi rgyal
<p>170a.4</p>po la sbran to/ /de'i tshe rgyal po'i btsun mos rgyal po la stong phyogs nas dge 'dun yul stor te 'khyams nas byon pa sun ma dang yo byad bdag sbyor na/ gdong dmar gyi yul du spyan drang bar ci gnang zhes gsol nas gnang ste/ dge 'dun rnams bzhon pa dang 'tsho bas bsu nas gdong dmar
<p>170a.5</p>gyi yul du phyin to/ /de nas gdong dmar gyi rgyal po dang / kong co 'khor dang bcas pas mchod rten la phyag byas nas dge slong 'di'i nang na sde snod gsum la mkhas pa'i mkhan po rnams ma gtogs par gzhan 'di ltar mkhas pa bzhugs sam zhes dris pa dang / mkhan po na re an se dang / shu
<p>170a.6</p>lig dang / bru sha dang / kha che zhes bya ba'i yul na 'di 'dra bar mkhas pa'i dge 'dun mang du yod do zhes smras pa dang / de'i mod la 'gugs pa'i pho nya btang ste/ dge 'dun ril gyis gdong dmar gyi yul du spyan drangs so/ /de'i tshe gdong dmar gyi yul du gtsug lag khang bdun brtsigs so/ /
<p>170a.7</p>mchod pa'i yo byad dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi mnga' ris kyang sngon pas bskyed nas dge 'dun rnams kyang gtsug lag khang bdun gyi nang du so sor bzhugs so/ /de'i rjes la lo gsum mam bzhi na kong co'i snying gar 'brum chen byung nas na ba'i tshe kong cos rgyal po la gsol pa/ bdag
<p>170b</p>
<p>170b.1</p>ni nad 'di las mi 'tsho ste/ nga 'gum na bdag gi bran dang / nor phyugs rnams dkon mchog gsum la ma gum par 'bul lo zhes gsol te phul lo/ /'khor drug brgya yang dge bsnyen gyi mtshan mas btab ste rab tu phyung ngo / /de'i rjes la kong co 'das so/ /kong co 'das pa'i 'og tu
<p>170b.2</p>rgyal po gdong dmar gyi khams su 'brum nad 'byung ste blon po dang / zhang blon gyi bu tsha la sogs pa mang du 'chi'o/ /de'i tshe blon po rnams 'dus te rgyal po la gsol pa/ sngon rgyal khams 'di na 'di 'dra ba'i 'brum nad ma byung na/ nga ltar lho bal gyi dge slong 'khyams pa mang
<p>170b.3</p>po 'ongs nas kong co yang 'das/ blon po dang zhang blon las kyang mang du gum pas ban de 'di kun yang rgyal khams su mi gzhag par bskrad pa'i rigs zhes gsol ba las rgyal pos 'di bskrad pa'i rigs sam mi rigs da dung zhib tu dpyod cig ces bsgo ba las blon po rnams ban de bskrad par kha
<p>170b.4</p>'dus nas rgyal po la gsol te/ rgyal khams su ban de ril gyis mi gnas par gros chad nas kun bskrad pa las gdong dmar gyi dge slong khros te/ dge slong 'di rnams bskrad nas bdag cag kyang 'di na mi 'dug go zhes byas pa dang / blon po rnams khros nas khyed rnams kyang
<p>170b.5</p>gang dga' bar dengs shig ces bsgo'o/ /kong co gdong dmar gyi yul du 'ongs pa'i 'og tu rgyal pos te'u shi'i chos bzung nas rgya'i dge slong yang ril gyis gdong dmar gyi yul du 'ongs so/ /de'i dus na rgyal khams de'i dge slong gis gdong dmar gyi khams kyi ring bsrel
<p>170b.6</p>dang / gsung rab dang / mchod pa'i yo byad dkon mchog gi mnga' ris gcig kyang ma lus par bkal nas nub phyogs su kha bltas te/ gan d+ha ra chen po'i yul du 'gro bar chas te song ngo / /de'i tshe rgya dang / gdong dmar dang / rgya gar dang / li la sogs pa gang+gA tshun chad na dam
<p>170b.7</p>pa'i chos spyod pa yang nub par 'gyur ro/ /gang+gA'i pha rol na kau shAm+bI'i yul du ni zla ba gsum zhig gnas te nub bo/ /gan d+ha ra'i yul gyi 'dab na klu'i rgyal po e la pa tra'i gnas mtsho'i 'gram du dge 'dun rnams phyin pa dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi byin gyi rlabs kyis mtsho
<p>171a</p>
<p>171a.1</p>yang rnyogs shing 'khrugs par gyur nas/ klu'i rgyal pos nga'i gnas ci ste rnyogs shing 'khrugs snyam ste/ 'phrul gyi mig gis bltas nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i gsung rab dang / dam pa'i chos nub tu nye ste/ dge 'dun phal mo che mthong ba'i dus 'di yin par
<p>171a.2</p>shes nas rgan po zhig tu sprul nas/ mtsho'i 'gram du byung nas dge 'dun la phyag byas te dris pa/ dge 'dun 'di snyed cig ga la byon/ gar gshegs/ dge 'dun gyis smras pa/ bdag cag rgyal po gdong dmar gyi yul na gnas pa las yon bdag dad pa bri/ dkon mchog gi
<p>171a.3</p>rten bshig pas bdag cag gan d+ha ra chen po'i yul du 'gro'o zhes smras pa dang / rgan pa na re dge 'dun 'di snyed cig la 'tsho ba ci mnga'/ gan d+ha ra chen po'i yul du mtsho chen po 'di bskor nas 'gro na zhag bzhi bcu'i lam yod do/ /dge 'dun la zhag nyi shu'i 'tsho ba las med na phyin tam
<p>171a.4</p>zhes smras pa dang / dge 'dun phal cher smre zhing ngu ba klu'i rgyal pos mthong ste/ klu'i rgyal po mi dga' nas gdung ba skyes te dge 'dun la smras pa/ thad ka 'di na nye lam sbrul kyi zam pa zhig yod de/ de'i steng du 'gro nus na myur du phyin zhes smras nas rgan po mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas klu'i
<p>171a.5</p>rgyal po des ri gar 'dzeg pa'i lam zhig snang bar byas/ bdag dngos sbrul chen po zhig tu sprul te/ mtsho'i steng du zam par bcas nas dge 'dun phal cher bsgral nas sngon sdig pa byas pa'i las kyis da ltar byol song gi lus thob pa 'di yang thar ram snyam bsams te/ smon lam btab nas sbrul
<p>171a.6</p>gyi zam pa btsugs so/ /de'i tshe nyin zhag bco lnga mi phyugs rnams rgal ba las mi phyugs kha cig ni sbrul gyi zam pa las lhung ste shi'o/ /mi phyugs mang po rgyu ba'i tshe sbrul gyi rgyab kyang la lar ni rdol/ la lar ni ral te rnag khrag gi thigs pa char bzhin du zags pas mtsho yang khrag can du byas so/ /
<p>171a.7</p>dge 'dun mang po sbrul gyi zam pa rgal ba'i mjug kyang gdong dmar gyis bcad do/ /de'i rjes la sbrul mtshor lhung ste/ tshe 'das nas dga' ldan gyi gnas su skyes so/ /mtsho yang bskams so/ /de'i dus na dge 'dun rnams gan d+ha ra'i rgyal po'i yul du lo gnyis kyi bar du 'tsho ba'i yo
<p>171b</p>
<p>171b.1</p>byad sbyar/ so sor ci bder gzhag go/ /lo gnyis lon pa dang rgyal po de tshe 'das so/ /rgyal po la bu gnyis yod pa gcig ni lha chos la dad/ gcig ni mu stegs kyi chos spyod pas rgyal thabs la rtsod par gyur nas lha chos spyod pa'i non ban des byas te/ de rgyal nas rgyal thabs kyang des
<p>171b.2</p>gzung ngo / /rgyal po de'i tshe dge 'dun yang sngar bas dbang thang bskyed de/ yo byad dang bde bar ldan par gyur nas lo phyed lon pa dang / ban de gcig gis rgyal po bsad nas rgyal srid ban des gzung bas gan d+ha ra'i rgyal 'bangs ril log ste/ ban de rgyal po byed pa de bsad do/ /ban de
<p>171b.3</p>gzhan rnams kyang rgyal khams de na mi gnas par ril gyis bskrad nas gan d+ha ra'i yul du yang chos nub po/ /de nas dge 'dun rnams kyang yul khams gzhan du 'khyams shing 'dong ngo / /de'i tshe de'i dus na nub phyogs kyi rgyal po dang / byang phyogs kyi rgyal po yan pa la sogs pa sngar
<p>171b.4</p>bas dbang thang bskyed de/ rgyal po gsum mjal dum byas nas rgyal po 'di gsum gyis nub phyogs dang / byang phyogs kyi yul yang bzung / rgyal po de gsum gcig cing yang dmag 'bum dang chas te/ kau shAm+bI'i yul du drangs pas kau shAm+bI'i rgyal pos dam gsum 'bum rgyal po
<p>171b.5</p>dang bcas te gcig kyang ma las par byas so/ /de nas kau shAm+b+hi'i rgyal pos dmag mang po bsad pa'i sdig sbyang ba'i phyir 'dzam bu'i gling gi dge slong ril spyan drangs nas kau shAm+bI'i yul du phyin pa'i rjes/ dge 'dun 'khrugs nas gcig gis gcig bsad de/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi
<p>171b.6</p>spyi'i lha chos kun der nub po/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das nas lo bye ba phrag lnga bcu rtsa bdun dang / sa ya phrag drug na sangs rgyas byams pa mi mjed kyi 'jig rten du sems can gyi don la gshegs so/ /tsan dra gar b+ha'i lung bstan pa dang mthun no/ /'phags
<p>171b.7</p>pa'i mchod rten go ma sa la gan d+ha dang / glang mgo ri'i steng na sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i sku gzugs chen po bzhugs pa'i yon tan mdo tsam btus pa'i gzhung la sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs nas 'gro ba mang po'i don du bla na med pa'i sangs
<p>172a</p>
<p>172a.1</p>rgyas te bzhugs pa'i pho brang spyir nyi shu rtsa gcig bzhugs pa la/ li yul 'di yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i pho brang nyi shu rtsa gcig pa lags te/ bzhugs pa'i pho brang gzhan pas yon tan lhag par che/ li yul ni gna' mtshor mchis pa'i dus na sangs
<p>172a.2</p>rgyas shAkya thub pas yul du 'gyur bar lung bstan cing byin gyis brlab pa'i slad du byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos dang / lha klu sde brgyad la sogs te 'khor khri phrag nyi shu dang / bya rgod phung po'i ri la bar snang las ldings te/ li yul mtshor gyur par gshegs
<p>172a.3</p>nas da ltar chu bo shel chab mgo ma'i 'gram na chab kyi steng pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs te/ mtsho 'di yul du 'gyur bar lung bstan byin gyis brlabs te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brgyad 'khor nyi khri dang / mgon po srung ma brgyad 'khor sum khri lnga stong lnga brgya
<p>172a.4</p>rtsa bdun rnams la 'phags pa'i mchod gnas 'di dang / yul srung bar bka' zhal gyis gtad de/ dam stsal ba'i rjes la/ shA ri'i bu dang / rnam thos kyi bus snag gi ri dril te chab pho nas dogs dga' pa dang / sangs rgyas sngar pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs te/ ri glang ru'i steng da ltar
<p>172a.5</p>shAkya thub pa'i sku gzugs chen po bzhugs pa'i sar gdugs mtshan bdun gyi bar du ting nge 'dzin gyis rnam par rol cing bzhugs nas slar rgya gar gyi yul yangs pa'i grong khyer du gshegs te/ mya ngan las 'das nas dgung lo brgya lon pa dang / li yul yang yul du gyur nas
<p>172a.6</p>sngar yang sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i steng na pad+mo la bzhugs pa'i thad kar da ltar go mas la gan d+ha'i mchod rten bzhugs pa'i nang na shel ljang gu'i pho brang gi steng glang mgo tsan+dan las bgyis pa'i mchod rten gyi nang na gnas pa'i sangs rgyas rabs bzhi'i ring bsrel bzhugs te/ la la gnas der
<p>172a.7</p>phyin te mchod pa gces spras kyi mchod do cog thams cad lung bstan cing phyir mi ldog par rig par bya ste/ gdugs tshan bdun gyi bar du bskor cing mchod pa bgyis na mtshams med pa lnga'i sdig pa 'byang bar 'gyur ro zhes 'byung ngo / /dngar ldan gyi grong khyer mkhar dge ba can gyi shar
<p>172b</p>
<p>172b.1</p>phyogs na 'phags pa'i mchod gnas sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan zhing byin gyis brlabs pa'i ad+ha ma'i mchod rten lcags thag can bzhugs pa yang mgon po sum cu rtsa gsum gyi gnas rten/ lha klu sde brgyad la sogs te srung ma rnams dus bzhi'i rab la 'du ba'i 'dus pa
<p>172b.2</p>chen po ste/ dge 'dun sde gnyis dang / yul gyi dpon sna rnams kyis gna' mchod rten 'di srid pa tshun chad deng sang gi bar du dus bzhi'i rab la nar mar mchod pa che thang du bgyid/ gzhung las kyang li yul du mi ngas dang phyi dgra la sogs te ma legs pa byung ba'i dus su theg pa chen po'i
<p>172b.3</p>mdo sde 'dus pa chen po dang / dam pa'i chos pad+ma dkar po'i mdo sde bklags na g.yul zhi bar 'gyur zhes 'byung bas gzhung la brten te lugs su stsal nas deng sang gi bar du dgung lo gcig bzhin dpyid dang / dbyar dang / ston 'u then gyi dge 'dun bzhugs so/ /'tshal gyi dgung
<p>172b.4</p>bdun gyi bar gong du smos pa'i mdo sde la sogs pa klog cing thugs dam bskul ba dang / bsngo bcol rgya cher bgyid/ mchod rten chen po brgyad la yul ser skya'i grong khyer lum pa'i tshal du mchod rten chen po gcig /yul ma ga d+hA rgyal po'i khab chu bo nai ra ny+dza na'i 'gram rdo rje'i gdan
<p>172b.5</p>la mngon par byang chub pa'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig yul ma ga d+d+hAr rgyal po'i khab tu bdud kyi dmag 'bum phrag bco brgyad btul ba'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig sangs rgyas mngon par byang chub nas gdugs tshan bdun gyi bar du cang mi gsung bar bzhugs pa dang / tshangs
<p>172b.6</p>pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gsol ba btab pa'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig /yul kA shi bA rA Na sI'i grong khyer gyi drung na ri dgas kyi tshal du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig /yul ko sa la mnyam du yod pa'i grong khyer du mar bdud sde dgu bcu rtsa drug
<p>172b.7</p>pham par mdzad nas cho 'phrul chen po bstan pa'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig /yul ba sang sang ga sha'i grong khyer du sangs rgyas sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha yul nas gshegs pa'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig /gyad yul rtsa mchog gi grong khyer shing sA la zung gi 'og tu mya ngan
<p>173a</p>
<p>173a.1</p>las 'das pa'i sar mchod rten chen po gcig /ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po brgyad la ra ma gra ma ka'i yul du mchod rten chen po gcig /pa pa'i yul du ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /gyad yul na ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /yangs
<p>173a.2</p>pa'i yul na ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /tsany+tsA kalpa'i yul na ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /baiSh+NU dwI pa'i yul na ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /ser skya'i yul na ring bsrel gyi mchod rten chen po gcig /rgyal po'i khab na ring bsrel gyi
<p>173a.3</p>mchod rten chen po gcig /li yul gyi lo rgyus dang / gtsug lag khang dang / dge 'dun sde gnyis kyi grangs ni gna' thog ma sangs rgyas 'od srungs 'jig rten du byung ba'i tshe li yul yang de tsam na yul du gyur te/ de na gnas pa'i mi rnams kyang chos bgyid/ slad kyi sangs rgyas 'od
<p>173a.4</p>srungs kyi chos bstan pa gzhag pa nub pa'i tshe/ li yul gyi chos kyang zhig nas drang srong khar shwa dang / kha re'u steng zhes bgyi ba la sogs pa drang srong mang po'i yul mi ring ba zhig tu li yul phyogs kyi ri rtsa dag na gnas te/ des na dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyid bgyid pa las slad kyi drang srong de
<p>173a.5</p>rnams la mi ngan kha cig gis gtses nas rngan can bgyis/ bkur sti dang rim gro ma bgyis pas drang srong de rnams kyang mi dga' nas li yul spangs te/ nam mkha' la ldings nas yul gzhan du mchis/ de nas ni li yul gyi mi rnams kyang chos la ma dad de lta ba log par gyur te/ klu rnams
<p>173a.6</p>mi dga' ste chab byung nas li yul yang mtshor gyur to/ /yun ring mo zhig tu mtshor mchis mchis pa las slad kyi yang sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa rgya gar yul du byung ste/ sems can gyi don mdzad cing chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la sogs pa sangs rgyas kyi phrin las su mdzad pa rnams
<p>173a.7</p>mdzad nas mya ngan las 'da' bar bstan pa nye ba zhig gi dus na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa rgyal po'i khab bya rgod phung po'i ri la bzhugs te zla ba'i snying po gsungs pa'i tshe yul khams so so'i mgon po dang / lha klu la sogs pa srung ma rnams la gtad pa'i
<p>173b</p>
<p>173b.1</p>dus na li yul yang lung bstan te/ rnam thos kyi sras dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po la sogs yang dag shes dang / rgyal po ma skyes dgra'i bu mo dri ma med pa'i 'od dang / gzhon nu rdo rje sde dang / lha'i bu mo blo rab brtan dang / lha mo 'phrog ma la
<p>173b.2</p>sogs pa 'khor dang bcas pa la gtad nas bcom ldan 'das nyid kyang 'khor rnam bzhi 'bum phrag du ma dang nam mkha' la ldings nas li yul du gshegs te/ da ltar 'gum tir gyi mchod rten chen po bzhugs pa'i thad kar mtsho'i steng du ta la bdun srid tsam gyi gnam 'phang gi nam
<p>173b.3</p>mkha' la pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs nas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing so so nas de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis li yul byin gyis brlab pa'i slad du bskul ba'i 'od zer phyogs su khyab par btang / phyogs bcu na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis kyang li yul
<p>173b.4</p>byin gyis brlab pa'i slad du sangs rgyas kyi zhing so so nas sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa la mchod pa bgyid pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor dang yul 'khor bsrung zhing byin gyis brlab pa'i sngags kyi snying po dang / 'od zer btang nas dus gcig tu sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa'i spyi gtsug tu
<p>173b.5</p>'dus par byin gyis brlabs nas dge'o zhes bya ba'i sgra chen po byung ngo / /de nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas kyang li yul mtshor gyur pa 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad nas 'od zer de dag las chu'i khar pad+ma sum brgya drug cu rtsa gsum byung / pad+ma re re'i khar yang me mar kha re re
<p>173b.6</p>byung de nas 'od zer de dag gcig tu 'dus nas chab kyi steng du g.yas phyogs su lan gsum bskor nas chu'i dkyil du nub par 'gyur ro/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis 'phags pa shA ri'i bu dang / rnam thos kyi sras la bka' stsal pa/ khyed kyis maM sa bar na barba ta zhes bya ba'i
<p>173b.7</p>ri snag gi kha dog 'dra ba'i mtsho 'di drol zhig ces bka' stsal nas/ 'phags pa shA ri'i bu'i gseg shang gi rtsa ba dang / rnam thos sras kyi mdung rtses mtsho dral nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyang glang mgo'i ri steng na sku gzugs chen po bzhugs pa'i g.yon logs kyi lha khang gi nang
<p>174a</p>
<p>174a.1</p>na da ltar mchod rten chung ngu zhig bzhugs pa'i sar sems can gyi don mdzad pa'i slad du dgung bdun de na bzhugs so/ /de nas 'phags pa kun dga' bos bcom ldan 'das la zhus pa/ bcom ldan 'das ci'i rgyu/ ci'i rkyen gyis 'od zer dang / pad+mo dang / me mar 'di
<p>174a.2</p>dag snang bar 'gyur/ ci'i rgyu ci'i rkyen gyis 'od zer 'di rnams gcig tu 'dus nas g.yas logs su lan gsum bskor te chab kyi dkyil du nub/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis kun dga' bo la bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bus gseg shang gi rtsa ba dang / rnam thos sras kyi
<p>174a.3</p>mdung rtses mtsho dral bas phyis 'tsho bskams nas nga mya ngan las 'das pa'i 'og tu yul li yul zhes bya ba 'di 'byung ste/ 'od zer lan gsum 'khor ba'i sar ni kho ra khor yug tu phyis 'u then gyis mkhar lnga ldan gyi grong khyer chen po brtsig par 'gyur ro/ /chu'i dkyil du 'od
<p>174a.4</p>zer nub pa'i sar ni yul byin gyis rlob cing srung ba'i rA dza gra ma'i sangs rgyas kyi sku gzugs ngas tsan+dan gyi nang du sku'i grib ma nub par byin gyis brlabs te byas pa zhig rgya gar yul nas nam mkha' las gshegs te bzhugs par 'gyur ro/ /chu'i nang na pad+mo dang me mar byung ba'i sar
<p>174a.5</p>ni phyis theg pa chen po spyod pa'i dge slong pho mo gnas pa'i gtsug lag khang chen po sum brgya drug cu rtsa gsum rgyal po la sogs pa yon bdag dad pa can rnams kyis brtsigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung la mchod pa byed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dge slong pho mo'i tshul
<p>174a.6</p>du gnas pa nyis brgya lnga bcu dang khyim pa skye bo'i tshul du gnas pa nyis brgya lnga bcu ste lnga brgya rtag tu gnas so/ /gzhan yang phyir mi ldog pa'i sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' theg pa chen po'i chos la rgyas par spyod pa phal cher gnas te/ 'di ni dus gsum du gshegs pa'i
<p>174a.7</p>sangs rgyas kyi zhing khud pa yin no zhes byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' brgyad dang / rnam thos kyi sras dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po yang dag shes dang / rigs kyi bu mo dri ma med pa'i 'od dang / gzhon nu
<p>174b</p>
<p>174b.1</p>rdo rje lcam dral dang / lha klu la sogs pa la dus thams cad du srungs shig par de bzhin gshegs pas gtad do/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal dang / byams pa dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang phyug dang / nam mkha'i snying po dang / sa'i snying po dang / 
<p>174b.2</p>kun du bzang po dang / mthu chen dang / sman gyi rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' dang / rnam thos kyi sras 'khor gnod sbyin sum stong dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes 'khor khri phrag bcu dang / lha gzhan gyis mi thub pa'i 'khor stong dang / nam mkha'i spyan 'khor brgyad stong
<p>174b.3</p>dang / lha'i bu gser phreng 'khor lnga brgya dang / klu'i rgyal po gnas dros po 'khor stong dang / lha mo lcags kyu can 'khor stong phrag bcu dang / lha mo gnas ldan ma 'khor lnga stong dang / rigs kyi bu mo dri ma med pa'i 'od dang / gzhon nu rdo rje sde dang / lha'i bu blo rab brtan dang / lha mo 'phrog
<p>174b.4</p>ma 'khor dang bcas pa la sogs pas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar dam tshig bcas nas li yul bsrung bar zhal gyis bzhes te/ deng sang gi bar du yang 'phags pa byang chub sems dpa' 'di brgyad dang / rnam thos kyi sras la sogs pa'i mgon po dang / lha dang / klu dang / lha mo rnams thog ma
<p>174b.5</p>sangs rgyas gau to shan du gshegs te 'khor mang pos bskor nas bzhugs pa'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' 'di rnams dang / mgon po dang lha klu rnams ga la bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas dang / dam tshig blangs pa'i sar da dung yang yul srung zhing byin gyis rlob/ mngon rtags dang mtshan ma dag kyang / 
<p>174b.6</p>'byung / de nas sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas dgung lo nyis brgya sum cu rtsa bzhi lon pa'i 'og tu rgya gar gyi rgyal po d+harma a sho ka zhes bgyi ba zhig gis sngon sems can mang po zhig bkum pa las slad kyi 'phags pa dgra bcom pa ya sho zhes bgyi ba zhig gis dge ba'i bshes gnyen
<p>174b.7</p>bgyis nas/ sngar sdig pa mi dge ba'i las ci bgyis pa mthol zhing bshags/ slad kyis mi bgyi bar yang yi dam bcas/ 'dzam bu'i gling na sangs rgyas shAkya thub pas byin gyis brlabs pa'i gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten bzhugs pa rnams su mchod pa bgyid cing / dogs
<p>175a</p>
<p>175a.1</p>byin can gnyen po byin gyis brlabs pa mchis so 'tshal du gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten brgyad khri bzhi stong brtsig tu mchis pa las mtsho bskams nas li yul yang stong du mchis pa'i tshe/ da ltar 'u then gyi sku mkhar mchis pa'i dog sar kus po yen du shul phyung nas
<p>175a.2</p>dro dgongs shig btab pa'i nub mo rgyal po'i btsun mo dam pa las khye'u mtshan dang ldan pa bzang po zhig btsas nas/ sngon rgyal po'i btsun mos de kun dga' ra ba'i skyed mos tshal du mchis pa las/ rdzing bu'i nang du khrus bgyid cing mchis pa'i dus na rnam thos sras 'khor dang bcas pa nam mkha'
<p>175a.3</p>la gshegs pas kyang gzigs/ rgyal po'i btsun mos kyang rnam thos sras kyi sras byad bzhin bzang po mthong bas sems kyi bur chags pas kus po yin du btsas nas/ rgyal po d+harma a sho kas ltas mkhan rnams bkug ste/ bu 'di'i tshe ring ngam thung / mtshan ma bzang ngan dang / dbang thang ci yod ces
<p>175a.4</p>brtags na/ ltas mkhan rnams kyi mchid nas bu 'di mtshan ma yang bzang / dbang thang yang rab tu che ste/ mi tha mal pa ma lags pas rgyal po yab sku tshe ma 'phos par rgyal po bgyid par 'gyur zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal po d+harma a sho ka phrag dog skyes te khros nas/ kho de ltar dbang thang che na kho bdag
<p>175a.5</p>'tsho zhing srid 'dzin grang / 'di nga la mi dgos kyis bor cig ces mchis nas/ mas kyang bu 'di mi bor du ni rgyal po khro zhing drag shul che bas bu bkum du dogs nas mas bu de bor ba las slad kyis sa las nu ma byung nas de 'tshal ba las ma gum nas ming yang phyis sa nur btags so/ /de'i rjes la rgya rje byang
<p>175a.6</p>chub sems dpa' chen po bu stong dbang ba cig byung ste/ de la bu dgu brgya dgu bcu rtsa dgu ni mchis na/ stong du bu gcig gis ma tshang bas rnam thos kyi sras la gsol ba btab ste bslangs pa las rnam thos kyi sras kyis bltas pa na khye'u sa nu bsod nams can por ba mthong nas blangs te rgya rje'i bu skal du
<p>175a.7</p>stsal/ de nas rgya rjes bu de gsos nas slad kyi khye'u chen por skyes nas rgya'i bu spun dang byis pa rtse rtse ba las 'thabs nas khyod rgya rje'i bu ma yin no zhes bgyis pa dang / khye'u de glo ba mi dga' nas mi gzhan dag la yang lo rgyus smras na yang de ltar gyur nas rgya rje la bdag thog ma skyes pa'i
<p>175b</p>
<p>175b.1</p>yul tshol/ sa tshol du mchi bar ci gnang zhes gsol ba las/ rgya rje'i zhal nas khyod nga'i bu yin te/ yul sa yang 'di yin mi dga' ma byed cig ces lan du ma bsgo ba las ma nyan nas rgya rjes rgyal bu sa nu rgyal po'i thabs stsal te/ dmag stong phrag bcu dang bsgrags te nub
<p>175b.2</p>phyogs su yul tshol/ sa tshol du btang ba las li yul gyi me skar du phyin te/ de nas mchis pa la rgya gar yul nas kyang rgyal po d+harma a sho ka'i blon po ya sha zhes bgyi pa la dku dar nas/ blon po ya sha spad spun rje khol 'khor yan chad rgyal po la mi dga' ba bdun stong yul nas byung ste/ nub phyogs
<p>175b.3</p>shar phyogs su yul tshol sa tshol du mchis mchis pa las/ 'u then gyi shel chab gong ma'i yul phyogs su mchis pa dang rgyal bu sa nu'i 'khor gyi tshong pa shel bgyi ba dang / zong bgyi ba gnyis la ba sbrum ma thun mong ba cig mchis pa las/ /ba bu nad langs nas me skar nas zhugs ngams thang kar
<p>175b.4</p>brtol te to lar bros pa las/ mi de gnyis kyis rjes bzhin du bdas pa las to lar slebs te/ ba be'u 'brangs pa las yul de'i ming yang be'u 'brangs pa'i sa 'bru so lo nya zhes btags/ to la'i zhugs ngams kyi ming yang li skad du sher bzang zhes btags te de nas mi gnyis kyis bltas nas/ yul
<p>175b.5</p>ljongs stong pa bzang po zhig gda' nas 'di bdag cag gi rgyal bu sa nu'i yul sar rung ngo zhes mchid gros su 'tshal nas yul sa de lta zhig mchis mchis pa dang / 'u then gyi shel chab gong mar mchis pa dang / blon po ya sha'i 'khor dang mjal nas khyed su'i mi/ ga las mchis zhes smras pa dang / mi de
<p>175b.6</p>gnyis kyis kyang rgyal bu sa nu'i lo rgyus zhib tu bshad pa dang / ya shas kyang rgyal bu sa nu me skar na mchis pa'i steng du pho nyas 'phrin pa las khyod ni rgyal rigs/ bdag ni blon po'i rigs na/ chu srid cig tu 'tham ste/ khyod kyis ni rgyal po byas/ bdag gis blon po byas te'u then gyi ljongs
<p>175b.7</p>'dir yul sar btsugs na rung ngo zhes mchi na/ de nas rgyal bu sa nu yang 'khor dang bcas te 'u then gyi shel chu gong mar mchis nas tshar 'di nya'i 'og yul hang gu dzo zhes bgyi bar mjal te/ rgyal bu dang blon po ya sha gnyis yul sa la ma dum ste/ dmag bkye ste 'thabs pa las nam mkha'
<p>176a</p>
<p>176a.1</p>las rnam thos kyi sras dang / dpal gyi lha mo byung nas bshug te/ 'thab tu ma stsal nas/ dog sa de nyid du rnam thos kyi sras dang / dpal gyi lha mo bzhugs pa'i steng khang re re zhig brtsigs pa yang deng sang gi bar du mchis te/ yul gyi srung mar gtso bo rnam thos kyi sras dang / 
<p>176a.2</p>dpal gyi lha mo mchod pa yang de lags/ de nas rgyal bu sa nu dang / blon po ya sha yang dum nas sa nus ni rgyal po bgyis/ ya shas ni blon po bgyis nas rgyal po sa nu'i 'khor rgya rnams ni'u than gyi shel chu 'og ma man chad mdo lo skor dang / skam sheng yan chad du bkod/ blon po
<p>176a.3</p>ya sha'i 'khor rgya gar rnams ni shel chu gong ma yan chad rgya dang / kong sheng man chad du bkod/ shel chu dbus ni rgya gar dang / rgya'i blon po dang / 'bangs stod rims 'dres par bkod nas yul btsugs mkhar brtsigs te/ rgya gar dang rgya phrad pa'i yul ni li lags te/ 'phral skad
<p>176a.4</p>ni rgya gar dang rgyar mi mthun pa/ yi ge ni rgya gar dang bags kyis mthun/ 'jig rten pa'i lugs ni rgya dang phal cher mthun/ chos kyi lugs dang chos skad ni rgya gar dang phal cher mthun/ li'i 'phral skad ni thog ma byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dpal nyan thos kyi dge slong gi tshul du sprul te/ 
<p>176a.5</p>mtshan bai ro tsa na zhes bgyi bas byis pa phyugs rdzi khye'u 'jos dang / mu le 'ji zhes bgyi ba gnyis la sogs pa la yul tsar ma zhes bgyi bar li skad phyung ste/ kun la bslabs nas/ khye'u de gnyis kyang gar mchis pa'i cha su la yang ma mchis te/ 'di skad kyang thog ma 'phags pa rnams
<p>176a.6</p>kyis bstan zhing bslabs pa las/ thog ma li yul byung nas dgung lo du lon pa ni gau to shan gyi mkhan po mo rgu de shing la sogs pa mkhan po bgres rims rnams kyis mkhan po snga rabs rnams la bka' mchid thos pa dang / 'phags pa rnams kyis lung bstan pa dang / li rje'i rgyal rabs
<p>176a.7</p>kyi yi ge dang zhib tu gtugs nas/ gna' thog ma rgya gar yul du rgyal po ma skyes dgras rgyal po bgyis pa nas brtsis na rgyal po ma skyes dgras spyir dgung lo sum cu rtsa gnyis rgyal po bgyis pa las/ rgyal srid bzung ste dgung lo lnga lags pa las sangs rgyas mya ngan las
<p>176b</p>
<p>176b.1</p>'das/ de tshun chad dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun rgyal po bgyis te/ rgyal po ma skyes dgra nas rgyal po d+harma a sho ka'i bar du rgya gar gyi rgyal po rabs bcus rgyal srid bzung ste/ d+harma a sho kas spyir rgyal po dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa lnga bgyis pa las rgyal por zhugs nas dgung lo
<p>176b.2</p>sum cu lags pa'i 'og tu rgyal bu sa nu btsas te/ sa nu dgung lo bcu gnyis lon pa'i tshe rgyal rje rgyal thabs btsal nas/ thog ma skyes pa'i yul tshol sa tshol du mchis pa las rgyal po sa nu dgung lo bcu dgu lon pa'i tshe li yul btsugs te/ thog ma li rjer zhugs pa
<p>176b.3</p>yan chad zhib tu brtsis nas sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas dgung lo nyis brgya sum cu rtsa bzhi lags nas li yul yang gdod byung bar 'gyur/ rgyal bu sa nu thog mar li rjer zhugs nas rgyal srid bzung tshun chad dang / li rje btsan bzang btsan la brtan thog mar li rjer bskos nas
<p>176b.4</p>li rje'i rabs lnga bcu rtsa drug dang / chag tshab cig byung ngo / /gna' dang po mtsho bskams nas rgyal bu sa nu dang / blon po ya sha la sogs pas thog mar gzhi bzung ste yul btsugs/ rgyal bu sa nu'i bu rgyal po ye'u la zhes bgyi bas 'u then gyi dngar ldan gyi grong khyer
<p>176b.5</p>brtsigs te/ li yul byung nas dgung lo brgya drug cu rtsa lnga 'das pa'i 'og tu rgyal bu ye'u la'i bu rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba zhes bgyi bas rgyal por zhugs nas dgung lo lnga lags nas li yul du thog mar chos byung ste/ 'jam dpal dang byams pa gnyis kyis li yul
<p>176b.6</p>'di dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi khud pa lags par thugs su chud nas byams pa ni mir skye ba blangs te/ rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba zhes bya ba sprul/ 'jam dpal ni dge slong 'phags pa bai ro tsa na'i gzugs su sprul nas las dang nyon mongs pa mthar phyin pa'i gnas yul
<p>176b.7</p>tsar ma tsu le'i tshal du gshegs te/ li yul na mchis pa'i sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mdzad cing li skad kyang byis pa phyugs rdzi rnams la bcos shing bstan/ li'i yi ge yang bslabs nas de'i 'og tu chos byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po ye'u la'i rgyal po bi
<p>177a</p>
<p>177a.1</p>dza ya saM b+ha bas yon bdag bgyis nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa bai ro tsa na'i slad du thog mar li yul du tsar ma'i gtsug lag khang chen po brtsig par bgyid pa las li rje bi dza ya saM b+ha ba'i blon po dang / 'bangs 'khor dang bcas pa kun gyis kyang
<p>177a.2</p>tsar mar gtsug lag khang re re brtsig par gsol nas brtsigs pa mang po zhig byung ba las rgyal pos bsams pa/ gtsug lag khang brtsig tu ma stsal na ni bdag la dngos sdig tu 'gyur/ /de snyed cig brtsigs na ni slad kyis zhig ral du gyur na yang mi slongs su glo ba chung nas
<p>177a.3</p>dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa bai ro tsa na la zhus pa na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung shA ri ram su la bzhugs pa rnams kyi gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten rtsig shig ces bsgo na/ sdig tu mi 'gyur ro zhes byung nas/ rgyal pos kyang blon po dang 'bangs rnams la de
<p>177a.4</p>bzhin du bsgo nas tsar mi'i gtsug lag khang chen po rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha bas brtsig pa'i tshe/ rgyal po'i 'khor dang blon po dang 'bangs rnams kyi rtsar ma'i gtsug lag khang chung ngu dang / mchod rten brtsigs so 'tshal gyi nang na shA ri ram ma stsal ba cig kyang ma mchis te/ gtsug lag
<p>177a.5</p>khang brtsigs pa lags nas/'phags pa bai ro tsa nas rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba la rgyal pos gaN+Di brdungs la 'phags pa rnams spyan drongs shig ces bgyis pa dang / rgyal po'i mchid nas de bzhin gshegs pa mngon sum du 'dir gshegs te bdag gi lag tu gaN+DI ma stsal gyi bar du bdag
<p>177a.6</p>gaN+DI mi brdung ngo zhes smon lam btab pa dang / de ma thag tu 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa dge slong bai ro tsa nas nam mkha' la de bzhin gshegs par sprul te/ nyan thos chen po bcu drug dang thabs cig tu tsar mar de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul bstan nas rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba'i lag tu gaN+DI stsal
<p>177a.7</p>nas/ rgyal pos gaN+DI brdungs pa dang dgung bdun gyi bar du gaN+DI de'i sgra ma chad par byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa mngon sum du gshegs pa'i dan rtags su gor ma la zhabs kyis bcags pa'i rjes da dung gi bar du tsar ma na mchis/ 'phags pa nyan thos chen po bcu drug la mchod pa
<p>177b</p>
<p>177b.1</p>rin po che sna tshogs las bgyis pa'i bshos cha bcu drug rgyal pos phul ba yang tsar ma'i gtsug khang gi nang du 'phags pa rnams kyis gter du stsal te/ phyir dus dmas shing dge 'dun la yon bdag ma mchis te 'tsho ba mi 'byor ba'i dus na rin po che'i bshos cha de rnams de'i tshe sa'i 'og nas 'byung
<p>177b.2</p>zhes 'phags pa dge 'dun 'phel gyis lung bstan pa dag las kyang 'byung / dge slong 'phags pa bai ro tsa na'i mchod pa'i rkyen du klu'i rgyal po hu lor zhes bgyi bas kha che'i yul nas de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sku gdung bzhugs pa'i mchod rten cig spyan drangs nas nam mkha' las gshegs pa da
<p>177b.3</p>ltar tsar ma na bzhugs te/ mchod rten 'di dri gtsang khang gi nang na bzhugs te/ grib ma slad rol du gsal bar 'byung / rgyal po bi dza ya sing ha zhes bgyi ba tsar ma'i gtsug lag khang du mchod pa bgyid du mchis pa las sku gzugs lder so bgyis pa cig 'chag cig gshegs par mthong nas mtshams med pa
<p>177b.4</p>lnga byang ngo zhes mchi ba yang da ltar bzhugs/ gtsug lag khang de'i srung mar zhal gyis bzhes pa yang / lha nam mkha'i spyan dang nor bu bzang po zhes bgyi ba lags te/ deng song gi bar du mngon rtags dang / mtshan ma dag kyang 'byung / 'phags pa'i lung bstan dag kyang sbyar na yang thog
<p>177b.5</p>ma gtsug lag khang 'di rnams brtsigs pa yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang / yon bdag 'phags pa sha stag gis mdzad la gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten bzhugs so 'tshal gyi nang na yang de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku gdung dang byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos dang / 
<p>177b.6</p>rang sangs rgyas kyi sku gdung bzhugs pas gnyan cing byin che rab ste/ thog ma li yul du gtsug lag khang byung ba yang 'di las snga ba ma mchis so/ /de nas tsar mar 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa dge slong 'phags pa bai ro tsa nas chos phyung rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha bas gtsug lag khang brtsigs tshun chad rgyal po li rje rabs
<p>177b.7</p>bdun gyi bar du gtsug lag khang gzhan ma brtsigs/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgya gar yul nas 'phags pa dgra bcom pa bud+d+ha du ta dang / kha gang ta dang / khag ro yang dang / khag drod dang bzhi byung ste/ gau to shan gyi Ar+ya sta nar bzhugs so/ /de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' byams pa yang li rje bi dza
<p>178a</p>
<p>178a.1</p>ya bIr+ya bya bar gyur te/ rgyal po de srog mkhar gyi steng nas bltas na mkhar gyi phyi rol na gser dang / dngul lta bur snang ba zhig mthong nas bsnyags pa dang / da ltar 'gum tir gyi mchod rten chen po bzhugs pa slebs nas bltas na/ sha ba ni gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po yang dag
<p>178a.2</p>shes su gyur te rgyal po la smras pa/ kye rgyal po khyod sangs rgyas kyis lung bstan pa bzhin 'dir gtsug lag khang gcig brtsigs pa rigs so zhes bgyis pa dang / su'i phyir brtsigs zhes rgyal pos zhus pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi pho nya zhes bgyi ba 'phags pa dgra bcom pa bud+d+ha ta la sogs pa bzhi khyed kyi
<p>178a.3</p>dge ba'i bshes gnyen du 'ongs pa 'di dag gi phyir brtsig ces bsgo ba dang / 'phags pa dgra bcom pa de dag kyang rgyal po bi dza ya bIR+Ya'i drung du byon nas chos bshad pas rgyal po yang tshe snga ma'i smon lam dran nas de ma thag tu dogs brtag pa'i phur bu der btab ste/ gtsug lag khang 'gum tir brtsigs
<p>178a.4</p>so/ /de nas rgyal po bi dza ya bIr+ya 'gum tir gyi gtsug lag khang du mchod pa bgyid du mchis pa'i tshe bu chung ngu zhig stor nas rjes bcang pa de btsal na/ gau to shan gyi lung bu'i nang nas sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi sku gdung bzhugs pa'i mchod rten gyi drung nas bu rnyed de/ de nas rgyal pos mchod rten 'di gang gi dus
<p>178a.5</p>na sus brtsigs zhes smras pa dang /dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa de dag gi zhal nas mchod rten 'di sangs rgyas 'od srungs mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshe brtsigs te sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi sku gdung bzhugs so/ /li yul sngon mtshor gyur pa'i dus na mchod rten 'di ris g.yogs te chus ma zhig la/ 
<p>178a.6</p>phyis kyang yul 'di mtshor 'gyur te/ yang mchod rten 'di ris g.yogs nas chus mi 'jig ste/ sangs rgyas byams pa byung ba'i tshe yang mtsho bskams nas yul du gyur pa'i dus na mchod rten 'di 'byung ste/ gnas 'di ni dus gsum du gshegs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing
<p>178a.7</p>khud pa'i nang na yang gau to shan 'di pho brang sa gcig yin te dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas rnams kyang kun 'dir gshegs shing lung ston/ sems can gyi don mdzod do/ /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing so so nas byang chub sems dpa' stong phrag nyi shu yang dus gsum du glang mgo ri 'di la mchod pa mdzad du byon
<p>178b</p>
<p>178b.1</p>nas slar gshegs so zhes bstan/ de nas rgyal po bi dza ya bIr+ya dad pa'i shugs chen pos glang mgo ri'i steng du gau to shan gyi gtsug lag khang brtsigs nas bu chung ngu de yang thar par btang ste phyis dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob nas/ li yul du dgra bcom par gyur pa 'di las snga ba ma byung bas 'di ni lam
<p>178b.2</p>ston pa'o zhes mo rgu bde shi bya bar btags te/ thog ma mo rgu bde shi'i ming ni de nas byung ste deng sang gi bar du yang thub ldan dang / dka' thub kyi mchog las btus te/ mo rgu bde shir bsgo ba lags/ gau to shan dang / 'gum tir gyi gtsug lag khang 'di gnyis bzhugs pa'i dog sa yang dus gsum gyi
<p>178b.3</p>de bzhin gshegs pa rim gyis 'byung ngo 'tshal gyi zhabs kyis bcags/ byin gyis brlabs pa'i steng du 'phags pa'i lung bstan dag dang sbyar nas yang / thog mar gtsug lag khang 'di rnams brtsigs pa yang dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang / yon bdag 'phags pa sha stag gis
<p>178b.4</p>mdzad la/ gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten bzhugs so 'tshal gyi nang na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi sku gdung bzhugs pas gnyan zhing byin che rab ste/ gtsug lag khang gi srung mar zhal gyis bzhes pa yang
<p>178b.5</p>rnam thos kyi sras dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes dang / klu'i rgyal po gnas dros po lags te deng song gi bar du yang mngon rtags dang mtshan ma dag kyang 'byung ba'i phyir/ li yul gyi gtsug lag khang bzhugs so 'tshal gyi nang na gtso bor bgyi ba lags/ rgyal po bi
<p>178b.6</p>dza ya bIr+yas 'gum tir gyi gtsug lag khang brtsigs tshun chad rgyal po rabs gnyis kyi bar du gtsug lag khang gzhan ma brtsigs/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya dza ya zhes bgyi bas rgya rje'i bu mo pu nye shwa ra zhes bgyi ba mchis 'brang du blangs nas rgya rje'i bu mo des li yul du srin bu'i
<p>178b.7</p>sa bon zhig 'tshal te mchis nas yul ma sha bgyi bar srin bu gsos pa dang / srin bu mtshar ba'i skabs su blon po rgyus ma 'tshal ba kha cig gis rgyal po bi dza ya dza ya rgya rje'i bu mo rgyal po'i btsun mo bgyid pa des sbrul gdug pa mang po ma zhar gso zhing mchis te chen por gyur
<p>179a</p>
<p>179a.1</p>pa dang / yul phyogs su gnod par glo ba chung na ji ltar bgyi zhes blon po dag gis zhus pa dang / sbrul gso ba'i khang par mes thong la kun sregs shig ces bsgo ba dang / rgyal mos de thos nas 'phral du ni rgyal po la rgyus kyis bshad pa'i rngo ma thogs nas/ srin
<p>179a.2</p>bu shas shig bskus te gsang thabs su gsos te/ slad kyis kha cher dar dang srin bal phyung nas dar dang men dri btags te/ rgyal po la bstan nas rgyus kyis zhib tu bshad pa dang /rgyal po yang 'gyod pa skyes te/ rgya gar yul nas dge slong 'phags pa sang g+ha g+ho Sha zhes
<p>179a.3</p>bgyi ba li yul du byon nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen du spyan drangs te/srin bu phal cher bkum pa'i dngos sdig bshags sbyang bgyis nas po tar+ya dang /ma zhi'i mchod rten dang / gtsug lag khang chen po brtsigs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung sha ri ram mang po tsam
<p>179a.4</p>zhig stsal te/ de'i slad du dpyid zla ra ba'i ngo thog thag bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i sku'i gzugs brnyan ma zho po tar+ya zhes bgyi ba'i gtsug lag khang na bzhugs so zhes 'phags pa dag gis lung bstan pas deng sang gi bar du yang / li yul gyi dge 'dun sde gnyis dang / 
<p>179a.5</p>rgyal po dang / blon po man chad 'bangs yan chad lo re zhing dpyid zla ra ba'i ngo la mchod par bgyid cing / ril gyis po tar+ya'i gtsug lag khang du mchis te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyen zhing byin che rab ste/ lha rat+na ba la dang / rat+na shU ra gnyis srung mar zhal gyis
<p>179a.6</p>bzhes pa lags te/ deng song gi bar du yang dngos rtags dang mtshan ma dag kyang 'byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po bi dza ya dza ya zhes bgyi ba la bu spun gsum mchis te/ phu bo rab 'dod 'dros zhes bgyi ba ni rgyal srid ma 'tshal te/ bsod nams bgyid cing rgya gar yul du mchis/ 
<p>179a.7</p>de'i nu bo bar ma yang rgyal srid ma 'tshal nas ban+der zhugs te ming d+harmA nan+da zhes btags nas rgya gar yul du chos slob tu mchis/ nu bo tha chungs rgyal sar zhugs te ming bi dza ya d+harmar btags rgyal po bi dza ya d+harma de dpa' zhing rtsal che bas gsod rkyen dag la dga' nas/ phu bo ban+de
<p>179b</p>
<p>179b.1</p>d+harmA nan+da rgya gar yul nas mchis pa chos mnyan zhing bslab nas bsgoms pas 'phags pa dgra bcom par gyur te/ 'phags pa d+harmA nan+das rgya gar yul nas bltas na/ nu bo rgyal po bi dza ya d+harma gsod rkyen bgyid cing sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos la zhen par mthong nas glo ba
<p>179b.2</p>brjes te/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyi ba'i slad du rgya gar yul nas li yul du mchis te/ nyon bgyir gyi ri rtsa shel chab 'og ma dang / nye ba zhig tu spyil po bgyis te de na bsgom bzhugs pa las nyin gcig cig /'phags pa de sha ba gser gyi kha dog 'dra ba zhig tu sprul
<p>179b.3</p>te/ 'u then gyi sku mkhar gyi slad rol shar phyogs logs na 'gus no zhes bgyi ba'i sgang bu zhig mchis pa'i khar byung ba dang / rgyal po bi dza ya d+harmas srog mkhar gyi steng nas mthong nas mda' gcig 'phangs pa dang / sha ba'i brlar phog nas sha ba ni bros/ rgyal po ni slad
<p>179b.4</p>bzhin du bsnyegs pa dang / sha ba de 'phags pa d+harmA nan+da'i spyi la bu'i nang du mchis/ rgyal po slad bzhin du mchis pas bltas na spyil po'i nang na sha ba ni cang ma mchis/ dge slong gcig brla la mdas phog pa 'byin cing mchis pa mthong nas/ phu bo lags par ni ngo ma 'tshal te/ 
<p>179b.5</p>phu bo dge slong d+harmA nan+das byin gyis brlabs nas phu bo lags par gdong ngo 'tshal te/ rgyal pos btsun pa ci nongs zhes bgyis pa dang /khyod kyis bdag la mda' 'phangs te ci bya zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal pos kyang sha ba ma lags par tshor nas bdag gis nongs na khri lan zhes
<p>179b.6</p>bgyis pa dang / dge slong de'i mchid nas gcig tu na nga khyod kyi phu bo yin/gnyis su na nga 'phags pa dgra bcom par gyur pas/ rgyal po khyod kyi mtshar gyi sdig pa thob ste/ mtshams med pa dang 'dra ba'i las byas par gyur te/ bshags sbyangs dang / bsod nams cher
<p>179b.7</p>ma byas na mi rung ngo zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal po de yang 'gyod pa skyes te rab tu ma dga' nas/ 'phags pa dgra bcom pa de'i zhabs la 'jus te/ bzod gsol bshags sbyangs bgyis nas bdag gi sdig pa 'di ji ltar 'byang zhes zhus pa dang / 'phags pa d+harmA nan+da'i
<p>180a</p>
<p>180a.1</p>zhal nas da 'phral du gzhan byar med kyi yul 'bro tir zhes bya ba'i ljongs pha bi na sngon sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ rgyal po zla 'od ces bgyi ba'i dus na bram zes mgo blangs te/ rgyal po nyid
<p>180a.2</p>kyis mgo bcad nas/ bram ze la stsal ba'i phrin yig las dka' ba rnam pa gcig mdzad pa'i sa 'di yin/ gnyis su na bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa rgyal po'i khab bya rgod phung po nas li yul byin gyis rlob cing / gau to shan du gshegs pa'i tshe byang chub sems
<p>180a.3</p>dpa'i 'khor mang pos bskor nas byang chub sems dpa' sa'i snying po dang / ri k+Sha ta a sho ka zhes bya ba 'di byin gyis brlabs te 'di na bzhugs bzhugs/ deng sang gi bar du yang gzugs brnyan 'di bzhugs/ rnam pa gsum du na 'bod b+ha long zhes bya ba'i tshal chung ngu pha ba'i na
<p>180a.4</p>yang bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs kyis bcags nas phyis 'phags pa 'byung ba rnams kyi sgom sar byin gyis brlabs te/ gnas 'di rnams srung bar lha dzi na ri sha ba dang / lha mo a sho ka dang / klu'i rgyal po ta k+Sha ka dang gsum gyis dam tshig blangs te/ deng sang gi bar du
<p>180a.5</p>yang gnas 'di srung zhing rgyal pos 'dir gtsug lag khang gcig brtsigs na snga phyi'i sdig pa mi dge ba'i las ci bgyis pa 'byong ngo zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal po bi dza yad+ha rma dad pa skyes nas slan chad gsod rkyen mi bgyid par dam bcas/ rgyal po zla 'od kyis bram ze la mgo
<p>180a.6</p>sbyin gtong du bgyis pa'i sar de ma thag tu dog sa brtags pa'i phur bu btab nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa d+harmA nan+da'i slad du 'bro tir gyi mchod rten dang / gtsug lag khang chen po brtsigs/ sku mkhar gyi nang du yang lho sgo'i sge'u chung mchis pa'i nang logs na
<p>180a.7</p>klu'i rgyal po chen po ba ru Na'i gnas kyi steng na pa ri tha zhes bgyi ba'i mchod rten gnyen po bzhugs pa'i drung na nang gi gtsug lag khang zhig dang / mchod rten chen po zhig brtsigs te/ mchod rten gyi nang du de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi sku gdung stsal/ sangs rgyas rin chen
<p>180b</p>
<p>180b.1</p>mang gi thog ma'i sku gdung ma zhig pa nyid spyan drangs te/ da ltar gtsug lag khang 'di'i nang na bzhugs/ 'bro tir gyi gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che ba ste/ deng sang gi bar du yang mngon rtags dang mtshan ma 'byung ngo / /li yul du thog ma ma hA sa ma g+hi ka'i sde yang dge slong
<p>180b.2</p>'phags pa d+harmA nan+da byung nas/ 'u then na 'bro tir gtogs par gtsug lag khang brgyad dang / kam sheng gtsug lag khang kha brgyad kyi dge 'dun yang ma hA saM g+hi ka'i sder gtogs/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya dza ya'i bu chen po rgyal bu 'don 'dros kyis sang tir gyi gtsug lag
<p>180b.3</p>khang brtsig par dog sa 'jal te brtsams pa las yo byad rgyu rkyen gyis ma 'tshal nas rgyal bu 'don 'dros kyis bsams pa/ gzhan nas ma phrogs pa/ma rkus pa/ dkon mchog gsum gyi dkor la ma 'bags par nor gtsang ma bdag nyid kyis rkang gis btsugs te/ btsal
<p>180b.4</p>la gtsug lag khang brtsig go snyam na thog ma rgya gar yul du mchis te/ mkhan po 'phags pa sa man+ta sid+d+hi mkhan por spyan drangs/ stod phyogs thog thog tu yang mchis nas nor gtsang ma btsal/ de nas slar log nas rgya yul du mchis pa dang rgya rje'i blon po gcig gyos
<p>180b.5</p>la chags te/ dgum par bgyis pa las/ 'don 'dros kyis rgya rje la blon po 'di'i skyin par bdag dgum par ci gnang gsol ba las rgya rjes kyang gnang ste/ gshed mas rgyal bu la ral gri btab pa na bcad 'phro nas 'o ma byung ste/ ma gum nas rgya rje la sogs pa
<p>180b.6</p>ngo mtshar rmad du gyur te mchod pa bgyis/ yon yang mang po tsam zhig phul/ blon po des kyang srog rin gyi yon phal cher phul ba blangs nas/ slar li yul gyi 'dab nye ba zhig tu 'khor mang po dang lhan cig tu mchis pa dang / rgyal po 'don 'dros kyis nu bo rgyal po bi dza ya
<p>180b.7</p>d+ha rma rgyal srid 'dzin zhing mchis pa las/ blon po kha cig gi mchid nas rgyal bu'i gcen rgyal bu 'don 'dros rgya rjes li yul gyi rgyal por bskos te/ rgyal po'i rgyal srid 'phrog tu 'ongs so zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal po bi dza ya d+harma yang phu bo 'don 'dros la mi dga' nas sku mkhar
<p>181a</p>
<p>181a.1</p>gyi nang du yang ma btang / phrad du yang ma btub nas/ sang tir gyi gtsug lag khang brtsigs pa'i sa gzhir mchis shig ces bsgo nas/ phu bo rgyal bu 'don 'dros kyang sang tir du mchis te/ nu bos kyang chu dang rtswa shing la yang dbang ma bskur te/ kho bdag gi rin gyis 'jal te/ yo
<p>181a.2</p>byad sbyor zhing mchis pa las/ thog ma rgya gar yul du mkhan po 'phags pa sa man+ta sid+d+hi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi phyogs la bltas nas phyag 'tshal te mchod pa bgyis nas smon lam btab/ spyan drangs pa dang / mkhan po yang rgya gar yul nas nam mkha' la lding ste/ li
<p>181a.3</p>yul du rgyal po 'don 'dros kyi drung du gshegs nas gtsug lag khang ji ltar brtsigs pa'i bshes gnyen yang bgyis/ rgyal po spun gnyis kyi bar du ma 'jal ba'i sdum bgyi ba'i slad du sum cu rtsa gsum gnam du gshegs nas bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas byang chub sems
<p>181a.4</p>dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe lus kyi yan lag dang / bu smad la sogs pa'i sbyin gtong bgyis shing phrin las dka' ba ji ltar mdzad pa bzhin du no le zhes bgyi ba dang / zlos chos li yul du mi bgyir mi rung zhes lha rnams la gsol nas sum cu rtsa gsum gnam gyi lha dang / 
<p>181a.5</p>rgyal chen ris bzhi'i lha rnams li yul sad tir bgyi bar gshegs te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sngon phrin las dka' ba ji ltar mdzad pa bzhin du lha rnams zlos chos bgyis pa'i tshe rgyal po bi dza ya d+harmas blon po dang / 'bangs rnams la gcig kyang der mchir mi rung ngo zhes bgyis pa
<p>181a.6</p>las/ lha'i rol mo bzang po snga na ma byung ba de thos nas mi gcig gis gcig sbran te ma bzod nas der mchis/slad kyis rgyal po'i 'khor kun gar mchis/ rgyal pos smras pa dang / blon po dag gis rgyus kyis zhib tu bshad pa dang / rgyal po bi dza ya d+ha rma yang ma bzod de/ sang tir gyi gtsug
<p>181a.7</p>lag khang gi 'dabs su mchis pa dang / phu bo rgyal po 'don 'dros kyis bsu nas spun der mjal ba dang / nu bo rgyal po bi dza ya d+harmas phu bo la phyag bgyis nas/ pus mo sa la btsugs thal mo sbyar te/ 'phags pa bdag gis khyod kyi mthu stobs ma rig nas nga rgyal gyi dbang du gyur nas bdag
<p>181b</p>
<p>181b.1</p>gis rab tu nongs pa bzod par gsol zhing mchis na/ bdag la dngos sdig tu mi 'gyur bar bzod pa bzhes par ci gnang zhes bgyid pa dang / phu bos kyang bzod pa blangs pa dang / des slar nu bo la bzod pa gsol nas lag sbrel te gtsug lag khang du mchis nas mchod pa bgyis/ lha klus no le
<p>181b.2</p>bgyis pa dang / gtsug lag khang rtsig pa la rjes su yi rang nas yon phul/ gtsug lag khang rtsig pa'i dang rogs bgyis te rkyen ris bkum ste phul/ thog ma spun ma mjal te/ bzod pa gsol ba'i sar mjal mo ka ka rong zhes bgyi ba'i gtsug lag khang zhig brtsigs nas thog ma li
<p>181b.3</p>yul du sarba ti bAng [(]kyi [,]gi [)]sde theg pa chung ngu pa yang mkhan po 'phags pa sa man+ta sid+d+hi las byung /gtsug lag khang gi srung ma yang lha ka bi la zhes bgyi bas zhal gyis bzhes gsungs/ deng sang gi bar du lo gcig cing yang rtag tu ston zla ra ba tshes bdun dang brgyad kyi gdugs la/ de bzhin gshegs
<p>181b.4</p>pas phrin las dka' ba mdzad pa'i zlos chos no le bgyid de/ yul mi ril gyis chos nyan cing der mchis te/gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyen zhing byin che bar bgyid do/ /de'i 'og tu rgyal po ba dzi ya d+harma'i bu rgyal po bi dza ya sing has rgyal po bgyid pa'i tshe ga 'jag gi rgyal pos li yul du dmag
<p>181b.5</p>mang po drangs te/ rgyal po ba dzi ya sing ha dang 'thabs pa las ga 'jag gi dmag pham ste/ ga 'jag gi rgyal po yang li rjes zhags pas zin nas 'gum par bgyid pa las thar par gsol nas rgyal po ba dzi ya sing ha'i mchid nas/ rgyal po khyod bdag gis mi dgum par thar par btang
<p>181b.6</p>gis/ nam khyod dgra choms pa'i dus ni bdag gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mdzad cing slar byon cig ces bgyis nas/ thar par stsal te ming yang A nan+da se nar btags te slar shu lig tu btang / de nas dge slong A nan+da se na slad kyis dgra bcom nas thog ma li rje dang dam bcas pa bzhin nam mkha'
<p>181b.7</p>la lding ste/ li yul gshegs nas/ rgyal po bi dza ya sing ha'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyi ba'i slang du snying rje yang dad pa skyes nas 'phags pa dgra bcom pa A nan+da se na'i slad du sam nya'i gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten brtsigs te/ gtsug lag khang gi srung ma ni rnam thos kyi sras dang / lha ka pi la
<p>182a</p>
<p>182a.1</p>bzhugs te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyid do/ /de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal bo bi dza ya kIrtis 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa kam sheng du chos spel ba'i dgra bcom pa spyi bri zhes bgyi bas dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyis nas dad pa skyes pa'i slad du
<p>182a.2</p>sru nyo'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ thog ma ka ni ka'i rgyal po dang / gu zan gyi rgyal po dang / li rje rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti la sogs pas rgya gar yul du dmag drangs nas so ked ces bgyi ba'i grong khyer phab pa'i tshe/ rgyal po bi dza ya kIrtis shar rim mang po zhig rnyed pa yang sru nyo'i mchod
<p>182a.3</p>rten de'i nang du stsal/ thog ma dog sa rtog pa'i phur bu 'debs pa'i tshe/ rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti la dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa spyi pri'i zhal nas phur bu 'di la rgyal pos lag pa mas yar lan lngar bya bas na mngon rtags 'byung ngo zhes bgyid pa dang / rgyal pos kyang dogs
<p>182a.4</p>brtag pa'i shug pa'i phur bu la lhag pas lan lngar byabs pa dang / phur bu de la shug pa'i yal kha khru gang pa lnga de ma thag tu de'i nyin par skyes nas slad kyis shug pa de'i drung du ban+de dag gis d+harma bklags pa dang shug pa de las chos bshad pa'i sgra dag byung nas slad kyis ban+de gzhon nu dag d+harma
<p>182a.5</p>thogs te chos nyan pa mchis na yang / de bzhin du chos 'chad pa'i sgra dag byung ba las slad kyis ban+de gcig gis d+harma log par bklags nas de ltar ma yin no zhes lhas bsgo ba dang / mnyan nas de tshun chad chos bshad pa'i sgra yang ma byung slad kyis gtsug lag khang 'di'i chab ka chab kyis
<p>182a.6</p>'tshal te chab ma byin nas gtsug lag khang zhig tu nye ba las/ dge slong btsun pa sum po na zhes bgyi ba dgra bcom du nye ba zhig gis gtsug lag khang de mi zhig par bgyi ba'i slad du dgra bcom par 'grub pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba des klur skye bar smon lam btab nas de ma thag tu lus las chad
<p>182a.7</p>byung nas mi'i lus la 'phos par shel chu chung ngu'i klur gyur na dog sa'i 'og tu nub nas deng sang gi bar du gtsug lag khang de'i chab shel chu chung ngu las drangs te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang deng sang gi bar du ma zhig ste/gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyid/ srung ma yang lha su dza
<p>182b</p>
<p>182b.1</p>ya dang / phyag brnyan sing ha mu kha dang / shel chab chung ngu'i klu sum pon gyis srung ngo // //de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti'i bu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma zhes bgyi ba dpa' zhing rtsal che ba zhig byung nas/ phyi dgra mang po zhig la bsdos nas sems
<p>182b.2</p>can phal cher bkum/ de'i 'og tu seng ge mi la rgol ba zhig byung ste/ dmag gis btab na yang 'khums te rgyal po gcig pus seng ge de la brgal te zin nas bkum/ de nas rgyal po de'i ming yang seng ger btags/ rgyal po de yang ri dgas shor du mchis pa las shel
<p>182b.3</p>chab chung ngu'i 'gram du tshal zhig tu dgongs btab pas/ de'i nub mo tshal de'i nang nas zhugs mar 'dra ba zhig rgyang nas gda' nas slad de nang bar bltas na/ dge slong 'phags pa dgra bcom pa dz+nyA na ya sho de na bzhugs pa las 'od byung bar mthong nas/ dad pa skyes te mchod pa bgyis nas
<p>182b.4</p>'phags pa 'di na ci mdzad ces zhus pa dang / dgra bcom pa dz+nyA na ya sho'i zhal nas sa 'di yang sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs pa lags te/ rgyal pos 'dir gtsug lag khang cig brtsig par rigs so zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal pos kyang 'phags pa de la dad pa
<p>182b.5</p>skye ba'i slad du bsgo ba bzhin du mnyan nas sdig pa bshags/ gtsug lag khang gi dogs brtag pa'i phur bu btab nas/ gser gyi gzhong pa cig spyi bo la bzung ste/ da bdag gis brtsigs pa gtsug lag khang 'di yun du tshugs shing brtan par 'gyur na phyogs bcu na bzhugs pa'i
<p>182b.6</p>'phags pa rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs shing de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung bdag gi gzhong pa 'di'i nang du stsal bar ci gnang zhes smon lam btab pa dang / nam mkha' las sha ri ram mang po tsam zhig gzhong pa'i nang du gshegs nas rgyal po sngar bas lhag par dad pa skyes te/ dge ba'i bshes
