<p>182b.7</p>gnyen ya sho'i slad du d+harma kIrtis gtsug lag khang mchod rten chen po brtsigs te/ nang du sha ri ram mang po tsam po zhig stsal bas gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che bas srung ma rnam thos kyi sras dang / lha ka pi las srung // //de nas rgyal po ba dzi ya d+harmas rgyal srid bzung
<p>183a</p>
<p>183a.1</p>ba man chad/ bi dza ya kIrtis rgyal po bgyis pa yan chad/ rgyal po rabs bcu bzhi'i bar du res 'ga' ni/ yul du phyi dgra gzhan gyis dmag drangs te gtses/ res 'ga' ni li rje dag gis yul gzhan du dmag drangs nas 'bangs kyi tshigs
<p>183a.2</p>gyur/ de'i 'og tu dru gu a no shod kyis li yul du dmag drangs nas/ gau to shan man chad kyi gtsug lag khang phal cher mes bsregs te yul dmas/ 'bangs 'gribs nas gtsug lag khang gsar pa rtsig pa'i rngo ma thogs/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti'i bu
<p>183a.3</p>rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma zhes bgyi ba dgung lo bdun lon pa zhig /rgyal por zhugs nas slad kyis mi thur son pa dang /yul 'di sus bshig /ci'i slad du dmas zhes/ dge 'dun rgan rabs dang /blon po dag la smras pa las/ dge 'dun dang / blon po rnams kyang dru gu
<p>183a.4</p>a mo no shod la sogs pas sngon yul ji ltar bshig pa'i lo rgyus zhib tu bshad pa dang / rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra mas blon po dag la dmag tshogs ci mchis pa sdus shig ces bsgo nas sngon gtses shing / yul bshig pa'i rgyal po rnams kyi yul du dmag drangs te/ lan glan
<p>183a.5</p>nas yul bshig /sems can phal cher bkum/ de nas slar log nas shel chab 'og ma'i 'gram du mchis pa dang /dge slong bdun zhig chab kyi nang du khrus bgyid cing rtsed mo sna tshogs bgyid pa mthong nas/ dge slong gis tshul ma yin par byed ces byas pa dang / dge slong de bdun
<p>183a.6</p>yang de ma thag tu nam mkha' la lding nas rgyal po de la rdzu 'phrul rnam pa bcu drug bstan pa dang / rgyal po de'i yid la bdag gis sngar yang sems can mang po zhig srog bcad de bkum/ da yang 'phags pa de rnams la ngan sems bskyed pa rab tu nyes so snyam pa'i 'gyod pa cher
<p>183a.7</p>skyes/ 'phags pa de dag gis rdzu 'phrul rnam pa sna tshogs bstan pa mthong nas dad pa yang cher skyes te/ 'phags pa de dag ga la bzhugs pa'i drung du bsnyen nas mchod pa dang / bshags sbyangs bgyis/ bzod par gsol nas 'phags pa dgra bcom pa po nyan re ta la
<p>183b</p>
<p>183b.1</p>sogs pa 'phags pa bdun gyi phyir 'gu zhan gyi gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ 'phags pa dgra bcom pa bdun gyis kyang dog sa de byin gyis brlabs nas/ zhi ba'i sa dgu zhan ta zhes bgyi bar gtsug lag khang gi mtshan ma yang brtags te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang
<p>183b.2</p>gnyan zhing byin che rab ste/ lha dzi na ri sha ba dang / nor bu bzang po gnyis kyis srung ngo // //de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma'i bu/ rgyal po bi dza ya sing ha zhes bgyi bas rgyal por zhugs nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa dgra bcom pa
<p>183b.3</p>d+harma pa la la 'phags pa khyod la rdzu 'phrul ci mnga' ba bdag la bstan par ci gnang zhes gsol pa las/ 'phags pa de'i rdzu 'phrul gyis rgyal po bi dza ya sing ha dga' ldan du khrid de/ 'phags pa byams pa bzhugs pa'i gnas dang / zhal bstan nas slar mchis pa dang / rgyal
<p>183b.4</p>po bi dza ya sing has bzha' ser ma'i gtsug lag khang rtsigs te/ dga' ldan na byams pa 'khor dang bcas pa ji ltar bzhugs pa'i sku gzugs bgyis/ slad kyis byams pa la mchod pa'i slad du mgon po dang / lha klu gshegs pa rnams kyis tshul ci 'dra ba mgon po'i rten
<p>183b.5</p>khang zhig brtsigs nas mgon po dang / lha klu'i gzugs bgyis pa da dung yang bzhugs te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyi/ lha gangs can dang / 'brog gnas zhes bgyi bas srung / deng sang gi bar du mngon rtags dang mtshan ma dag kyang 'byung
<p>183b.6</p>ngo // //de nas de'i 'og tu yang rgyal po bi dza ya ba la man chad/ rgyal rabs drug gi bar du gtsug lag khang gzhan ma brtsigs so/ /de nas de'i 'og tu yang rgyal po bi dza ya ba la zhes bya ba'i bu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma zhes bgyi ba rgyal por bgyid pa'i tshe/ 
<p>183b.7</p>cu gu pan nas tshe'u pa na'i sku gzugs nam mkha' las lding ste/ li yul du gshegs pa rgyal pos mthong nas dad pa'i shugs kyis sangs rgyas bzhugs pa'i dri gtsang khang brtsigs/ de nas slad kyis rgyal po de'u then gyi sku mkhar gyi steng gi /byang sgo'i sgo
<p>184a</p>
<p>184a.1</p>khang na mchis pa zhig gi tshe na bltas na sku mkhar gyi slad rol na dge slong cig khyim pa skye bo la phyag 'tshal te bka' mchid mchi ba mthong nas ngo mtshar du mthong ste/ rgyal po des blon po zhig mngags nas zhib tu rtog tu btang ba las/ blon po des dge
<p>184a.2</p>slong dang / skye bo la so sor rmas nas dge slong gi mchid nas khyim pa skye bo 'di ni 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sprul pa lags zhes mchi/ khyim pa skye ba de'i mchid nas dge slong 'di 'phags pa sa'i snying po'i sprul pa lags zhes mchi ba dang / blon po des kyang rgyal po la de bzhin du
<p>184a.3</p>slar gsol ba dang / rgyal po bi dza ya sang gram yang de ma thag tu 'phags pa de dag gi drung du bsnyen nas phyag 'tshal mchod pa bgyis nas/ 'phags pa dag ga las gshegs zhes zhus pa dang / 'phags pa gnyis kyi zhal nas bdag cag gnyis kyang shar phyogs de bzhin
<p>184a.4</p>gshegs pa mi 'khrugs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sems can gyi don la 'dir 'ongs so zhes 'byung ba dang / de nas rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma'i mchid nas 'phags pa thugs rje dang ldan pa gnyis kyis rdzu 'phrul gyi mthu stobs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'khrugs
<p>184a.5</p>pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing bdag la bstan par ci gnang zhes gsol pa dang / de bzhin du gnang nas de bzhin gshags pa mi 'khrugs pa'i zhal nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang bstan pa dang / rgyal po des de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yang mthong / 
<p>184a.6</p>nam mkha' las shing rta'i steng nas sangs rgyas mang po zhig gshegs nas/ de dag gis 'od zer btang ba rgyal po'i spyi bor rig par mthong ste/ dad pa'i shugs kyis sangs rgyas kyi gzugs ji ltar mthong ba bzhin du gzugs su yang bgyis te/ shing rta'i nang du byang srang
<p>184a.7</p>du yang drangs nas mchod pa chen po bgyis te/deng sang gi bar du yang dpyid zlar ba yar gyi ngo la byang srang du sku gzugs chen po 'dren pa dang / dge 'dun sde gnyis spyan drangs nas byang chub 'byung gnas bkra shis bsil ba'i tshul du mchod rten gsol zhing / mo h+yo ra'i
<p>184b</p>
<p>184b.1</p>mchod pa chen po bgyis pa yang rgyal po des bgyis nas dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa dgra bcom pa mo dgu de shi a ba ya d+hang gi slad du bzha' sang gre re ma'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ rnam thos kyi sras dang / yang dag shes bgyi ba yang srung ngo // //de nas rgyal
<p>184b.2</p>po bi dza ya sha sta man chad rgyal po rabs bzhi'i bar du gtsug lag khang gsar pa gzhan ma brtsigs/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti zhes bgyi ba 'gum tir du mchis pa las/ da ltar b+ha ba nya'i gtsug lag khang bzhugs pa'i sar mchis pa dang / klu'i rgyal po zhig
<p>184b.3</p>der byung nas rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti la smras pa/ sngon sangs rgyas 'od srungs kyi tshe dogs 'di byin gyis brlabs nas gtsug lag khang brtsigs pa'i sa 'di yin te/ de yang rgyal po khyod kyis gtsug lag khang gcig brtsig pa'i rigs so zhes bgyis pa dang / rgyal pos smon lam btab
<p>184b.4</p>pa/ da ltar 'dzam bu'i gling na 'phags pa dag gis byin gyis brlabs te 'dir gshegs par gnang na/ bdag gis gtsug lag khang brtsig par 'tshal lo zhes smon lam btab pa dang / de ma thag tu nam mkha' las 'phags pa dgra bcom pa bcu bdun gshegs nas rgyal po
<p>184b.5</p>bi dza ya kIrti yang dad pa'i shugs chen po skyes te/ rgyal po dang btsun mo lag dar te/ b+ha ba nya'i bsgom sa dang / gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyid/ lha gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang nor bu bzang pos srung ngo / /gtsug lag khang 'di
<p>184b.6</p>yang gna' bod kyi mnga' ris su gtogs pa'i tshe mgar blon btsan nyen gung ston li yul gyi dbang po bgyid pa'i tshe brtsigs pa lags/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma dang bu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma spang rgya yul du mchis nas slar li yul du mchi ba'i bar du dru gu'i
<p>184b.7</p>dmag gis shul khums pa las pha ni rgya yul du gum/ bu chung ste slar mchi ba'i rngo ma thogs pa'i skabs su/ li'i blo na po a ma cha khe meg ces bgyi bas dgung lo bcu gnyis kyi bar du rgyal tshab bgyis nas rgyal srid bzung ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen dge slong 'phags pa ba ru na tsa zhes
<p>185a</p>
<p>185a.1</p>bgyi ba'i slad du ma na 'di'i mchod rten dang / gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung sha ri ram mang du btsal te/ de ltar gtsug lag khang 'di lha nam mkha'i spyan dang gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes zhes bgyi bas srung ngo / /de nas rgyal
<p>185a.2</p>bo bi dza ya sang gra ma'i bu rgyal po bi dza ya bi kra ma zhes pas slar li yul du mchis nas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'phags pa dgra bcom pa de ben+d+ra chen gyi slad du gtsug lag khang byi zha gre rma brtsigs te/ da ltar lha gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / nor bu bzang pos srung
<p>185a.3</p>ngo // //de nas de'i 'og tu rgya'i blon po ser the shi dang rgyal bo bi dza ya d+harma gnyis kyis dge ba'i bshes 'gum tir gyi bar mag 'dzin se na zhes bgyi ba'i slad du bong mkhar gyi byams pa mai tri'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar gtsug lag khang 'di rnam thos
<p>185a.4</p>sras kyis srung ngo / /de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po'i blon po ka the shi dang / rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba zhes bya ba gnyis kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen u de na dra rod ci dang /d+harmA nan+nga gnyis kyi slad du khe gan rtse'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar gtsug lag khang 'di
<p>185a.5</p>rnam thos sras kyis srung ngo / /thog ma dge slong 'phags pa bai ro tsa na tsar ma'i tshal du gshegs pa phyugs rdzi la sogs pa mi 'og ma dag gis mthong nas/rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba la bdag cag gis snga na ma mthong ba'i mi 'di lta bu zhig tsar ma'i tshal du mchis so zhes gsol ba
<p>185a.6</p>dang / rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba yang de ma thag tu tsar mar mchis nas 'phags pa bai ro tsa na mthong ba dang /dad pa skyes nas phyag 'tshal mchod pa bgyis nas/ 'phags pa des kyang rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyis nas legs nyes gnyis kyi 'bras bu bstan
<p>185a.7</p>to/ /chos bshad bshags sbyong bgyid du stsal ba las/ rgyal po de yang chos kyi mig bye nas lhag par yang dad pa skyes nas rgyal po slar sku mkhar du mchis nas thog ma 'phags pa bai ro tsa na gshegs so zhes bka' mchid snyan pa thos pa'i sar mchod rten chen po zhig brtsigs te/ ming
<p>185b</p>
<p>185b.1</p>yang su stong nyar btags/ slad kyis mchod rten de yun rings pas zhig nas/ de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya bo han chen po dang / rgya yul nas mchis pa'i dge slong 'ba' la shi zhes bgyi ba mchis pas tsar ma'i dge 'dun dge ba'i bshes gnyen du spyan drangs nas su stong nya'i gtsug lag khang
<p>185b.2</p>brtsigs te/ da ltar rnam thos kyi sras kyis srung ngo // //dge slong ma'i gtsug lag khang rnams kyi gtan tshigs dang / snga phyi'i go rims la rgyal bo bi dza ya sing ha zhes bgyi ba zhig chung ngu nas rgyal por zhugs te/ chungs pa'i skabs su blon po kha cig gis rngan can bgyis
<p>185b.3</p>te/ rgyal mo dang / mchis 'brang slas dang / nang 'khor ma rnams dag mi rigs pa bgyis nas slad kyis rgyal po de chen por gyur nas/ sngar blon po de dag gis rngan can bgyis shing brnyas pa de dran nas/ khon dran par gyur te/ slad kyis rgyal po des blon po rnams ri dgas shor ba ltar
<p>185b.4</p>thabs kyis brid nas 'u then gyi shel chab gong ma'i yul pa ro gza' zhes bgyi blon po bdun cu rtsa lnga bkum nas/ slad kyis rgyal po der gtsug lag khang zhig kyang brtsigs/ de nas sku mkhar du mchis nas rgyal po mchis pa'i gnas nas rgyal mo dang / slas dang / nang 'khor ma mchis
<p>185b.5</p>pa'i khang pa phyi sgo bkum nas 'grul bcad/ de bzhin du 'gum par bgyis pa las/ rgyal po de'i btsun mo 'khor dang bcas pa phongs te nyam thag nas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i mtshan nas brjod/ mchod pa bgyis te/ lha khang bskor d+harma bklags/ bsod nams
<p>185b.6</p>cher bgyis pa'i mthus rgya gar yul nas 'phags pa dgra bcom pa ma ya sha pradz+nyA dang / s+th+ya shu ta dang / sang han+da la sogs pa nam mkha' la lding ste/ rgyal mo mog sha ko sha dang / sa lu ca la sogs pa 'khor mchis pa'i drung du gshegs nas rgyal mo de dag la chos bshad de
<p>185b.7</p>rab tu byung ba las dad pa'i shugs kyis de ma thag tu rgyal mo de dag gi 'khor las brgya rtsa bcu gnyis dgra bcom par gyur nas nam mkha' la lding ste/ bsod snyoms len du gshegs pa rgyal po bi dza ya sing has mthong nas/ de ma thag tu gnas der mchis te bltas na rgyal mo mog sha ko sha
<p>186a</p>
<p>186a.1</p>dang / sa lu ca la sogs pa'i 'khor ril rab tu byung ste/ phal cher dgra bcom par gyur te/ rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs bstan pa mthong nas rgyal po yang rab tu dga' nas dad pa'i shugs kyis gnas de nyid du gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ bran zhing dang / nor phyugs la sogs pa mchod pa'i
<p>186a.2</p>yo byad mang po tsam zhig phul nas gtsug lag khang de'i ming yang nu'o nya zhes btags te/ gtsug lag khang 'di yang gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyid/ da ltar lha phur pa'i lag pa zhes bgyi bas srung // //de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po 'don 'dros kyi btsun mo rgya rje'i sras mo sho rgya zhes
<p>186a.3</p>bgyi ba'i bu mo dge slong ma sho'i dza ya zhes bgyi ba dgra bcom nas nu mo yo sha rgya'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen bgyi ba'i slad du rgya yul nas 'u then du mchi ba'i phyir nu mo rgyal mo sho rgyas yo zo 'jo'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar klu'i rgyal po da ci dang / da ra gnyis srung // //de
<p>186a.4</p>nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya sha ta'i nu bo a ma ca ze ro'i mchis 'brang du su ha tsho ha zhes bgyi ba khyim thab gums pa dang / bud med de la rgyal po'i mchid nas bdag dang mi phrad du mi rung ngo zhes bgyis pa dang / bud med de'i mchid nas bdag dgung bdun zhig khyim thab kyi 'dun bgyid
<p>186a.5</p>cing slad rol du mi mchi bar ci gnang zhes gsol pa/ rgyal pos kyang de bzhin du gnang nas de ma thag tu bud med de yang gsang ste rab tu byung nas dgung bdun gyi bar du sems rtse gcig tu sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i ting nge 'dzin bsgoms nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal yang
<p>186a.6</p>mngon sum du mthong nas dgra bcom ste ming yang bud+d+ha nan+dar btags/ de nas dgung bdun lags pa dang /rgyal pos bud med de 'gugs pa zhig btang ba de'i mchid nas mo rab tu byung ste/'phags ma dgra bcom mar gyur nas/ da ltar 'od kyang 'byung zhing mchis so zhes
<p>186a.7</p>bgyis pa dang / rgyal po der mchis nas 'phags ma de la 'od kyang 'byung / rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs bstan pa yang mthong nas dad pa skyes te/ de nas 'phags ma bud+he nan+da'i slad du zer ro/ /'dzo'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te gnyan zhing byin che bar bgyid/ da ltar
<p>186b</p>
<p>186b.1</p>lha dga' ba'i dbang phyug ces bya bas srung // //de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya nan+da skye ba nam gyi rgyal po hu mar bya ba'i mchis 'brang dang / mjal ba'i bu mo gcig cig mchis pa rab tu byung nas dgra bcom par gyur pas bltas na/ bdag ni li rje bi dza ya ma
<p>186b.2</p>ti'i bu mo lags par thugs su chud nas 'phags pa d+harma ba la de dang / dge slong ma 'phags ma nyi shu shu lig nas nam mkha' las lding ste li yul du gshegs nas rgyal po yab la thog ma'i lo rgyus kyang bshad/ rdzu 'phrul rnam pa sna tshogs kyang bstan pas rgyal po yang
<p>186b.3</p>dang pa skyes nas bu mo 'phags ma dgra bcom ma d+harma ba la'i slad du po yen do'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar rnam thos kyi sras dang / klu'i rgyal po hu lor bgyi bas srung / de nas de'i 'og tu rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma seng ge zhes bgyi ba'i ma rgyal mo d+harma zhes bgyi ba rab tu byung nas
<p>186b.4</p>dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob nas spyil po'i nang du bsgom zhing mchis pa las nub mo 'od phyung ste/ rgyal pos mtshan ma gzugs pa'i phyir mda' cig 'phangs/ nang par mda' tshol du btang ba'i sa de na rgyal po'i ma d+harma de bzhugs pa mthong nas rgyal po yang dad pa skyes te/ ma 'phags ma
<p>186b.5</p>dgra bcom ma d+harma zhes bgyi ba'i slad du rgyal pos dro mo mdza' zhes bgyi ba'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar lha ser skyas srung / de nas rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma'i nu bo bre s+ya stu lag ces bgyi ba zhig gis rgyal po gru gu mo zhig rab tu byung nas ming yang a shu ka su ma zhes
<p>186b.6</p>bgyi bar btags te dgra bcom pa'i slad du dad pa skyes nas/ tra ke 'dzo zhes bgyi ba'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/da ltar gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes kyis srung // //de nas gtsug lag khang 'gu zhan brtsigs pa'i rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma'i mchis 'brang rgyal po
<p>186b.7</p>'phrom ge sar gyi bu mo'u rong ga zhes bgyi ba'i bu mo gnyis rab tu byung nas dgra bcom ste 'phags ma de gnyis gcig gi mtshan ni shil ma ta zhes bgyi/ gcig gi mtshan ni gau sha ra zhes bgyi ste/ 'phags ma de gnyis kha che yul nas nam mkha' la lding ste/ ma rgyal mo'u rong gi dge ba'i
<p>187a</p>
<p>187a.1</p>bshes gnyen du gshegs te/ 'phags ma de nyid gnyis kyi slad du rgyal mos ho ran 'dzo'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar klu'i rgyal po hu lor bgyi ba dang / gser gyi skra zhes bgyi ba gnyis srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya kIrti'i bu mo bi zha dza
<p>187a.2</p>yas bu mo 'phags ma dgra bcom ma bi ta she ca'i slad du po lon jo'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes kyis srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya ba la'i bu mo gu zan gyi rgyal mo'i mchis 'brang bgyid pa'i zha phra ba zhes bgyi bas bu mo dge
<p>187a.3</p>slong ma 'phags ma dgra bcom ma bi zha dza ya'i slad du en mo no'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar ser skyas srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya ba la zhes bgyi bas snga slad du sems can mang po zhig bkum nas 'gyod pa skyes te/ bsod nams phal cher bgyis/ mchis 'brang yang thar par
<p>187a.4</p>btang nas 'phags ma dgra bcom mar gyur pa'i slad du dad pa skyes nas kho mo no no'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar rnam thos kyi sras kyis srung ngo // //de nas li rje'i blon po a ma ca khe meg ces bgyi bas phu bo'o spun gsum gdugs gcig tu bkum nas/ ma yang thar bar zhugs
<p>187a.5</p>nas de nyid du a ma ca khe meg gis gus sde re ma'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ de ltar lha nam mkha'i spyan dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon yang dag shes kyis srung / de nas rgyal po bi dza ya dza ya zhes bgyi bas o sku'i rgyal po'i bu mo mchis 'brang du blangs te/ rgyal mo des dge ba'i bshes gnyen
<p>187a.6</p>'phags ma dgra bcom ma gzhe ma'i slad du o ska no'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar lha mo zhes bgyi bas srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra mas kus pa'i or myong nag gi gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ nang kor ma mang zhig thar par skyes nas da ltar rgyal po ku na'i srung ma'i lha mo
<p>187a.7</p>gser gyi me tog dang / lha mo dung can gnyis srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya ba las cu gun pan gyi rgyal po'i bu mo shu to ka zhes bgyi ba mchis 'brang du blangs pa'i bu mo dge slong ma dgra bcom ma a sho ka shI la'i slad du gtso'u no'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/ da ltar lha a ba lha dang / lha 'dzam
<p>187b</p>
<p>187b.1</p>b+ha ke ru ta zhes bgyi ba gnyis srung // //de nas rgyal po bi dza ya sing ha'i mchis 'brang ga 'jag gi rgyal mo a l+yong dza zhes bgyi ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen du shu lig nas dge slong ma 'phags ma dgra bcom ma bdun gshegs pa'i slad du rgyal po bi dza ya sing has khye sho no'i gtsug lag khang
<p>187b.2</p>brtsigs te/ da ltar lha ser skyas srung / rgyal po bi dza ya sang gra ma rgyal po bgyid pa'i tshe kha che'i yul nas dge slong ma 'phags ma dgra bcom ma shI la ta dang / gau shur+ya zhes bya ba gnyis nam mkha' las lding ste gshegs nas slad kyis khyim bdag na no bod bgyi ba'i khyim drung du bzhugs nas rgyal
<p>187b.3</p>po bi dza ya sang gra ma la smras pa/ rgyal po chen po dog sa 'di ni sngon sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' swa shang zhes bgyi bar gyur pa na/ bram ze la bu ming sring gnyis yon du phul te/ phrin las dka' ba rnam gcig mdzad
<p>187b.4</p>pa'i sa 'dir lags pas 'dir gtsug lag khang cig brtsig par rigs so zhes bgyis pa dang / khyim bdag na mo bod ces bgyi ba de yang dad pa skyes nas/ khang khyim dang sa de yang yon du phul nas/ rgyal pos kyang gtsug lag khang zhig brtsigs/ yon bdag
<p>187b.5</p>las kyang ming dras nas gtsug lag khang gi mtshan yang na mo 'bu gdong zhes bya bar btags/ da ltar klu'i rgyal po hu lor dang / lha gser gyi skra zhes bgyi bas srung / de nas li rje'i blon po 'da' no ya zhes bgyi ba zhig gis tshong 'dus bar mar sku gzugs chen po bgyis pa las
<p>187b.6</p>slad kyis yang li'i blon po a ma bi dad kyi sku gzugs chen po'i lha zhig ral du gyur pa yang gsos/ kong sheng gi dge slong ma'i slad du 'da' no yo na'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs te/da ltar rnam thos sras kyis srung / 'u then na dge 'dun sde gnyis bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag
<p>187b.7</p>khang chen por rtse ba ni sku mkhar gyi nang dang / slad rol na drug cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs/ gtsug lag khang 'bring du bgyi ba ni dgu bcu rtsa lnga lags/ gtsug lag khang chung ngur bgyi ba ni brgya bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad bzhugs/sgo sgo'i mchod pa'i lha khang chung ngu dang / yon bdag ma mchis pa'i
<p>188a</p>
<p>188a.1</p>lha khang dang / mchod rten gyi sku mkhar gyi nang dang / slad rol gyi tshar yan chad na sum stong drug brgya brgyad cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs/ 'u then na dge 'dun sgos 'tsho yan chad byi ba lo la brtsis na khri tsam zhig bzhugs/ mdo lo dang me skar phyogs na gtsug lag khang chen po ni
<p>188a.2</p>bzhi zhig bzhugs/ sgo sgo'i lha khang dang yon bdag ma mchis pa'i lha khang chung ngu ni brgya lhag tsam bzhugs/ dge 'dun nyi shu tsam bzhugs/ kam shed dang pho nya dang / be+e rga 'dra dang / o rgu yan chad ji la man chad sku mkhar gyi nang dang / slad rol gyi mtshar yan chad na gtsug lag khang chen po nyi shu
<p>188a.3</p>rtsa gsum bzhugs/ gtsug lag khang 'bring ni nyi shu rtsa gcig bzhugs/ gtsug lag khang chung ngu nyi shu rtsa gsum tsam bzhugs/ sgo sgo'i mchod pa'i lha khang chung ngu dang chod rten chung ngu ni spyir brgyad brgya sum cu rtsa dgu bzhugs/ dge 'dun sde gnyis las rkyen pa dang / sgo 'tsho
<p>188a.4</p>yan chad spyir bzhi brgya sum cu rtsa brgyad bzhugs/ gyil kyang man chad kong sheng dang / dur+ya yan chad sku mkhar gyi nang dang / slad rol gyi tshar yan chad na gtsug lag khang chen po bco lnga tsam bzhugs/ sgo sgo'i lha khang chung ngu dang / yon bdag ma mchis pa'i lha khang chung ngu dang / mchod
<p>188a.5</p>rten yan chad bzhugs/ dge 'dun sde gnyis las rkyen pa dang / sgo 'tsho yan chad spyir dgu brgya drug cu rtsa gsum bzhugs/ rgyal po sa nu'i tsha po rgyal po bi dza ya saM b+ha ba zhes bgyi ba'i tshe/ thog ma li yul du chos byung ste brtsis na khyi lo'i shol bor ba'i ston zla tha chungs yan chad
<p>188a.6</p>dgung lo stong nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa drug tsam lags/ 'phags pa zla ba'i snying pos zhus pa dang / lha mo dri ma med pa'i 'od kyis zhus pa dang / 'phags pa dgra bcom pa dge 'dun 'phel gyis lung bstan pa rnams dang mthun par li'i yul dang / der li rje'i rgyal po rnams kyis
<p>188a.7</p>'phags pa rnams spyan drangs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / de'i gzhi gtsug lag khang dang / lha khang dang / mchod rten rnams ji ltar bzhengs pa dang / dge 'dun sde gnyis ji ltar spel ba'i tshul rgyas par bstan pa li yul lung bstan pa zhes bya ba rdzogs so// //
